Ayssi comensan las paraulas de Albucasim .	The words of Albuquisim begin here.
O, filhs, pus yeu he a vos complit aquest libre, le qual es le derier de la sciencia de medicina, per le compliment de lu so consequit la fi en lu, e per las exposicios de lu, e per las declaracios de lu, es a mi vist que yeu complesca aquel a vos am aquest tractat, le qual es partida de la operacio am ma, so es cyrurgia.	Oh sons, I have now completed this book for you, which is the last of the science of medicine, because its conclusion was reached through him, and through his explanations, and through his declarations, it seems to me that you will be able to complete that which belongs to you in this treatise, which is a part of my operation, namely surgery.
Quar la operacio am ma es prostrada en nostre regio e en nostre temps de tot privada, entro que fort leu peric la sciencia de lu, e le vistigi de lu es ostat; e no romasero de lu sino alcunas petitas descripcios en les libres dels Antics, les quals mudero las mas e endevenc ad aquels error e heyssitacio entro que son clausas las entencios de lu e es elonguada la forsa de lu e l’art.	Since my operation is now obsolete in our region and in our time, completely private within itself, except that a little bit of science remains, and the vestiges remain, but there are no more than some small descriptions in the books of the Ancients, which have changed the most and deviated into those errors and aberrations, until the intentions of it are closed and the force of it is elongated and the art.
E es vist a mi que yeu vivifique aquela am ordenacio de aquest tractat en aquela segon la via de exposicio e de declaracio e de abreviacio; e per que vengua am las formas dels ferramentz de cautheri e dels autres instrumentz de la obra cum sia per addicio de la declaracio, e per preparacio de lu, la qual causa es necessaria.	And it seems to me that you revitalize that ancient order of this treatise through the way of exposition and declaration and abbreviation; and because I added the forms of instruments such as cauterizers and other tools of the work for the purpose of supplementation of declaration, and preparation for use, which is necessary.
Mays la causa per la qual no es atrobat bo artifex am la sieua ma en aquest nostre temps, es quar la art de medicina es longua, e que cove le sieu actor denant aquo esser excercitat en la sciencia de anotomia la qual recontec Gualia entro que sapia les juvament dels membres e las formas de aquels, e la conjunctio e la separacio de lor; e haia la conoyssensa dels osses, dels nervis e dels lacertz, e·l nombre de aquels, e la egrecio de lor; e de las venas pulsatils e de las quietas, e dels locs del eyssiment de lor.	However, the reason why a good craftsman cannot be found with his own hand in our present time is because the art of medicine is long, and it requires its practitioner to be exercised in the science of anatomy which was known by Galen so that he could know the joints of the members and their forms, and their conjunction and separation; and have knowledge of bones, nerves, and ligaments, and their number, and their arrangement; and of the pulsating veins and quiet ones, and the places of their effusion.
E per aquo ditz Ypocras que am u nom es mot, mays en l’obra petit, e majorment en la art de la ma.	And therefore Hippocrates says that a name is a mere sound, but in the work small, and most of all in the art of surgery.
Mays nos ja avem dit de aquel en l’introit de aquest libre; quar qui no es scient aquo que li avem dit de anotomia, no es evacuat que no caia en error per la qual siran mortz les homes, ayssi cum yeu he vist trops de aquels, quar alscus son formatz en esta sciencia e gettan se de aquela ses sciencia e ses experiment.	But we have already said that about him in the introduction to this book; because whoever is not knowledgeable about what we have said about anatomy will not be spared from falling into error, by which men will die, just as I have seen many of them, since some are formed in this science and take themselves for experts without knowledge or experience.
Quar yeu vi un metge folh e enperit aver incidit un apostema escrophilos en le colh de una femna, e incidic alcunas arterias del colh per que fluic gran sanc entro que la femna cazec morta entre las mas de lu.	Because you saw a foolish and inexperienced doctor who had inserted an abscess on the throat of a woman, and had cut some arteries in the throat so that a great deal of blood flowed, and the woman died between the others.
E vi un autre metge que pres que el traguera una peyra d’un home le qual avia procesit en sa etat, e la peyra era gran, e venguet a lu e trayssec aquela peyra am un tros de la vesiqua, per que aquel home al tertz dia es mort.	And I saw another doctor who, without realizing it, pulled out a gallstone from a man who had already developed an illness in his condition, and the gallstone was large, and he brought it to him and left that gallstone with a piece of the bladder, so that that man died three days later.
E yeu ja apelat fuy a estrayre aquela, e vi que per la grandesa de la peyra e per la disposicio del malaute conogui subre lu que morira.	And you had already asked to remove it, and I saw that because of the size of the gallstone and the condition of the patient, one could infer that he would die.
E vi un autre metge le qual prenia stipendic de un duc de nostra terra per cyrurgia, e endeven a un crastrat negre le qual era deves lu fractura en la coyssa de lu; e perparec le metge am la sua ignorancia, estrayssec la fractura, sobre la plagua, am pulvinas e astelas am forta strectura, e no layssec a la plagua espiracio.	And I saw another doctor who received payment from a duke of our land for surgery, and he set to work on a blacksmith's Negro who had a fracture in his thigh; and the doctor, with his ignorance, removed the fracture, on top of the wound, with pulleys and stays with strong tension, and did not allow the wound to breathe.
E aprop le desliet segons los sieus desiriers, e aprop le relieg, e aprop le leyssec per alcus jorns e comandec que nos deslies le liament; e estec ayssi entro que la coyssa e·l pe foro apostematz, e pervenguet a perdicio.	And then he bound it according to his desires, and then he re-laced it, and then he let it stay for some days and commanded that we loosen the bandage; and it became such that the thigh and leg were gangrened, and it led to destruction.
E yeu fuy apelat a lu, e aparelhegui a desliar le liament, e conseguida es tranquilitat e enayssi amermet de sas dolors.	And you were called to him, and we loosened the bandage, and subsequently he experienced calmness and alleviation from his pains.
Mays empero ja corrupcio era confermada en le membre, per que no pogui refrenar aquela, e no cessec perambular la corrupcio en le membre entro que·l malaute peric.	But meanwhile corruption was already confirmed in the member, so that it could not be restrained, and did not cease to spread corruption in the member until the patient peril.
E vi un autre metge le qual perforec un apostema cancros, e fo ulcerat aprop alscus dias, entro que foc magnificada la malicia de lu am lo senhor de lu.	And I saw another doctor who opened up a cancerous abscess and had it ulcerated about four days later, until the great evil of his patient's lordship was revealed.
La qual causa es quar le cranc caut es pur de humor melencolic, lahoras no cove que pervengua a lu am ferr de tot, sino que sia an membre le qual suffertes que de tot fos hostat.	Which is because the cancerous abscess is pure of melancholic humor, so that it does not need to come to him with force from all sides, but rather be in a member which suffered as if it was being hosted.
E per aquo, filhs, necessari es a vos que la operacio am ma sia devisada en dos devesios: so es en operacio a lu qual es associada salut, e en obra am la qual es perilh en las majors disposicios.	And therefore, sons, it is necessary for you that my operation be divided into two parts: one being the operation associated with health, and another being the work in which there is danger in the greater dispositions.
E yeu ja he exsitat aquo en tot loc de aquest libre en le qual venc opperacio en la qual es error e temor; per que necessari es a vos que guardetz aquo e layssetz aquel, per que les folhs no atrobo via a parlar e a vos desonestar.	And you have already existed in every place of this book where the operation is in which there is error and fear; therefore it is necessary for you to guard this and leave that aside, so that foolish people do not find a way to speak and to deceive you.
E donc prenetz las vostras armas am sollicitut e am proteccio de Dieu , e les vostres malautes am falicitat e am fermetat.	And therefore take up your arms with solicitude and protection of God, and your patients with felicity and firmness.
E usatz de la milhor via per la gracia de Dieu perdusent a salut e a lausabla successio, e laysatz las malautias terriblas de difficil sanacio, e ostatz las vostras armas de aquo que vos fa temer, per so que ysitatio en vostra fe e en le vostre nom no vos evasisca: quar mays es remanent a la vostra gloria, e pus aut en le mon e en derier a las vostras sanctitatz.	And use the best way with the grace of God and persevere in losing one's life and gaining a glorious succession, and leave behind terrible diseases that are difficult to heal, and keep your arms from this which makes you fear, so that your station remains in your faith and in your name, lest it escapes: for it is more remaining at your glory, and more so in the world and in the end to your sanctity.
Gualia ja diyssec en alcunas sieuas monicios:	Galen has said in some of his own writings:
“No mediquetz malautia mala, per so que mals metges no siatz nompnatz”.	"Do not medicate bad diseases, lest bad doctors be unnamed".
E yeu ja he devesit aquest libre segontz tres capitols.	And you have already divided this book into three chapters.
Comensa la divisio del libre, e primier de la primieyra partida.	Here begins the division of the book, and first of the first part.
Le primier capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, en las formas dels instrumentz e en les ferrementz dels cauteris, e de aquo que necessari es en la opperacio.	The first chapter arranged from head to foot, in the forms of instruments and in the ironworks of cauterizers, and from what is necessary in the operation.
La divisio de la segonda partida.	The division of the second part.
Le segon capitol, de siccio e perforacio, e de ventosas, e de plaguas, e de extractio de sagetas e de semblantz ad aquelas, tot capitolat e ordenat de las formas dels instrumentz.	The second chapter, on cicatrization and perforation, and on cupping, and on wounds, and on the extraction of splinters and similar things to those, all chaptered and ordered in the forms of instruments.
Divisio de la tersa partida.	Division of the third part.
Le tertz capitol, de restauracio e de dislocacio, e de curacio de torcio e de semblantz ad aquels; capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, e de las formas dels instrumentz.	The third chapter, on restoration and relocation, and on the cure of torticollis and similar things to those; chapter ordered from head to foot, and in the forms of instruments.
De cauteri am foc e am medicina aguda e rememoracio de la opperacio.	Of cauterizers with fire and acute medicine, and remembrance of the operation.
Am aquel comensa le tractat de tot le libre.	With that begins the treatise of this entire book.
Cove que yeu digua la qualitat dels juvamentz de aquel cauteri e dels noccumentz de lu, e en qual compleccio sia prohibit cauteri.	You should know what kind of joints that cauterizer is suited for and which ones it is not suitable for, and in what condition it should be prohibited to use.
Donc dic que·l sermo de la qualitat del juvament de cauteri e del noccument de lu es sermo lonc e prolixs, e subtil per sciensa, e secret amaguat; e ja de lu a parlat gran multitut de savis, e de lu se son desacordatz, et a mi abasta un petit dels sermons de lor, temen perlonguacio.	So I say that the sermon on the quality of the joint of cauterizer and its necessity is a long and prolix one, subtle by science, and secret hidden; and already many wise men have spoken about it, and they have disagreed among themselves, and to me it suffices to share a small part of their sermons, fearing prolivity.
E donc dic que cauteri comfereys a tota compleccio universalment la qual es am materia o ses materia, exceptat dos compleccios, las quals son compleccios caudas ses materia .	And so I say that cauterizer is suitable for every universal condition that is in material or its matter, except for two conditions, which are conditions where the material is lacking.
En la compleccio cauda e secca am materia se desecordero; quar alcus dyssero que cauteri es juvatiu ad aquela, e les autres dyssero le contrari de aquel, que cauteri no es convenient en malautia la qual es per qualiditat e per siccitat, quar natura del foc es qualiditat e siccitat, e enconvenient es que malautia cauda e secca am aquo que es caut e sec sia sanada.	In the dry and parched condition with material that dries out; for some will say that cauterizer is helpful in this case, while others will say the opposite of this, that cauterizer is not suitable for a disease that is due to quality and dryness, because the nature of fire is quality and dryness, and it would be inconvenient to apply heat and dryness to a dry and parched condition.
E diysec aquel que ditz le contrari de aquel, que per cauteri es fayt juvament en tota malautia cauda e secca que ve en les cors dels homes, quar quan tu comparas le cors de home e las humiditatz de lu a la compleccio del foc, atrobas le cors de home freg.	And those who say the opposite of this will say that by cauterizer it is made to join together in all dry and parched diseases that are found in the bodies of men, for when you compare the body of man and its moistures to the condition of fire, you find the body of man cold.
E yeu dic per le sermo de aquel, que esperiment aquo ja a mi alscunas vetz a descubert.	And I say by this sermon that I have experimented with it many times to discover.
Mays empero no cove que vengua sobre aquo aquel que ja es exproat e excersitat en le capitol de cauteri per derier exercici, e a conogut la diversitat de la compleccio dels homes e la disposicio de las malautias en lor meteyssas, e las causas de aquelas, e·ls accidentz de lor, e l’espasi del temps de aquelas.	But I do not think it necessary to repeat what has already been explored and exercised in the chapter on cauterizing by last exercise, and to be familiar with the diversity of human conditions and the disposition of diseases in their respective cases, and the causes of those, and the accidents that occur in them, and the space of time that those take.
Mays en las autras compleccios, no es sobre vos temor, e majorment en las malautias fregas e humidas, quar ja totz les metges se son acordatz sobre aquels, e no so desecordatz en le juvament am cauteri en aquelas.	But in other conditions, there is no fear for you, and especially in cold and humid diseases, since all doctors have agreed on those, and are not discordant in the joining of cauterizing in those.
E sapiatz, filhs, que del secret de curacio per cauteri am foc e de la bontat de lu, so sobre cauteri am medicina comburent, es quar le foc es simple, la accio del qual no perven sino al membre le qual es cauterizat e no notz al autre membre am lu ajustat sino am petit nocument.	And know, sons, that from the secret of cure by cauterizing with fire and its goodness, so much is said about cauterizing with medicine, it is because fire is simple, whose action only reaches the member being cauterized and does not harm another member adjusted to it except for a small disturbance.
Mays la accio de medicina comburent perven ad aquel en les membres le qual de lu alunhat, e fort leu fa venir en le membre malautia de dificil sanacio e fort leu ausit.	But the action of medicine combined reaches that member which is distant from it, and very easily brings illness to the affected member with difficult healing and often stays.
Mays le foc, per la sua sublimitat e de la sua substancia bontat, no fa aquo sino que superfluisca E ja es a nos conogut per experiment e per longitut de servitut de studi am l’art sobre le veritat de las causas; e per aquo yeu so excusat de la longitut del sermo E si no fos que no es legut al mieu libre en aquest pausero a vos secret amaguat am le foc, e la qualitat de la operacio de lu en les cors e de la sieua expulcio per la qual expellis las malautias, am sermo philosophic demostratiu, le qual siria acuit en las vostras pessas.	But the fire, by its subtlety and good substance, does nothing more than to superfluously add. Already we have known through experiment and long service of study in the art over the truth of causes; and therefore I am excused from the length of this sermon. And if it were not that the secret hidden with the fire is not read well in this pause to you, and the quality of the operation of it in the bodies and its expulsion by which it expels diseases, with a philosophical demonstration sermon, which would be sharp in your breasts.
E sapiatz, filhs, que els se desacordan del temps en le qual es convenient far cauteri e pausan le milhor temps de primaveyra.	And know, sons, that they disagree on the time when it is suitable to perform cauterizing and pause the best time of spring.
E yeu dic que cauteri es convenient en tot temps, per so que le nocument per le temps accident es submergit en le juvament de aquo que am le cauteri es atirat, e majorment si le cauteri es per dolors o de dolors necessaries, fortz e fistinas, las quals no suffertan tarditat per so que es temut de aquelas que vengua malicia, que es major que petit nocument entrant per lo temps.	And I say that cauterizing is suitable at any time, because the harm caused by the timing of an accident is submerged in the joining of what attracts to cauterizing, and most especially if the cauterizing is for pains or necessary pains, strong and fierce, which do not suffer delay for fear of those that would bring malice, which is greater than a small harm entering through time.
E aysso no catz en vostras pessas, o, filhs, aquo no estiman sino le poble vulguar e les fols metges, so es que ad aquela malautia que es sanada per cauteri no es redicio tot temps, e pausan aquel consequen.	And thus it does not occur in your minds, or sons, that this is not esteemed except by the common folk and foolish doctors, so that for that disease which is cured by cauterizing, there is no reduction of time, and pause that consequence.
E la causa no es ges ayssi quo els cuydan per aquo, quar cauteri no es sino en loc de medicina la qual altera la compleccio e esicca las humiditatz las quals son causa per que veno las dolors.	And the cause is not thus as they say for that reason, because cauterizing is only a place of medicine which alters the condition and dries out the humors which are the cause why pains come.
Mays empero cauteri superflueys sobre la medicina per volicitat de la sua valitut e vertut de la sua operacio e grandesa del sieu senhor.	But in any case, cauterizing is superfluous over medicine due to the desire for its value and virtue of its operation and greatness of its lord.
E es possible que la sua malautia retorne en alcuna hora del temps, segon la compleccio del malaute e la locacio de la sua malautia, e la vertut de lu, e aquo que es preparat en le cors de lu de la agreguacio de las superfluitatz en lu, e aquo que es pervengut a lu en la sua acquisicio en viandas e semblantz de aquelas causas; sino que la malautia en la qual sia aministrat cauteri sia malautia subtil en membre de paucas superfluitatz e humiditatz, ayssi cum cauteri de dent per dolor e semblantz ad aquel, possible es que en lu no retorne aquela dolor, mays aquo se fa en petitz.	And it is possible that its disease may return at some hour of time, according to the condition of the patient and the location of his disease, and the virtue of it, and what is prepared in his body from the aggregation of superfluous things, and what is arrived at him in his acquisition through foods and similar causes; unless the disease for which cauterizing is administered is a subtle disease in a member with few superfluous things and humors, such as a tooth cauterization for pain and similar cases, it is possible that it will not return to him, but rather it will be reduced to smallness.
E mays sermo vulgar es que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, e es sermo dreyturier, no ad aquo que els entendo en lu, quar els crezo que no es curacio que aprofieyta am medicina ni am autra causa aprop cauteri.	And it is also said that cauterizing is the last resort of medicine, and it is a sermon of desperation, not because I understand what they mean in that, for I believe that there is no cure that profits through medicine or any other cause approaching cauterizing.
E la causa es en contrari de aquo; e la entencio que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina no es sino quan administram las manieyras de curacio en alcunas malautias, e aquelas medicinas no conferieysso, e aprop en la fi de la causa aministra hom cauteri, e aprofieyta ad aquela.	And the cause is contrary to that; and I understand that cauterizing is the last resort of medicine not just when we administer the methods of cure in some diseases, and those medicines do not concur, and it approaches the end of the cause, then one administers cauterizing, and profits from it.
E lahoras de aqui cat16 que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, no segon la entencio la qual entendo les vulgars e trops dels fols metges.	And hours ago, I said that cauterizing is the last resort of medicine, not according to my understanding which I understand from the common people and the foolish doctors.
E diyssero les antics que cauteri am aur es milhor que cauteri am ferr, e no diyssero aquo sino per la equalitat del aur e sublimitat de la sua sustancia.	And the ancients said that cauterizing with gold is better than cauterizing with iron, and they did not say this except for the equality of gold and its subtlety.
E diyssero que le loc de cauteri no fa brac, cum aquo no sia absolutament vertat, quar yeu ja he aquo proat e he atrobat que aquel no fa aquo sino en alcus cors ses les autres, e cauteri am aquel es bo e milhor que am ferr ayssi quo els diyssero; mays empero quan tu fas cauteri am foc am de aur, no es a tu declarat, quar es egnit segon la quantitat que tu vols per la rugor de l’aur, e quar prepara a recebre freg; e si ajustas sobre lu ignicio se fon l’aur per le foc, e caso en le foc alcunas laminas per que le artifex catz per la occupacio de aquel.	And they said that the place of cauterizing does not take away from it, as this is not absolutely true, for I have already experienced and discovered that it does not do so except in certain bodies where others are not, and cauterizing with gold is good and better than with iron as they say; but when you do cauterizing with fire using gold, it is not declared to you, because it is hidden according to the quantity that you want by the roughness of the gold, and prepares to receive heat; and if you place upon it ignition so that the gold melts by the fire, and case in the fire some plates so that the craftsman can see through the occupation of that.
E per aquo es fayt cauteri am ferr deves nos pus leugerament e pus propdanament a rectitut de operacio.	And therefore it is made to cauterize with iron, that we may proceed more lightly and more promptly to the rectitude of operation.
E yeu ja he ordenat aquest capitol en le cauteri segon capitols, et he ordenat aquels del cap entro les pes, per so que aleugo le demandant aquo que vol de lu.	And I have already arranged this chapter on cauterizing according to chapters, and arranged those from head to foot, in order that the one demanding this may easily find what they want.
De cauteri de dolor de cap per frigiditat e humiditat.	On Cauterizing of Headache due to Frigidity and Humidity.
Le capitol primier.	The First Chapter.
Aquesta cauterizacio confereys a la humiditat e frigiditat sobre le servel accident de la qual so doas causas, so es causa de soda e multitut de flux raumatic, apelat corissa, del cap a las partidas dels huelhs e de las aurelhas fluent, e multitut de dormir, e de dolor de dentz e del guolayro, e universalment de tota malautia que ve per fregiditat, ayssi cum paraliticament, sodo e apoplexio, e semblantz en aquelas malautias.	This cauterizing refers to the humidity and frigidity on the serving of the accident which is caused by two causes, one being the cause of soda and the other being the multitude of raumatic fluxes, called corissa, from the head to the parties of the eyes and ears flowing, and the multitude of sleepiness, and pain in the teeth and the throat, and universally all disease that comes through frigidity, such as paralysis, apoplexy, and similar ones in those diseases.
La forma de aquesta cauterizacio es aquesta, que primieyrament comandes al malaute que sia evacuat am medicina lacsativa le cap mondificant, per tres o per quatre nueytz, segon que exhigeys la vertut del malaute e la edat de lu e la sua costuma.	The form of this cauterizing is this: first, I command the patient to be purged with medicine lactative in the head, for three or four nights, according to what is required by the virtue of the patient and their age and habit.
E aprop comanda li que raza le sieu cap am razor, e aprop fay aquel sezer entre las tuas mas sobre una banca cayrada e que pause las suas mas sobre le pietz sieu.	And then I command him to shave his head with a razor, and have him sit between two mats on a well-cushioned bench, and let his mats rest on his own feet.
E aprop pausa la razit de la tua palma aprop le pous sobre la razit del nas entre les huels sieus.	And then pause the razor's edge on your palm near the nose between their eyebrows.
Mays empero, cum le tieu dit del mieg loc es pervengut, signa aquel loc am tenta, e aprop igneys le cauteri olivar del qual aquesta es la forma:	But since the time has come as you said, mark that place with a tent, and then light the cauterizing oil of which this is the form:
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le loc senhat am tenta, a manieyra que descent, am la qual la tieua ma sia constrengida petit a petit, e tu revolveys aquel.	And then place it on that marked spot with the tent, in a way that descends, so that your hand is gradually constrained little by little, and you revolve it.
E aprop leva la tua ma leugerament e reguarda le loc, e si veses ja del os esser descubert alcuna quantitat del cap, ayssi cum la quantitat de gra de errs, lahoras eleva la tua ma, e si no torno la tua ma am aquel ferr, am autre de aquel, si es enfrigidat, entro que sia vist del os aquo que yeu he dit a tu.	And then lift your hand lightly and gaze at the spot, and if you see that some quantity of bone has been revealed, like the amount of grain of errors, hours elevate your hand, and if it does not return to its original position with that iron, but rather becomes frigidated, until what I have told you is visible to the bone.
E aprop pren un petit de sal e disolveys aquel sobre le loc e leyssa aquel per tres jorns.	And then take a small amount of salt and dissolve it on the spot, and let it stay for three days.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto enbegut en boder e leyssa aquel sobre lu entro que sia destrusida la scara del foc.	And then place it on the wound that is covered with border and let it stay on it until the scar of the fire is destroyed.
E aprop cura le loc am anguent tetrafarmacon entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the spot with four-herb ointment until it is healed.
E ja diyssero que quant la plagua roman uberta, tant mielhs geta le brac, per que es milhor e mays juvatiu.	And they said that as long as the wound remains open, so much the better it gets, for it is better and more healing.
E diyssero alcus de lor que sia cauterizada la codena entro al os, e sia tengut le cauteri entro que sia adhurida alcuna partida de la specitut del os.	And some of them said that the cauterized part should be cauterized to the bone, and held in place until some part of the specificity of the bone is absorbed.
E aprop sia ras aquo que es adhust del os, e aprop sia curat.	And then it should be razed what has been adjusted to the bone, and then it should be cured.
E diyssero autres que am lo cauteri pervengua al derier, entro que enprema en le os forta enprecio entro que le os caga, e aquesta es la forma de alphecati petit:	And others said that with the cauterizing it should come to an end, and then it should press strongly into the bone until the bone cracks, and this is the form of little alphecati.
E estiman de aquel loc expiran la vapors del cap.	And they believe that from that spot the vapors of the head will evaporate.
E sia tenguda la plagua uberta per lonc temps, e aprop sia curada entro que sia consolidada.	And the open wound should be kept for a long time, and then it should be cured until it is consolidated.
Mays a mi no so vistas aquestas doas specias de cauteri de tot, sino en alcus homes segon via de temor; e layssa aquel, deves mi, milhor es am salut, quan es; quar le cap es develitat per solucio de continuitat de lu ayssi cum havem testificat en les autres membres, e majorment quan le cap del malaute es de freul natura.	But to me, it is not visible in these two species of cauterizing at all, except in some men according to the way of fear; and I leave that, you should know, better for health when it is so; because the head has been developed by the solution of continuity there, just as we have testified in other members, and especially when the patient's head is of a frigid nature.
E la specia de cauteri primieyra es mays salva e milhor deves mi; e de aquela husi e am aquela obra am salut.	And the first species of cauterizing is more saved and better, according to my judgment; and from that house and with that work, there is health.
Capitol segon.	Second Chapter.
Del cauteri del cap.	On Cauterizing of the Head.
Quan en tot le cap accideys dolor cronica e longua e aquo es en le malaute prolonguat, e usa de gerras e de cochias e de capipurges e de emplaustres e de guatz e de cadels e de gualinas e de semblantz, e majorment si ja es cauterizat am un cautere le qual recontam e no aprofieyta a lu deguna de aquelas causas, lahoras considera quar si le cap del malaute es de fort creacio en la sua natura; e no es freul et atroba mot gran freg, lahoras aquel cauterisa am autra cauteri dejos aquel un pauc.	When chronic and long-lasting pain occurs throughout the head in a patient who is prolonged, and uses various remedies such as plasters, poultices, ointments, powders, and balms, and especially if it has already been cauterized with one cauterizing which does not benefit him at all, then consider whether the patient's head is of strong creation in its nature; and since it is not frigid and finds no great relief, then cauterize another cauterizing over that little bit.
E aprop cauterisa aquel sobre le corn del sieu cap am cauteri entro que la codena es partida.	And then cauterize it on the horn of his head with a cauterizing until the bone is split apart.
Incisa la codena e sia descuberta del os la quantitat la qual havem recontat e cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en la partida deriera del cap en le loc le qual es apelat vas, — e es aquel loc en le qual es pausada ventosa.	Cut the bone and uncover the quantity of bone that we have described, and then cauterize it with a cauterizing in the rear part of the head at the location called "vas", which is the place where the wind blows.
Et alleuja la tua ma en aysso, e no descobras le os, quar le malaute per aquo atroba mot gran dolor diversa de la dolor de totz les autres cauteris del cap.	And raise your hand in this way, and do not uncover the bone, for the patient by doing so will experience a great deal of pain different from the pain of all other cauterizations on the head.
E yeu diyre aquest cauteri en son loc, quar cove que·l cauteri am le qual so cauterisatz les corns del cap e le occiput es pus subtil cauteri que aquel am le qual es cauterisat le mieg loc del cap; e aquesta es la forma de lu.	And you should say this cauterizing in its place, for it is necessary that the cauterizing which cauterizes the horns of the head and the occiput is more subtle than that with which the middle part of the head is cauterized; and this is its form.
Capitol ters.	Fourth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de emigranea no-antiqua.	On Cauterizing of Old Hiccups.
Quan endeve en la partida del cap dolor sodo, o es stenduda dolor entro al uelh, sia evacuat am medicinas le cap mondificantz, e sia aministrada l’autra curacio, la qual yeu he dita en las devesios de las malautias; e tot no aprofieyta, lahoras cauterisacio en lu es en dos manieyras: o cauterisacio am medicina acuta comburent, o am ferr.	When there is dull pain in the head or it spreads to the eye, and medicine lactative has been purged, and another cure has been administered, which I have described in the divisions of diseases; and all does not benefit, then cauterizing in two ways: either with medicinal acuteness combined, or with iron.
Mays cauteri am medicina comburent es que tu prenguas una dolsa de alh, e escorgas aquela e abcindas las extremitatz de lu de amdos les caps.	But cauterizing with medicinal acuteness is when you take a piece of aloes, scrape it and cut off the extremities from both ends.
E aprop incideys le loc de la dolor en la templa am una lanceta lada entro que sia en lu feyt loc dejos la codena, entro que sia occultada.	And then make an incision in the place of pain on the temple with a well-sharpened lancet until it makes a spot below the bone, so that it is hidden.
E aprop strenh sobre lu am stopada per descent constreccio, e layssa aquel per le spazi de tres horas; e aprop deslia le e tratz le alh, e laysa la plagua per dos o per tres jorn, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto submergit en boder entro que le loc fassa brac.	And then press strongly on it with a stopper to prevent further constriction, and leave it for the space of three hours; and then remove the aloes, treat the wound, and let it stay for two or three days, and then place on it a poultice submerged in border until the spot becomes healed.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment until it is healed.
E si tu voys, fe aquo am alcunas medicinas comburentz las quals yeu he scriutas en le douse tractat de medicinas comburentz.	And if you wish, do the same with some medicinal combinations which I have written in the two treatises on medicinal combinations.
Mays la cauterisacio am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: igneys per cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	But the cauterizing with iron according to this manner: ignite by fire of which this is the form:
e es apelat claus clavilhs, quar le cap de lu es ayssi cum forma de clavel en le qual es alcuna curvitat, e·n le mieg loc de lu es eminensia petita.	and it is called "claus clavilhs", because the head of it is like a shape of a clove in which there is some curvature, and in the middle part of it is a small prominence.
E aprop pausa sobre loc de la dolor, e rete la tua ma — per que no sia adhurida la arceria la qual es dejos — e revol le ferr petit a petit am velocitat.	And then place it on the spot of pain, and hold your hand steady - so that the arrowhead is not absorbed by the surrounding tissue - and rotate the iron slowly little by little with speed.
E si la quantitat de lu que es adhurida per la specitut de la codena ayssi quo la maytat de lu, e elava la tua ma per so que la arteria no sia adhurida la qual es dejos, per so que no vengua flux de sanc.	And if the quantity of blood that is absorbed by the specificity of the bone is as much as the majority of it, and lift your hand for fear that the artery which is left behind will not be absorbed, so that no flow of blood comes forth.
E aprop enbibeys coto en aygua de sal e pausa aquel sobre le loc, e layssa aquel per tres dias; e aprop pausa coto mulhat am boder, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then soak the cloth in saltwater and place it on the spot, and leave it for three days; and then change the cloth with border, and then cure with ointment until it is healed.
E si voys, cauterisa am la extremitat del cutellari segon cauteri, e guarda te de incisio de arteria en aquesta emigranea propriament no-antiqua.	And if you wish, cauterize with the edge of the cutlery according to the cauterizing, and beware of cutting into the artery in this old hiccup properly.
Capitol quart.	Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio d’emigranea antiqua.	On Cauterizing of Old Hiccups Properly.
Quan tu curas emigranea am aquo que havem dit de la curacio precedent, e aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias, e no aprofieyta la curacio, e vezes per la malautia que no abasta a lu aquo que havem dit del primier cauteri am medicina o del cauteri am foc, lahoras cove que tu igniscas le cauteri cutellar entro que sia albificat, pus que significas sobre le loc de la dolor am linha de longuesa de la qual sia la maytat del dit, o quays aquel; e depausa la tua ma per una veguada e strenh aquela entro incidiscas la arceria e pervengua entro al os.	When you cure emigranea with what we have said about the previous cure and what we have described in the divisions of diseases, and if the cure does not benefit and sometimes the disease is so severe that it does not respond to what we have said about the first cauterizing with medicine or with fire, then you must ignite the cutlery cauterization until it is whitened, because it means on the spot of pain with a line of length which is most of the digit, or whatever; and hold your hand steady for one moment and press strongly there until the artery is incised and reaches the bone.
Empero necessari es a tu que guardes de la continuacio de la mandibula, la qual es mauguda deves la masticacio, e que le lacert no sia adhurit e le nervi le qual mau aquela, e que no s’endevengua espasme.	However, it is necessary for you to be mindful of the continuation of the jawbone, which is damaged by mastication, and that the ligament not be absorbed and the nerves which are affected by this, and that there be no spasms.
E si es sobre la custodia e cautela de flux de sanc de l’arteria que es abciza, quar en la abcizio de lu es temor, e majorment ad aquel le qual ignora aquo que fa e no es studios e esproat; e layssa la operacio en lu al comensament.	And if it is about the custody and caution of the flow of blood from the artery that is severed, for in the severing of it there is fear, and especially for him who is ignorant of what he does and has not studied or practiced; and leave the operation at the beginning.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio del regiment de flux de sanc accident de la arceria segon la sieua manieyra, en le sieu loc de aquest libre.	And you will find it in the memory of the regimen of accidental bleeding from the artery according to its own manner, in its own place in this book.
E si veses de aquesta malautia que no abaste aquest cauteri e veses le cors del malaute tollerable, cauteriza aquel en le mieg loc del cap ayssi cum havem recontat, e cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And if you see that this disease does not respond to this cauterizing and see the patient's body is tolerable, then cauterize it in the middle part of the head just as we have described, and cure the wound until it is healed.
E si voys, aministra le cauteri le qual havem dit en le capitol de streccio de arceria am cauteri havent dos cotels, e es milhor cauterizacio aquesta e mays conferent.	And if you wish, administer the cauterizing which we have described in the chapter on stretching of artery with two cloths, and it is better this cauterizing and more relevant.
Capitol .v.	Fifth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dolors de aurelhas.	On Cauterizing of Earaches.
Quan en la aurelha ve dolor per freg e es curat am causas lacsativas e am l’autra curacio la qual he dita en la divisio, e no es remauguda la dolor, lahoras igneys le cauteri, e es aquest le qual ha nom puncta, del qual aquesta es la forma:	When in the ear there is pain due to cold and it is cured with lactative causes and with another cure which I have described in the division, and the pain does not subside, then ignite the cauterizing, and this is the one called "puncta", of which this is the form:
E aprop puncta aprop la ignicio, e sia menat al enviro de tota la aurelha ayssi cum roda es revolguda, o en le circuit de quascuna essemps si la dolor es en quascuna.	And then make the puncta approach the ignition, and be brought to the surroundings of all the ear as a wheel is revolved, or in the circle of each example if the pain is in each.
Alonga te am le cauteri de la razit de la aurelha pauc a pauc pus que aias senhat le loc am tenta.	Draw out the cauterizing from the root of the ear little by little until you have marked the spot with intent.
E si le cauteri de detz puntz en tota aurelha, e quays aquela, e aprop cura les locz entro que sian sanatz.	And if the cauterizing is applied to all the points in the entire ear, and those places, and then cure them until they are healed.
Capitol .vi.	Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de turtura.	On Cauterizing of Torture.
Turtura la qual es curada e am cauterizacio no es sino de las specias las quals veno per flecma, segon que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias.	Torture which is cured and by cauterizing there is only of the species that come through flux, according to what we have said in the divisions of diseases.
Esquiva cauterizacio de la specia que endeve per siccacio o per spasme del nervi.	Avoid cauterizing the species which occurs due to dryness or spasm of the nerve.
Quan tu curas aquela specia de turtura am jerras e capipurgi e guarguarismes, e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas le malaute am tres cauteris: la i deves la razit de la aurelha, e·l segon un petit dejos le sieu templar, e le ters deves la conjunccio de doas labias.	When you cure that species of torture with jarrings and capipurgi and guarguarismes, and your cure does not conform, then it is necessary to cauterize the patient with three cauterizations: the first at the root of the ear, and the second a little behind the temple, and the third at the conjunction of two lips.
E pausa lo tieu cauteri per le contrari de la partida malauta, quar mollificacio no ve sino en la partida que apar sana.	And pause your cauterization on the contrary side of the affected part, for softening does not come except in the part that appears to be healing.
E la forma de cauterisacio es que cauterizas aquel am le cauteri en le dreyt de la extremitat de la aurelha pus sobirana un petit sobre le corn del cap, e en le templar autre, la longuesa del qual sia segon la longitut del dit pous, e depausa la tua ma am cauteri entro que sia comburida la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena.	And the form of cauterization is that you cauterize it with the cauterizing on the right side of the extremity of the ear, a little above the horn of the head, and in the temple another, the length of which is according to the length of the thumb's tip, and hold your hand with the cauterizing until the quantity of the majority of the bone's specificity is consumed.
E aquesta es la forma del cauteri, e es specia del cutellari, la forma del qual es denant mesa.	And this is the form of the cauterizing, and it is a type of cutlery, the shape of which is before the table.
Mays empero pus subtil es que aquel un pauc ayssi co vesas; e cove que cotel en lu de superflua groceza un pauc.	But even more subtle is that which you see a little, and it is necessary to temper in it a little of superfluous grossness.
E aprop cura le loc am aquo que es denant procezit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the spot with this water which is before processed until it is healed.
Capitol .vii.	Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio de apoplextia antiqua.	On Cauterizing of Old Apoplexy.
Quan apoplextia es antiquada e curas aquela am aquo que havem dit e no confereys la tua medicacio e le malaute no ha febre, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris: sobre totz les corn del sieu cap; e am cauteri e le mieg loc del cap, ayssi cum havem dit; e am cauteri en le coguot.	When apoplexy is old and you cure it with what we have said and your medicine does not conform and the patient has no fever, then cauterize it with four cauterizations: on all the horns of his head; and with cauterization in the middle part of the head, just as we have said; and with cauterization in the back of the head.
E la manieyra del cauteri es fayta segon que es desus dit.	And the manner of the cauterizing is done according to what has been said above.
E ja es cauterizat sobre la boca del estomac; e es mays derier; e aprop sia curat am aquo que procezeys.	And it is cauterized on the mouth of the stomach; and it is more posterior; and then be cured with water that is processed.
Capitol .viii.	Eighth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de obblivio fayta per flacma.	On Cauterizing of Oblivion caused by Flux.
Cove que sian donatz al malaute en le comensament jerras grans e pilulas le servel mondificantz.	It is necessary that the patient be given in the beginning large jarrings and pills of purgative medicine.
E aprop ras le cap tot del malaute e pausa sus le coguot de lu emplaustre de cetre descrit en le tractat dels emplastres.	And then shave the head of the patient and place on it an ointment described in the treatise on ointments, on the back of the head.
E pausa aquel alcunas veguadas, quar aquel es manieyra de cauteri.	And pause for a few moments, because that is the manner of cauterizing.
E fay aquo segon aquel meteys orde le qual ja he dit.	And do so according to the order which I have already said.
E donc si per aqueles sanat bo es; e sino, lahoras fay a lu tres cauteris en la deriera partida de sieu cap, les quals sian deysendentz de la partida pus sobirana del cap entro a la partida pus dejos del col.	And then if he is healed by that; and otherwise, then do three cauterizations in the back part of his head, which are descendants from the upper part of the head down to the lower part of the neck.
E pausa entre quascun cauteri la grossetut del dit, e aprop cura lo cauteri am aquo que es procedit.	And pause between each cauterization the length of the finger, and then cure with water that has been processed.
Mays si tu vos addicio e le malaute es aquo tollerant, lahoras fay a lu cauteri en le mieg loc; e si voys major addicio, lahora cauteriza aquel sobre les dos corns.	But if you wish to add more and the patient is tolerant, then do the cauterization in the middle part; and if you wish to add even more, then cauterize that on both horns.
Aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat; e sia le cauteri olivar segon la forma denant donat.	And then cure that until it is healed; and be the olive cauterization according to the form given above.
Capitol .ix.	Ninth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de parazili e de mollificacio de tot le cors.	On Cauterizing of Paralysis and Softening of the Whole Body.
Cove que tu procesiscas en mondificacio del cap am jerras e am aquo que havem dit; e aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap, e am cauteri sobre totz les corns del cap, e am cauteri sobre la deriera partida de lu, e am tres cauteris sobre les spondils del col.	It is necessary that you process in the softening of the head with jarrings and with water as we have said; and then shave the head of the patient, and then cauterize it with cauterization in the middle part of the head, and with cauterization on all the horns of the head, and with cauterization on the back part of the neck, and with three cauterizations on the vertebrae of the neck.
E si es necessari en la malautia de mollificacio del cors de trops aquel e les malautes tollerantz e la malautia es fort, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris sobre les spondils del dos, e dererament am cauteri entro que sia comborit de la codena mot de lu, e aleva la tieua ma.	And if it is necessary in the disease of softening of the body for many and the patients are tolerant, and the disease is strong, then cauterize that with four cauterizations on the vertebrae of the back, and gradually with cauterization until it is consumed by the bone's motion, and lift your hand.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat, e aquest sia cauteri olivar.	And then cure that until it is healed, and this be olive cauterizing.
Capitol .x.	Tenth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de epilemcia.	On Cauterizing of Epilepsy.
No es cauterizat le epilemtic sino aquella epilemcia es per flecma.	It is not cauterized the epiletic, but that epilepsy is caused by flux.
E donc cove que mondifiques le cervel de lu al comensament de lu am yeras e am l’autra curacio la qual havem dicta en la divisio quan le malaute es gran e es tollerant la exceperacio de las medicinas.	And therefore it is necessary to soften the brain at first with jarrings and with other cure which we have described in the division when the patient is great and the exception of medicines is tolerated.
E si es enfant le qual no sufferte las medicinas, lahoras aministra guarguarissmes e mastiguatoris le servel mondifican, denant aquo per motz dias, am bonifficacio de las viandas.	And if it is a child who cannot tolerate medicines, then administer guarguarismes and mastiguation with purgative medicine, for four days in advance, with good provision of food.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en le mieg loc del cap segon la manieyra precedent, e am autre cauteri en le occiput de lu, e sobre quascun corn del cap sieu cauterisa.	And then shave the head of the patient, and then cauterize it with one cauterization in the middle part of the head according to the previous manner, and with another cauterization on the back of the neck, and on each horn of the head.
E si le malaute es fort e es tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteris les quals he ditz, en havent paraliticament e mollificacio del cors sobre les spondils del col e les spondils del dos.	And if the patient is strong and is tolerant, then cauterize it with the cauterizations which I say, having paralysis and softening of the body on the vertebrae of the neck and the back.
E sia cauteri olivar segon qu’es precedit.	And be the olive cauterizing according to what has been said before.
Mays si le malaute es enfant, lahoras pausa cauteri subtil segon aquesta manieyra.	But if the patient is a child, then pause with subtle cauterization according to this manner.
Capitol .xi.	Eleventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio de melencolia.	On Cauterizing of Melancholy.
Quan las causas de melencolia so humiditatz corrompudas e flacma gros, lahoras cauteriza aquel am les cauteris les quals havem ditz en le havent paralisi.	When the causes of melancholy are humid and corrupted flux, then cauterize that with the cauterizations which we have said in having paralysis.
E si la causa de melencolia es superfluitat declinant a melencolia, e le cors del malaute es humit, lahoras da ha beure aquo que mundifica le cervel de lu segon aquo que ha precedut en la divisio.	And if the cause of melancholy is superfluity declining into melancholy, and the body of the patient is humid, then give him to drink water that softens the brain according to what has preceded in the division.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop fay tortora decentment fayta de li sobre le cercle, e aprop depausa aquela en le mieg loc del cap.	And then shave the head of the patient, and then make a turban decently made from it over the circle, and then place that in the middle part of the head.
E le malaute sia sesent cayrat, e sia tengut de tota partida.	And the patient shall be kept seated comfortably, and held from all sides.
E aprop pausa liniment; et es pus digne de boder antic de ovelhas.	And then pause with a liniment; and it is more worthy of an ancient border of sheep.
E escalfa aquel sobre le foc per calefaccio temprada per mesura, le qual le dit sufferta quan es mes en lu.	And warm that over the fire with gentle heat, measured by measure, which the patient suffered when it was most in him.
E aprop vuo’ aquel en le mieg loc del cap de lu en le cercle, e leysa lu entro que sia enfregidat.	And then place that in the middle part of the head of him in the circle, and let it be there until it is warmed.
E fay aquo am le malaute en tota semmana una veguada, am le autre regiment de lu bo entro que sia sanat; o si vols, cauteriza aquel fazen petitz puntz segon lo mays de lu, sino que tenguas la ma am un cauteri ayssi ordenat: aquesta es specia de cauteri la qual humecta le cervel am equalitat.	And do this with the patient for one week at a time, with another regimen of good medicine until he is healed; or if you wish, cauterize that making small points according to what is most of it, but keep your hand with a cauterization thus ordered: this is a species of cauterizing which moistens the brain with equality.
E aprop pausa aquel coto enbegut en boder o en grays de gualina.	And then pause that covered in beggar's cloth or in grayish gallinaceous (i.e., old hen) skin.
Capitol .xii.	Twelfth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de aygua descendent en le huel.	On Cauterizing of Water Descending into the Womb.
Quan a tu es declarat le comensament de aygua en le huel per les senhals les quals yeu he ditz en la divisio, lahoras comensa e dona en beure al malaute aquo que mondifique le cap de lu, e guarda aquel de totas humiditatz.	When you are declared the beginning of water in the womb by the signs which I have said in the division, then begin and give to drink to the patient water that softens the head of him, and keep that from all humidities.
E fay aquel suzar en banh en degu per alcus jorns.	And make that sweat in a bath in the degree for some days.
E aprop comanda a lu que raza le sieu cap, e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap; e aprop cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre dos templas si es le comensament de ysement de aygua en dos huels, o de la un latz si es comensamen de l’aygua en un huel.	And then command him to shave his head, and cauterize that with cauterization in the middle part of the head; and then cauterize that with two cauterizations on both temples if it is the beginning of water in two wombs, or on one side if it is the beginning of water in one womb.
Incideys am cauteri totas las venas e arcerias las quals so dejos la codena; e sian les cauteris en aquela lonh en la latitut de las templas.	Cut with the cauterizer all the veins and arteries which are left by the bone; and let the cauterizations be in that length in the latitude of the temples.
E guarda te de fluxs de sanc quan es cauterizat; e si veses de lu fluxs de sanc, osta le am alcuna medicina, la qual es a tu possible.	And beware of fluxes of blood when it is being cauterized; and if you see from him fluxes of blood, stop it with some medicine which is to your power.
E yeu vindre am savieza la qual es en extraccio de arcerias e am abscizio de aquelas e cautela de fluxs de sanc.	And you will come to wisdom, which is in the extraction of arteries and in the absorption of those and caution regarding fluxes of blood.
E alcunas vetz es cauterizat en le cervitz dejos dos osses am dos cauteris dererament produzitz.	And sometimes it is cauterized on the cervical vertebrae left between two bones with two cauterizations produced gradually.
Capitol .xiii.	Thirteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de lacrimas antiquas.	On Cauterizing of Old Tears.
Quan lacrimas dels huels so antiquas assuduament e per las venas e arterias las quals so en le loc manifest del cap defora e es verificat que aquo es superfluitatz frejas flecmatiquas, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteri le qual havem recontat en le capitol de comensament de aygua cazent en les huels, e am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos templas, e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos osses.	When the tears of the womb are old and superfluous, and through the veins and arteries which are in the manifest location on the outside of the head, it is verified that this is a flux of cold and humid fluid, then cauterize that with the cauterization which we have recounted in the chapter of the beginning of water flowing into the womb, and with cauterization in the middle part of the head, and with two cauterizations on the cervical vertebrae left between two temples, and with two cauterizations on the cervical vertebrae left between two bones.
E si indigeyses de addicio, lahoras cauteriza aquel en tot latz de la coa del huel sobre la extremitat del sobrecilh am petit cauteri.	And if you need addition, then cauterize that on the entire back of the womb over the extremity of the forehead with a small cauterization.
Capitol .xiiii.	Fourteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fetor de nas.	On Cauterizing of Stench from the Nose.
Quan tu medicas aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no aprofieyta la tua medicacio, lahoras tu aparelha e dona en beure al malaute las cochias per tres noytz; e aprop ras le cap de lu, e cauteriza le am cauteri migier am cauteri olivar.	When you medicate that with water as we have said in the division and your medicine does not benefit, then prepare and give to drink to the patient cockroaches for three nights; and then shave the head of him, and cauterize it with a gentle olive cauterization.
E aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri clavelh am dos cauteris sobre les dos sobrecilhs dejos les cabels un petit.	And then cauterize that with a clove cauterization and two cauterizations on both sides of the forehead, just above the hair.
E guarda te de la arceria que no incindas aquela.	And beware not to cut into the artery that you find.
E del cauteri clavilh aquesta es la forma.	And of the clove cauterization, this is the form.
Capitol .xv.	Fifteenth Chapter.
De cauteri de mollificacio de palpebras dels huels.	On Cauterizing of Softening of Eyelids of the Womb.
Quan la palpebra del huel es mollificada per malautia o per humiditat, lahoras cauteriza aquela palpebre1 am un cauteri am aquest cauteri lunar; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When the eyelid of the womb is softened by disease or humidity, then cauterize that eyelid with one cauterization with this lunar cauterization; and this is the form of it:
E si vos, cauteriza aquel sobre les dos sobrecils un petit am dos cauteris en tota partida, e sian elonguatz de las timporas.	And if you, then cauterize that on both sides a little above the eyebrows with two cauterizations in all parts, and be extended from the temples.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la quantitat del sobrecil.	And let the length of each cauterization be according to the quantity of the eyebrow.
E no premas trop la tua ma am le cauteri, mays segon la quantitat que la tersa partida de la palpebre sia adhurida.	And do not press too hard with your hand on the cauterizer, but according to the quantity that the third part of the eyelid is absorbed.
Capitol .xvi.	Sixteenth Chapter.
De cauteri de la palpebre del huel quan les pels so convertitz a las partidas dedintz e punho le huel.	On Cauterizing of the Eyelid of the Womb When the Hairs are Converted to the Inner Parts and Punch the Womb.
Quan les pels del huel son convertitz a las partidas dedintz ayssi que pungo le huel, cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, quar cauteri o es am fer o es am medicina comburent.	When the hairs of the womb are converted to the inner parts in such a way that they punch the womb, then cauterize those in two ways, either by fire or by medicine which is complementary.
Si am cauteri de lu am foc, comanda al malaute denant aquo que leyse les sieus pels ayssi cum aquels les quals les mundan, entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz; e si punho aquel deves le lor naysement, lahoras tu strenh les huels de lu am una benda per so que no sia maugut entro que·ls pels sian nascutz.	If by cauterization of fire, command the patient before that they may comb their own hairs as if they were making them smooth, until they are prolonged and equalized; and if you punch that, then you should bind the womb with a bandage so that it is not harmed until the hairs are born.
Donc cum siran nascutz e engualhatz, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop senha sobre la palpebre dels huels de lu am tenta, am senhal le qual sia segon la figura de fulha de merta, e sia le comensament del senhal prop dels pels.	Then when they are born and equalized, pause the head of the patient in your seat, and then sign on the eyelid of the womb with a tent, with a signal which is according to the figure of a mullein leaf, and be the beginning of the signal near the hairs.
E aprop pausa coto enbegut en album de huou o en mucillatge de ptilli sobre le huel.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in almond oil or mucus from papyrus over the womb.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu.	And then ignite the cauterization which this is the form of it.
E aprop cauteriza sobre la figura la qual as senhada, petit a petit, em motas veguadas, entro que sia comburida la superficia de la codena la qual es ayssi cum fuelha de mirta, tota aparent propriament.	And then cauterize on the figure which you have signed, little by little, in many times, until the surface of the bone is burned like a mullein leaf, all appearing properly.
E senhal de sanetat de la tieua obra es que tu vegus la palpebre de l’huel ja esser contrayta e·ls pels de lu esser elevatz deves la punctura del huel.	And the sign of health for this work is that you see the eyelid of the womb already contracted and the hairs of it elevated above the puncture of the womb.
E donc eleva la tua ma e laysa aquel per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eredicada la scara.	And then elevate your hand and leave that for three days, and then pause with a cloth wrapped in borders until the scar is eradicated.
E aprop cura aquela am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with an ointment until it is healed.
Mays si retorna per les pels alcuna causa aprop lor naysement e la palpebra es mollificada, lahoras fay autra vetz le cauteri sobre aquel tot ayssi cum avias fayt primieyrament.	But if some cause returns to the hairs and the eyelid is softened, then do another time the cauterization on that just as you did initially.
Mays si les pels so en la palpebra dejos, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que sia elevada al sieu loc natural e sia engualhat e que les pels no punhan le huelh.	But if the hairs are left in the eyelid, then cauterize that until it is elevated to its natural place and equalized, so that the hairs do not harm the womb.
Mays le cauteri am medicina comburent aquest es que comandes al malaute que leyse les pels entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz, e aprop sia fayta de carta de drap la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	But the cauterization with complementary medicine is that you command the patient to comb their hairs until they are prolonged and equalized, and then make a bandage like a mullein leaf.
E aprop pren de sabo conogut e de caus viva ana unc. .i., o quays aquo, e aprop mescle3 aquelas causas be, e fay aquo am festinacio per so que no sia enfregidat; e aprop expandeys de aquo sobre la carta la qual es fayta ayssi cum forma de fulha de mirtra, e pausa aquel sobre la un huel od amdos; e pausa dejos le huel coto enbegut en album de huou, e el cap del malaute sia en le tieu se.	And take a known saponin and a living cause of an inch. The end. And thus, and then mix those causes well, and make this with a feast for so that it is not warmed; and then spread that water on the bandage which is made like the form of a mullein leaf, and pause that over one womb or both; and pause below the womb cloth wrapped in almond oil, and the head of the patient be in your seat.
E pausa le dit sobre le medicina e prem aquela un petit e no la mauguas entro que lo malaute senta la mordicacio de la medicina, quar mordicacio es en lu ayssi cum de foc.	And then pause the said thing on the medicine and press that a little and not harm it until the patient feels the sting of the medicine, for sting is in him like fire.
E donc cum percevera aquo que el atrobo mordicacio, lahoras leyssa la medicina e mau aquela am le tieu dit; donc cum cessa la mordicacio, lahoras remau la medicina he lava le huel am aygua; e lahoras considera si vezes la palpebra ja es levada ayssi cum es lavada deves la costriccio am foc o am incisio, quar lahoras esta be; e si no torna sobre aquela de la medicina sobre le loc en le qual no ha empremut la medicina e no se denigra entro que sia engualhada la tua operacio e sia contrayt le huel.	And then, when the patient perceives that he feels the sting of the medicine, pause and say to him "Be quiet" and do not harm it until the sting ceases; and then, when the sting ceases, rinse the womb with water; and then consider if the eyelid has already been lifted like it is washed away by fire or incision, for then you are well; and if not, return to that medicine on the location where you did not apply the medicine and do not neglect until your operation is equalized and the womb is contracted.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eradicada la codena de la adhustio, e aprop cura aquel am enguent deafinicon o am autre entro que sia sanat.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in borders until the scar of adjustment is eradicated, and then cure that with an ointment or another until it is healed.
E es necessari a tu, deves la tua operacio que guardes am pervigil diligencia que en le huel no caia re de la medicina, e si la palpebre aprop alscus dias es mollificada e alcuna causa dels pels punh en le huel, lahoras itera la tua medicina sobre aquel loc le qual de la palpebre es mollificat, e propriamen ayssi quo as fayt al comensament, e aprop enaviro lu entro que sia sanat.	And it is necessary for you to diligently watch over your operation so that no residue of the medicine falls into the womb, and if the eyelid becomes softened after some days and any cause of the hairs hurts the womb, then repeat your medicine on that location where the eyelid has become softened, and do it in the same way as at the beginning, and guide it until it is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	And this is the form of mullein leaf.
E sapias que les huels dels homes son diversificatz segon la magnitut e la parvitat, e donc segon aquo es fayta la tua contraccio.	And know that the wombs of men are diversified according to their magnitude and smallness, and therefore, according to this, is made your contraction.
E no sira amaguada la via de rectetut ad aquel al qual es studi en aquesta art.	And let not the way of rightness be hidden from him who studies in this art.
Capitol .xvii.	Seventeenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula que es en le lacrimal de l’huel.	On Cauterizing of Fistula that is in the Lacrimal of the Womb.
Quan tu curas fistula am aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas aquela segon aquesta manieyra: comanda al malaute que pause le cap sieu en le tieu se, e tengua le cap de lu alcun ministre entre las tieuas mas en tal manieyra que no sia maugut ni agitat am le sieu cap.	When you cure a fistula with water as we have said in the divisions of diseases and do not confer your cure, then command that you cauterize it according to this manner: command the patient to pause their head in your seat, and hold the head of them with some attendant between your thighs in such a way that it is not harmed nor agitated with their own head.
E aprop pausa coto enfus en album de huou o en mucellage de ptilli sobre le huel de lu.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in almond oil or mucus from papyrus over the womb of it.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then ignite the cauterization which this is the form:
le qual sia conquau, ayssi cum es forma de cana o de pena de voltor, de la una extremitat am la qual es fayta lo cauteri.	...which shall be curved, like the shape of a cane or a pheasant's tail, from one end to which is made the cauterization.
E si voys, sia penetrant entro a la autra extremitat.	And if you wish, it shall penetrate into the other extremity.
E si vols sia sort ayssi cum tenta.	And if you wish, let it be so as a signal.
Mays empero aquel que es concau es milhor a la tieua obra.	But in any case, that which is curved is better for your work.
E aprop prem la fistula si es uberta, e tra de lu sania et exsicca aquela.	And then press the fistula if it is open, and draw out pus and dry it.
E si no es uberta, lahoras obre aquela e extratz la poyredura de lu.	And if it is not open, then open it and extract the tumor from it.
E aprop pausa sobre lu le cauteri le qual sia be ignit, e te am aquel la tieua ma un petit deves le cauteri del huel a la partida del nas, per so que no erre la tua ma o le malaute sia enquietat, e lahoras pausa le cauteri en le grays del huel e corrompas aquel.	And then pause with the cauterization which is well ignited, and take with that your hand a little bit to apply the cauterization to the womb at the parting of the nose, so that you do not err or disturb the patient, and then pause the cauterization in the gray matter of the womb and corrupt it.
E donc si al comensament del tieu cauteri perve entro al os, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera le cauteri una veguada o dos, si mestiers era; e layssa aquel ayssi per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre aquel coto am boder e enviro lu am enguent exsiccatiu entro que sia sanat.	And then if at the beginning of your cauterization it enters into the bone, that is good; and otherwise, then repeat the cauterization one or two times as needed; and leave that so for three days, and then pause with a cloth wrapped in borders and surround it with an ointment to dry until it is healed.
Mays si eran passatz xi dias e no es sanat, lahoras pausa sobre lu medicina aguda corrosiva entro que l’os sia descubert e sia ras segon que conveneys en le sieu capitol.	But if it is passed eleven days and not healed, then pause with sharp and corrosive medicine until the bone is uncovered and shaved according to what is suitable in your own chapter.
E es autra manieyra de cauteri de fistula la qual alscus primiers diysero: enten al loc de la fistula e fen aquela e aprop pausa en aquela fissura camaen subtil del qual es la forma de lu: E fon en aquela la quantitat de i unc de plom fundut; e te la tua ma am camaem am bona retencio, e no sia maugut le malaute per so que le plom fundut no pervengua al huel de aquel; e cove que pausas sobre le huel del malaute coto enfus en album de huou o en aygua, quar plom adhureys le loc de la fistula e sana aquela per sanacio meravilhora.	And there is another method of cauterizing a fistula which some first doctors said: insert the instrument into the location of the fistula and then pause in that subtle fissure, which is the form of it: And pour into that the quantity of one inch of melted lead; and take your hand with a camel with good retention, and do not let the patient be harmed because the melted lead may penetrate to the womb of him; and pause over the womb of the patient with a cloth wrapped in almond oil or water, for lead adheres to the location of the fistula and heals it through marvelous healing.
E si la fistula es sanada am aquo que havem dit del cauteri e de la curacio, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari aministrar trauc del nas e reduzir la fistula al cors del nas segon que vindra en son loc propri.	And if the fistula is healed with the water that we have said about cauterizing and curing, that is good; and otherwise, then it is necessary to administer a blow through the nose and reduce the fistula to the body of the nose according to what will come in its own place.
Capitol .xviii.	Eighteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la fendedura des potz.	On Cauterizing of the Wound of the Paps.
Motas veguadas accideysso fissuras en las labias, e majorment en las labias dels enfantz.	Many times these fissures occur in the lips, and most especially in the lips of children.
Donc cum tu curas aquelas fissuras am aquo que nos havem dit en las divisios e no aprofieyta la tua cura, lahoras igneys le cauteri petit cutellar segon aquesta forma que s’ensiec:	Then when you cure those fissures with water as we have said in the divisions and your cure does not take effect, then ignite the cauterization with a small knife according to this form that is shown:
E sia la conquavitat de lu segon la subtilitat de cotella.	And be the curvature of it according to the subtlety of a cuttlebone.
Aprop pausa aquel init cuytadament en aquelas fissuras entro que·l cauteri pervengua al preon de las fissuras.	And then pause that instrument carefully in those fissures until the cauterization reaches the root of the fissures.
E aprop cura aquel am cerotz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment until it is healed.
Capitol .xix.	Nineteenth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula en la boca.	On Cauterizing of Fistula in the Mouth.
Quan en la razit de uvula o en le paladar o en las razitz de las dentz endeve apostema e aprop fa brac, e aprop es rompuda, e aprop es antiquada, e corr brac e es fayta fistula, e aprop tu curas aquela e no aprofieyta a curacio, lahoras cove que tu igniscas cauteri segon la quantitat que sia receubuda en la fistula, e aprop met aquel ignit en le trauc de la fistola, e te la tua ma entro que pervengua le ferr ignit al preon de lu, e al derier de lu fazen aysso una veguada o dos; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que nos havem dit de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	When in the root of uvula or on the palate or in the roots of the teeth an apostema forms and begins to break, is broken, and becomes antiquated, and a fistula is formed, and you cure it but your cure does not take effect, then it is necessary that you ignite a cauterization according to the quantity received in the fistula, and then insert that ignited instrument into the track of the fistula, and take your hand until the hot iron reaches the root of it, and at the end of it do so one or two times; and then cure it with water as we have said about curing until it is healed.
E donc si la sania es abscindita e es sanat, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari de descubrir le loc e hostar le os corrumput segon que vindra en son capitol.	And then if the pus is discharged and it is healed, that is good; and otherwise, then it is necessary to uncover the location and expose the corrupted bone according to what will come in its own chapter.
Capitol .xx.	Twentieth Chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dentz e de mollificacio de las angivas.	On Cauterizing of the Teeth and Softening of the Gingivae.
Quan las angivas son mollificadas per humiditat e las dentz son maugudas, e curas aquelas am medicinas e no confereys, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra aprop aysso, enayssi que tu pauses la quanula sobre la dent e entromet en aquela le cauteri ignit festinantment, e te la tieua ma un petit entro que·l malaute cente la calor del foc a la razit de la dent esser pervenguda.	When the gingivae are softened by humidity and the teeth are decayed, and you cure them with medicines but they do not confer, then pause the head of the patient in your seat, and then ignite the cauterization which will come to this, so that you pause the quantity on the tooth and insert into it the ignited cauterization hastily, and take your hand a little bit until the patient feels the heat of the fire at the root of the tooth being reached.
E aprop leva la tua ma, e aprop itera le cauteri alcunas veguadas segon que vols.	And then lift your hand, and then repeat the cauterization several times according to what you wish.
E aprop le malaute huompla la sua boca de aygua de sal e tengua aquela per una hora, e pueys stupa aquela, quar la dent mauguda es fermada e la gengiva mollificada es strenguda e la humiditat corrompuda es exsiccada.	And then the patient will open their mouth with water of salt and hold it for an hour, and afterwards stop it, because the decayed tooth is sealed and the softened gingivae are strengthened and the corrupted humidity is dried up.
Capitol .xxi.	Twenty-First Chapter.
De cauterisacio de dolor de dent.	On Cauterizing of Toothache.
Quan dolor de dent es per fregiditat, o en lu es freg o verm, o no comfereys la curacio am medicina, lahoras cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am boder de vacas, o cauteri am foc.	When toothache is due to coldness, or the tooth is cold or warm, and your cure with medicine does not confer, then cauterize in that location according to two ways: either cauterize with a border of oxen, or cauterize with fire.
Cauteri am boder es que tu prenguas boder de vacas e bulhas aquel en culhe de ferr , e aprop pren coto e envolopa le sobre la extremitat de la tenta, e aprop enmergeys aquel am boder bulhit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolorosa festinantment entro que sia enfregidat.	Cauteri with border is that you take the border of oxen and boil it in a cauldron of iron, and then take a cloth and wrap it around the extremity of the tent, and then immerse that in boiling border, and pause that over the toothache festinatingly until it is cooled.
E aprop itera aquela alcunas veguadas entro que la vertut del foc pervengua a la razit de la dentz.	And then repeat that several times until the virtue of fire reaches to the root of the teeth.
E si voys, submergeys lana o coto en le boder desus dit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolent, e pausa sobre aquel ferr ignit entro que·l ferr pervengua al preon de la conquavitat de la dent.	And if you wish, immerse wool or cloth in the border as said above, and pause that over the aching tooth, and pause on top of that iron ignited until the iron reaches to the root of the curvature of the tooth.
Mays empero la cauterizacio am foc es que tu atendas a la quannula de eram o de ferr, e sia en le cor de lu alcuna grocesa e la acuitat del foc no pervengua a la boca del malaute.	But in any case, the cauterization with fire is that you attend to the quantity of iron or steel, and be in the core of it some roughness, and the sharpness of the fire does not reach the mouth of the patient.
E aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra, e pausa aquel sobre la dent e te la tua ma entro que·l cauteri sia enfregidat; e fay aquo alcunas veguadas quar la dolor sira remauguda o en aquel dia o en l’autre dia.	And then ignite the cauterization according to its form, and pause that over the tooth and take your hand until the cauterization is cooled; and do this several times because the pain will be relieved or in one day or another.
E cove que per empressio de aquel cauteri que·l malaute umpla la sieua boca de bon boder e tengua aquel per una hora e aprop scupa le; e aquesta es la forma del cauteri.	And it is necessary for the patient to fill their mouth with good border and hold it for an hour, and then spit it out; and this is the form of the cauterization.
E cauteriza am qual que tu voys extremittat segon que a tu es possible.	And cauterize as you wish, with whatever instrument or method you can use.
E aquesta es la forma de la cannula:	And this is the form of the cauterizing instrument:
Capitol .xxii.	Twenty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de extrophulos.	On Cauterizing of Exostoses.
