Quan extrophulos so de flecma e de humors fregas e no so hobedientz a digistio per medicinas e tu voys la digistio de aquelas leugerament, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri conquau la forma del qual es aquesta seguen, havent dos extremitatz hubertas per que yesca le fum deves le cauteri per l’autra extremitat, e pausa aquel ignit sobre aquel apostema una veguada, e autre si indigeyses de aquel, entro que pervengua al preon del apostema.	When exostoses are of flesh and humors that are cold and not obedient to digestion by medicines, and you wish the digestion of those slightly, then you ignite the cauterization with a curved shape according to this form, having two extremities humps for the smoke of the cauterization to escape through one side, and pause that ignited instrument on that apostema once, and another if it is needed of that, until it reaches the root of the apostema.
E si l’apostema es pauca, lahoras pausa le cauteri segon la quantitat del apostema, e aprop leyssa le per tres jorns e pausa sobre lu coto enfus en boder entro que sia remaugut aquo que·l foc ha comburit.	And if the apostema is small, then pause the cauterization according to the quantity of the apostema, and then leave it for three days and pause over it with a cloth wrapped in borders until what the fire has burned off is relieved.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent e tentas e draps entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment, poultices, and cloths until it is healed.
E la forma de la cannula o deu cauteri a tal es comveyter.	And the form of the cauterizing instrument or of the two cauterizations to such is as follows:
Capitol .xxiii.	Twenty-Third Chapter.
De cauterizacio de rauquiera de votz e de constriccio de ale.	On Cauterizing of Aphonia of the Voice and Constriction of the Larynx.
Quan las humiditatz veno sobre le quanal del pulmo, e majorment quan aquo es am fregiditat de compleccio, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia evacuat al comensament am medicinas laxativas, e aprop cauteriza aquel deves la razit del golayro en le loc depremegut.	When the humidities come over the quantity of the lung, and most especially when this is due to coldness of constriction, then it is necessary that the patient be evacuated at the beginning with medicines laxative, and then cauterize that in the root of the throat in the location affected.
E guarda te que no pervenguas am le cauteri al golayro ni no comburas de la codena de lu sino un pauc.	And take care not to reach with the cauterization to the larynx nor burn the cord of it, but only a little.
E cauteriza aquel am autra cauteri deves la junctura del col en le derier espondil de lu.	And then cauterize that with another cauterization at the junction of the vertebrae in the last thoracic spine.
E·l cauteri de lu sia clavilh sego la maniera precedent.	And the cauterization of it shall be like a key, as previously said.
E aprop cura aquel am aquo que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with water as preceded until it is healed.
Capitol .xxiiii.	Twenty-Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de malautia del pulmo e de tos.	On Cauterizing of Lung Disease and Cough.
Quan tos e malautia de pulmo so de humiditatz fregas e le malaute no ha febre ni tisic e es malautia antiqua, lahoras cauterisa aquel am dos cauteris sobre la furcula en les locz depremegutz leontz e buoytz; e am autra cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz entre dos mamillos; e sia le cauteri clavilh segon la forma precedent.	When cough and lung disease are of cold humidities, and the patient has no fever nor hiccup, and it is an old disease, then cauterize that with two cauterizations on the furcula in the affected locations; and with another cauterization in the middle location of the chest between two nipples; and let the cauterization be like a key according to the previous form.
E si vols, sia la tua cauterizacio punctan am le cauteri que es apelat puncta, la forma del qual precedeys en la ponctacio de dolor de aurelhas.	And if you wish, make your cauterization punctate with the cauteries that are called puncture, the form of which precedes in the puncturing of earache.
E sian puntz entro cays ad aquels; e aprop cura aquel am aquo meteys que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And make points into those; and then cure that with water, applying as preceded until it is healed.
E ya sia le cauteri haventz tres ramps quar cauterizacio es am aquel: am una veguada podes far tres cauteris segon aquesta forma:	And now the cauteries have three ramps, where cauterization is in that: in one go, you can make three cauteries according to this form:
Capitol .xxv.	Twenty-Fifth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de titillic que es le cap del ajutori.	On Cauterizing of Tittil, which is the Head of the Assistant.
Quan le cap del ajutori es dislocat per causa de humiditatz lubricas e no es fermat en la hora del sieu retornament deves la sua dislocacio entro que sia a lu aquo costuma de retornar, e aprop per un petit movement es deslocat ayssi que s’endeve, ayssi cum nos havem testificat, lahoras cove que primieyrament redusiscas la dislocacio, e aprop le malaute sia reversat sobre le sieu dos o sobre le latz sa; e aprop eleva la codena la qual es en la partida dedintz del citillic a las partidas desus am les ditz de la tua ma sinistra, si la junctura es dislocada a las partidas dedintz.	When the head of the assistant is dislocated due to lubricating humidities and is not fixed in its return movement, and it becomes dislocated again as we have testified, then it is necessary first to reduce the dislocation, and then the patient shall be reversed onto their back or side; and then elevate the cord which is in the departure from behind the citillic to the upper parts with the fingers of your left hand, if the joint is dislocated from behind.
E aprop igneys le cauteri havent dos caps; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cautery with two heads; and this is the form of it:
E aprop cauteriza la codena entro que penetre aquela entro al autre latz; e vindra la figura de cauterizacio lahoras de iv caps cauteris.	And then cauterize the cord until it penetrates that into another side; and the figure of cauterization will be like this, when there are five cauteries.
e so aquel subtils segon la quantitat de tenta; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	and so those subtleties according to the quantity of the tent; and this is the form of it:
E alcunas veguadas es ajustat segon aquest comte i per que son les cauteris .viii.	And some times it is adjusted according to this count, because there are eight cauteries.
E aprop pausa sobre le cauteri porys cuytz am sal, e aprop fay adherir le malaute a trenquilitat, e lo membre no sia maugut per alcun temps entro que sia confortat.	And then pause over the cautery with pores full of salt, and then make the patient adhere to tranquility, and let the member not be decayed for any time until it is comforted.
E si la dislocacio es a las partidas desus e tart es fayt aquo, lahoras cauteriza sobre le muscle am cauteri clavilh o am motz cauteris puntan, quar la junctura es confermada e la humiditat es romauguda e le malaute es sanat.	And if the dislocation is in the upper parts and there is no remedy, then cauterize over the muscle with a cauterization like a key or with multiple punctate cauteries, because the joint is confirmed and the humidity is dried up and the patient is healed.
Capitol .xxvi.	Twenty-Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio del stomac.	On Cauterizing of the Stomach.
Quan veno en l’estomac freg e motas humiditatz entro que aquel extrazo de la sua compleccio e so multiplicatz raumases a lu, e si tu continuas las manieyras de curacio e no confereyso, lahoras cove que le malaute sia sobre le sieu dos ressupinat, e extenda las suas mas e las suas coysas, e aprop cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris: an un cauteri dejos le pietz per la quantitat d’un dit am cauteri clavilh, e am dos cauteris dejos del dos costatz del cauteri, entro que vengua la figura de cauteri triangulada; e elonga entre els que no sian ajustatz que faran poyredura.	When cold and many humidities come into the stomach, and it is thrown out of its composition and becomes multiple rumblings in it, and if you continue with the methods of curing and do not concur, then it is necessary that the patient be turned onto their back and stretched out their arms and legs, and then cauterize that with three cauteries: one on the chest for the quantity of a finger with a key-shaped cautery, and two on both sides of the cautery, so that the figure of triangular cautery appears; and elongate between them so that they are not adjusted to cause pressure.
E si la profunditat del cauteri la quantitat de les dos terses de la grocesa de la codena.	And if the depth of the cautery is equal to the quantity of two-thirds of the thickness of the cord.
E sia la figura del cauteri segon aquesta forma ses addicio, E si vols, cauteriza am gran cauteri en le mieg loc del estomac segon aquesta forma; et aquest sia un cauteri segon la forma de cercle segon aquesta forma:	And let the figure of the cautery be according to this form, and if you wish, cauterize with a large cautery in the middle location of the stomach according to this form; and this shall be one cautery according to the form of a circle, according to this form:
E sia cauterizat l’estomac punctan ad aquel que de aquest cauteri es spaventat: e es que tu senhes sobre l’estomac punt segon la quantitat que voles am tenta, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en les puntz; e aprop cura aquel am la curacio qu’es precedita entro que sia sanat.	And let the stomach be punctured with that which is frightened of this cautery: and it is that you sense on the stomach point according to the quantity you want in tent, and then cauterize those points with a cautery; and then cure that with the curing that preceded until it is healed.
Capitol .xxvii.	Twenty-Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio del fietge fret.	On Cauterizing of the Fettered Foot.
Quan endeve en le fietge dolor per fregiditat o per humiditat o per grossa ventositat entro que de la sieua normal compleccio sia getat per egressio superflua, e es curat le malaute am aquo que havem dit e no comfereys, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre la sua cervitz, e senhes am tenta tres cauteris segon aquesta forma et aquesta quantitat meteyssa sobre le fietge dejos dels ipocondres, la hon perve le decubit de home.	When the pain is in the foot due to coldness or humidity or excessive ventosity, and it has departed from its normal composition by superfluous egression, and the patient is cured with water as we have said but does not concur, then it is necessary that the patient be turned onto their back and stretched out their arms and legs, and sense three cauteries according to this form and quantity on the foot behind the hip bones, so that it reaches the position of a man lying down.
E sia l’espazi le qual es entre quascun cauteri segon la grossetut del dit, e sia le cauteri segon la longitut del cors dreyta.	And let the space between each cautery be according to the thickness of the finger, and let the cauteries be according to the length of a straight arm.
E no compremas la tua am le cauteri mot.	And do not compress your hand with the cauterous motion.
E si la quantitat de aquo que es adhurit la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena, e no y sia pus ajustat; e si le malaute stant sobre les pes de lu; e si no es estant, lahoras sia jassent, le qual ja ha extendudas las suas coysas, e eleve les sieus brasses.	And if the quantity of water that is absorbed is equal to the quantity of the majority of the cord's thickness, and it is not yet adjusted; and if the patient stands on their feet; and if they are not standing, then let them lie down, which has stretched out its legs, and raised its arms.
E es aquesta la forma del cauteri:	And this is the form of the cautery:
E a tu es possible que cauterizes aquestz cauteris am cauteri cutellar, quan es am tu subtilitat e prudencia en l’art.	And it is possible for you to cauterize these cauteries with a knife-shaped cautery, when it is according to your subtlety and prudence in the art.
E guarda te que trop no procesiscas en la cauterizacio, e sia adhurida la specitut de tota la codena per que sia adhurit tot le cors e pervengua entro als budels, quar la codena aqui es subtil; e sapias aquo.	And take care that you do not proceed too quickly in the cauterization, and be careful with the subtlety of all the cord so that it is absorbed throughout the body and reaches into the vessels, for this cord here is subtle; and know this.
Capitol .xxviii.	Twenty-Eighth Chapter.
De perforacio de apostema del fietge am cauteri.	On Perforation of the Aposteme of the Foot with a Cautery.
Quan endeve excitura o apostema en le fietge e voles saber si aquel apostema es en le carn del fietge o en la tunica de lu, lahoras si es en la carn del fietge, le malaute atrobo gravitat e dolor ses acuitat.	When there is an aposteme or excrescence on the foot and you wish to know if that aposteme is in the flesh of the foot or in the skin, then if it is in the flesh of the foot, the patient will be afflicted with gravity and pain with no acuteness.
E si es en la tunica del fietge, am la dolor es acuitat gran e vezes que ja afatiguatz les metges la cura de lu.	And if it is in the skin of the foot, then with great pain and many times that will fatigue even the doctors to cure it.
Donc cove que·l malaute sia enversat sobre la sieua cervit; e aprop senha le loc de l’apostema am tenta; e aprop igneys le cauteri le quel es asemblat a rag, la forma del qual a precedit en l’autra pagina.	Therefore, it is necessary that the patient be turned over onto their back on the pillow; and then sense the location of the aposteme with tentation; and then ignite the cautery which is similar to rag, the form of which has preceded in another page.
E cauteriza am aquel i cauteri entro que tota la codena sia comborida, entro que pervengua al ciphac, entro qu’en yesca sania.	And then cauterize with that same cautery until all the cord is consumed, until it reaches the ciphac, until in such a way that health may ensue.
E aprop cura aquel per curacio dels autres apostemas entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with the curing of other apostemes until it is healed.
E no cove que de aquesta forma de cauteri use sino aquel del qual le estudi en l’art de medicina es prolonguat, e en las mas del qual motas malautias an conogut; mays aquest am esperiment alcunas veguadas sia ardit sobre aquesta operacio, mays empero leyssa aquela deves nos, e es miels.	And it is not necessary that one use this form of cautery except for the one who has studied in the art of medicine and has prolonged it, and whose many maladies have known; but this one may be bold at times on this operation, yet always heed the warning and it will be better.
Capitol .xxix.	Twenty-Ninth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de plauresi.	On Cauterizing of Pleurisy.
Diyssero les antics cauteri de las razitz de aristologia a plauresi frega segon aquesta manieyra esser fazedor, e es aquest que tu prenguas de las razitz de aristologia longa secca una razit pun longua que es trobada, e sia de la grossetut del dit.	The ancient cauteries of the roots of aristology have declared that for pleurisy, it is necessary to cauterize according to this manner, and this is what you take from the roots of aristology, a long dry root that is found, and it is of the thickness of a finger.
E aprop submergeys aquela en oli e eysen aquela al foc, e aprop cauteriza per un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre la continuacio de la furcula am le col; e am dos cauteris petitz dejos guidazi, un pauc declinans a la partida que es dejus la barba, e am dos cauteris en aquo que es declinant entre la quinta costa e la cizena, declinant un pauc a las partidas detras; e am autre cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz; et am autre sobre l’estomac, et am tres cauteris de las partidas detras; et am un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre las dos spallas, e am dos cauteris dels dos latz del pietz, dejos le cauteri le qual es entre doas spallas.	And then submerge that in oil and ignite it at the fire, and then cauterize with a cautery in that location which is between the continuation of the furcula and the collarbone; and with two small cauteries guided by that, one slightly declining towards the party that is below the beard, and with two cauteries on that part that declines between the fifth rib and the navel, declining slightly to the parts behind; and with another cautery in the middle location of the foot; and with another on the stomach, and with three cauteries from behind; and with one cautery in that location which is between the two shoulders, and with two cauteries from both sides of the foot, leaving the cautery which is between two shoulders.
E no cove que compremas la tua ma am le cauteri, ans sia en le manifest de la codena en obra.	And it is not necessary that you compress your hand with the cautery, but rather let it be in the manifestation of the cord in action.
E ja diyssero alscus antics que so alscus dels homes les quals uson de cauteri de ferr semblant a ray e igneysso aquel, e meto aquel en aquel loc le qual es entre las costas, entro que pervenguam am aquel ad aquel apostema e sia foragetada sania, ayssi cum havem dit en l’apostema del fietge.	And already the ancient ones have said that some of the men who used iron cautery like a ray and ignited it, and put it in that location which is between the ribs, until it reaches that aposteme and healthiness is promoted, just as we have said in the aposteme of the foot.
Mays en aquesta perforacio am cauteri no es ses temor, quar hu mor tantost ho accideys en le loc fistula a la qual no es sanacio.	But in this perforation with cautery there is no fear, for as it happens soon after the location of fistula to which there is no healing.
Capitol .xxx.	Thirty-First Chapter.
De la cauterizacio de la melsa.	On Cauterizing of the Melancholy.
Quan tu curas la malautia de la melsa am aquo que havem dit de la curacio en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cauteri en lu es segon tres manieras, las quals totas son dreyturieras, de las quals la una es que fassas tres cauteris o quatre linhan segon la longitut de la melsa segon la figura dels cauteris del fietge, la figura dels quals ha precedit.	When you cure the disease of melancholy with water as we have said in the division and do not concur with your curing, then cauterize there according to three manners, all of which are right, one of which is that you make three or four lines according to the length of the melancholy, following the figure of the cauteries of the foot, the figure of which has preceded.
E sia entre quascun cauteri la grossetut d’un dit o un pauc mes, e la manieyra del cauteri sia la manieyra la qual havem dita en le cauteri del fietge engualment.	And between each cautery the thickness of a finger or a little more, and the manner of the cautery is the same manner which we have said in the cauteries of the foot, equally.
E no compremas la tua ma am le cauteri; e le malaute sia eves sobre lo sieu dos.	And do not compress your hand with the cautery; and let the patient lie on their back.
E es autra manieyra de cauterizar, so es que tu igniscas le cauteri haventz dos vertimentz, la qual causa havem dita en le capitol de dislocacio del muscle, e elava la codena la qual es en le endreyt de la melsa la hon perve le jazer del malaute sinistre.	And there is another manner of cauterizing, so that you ignite the cautery having two handles, which cause we have said in the chapter on dislocation of the muscle, and elevate the cord which is in the end of the melancholy, where it reaches the bed of the patient's left side.
E sia la tua elevacio am la qual elevas la codena segon la longuesa del cors, per que sian faytz cauteris segon la latitut del cos.	And be your elevation according to which you elevate the cord as long as the body is, so that you may make cauteries according to the latitude of the body.
E aprop entromet les dos vernimentz, ignitz mot, en aquel entro que am aquels penetres la codena de la autra part.	And then insert the two handles, ignite one, and enter into that which with those you will pierce the cord from the other side.
E aprop extrayt le cauteri; e donc son faytz quatre cauteris.	And then extract the cautery; and thus four cauteries are made.
E si voys, cauteriza am cauteri havent tres vernimentz.	And if you wish, cauterize with a cautery having three handles.
E aprop tu cura le cauteri pus que aia laysat de getar brac per trops jorns, quar mays es comferent que las autras causas precedentz en la curacio.	And then you cure the cautery more than I have said to get it out for too many days, because it is more certain that other causes preceding in the curing.
Capitol .xxxi.	Thirty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de ydropici.	On Cauterizing of Hydropepticus.
Cauteri no catz en ydropici sino en alcinte3 propriament.	Cauteries are not used in hydropepticus, but rather in acute properment.
Quan tu curas le ydropic am las manieyras de curacio las quals havem ditas en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que aquel cauterizes am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic e am un cauteri sobre l’estomac, e am autre cauteri sobre le fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa, e am dos cauteris entre les spondils del dos, e un cauteri en lo dreyt del pietz, e am autre cauteri sobre l’estomac.	When you cure the hydropepticus with the manners of curing which we have said in the division and do not concur with your curing, then it is necessary that one cauterizes with four cauteries in the circle of the navel and with one cautery on the stomach, and with another cautery on the foot, and with another cautery on the melancholy, and with two cauteries between the vertebrae of the back, and with one cautery in the right side of the foot, and with another cautery on the stomach.
E la quantitat de la profunditat del cauteri sia propdana a la spicitut de la codena.	And the quantity of the depth of the cautery should be proportioned to the subtlety of the cord.
E aprop layssa le cauteri ubert per so que gete brac per lonc temps.	And then leave the cautery under for so that it gets out slowly over a long time.
E no evacuas le malaute de curacio aprop le cauteri am aquo que cove per que sian agreguadas a lu doas entencios, e sira festinada a lu am ajutori sanacio.	And do not evacuate the patient from curing immediately after the cautery with water as is necessary for two intentions, and thus it will be hastened to him with the aid of healing.
La forma del cauteri am lo qual es cauterizat lo ventre sia clavilh segon que la forma de aquel es desus precedent, e es aquel am le qual es cauterizat le dos sia olivar segon qu’es precedent a la sua forma.	The form of the cautery with which the belly is cauterized is like a key according to the previous form above, and it is that with which the back is cauterized is olive-shaped according to its previous form.
Capitol .xxxii.	Thirty-Second Chapter.
De cauterizacio de pes e de las coyssas.	On Cauterizing of Feet and Limbs.
Quan les pes so apostematz en ydropitz e so repletz de aygua sitrina, cove que cauterisas les pes sobre le dos del pe in nocrati aquo que es entre le auricular e le anular, e eleva la tua ma am le cauteri e no torses aquel; e aprop eleva la tua ma, e no retornes aquela de tot, quar l’aygua satrina rezuda.	When the feet are apostemated in dropsy and filled with sitten water, it is necessary that you cauterize the feet on the top of the heel with a cautery that is between the auricular and anular, and elevate your hand with the cautery and do not twist it; and then elevate your hand, and do not return to it completely, for the sitten water resists.
Es le cauteri segon aquesta forma: E aprop fay sobre las doas coyssas dos cauteris, e en quascuna coysa sia feyt cauteri am la extremitat del cauteri cutellar.	The cautery is according to this form: And then make two cauteries on each limb, and in each limb be made a cautery at the extremity of the knife-shaped cautery.
E sia le cauteri segon la longitut de la coyssa: i dejos le denolh e l’autre jos le mieg loc de la coyssa; e sobre quascuna coyssa dos cauteris.	And be the cauteries according to the length of the limb: one below the knuckle and another below the middle part of the limb; and on each limb, two cauteries.
E layssa la plagua uberta ses curacio per lonc temps per so que alcuna aygua resuda de lu.	And leave the wound open without cure for a long time in order that some water may flow from it.
E aprop cura le am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas.	And then cure it with those causes which we have said.
Capitol .xxxiii.	Thirty-Third Chapter.
De cauterizacio de cos de ventre.	On Cauterizing of Belly.
Quan cos de ventre es per freg e per humiditat entro que debelice las vertutz, so es la vertut digestiva e retentiva, las quals so en l’estomac e en les budels, e es curat aquo am las manieyras de curacio e no confereys, e vezes le malaute suffertan cauteri de vertut exhiberant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am gran cauteri sobre le sieu stomac segon que a precedit en la cauterizacio del estomac, am le cauteri del cercle e am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic subtils, am cauteri clavilh subtil; e am cauteri sobre le alcatin sobre alozis gran, o am dos cauteris.	When the belly is weakened by cold and humidity to such an extent that it loses its virtues, namely the digestive and retentive virtues which are in the stomach and intestines, and it is cured with water as we have said in the curing methods, but does not concur, and at times the patient suffers from a cauterization of virtue exhibiting, then cauterize that with a great cautery on the natural stomach according to what has preceded in the cauterization of the stomach, with the circle cautery and four subtle cauteries in the circle of the navel, with a key-shaped cautery; and with another cautery over the loin over aloes granules, or with two cauteries.
E si vezes las humiditatz exhuberants e le malaute aquo tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le pentenilh e sobre les budels, e fort leu ajustant dos cauteris sobre l’estomac e prop dels inguonas, quar es curacio perficent de juvament de la qual no erras.	And if at times excessive humidity and the patient's water tolerates, then cauterize that on the intestines and over the intestines, and slightly adjusting two cauteries over the stomach and near the groin, for it is perfect curing of which you will not err.
Capitol .xxxiv.	Thirty-Fourth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de emorroydas antiquas.	On Cauterizing of Old Hemorrhoids.
Quan so en la natura derier emorroydas antiquas o una de humors grossas fregas o de humiditatz corrompudas, e son curadas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no confereys la tieua curacio, lahoras cauterisa am tres cauteris sobre le pus dejos spondilh del dos petit e petit triangular, e am cauteri desus le ombelic cays per dos ditz.	When such old hemorrhoids or one of gross humors or corrupted humidity are in nature and are cured with water as we have said in the division, but do not concur with your curing, then cauterize with three cauteries on the pus left behind from the vertebrae of the little back and triangular, and with a cautery above the navel that falls between two ditties.
E si doptas que l’estomac de lu sia enfregidat e la vianda de lu no sia degerida, e la cara de lu vezes apostemada, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre l’estomac am gran cauteri segon que es precedit; e am un cauteri sobre fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa de lu am cauteri clavilh, e leyssa le cauteri per alcun temps ubert, e aprop cura lu entro que sia sanat.	And if you think that the stomach of him is enfeebled and his food not digested, and his face at times apostemated, then cauterize that on the stomach with a great cautery according to what has preceded; and with one cautery on the foot, and with another cautery on the melancholy of him with a key-shaped cautery; and leave the cautery open for some time, and then cure him until he is healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	Thirty-Fifth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de atheyl aprop la abscizio de lor.	On Cauterizing of Athies Properly for their Abscission.
Quan tu abscindes atheyl, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri que es asemblat a ray.	When you abscess the athies, then ignite the cautery which is similar to a ray.
Aprop entremet aquel ignit en aquel atheyl abscis, e ultima la tieua ma entro que pervengua le cauteri al orifici de la vena de la qual ve la sanc.	Then insert that ignited cautery into the abscessed athie, and lastly extend your hand until the cautery reaches the opening of the vein from which blood flows.
E fay aquo una vetz o doas, quar si achieyl son trops, lahoras cauteriza quascun de lor segon que havem recontat, e aprop cura aquels am aquo que confereys a lor dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And make it once or twice, for if the athies are too many, then cauterize each of them according to what we have recounted, and then cure those with water that concurs with their wounds until they are healed.
E si cauterizas am gran cauteri sobre alquatin, es mays derier en juvament.	And if you cauterize with a great cautery on something, it is more certain in judgment.
Capitol .xxxvi.	Thirty-Sixth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistolas que son faytas en la natura derie en las partidas de lu.	On Cauterizing of Fistulas that are formed in the natural parts of him.
Quan la natura no obeziys a la obra la qual havem recomtada en son loc, e·l pacient es espaventat per aquo, sia sanat am cauteri.	When nature does not obey the work which we have recommended in its place, and the patient is frightened by that, be healed with a cautery.
Donc quan ad alcun ve fistola en la natura derier, e es antiquada, corro sania de lu e humiditatz corrompudas, e donc aquo que es pus digne que cove es que proes aquela am tenta subtil, e aprop conoys la quantitat de la profunditat de lu am la devant dita tenta.	Therefore, when you find some fistula in the natural parts of him, and it is old, rotten blood and corrupted humidity are flowing from it, and thus what is most worthy to be done is that you probe that with a subtle tent and know the quantity of the depth of it with the aforementioned tent.
Aprop igneys le cauteri que es semblant a ray.	Then ignite the cautery which is similar to a ray.
E aprop met aquel cauteri ignit en aquesta fistula, e segon la quantitat en la qual intrec la tenta.	And then insert that ignited cautery into this fistula, and according to the quantity in which the tent enters.
E itera sobre aquela le cauteri entro que sian comburitz aquels cors corrumputz tost una veguada o dos o tres, segon la quantitat de la tua necessitat.	And iterate over that with the cautery until those corrupted bodies are consumed in one, two, or three passes, according to the quantity of your necessity.
E guarda te de combustio de nervi e de vena; o si fistula va al cors de la vesica o al cors del budel, lahoras guarda te de totz aquels locz; e no fassas aquo sino quan la fistula es en loc carnos e cogitas que no es penetrant.	And take care not to burn the nerves and veins; or if the fistula goes to the bladder or intestines, then take care of all those places; and do not do so unless the fistula is in a fleshly location and you are certain that it is not penetrating.
E aprop cura le loc entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the place until it is healed.
E si le loc es sigillat, e so abscindidas de lu las materias, e roman ayssi per lonc temps, lahoras sapias que ja es curat entierament.	And if the place is sealed, and all the matters have abscessed from it, and thus remains for a long time, then know that it has been completely cured.
E si las materias no so de lu ostadas, lahoras sapias que es penetrant o en le preon de lu os corromput, o cays aquo de aquelas causas de las quals vindra rememoracio en son loc.	And if the matters are not removed from him, then know that it is penetrating or into the preone of him or corrupting his flesh, or that there will be remembrance of those causes in its place.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Thirty-Seventh Chapter.
De cauterizacio dels ronhos.	On Cauterizing the Tonsils.
Quan en les ronhos endeve dolor per freg o per grossa ventozitat, e per aysso le coyt del malaute es amermat, lahoras cove que cauterizes aquel sobre les ronhos am cauteri sobre quascun ronho am cauteri clavilh del qual precesic la rememoracio.	When in the tonsils there is great pain due to cold or gross ventosity, and because of this the patient's throat is sore, then it is necessary that you cauterize that on each tonsil with a key-shaped cautery, of which the remembrance precedes.
E fort leu cauterizam am le segon un petit dejos, per que vindran tres cauteris liniatz, e donc siran mays deriers en juvament.	And then cauterize with a little more, so that three lined cauteries will be made, and thus they will be more certain in judgment.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Thirty-Eighth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vesica.	On Cauterizing the Bladder.
Quan accideys en la vesica debelitat e mollificacio per freg e per humiditatz ayssi que·l malaute la urina no retengua, lahoras cauteriza aquel en la partida pus dejos sobre la vesiqua, la hon comensan les pels del pentenilh, e cauteriza am un cauteri en la partida dreyta, e am autre en la senestra de lu.	When debilitation and softening occur in the bladder due to cold and humidity such that the patient's urine does not retain, then cauterize that on the posterior part of the bladder, where the hair of the small intestine begins, and cauterize with one cautery on the right side and another on the left side.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la cantitat dels not del pous; e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en la partida pus bassa del dos, o am dos cauteris si es necessitat.	And be the length of each cautery according to the quantity of the nodules on the pustule; and cauterize that with a cautery in the lowest part of the back, or with two cauteries if necessary.
E sia cauteri clavilh segon que es procesit.	And be the key-shaped cautery according to what has proceeded.
Capitol .xxxix.	Thirty-Ninth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la mayra.	On Cauterizing the Malar.
Quan veno en la mayra freg e humiditatz, e per aysso es prohibida enpreignacio, e son corrompudas las mestruas de lu, e es tardada la provocacio de lor, e accideys dolor deves le haveniment de lor, lahoras cove que·l loc sia cauterizat am tres cauteris en le circuit del ombelic, ayssi cum havem dit en le cauteri de la vesica; e am cauteri sobre le loc pus dejos del dos, o am dos cauteris, e sia le cauteri clavilh.	When cold and humidity come to the malar, and because of this impregnation is prohibited, and the menstrual fluxes are corrupted, and the provocation of them is delayed, and pain occurs in the lower abdomen due to their retention, then it is necessary that the place be cauterized with three cauteries in the circle of the navel, just as we have said in the cauterization of the bladder; and with a cautery on the lowest part of the back, or with two cauteries, and let the key-shaped cautery be.
Capitol .xl.	Fortieth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua.	On Cauterizing the Dislocation of the Hip.
Quan humiditatz moucozas so efundudas a la partida de la anqua, e so faytas causas del yssiment del sieu loc, e senhal de lu es que la coyssa es prolonguada sobre l’autre quan so comparadas entre lor.	When moist humors are abundant in the part of the hip, and the causes of its swelling are made manifest, and the sign is that the limb is prolonged over the other when compared between them.
E le loc de la dislocacio es atrobat en lu quays boyt.	And the place of the dislocation is located in the part which is above.
Adonc cove que cauterizas le malaute sobre la partida de la anqua de lu am cauteri a sercle semblant, pus que tu auras senhat am tenta en le cercuit de la partida ayssi cum es revolguda, e per so que la partida caia el mieg loc del cercle.	Therefore it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the part of the hip with a circular cautery similar to a circle, as soon as you have sensed with a tent in the circle of the part thus revolved, and so that the part falls in the middle location of the circle.
E sia le cauteri del qual precedit la forma en la cauterizacio del estomac.	And be the cautery of which the form proceeded in the cauterization of the stomach.
E si aquest cauteri no es a tu present, lahoras cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris am cauteri olivar gran.	And if this cautery is not before you, then cauterize that with three cauteries and a large olive-shaped cautery.
E sia fayt le cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de tota la codena; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And make the cautery according to the quantity of the subtlety of all the cord; and then cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .xli.	Fortieth Chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vena sciatica.	On Cauterizing the Sciatic Vein.
Quan dolor ve en la partida de anqua, e so causa de lu freg et humiditatz, le malaute es curat am aquo que havem dit e no confereys, e aquo es antiquat, lahoras cove que tu lacses le malaute de humors grosses am pillulas fetidas o am pillulas artificials o semblantz; e aprop cauteriza aquel.	When pain comes in the part of the hip, and its cause is cold and humidity, the patient is cured with water as we have said and does not concur, and this is old, then it is necessary that you apply to the patient with gross humors by fetid pills or artificial pills or semblances; and then cauterize that.
E la manieyra del cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am medicinas comburentz, o cauteri am foc.	And the manner of the cautery in that is according to two manners: or a cautery with burning medicines, or a cautery with fire.
Sira segon dos manieyras scientas, de las quals es la una que cauterizes aquel sobre la partida de l’ancha de lu am tres cauteris triangulatz segon aquesta forma; e fay am aquels bona profunditat.	There are according to two scientific manners, of which one is that you cauterize that on the part of the hip of him with three triangular cauteries in this shape; and make them good depth.
E sia le spazi le qual es entre cascun cauteri la quantitat de la grossitut del dit e si le cauteri olivar o gran.	And be the space which is between each cautery the quantity of the thickness of the said, and if it is an olive-shaped or large cautery.
Mays alcunas veguadas sia le cauteri sobre le mieg loc sobre le cap de l’anquan per que son quatre cauteris.	But sometimes there are four cauteries, with the one on the middle location on the head of the hip, for that reason.
E si vols, cauteriza am le cercle del qual es precesida la forma en la cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua, la i que sia cercle continent e comburey la ispicitut de tota la codena.	And if you wish, cauterize with the circle of which the form precedes in the cauterization of the dislocation of the hip, that is a circle that contains and burns the subtlety of all the cord.
E aquesta es la manieyra de cauteri in ciatiqua quan dolor es adherent al anqua e no es estenduda entro a la coyssa.	And this is the manner of cauterization in sciatica when pain is attached to the hip and does not extend into the joint.
Mays si es estenduda entro a la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre la coyssa sobre le loc al qual envireys le malaute que es la dolor; e am un cauteri sobre la cavilha per quatre ditz un pauc deves la part cilvestra.	But if it extends into the joint, then cauterize that with two cauteries on the joint on the location where the patient feels the pain; and with one cautery on the pelvis for four times, a little distance from the hairy part.
E si le cauteri cutellar, e sia la profunditat del cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de la codena.	And if the cautery is cutelliform, and be the depth of the cautery according to the quantity of the subtlety of the cord.
E si le malaute envireys que la dolor es estenduda entro al loc prop les ditz des pes, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui on envireys am cauteri per tres puntz o quatre o mays si indigeys de aquel.	And if the patient says that the pain is extended to the place near the digits of the feet, then cauterize that here where it is felt with a cautery for three points or four or more as needed.
E si le malaute envireys dolor esser dejos le donolh ves la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui am un cauteri cutellar.	And if the patient says that the pain is left below the donut-shaped vein near the joint, then cauterize that with a cutelliform cautery.
E guarda te en tota cauterizacio que no ultimes am le cauteri en tant que comburas nervi o gran arceria, e que per aquo a tu es sobre le malaute mal noccument o contraccio.	And be careful in all cautery that you do not leave the cautery until it has burned nerves or large arteries, and that because of this, it is bad for your patient to suffer or contract.
E yeu ja e vist un e autre de aquels les quals cauterizero sobre la cavilha e ultimero en la cauterizacio, e la cama foc inflada entro que la tumor aconseguit lo pe, e foc perforat e corromput tot le pe.	And behold, I have seen one and another of those who will be cauterized on the pelvis and finally in the cautery, and the inflamed fire burning inside until the tumor reaches its peak, and the pierced and corrupted foot is made.
E aprop accidic fort solucio de ventre, e aprop aquo la mort.	And thus a great solution of the belly occurs, and thus death ensues.
E si la dolor es en dos partidas ensemps cauteriza quascuna segon aquesta manieyra.	And if the pain is in two parts together, then cauterize each one according to this manner.
E diysero les savis alcus en la cauterizacio de anqua cauteri del qual aquesta es la manieyra: fay semblant a cercle de ferr del qual le cercuit sia la maytat de un palm; e sia deves le sieu orrifici segon la grossesa de un os de datil o mens un pauc.	And thus the wise ones say in the cauterization of the hip, that this is the manner: make it similar to a circle of iron with a circumference equal to half a palm; and be the shape of your orifice according to the thickness of a walnut shell or less.
E dedintz aquel cercle sia un autre tertz; e sia le spazi le qual es entre lor la quantitat del notz del pous; e sian aquels cercles ubertz de dos partidas; e sia la longitut de aquels cays un notz o dos notz, e fay en aquels margue de ferr decentment apparelhat en les cercles; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And within that circle be another third; and be the space which is between them the quantity of the nodules of the pustule; and be those circles about two parts; and be the length of them one nodule or two nodules, and make in those margins of iron decently apparelled in the circles; and this is the form of it:
Aprop sia ignit en le foc entro que s’enrogesisca e gete scintillas, e aprop sia pausat sobre la partida del anqua, le malaute colcat sobre le latz sa.	And be ignited in the fire until it reddens and gives sparks, and be paused above the part of the hip, the patient lying on his side.
E donc cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris redontz en una veguada.	And then cauterize that with three circular cauteries in one pass.
E aprop layssa aquel per tres jorns; aprop emplastre aquel am boder e layssa la plagua uberta per trops dias; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then leave that for three days; apply a poultice to it with border and leave the wound open for many days; and then cure that with ointments until it is healed.
Diys Albucasis : o, filhs, de aquesta specia de cauteri pauc havem usat per la terror del reguardament de lu, e per aquo que paucs havem trobatz les quals reguardan sobre lu.	Thus speaks Albucasis: Ah, children, we have used this type of cautery rarely because of the fear of looking at it, and therefore few have found those who look upon it.
Mays dels bos cauteris a lu qui les sufferta, et atroba am aquel le loc de lu.	But from good cauteries, they have suffered at him, and found the place of him.
Mays cauteri am medicinas adhurentz es que tu fassas dos cercles haventz armula perforada en la qual deyssen le guaffo de la porta de ferr; sia la longuitut de la paretz en la nauteza de lor sian dos nozes o quays aquels.	But the cautery with burning medicines is one that you make two circles having a perforated armula in which should be placed the goaf of the iron door; be the length of the partitions in the neatness of their being two nodules or as many as those.
E si le spazi le qual es entre quascu la quantitat de la grossitut del dit; e sian ubertz dejos e desus, e sian que contenguan se entre lor segon aquesta forma:	And if the space which is between each one is the quantity of the thickness of the said; and be above and below, and be that contain themselves between them according to this form:
E aprop pausa sobre la partida de la anqua le malaut jasent sobre le latz sa, e comprem la tua ma sobre la partida de la anqua; e aprop pren de aygua cauda e fon la entre dos cercles, e la qualiditat de aquela sia am le foc petit a petit, e te aquela per la quantitat de una hora, e sufferta le malaute la mordicacio e la adhustio de lu — quar aquel atrobo mordicacio ayssi cum de foc — entro que cesse la mordicacio.	And then pause above the part of the hip the patient lying on his side, and compress your hand over the part of the hip; and then take cold water and pour it between two circles, and let its quality be in a small fire little by little, and hold that for the quantity of an hour, and cause the patient to suffer the biting and adaptation of him — as if from fire — until the biting ceases.
E aprop eleva la tua ma am le instrument et abstergeys l’aygua cauda de tota la anqua am aygua dousa.	And then lift your hand with the instrument and wash away the cold water from all of the hip with warm water.
E aprop leyssa aquel per tres jorns e pausa sobre aquel boder entro que sia la negror de la adhustio remauguda, e leyssa aquo per alcus jorns, e correra de lu poyredura; aquest es derier en juvament.	And then leave that for three days and pause over it with border until the darkness of adaptation is regained, and leave that too for some days, and run from him purulence; this is the last in judgment.
E aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointments until it is healed.
E si la dolor es extenduda entro la coyssa o la camba, fay a lu estatua en lu que contengua aygua segon que es feyt en la anqua engualment.	And if the pain is extended to the joint or the thigh, make it like a statue in him that contains water according to how it is made in the hip equally.
E aquesta es la manieyra de aygua cauda, e yeu ja he scrit aquela en le tractat de la rectificacio de medicinas.	And this is the manner of cold water, and you have already written it in the treatise on the rectification of medicines.
Recipe de alcali e de caus no extinta de amdos ana partida una, e trissa les e pausa en una ola nova de la qual la partida dejos sia perforada per un petit trauc, segon la quantitat que intre en lu ray.	Recipe of alkali and of both non-extinguished causes, one for each hip, and crush them and pause in a new wave of which the left part is pierced by a small hole, according to the quantity that enters into the ray.
E pausa dejos le fons de la ola autra ola enveyriada, e gete sobre aquel alcali e caus viva de aygua doussa la qual cobra aquels per un dit, e pus que tu compremes aquels am la tieua ma per bona compressio, e leyssa la hola que deyssenda de lu aygua aguda en la partida dejos a la ola enveyriada.	And pause the bottom of the wave in another enveloped wave, and pour on that alkali and living causes with warm water which absorbs those for one finger, and then compress them with your thumb for good compression, and leave the hole to descend from it into the parted-off wave in the enveloped wave.
E aprop ajusta tota aquela aygua, e geta la sobre autra caus viva e autre alcali renovelatz, quar aquela lahoras sira de mot forta acuitat, la qual es aministrada en motas operacios de medicina e en cauterizacio dels autres membres, quar operacio fa de foc.	And then adjust all that water, and pour it on other living causes and another alkali renewed, because that water is now of very strong acidity, which is administered in many operations of medicine and in cauterization of the other members, because operation makes fire.
E so de las medicinas alcunas am las quals es cauterizat ancha, ayssi cum tezizic e mel anacrat e caus am sabo enayssi que sian mesclatz.	And some of the medicines with which the hip is cauterized, such as tea-zit and mulberry juice, and causes with savory in such a way that they are mixed.
E Gualia recontet de un home dels antics la operacio e la curacio am la qual es curada dolor de anqua e de vena sciatica, e magnifiquet mot be esser de aquel, e diys que no hac necessitat de autra curacio, e quar es sanat per una veguada ayssi cum recomtec, quar fort leu aquel intrec en banh e eysic ja sa d’aquel.	And Gualia recounts the story of a man from ancient times who was operated on and cured for hip pain and sciatic vein pain, and magnified much about him, saying that no other cure was needed, and that it was healed in one pass, just as he had recommended, because very little effort was required to achieve this.
Et es que sia pres de certarragi vert, e si no es atrobat vert, sia presa figua recent; e mot sia trissada am un pauc de grays e sia pausat sus la anqua en la qual es la dolor, o en la coyssa, o en la camba, e sia liat.	And it is that you should be taken with certain vertebrae, and if not found, take a fresh fig; and much be crushed with a little grey matter, and paused above the hip where there is pain, or in the joint, or in the thigh, and tied.
E sia layssat per la cantitat de tres horas o per la quantitat que·l malaute centa cedacio de la adhustio.	And be left for the quantity of three hours or for the quantity that the patient feels relaxation of adaptation.
E aprop met aquel en banh e donc quan le cors de lu sia enrozat, entromet aquel en le sol, quar la dolor cessa e es sanat.	And then immerse that in water and therefore when the body of him is relaxed, interpose it in the sun, so that the pain ceases and he is healed.
E sapias que no cove que alcu use de cauteri am aquestas medicinas sino aprop la evacuacio del cors.	And know that no one should use these medicines for cauterization except in the event of evacuation from the body.
Mays ja Escorides diysec que quan am fenda de cabra la vena stretica es cauterizada, aprofieyra a lu mo be; e sia le cauteri am lu segon aquesta manieyra: sia presa lana e sia enbeguda en oli antic, e sia pausat entre le pous del pe e entre le fossil.	But already Escorides has said that when the sciatic vein is cauterized in a wound of goat, it is cured with ease; and this cautery is done according to this manner: take wool and soak it in old oil, and place it between the toes of the foot and between the bones.
E aprop pren fenda de cabra secca e emflasma aquela am foc entro que sia fayta carbo; e aprop pausa lu sobre la lana e leysa la entro que sia estengida.	And then take dried goat's hide and inflame it with fire until it is made of charcoal; and then pause it over the wool and leave it inside until it is stretched.
E aprop itera aquo, e no cessas far aquo entro que·l scintiment de la mordicacio pervengua entro al anqua e repausa la dolor.	And then repeat this process, and do not stop until the sensation of biting reaches into the hip and brings relief to the pain.
Et aquesta manieyra de cauteri es apelat cauteri de vaquas.	And this manner of cauterization is called "cauteri de vaquas".
Capitol .xlii.	Chapter 42.
De cauterizacio de dolor de dos.	On the Cauterization of Pain in Two Places.
Alcunas veguadas dolor es en le dos per tropas causas, cum per cazement o per percucio o per superflua evacuacio, e per causas ad aquelas semblantz, per infusio de materia frega e humida.	At times pain is in both places due to various causes, such as bruising or striking or excessive evacuation, and by causes similar to those, through the infusion of wet and humid matter.
E cauteri no catz sino en aquesta sola specia la qual es fayta per efusio de materia frega.	And the cautery is not done except in this one species which is made by effusion of wet matter.
Donc cove, aprop evacuacio del malaute am pillulas fitidas e am semblant a lor, que sian faytas sobre·l dos en le qual es la dolor tres linhas segon la latitut de lu, pus que senhas am tentha en quascuna linha v cauteris o mays, segon la quantitat que ve de la tolleransa del malaute e de la vertut de lu.	Therefore, it is good to evacuate the patient with pillules fitidas and similar ones that are made on both places where there is pain, three lines according to the latitude of him, plus one tenths in each line or more, depending on the quantity that comes from the tolerance of the patient and the virtue of him.
E sia fayta cauterizacio am cauteri de punt.	And make a cautery with pointed cauteries.
E si vols, cauteriza am tres cauteris o am quatre am cauteri clavilh medial segon aquesta forma:	And if you wish, cauterize with three or four pointed cauteries in the middle of the joint according to this form:
Capitol .xliii.	Chapter 43.
De cauterizacio al comensament de gilbositat.	On the Cauterization at the Beginning of Giltiness.
Motas veguadas endeve aquesta malautia als petitz enfantz; e senhal del comensament de lu en les enfantz es que accideys sobre lor estrectura en le ale eves la elevacio e·l movement.	Many times this illness attacks little children; and the sign of its beginning in children is that it happens to their structure in the ear, with a sudden elevation and movement.
E atrobas en le derier espondil del dos e dels notz de lu que ja comensa a sobremontar sobre les autres spondils.	And you find it in the last cervical vertebra of the spine, and in the nodes of him that already begins to rise above the other vertebrae.

que prengua le cauteri sobre tota partida del spondilh engualment.	which takes the cautery on all parts of the vertebra equally.

Capitol .xliv.	Chapter 44.
De cauterizacio de podagra e de dolor de juncturas.	On the Cauterization of Gout and Joint Pain.
Quan dolor de juncturas son faytas per humors fregas les quals so enfundutz a quascun membre del cors, lahoras quan veno dolors en los pes, de costuma dels metges es que aquo apelen podragua propriament.	When joint pain is caused by wet humors that are poured into each member of the body, then when pains come in the feet, it is customary for doctors to call this gout properly.
E donc cum es curada podagra de causa frega am manieyra de cura e no so remaugudas las dolors, lahoras las remau cauteri.	And therefore when gout caused by wetness is cured by a method of cure and the pains are not relapsed, then relapse them with cautery.

And if many cauteries are needed to produce this effect, then cauterize that and do not press too hard with your hand on the cautery, so as to be only about the thickness of a cord.
E si las dolors pugan entro al donolh e·l dos, lahoras aministra le cauteri le qual havem dit en le sieu capitol.	And if the pains rise into the finger and the toe, then administer the cautery which we have said in our chapter.
E si las dolors so en las mas tant solament, e es apelada suagra, lahoras puncta en le circuit dels focils ayssi cum se revolvo, puncta en aquels dos linhas.	And if the pains are only in the toes and are called "suagra", then puncture in the circle of the phalanges as they revolve, puncturing those two lines.
E si reman de las dolors en les ditz, lahoras puncta en le cercuit dels focils sobre quascun notz e sobre la pinche de la ma.	And if the pains remain in the said toes, then puncture in the circle of the phalanges on each digit and on the tip of the finger.
E si las dolors pugan aprop alscus jorns als coydes o als muscles, lahoras cauteriza les quascus de tota part dels ajutoris.	And if the pains rise approximately after some days to the joints or muscles, then cauterize all of them on all parts of the aids.
E no evacuas le malaute de bon regiment e de recepcio de medicinas, quar si es fayt bon regiment e flacma es evacuada am aquest cauteri sira sanat, Dieus ajudan.	And do not evacuate the patient from good regime and reception of medicines, for if it is made good regime and evacuation is done with this cautery, then the patient will be healed, God help.
Capitol .xlv.	Chapter 45.
De cauterizacio de rompeduras.	On the Cauterization of Wounds.
Quan endeve rompedura en les angonars e diysendo les budels denant l’atela al genetiu, e aquo es comensan de aprop, lahoras cove que tu mandas al malaute layssar la sua comestio en le sieu dia e que use de causas leniens per so que la fenda deyssenda del sieu ventre.	When the wound occurs in the thighs and says that it is spreading the bladders before the navel to the belly, and this is beginning to approach, then it is good for you to order the patient to leave his diet for a day and to use lenient causes so that the wound may come out of his belly.
E aprop segua le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e comanda a lu que tengua le sieu ale entro que sia foro getat o aparesca l’atela o·l budels.	And then follow the patient between your fingers on his back, and command him to keep his arm bent until the orifice is made or the navel or bladders appear.
E aprop retorna aquel am les tieus ditz e senha am tenta la ruptura sobre le os del pentenilh am senhal la extremitat del qual sia semblant a la maytat de cercle a las subiranas partidas del cors.	And then return that to the said digits and signal by attempting the rupture on the bone of the pelvis, signaling the extremity of which is similar to the half-circle of the upper parts of the body.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cautery of which this is the form:
entro que sia mot rog e gete cintilhas.	until it is hot enough to produce sparks.
E aprop reduzeys le budel o l’atela a la sua conquavitat, e aprop pause la sua ma sobre le loc per so que le budel no yesqua.	And then reduce the navel or bladder to its natural curvature, and then pause your hand over the location so that the navel does not burst.
E tu ja has ubert entre las coyssas del malaute e dejos lu as pausat un coyssi, et autre servent sia sus las cambas de lu, e autre sus le pietz de lu, le qual tengua las suas mas.	And you have already opened between the joints of the patient and left one joint paused, another serving on his thighs, and another on his feet, which has its own fingers.
E aprop pausa le cauteri sobre aquel senhal am la tua ma am cauteri stan dreyt, e te aquel entro que am lu consieguas le os del pentenilh entro al mieg del duiduni; e itera am aquel autra veguada si a tu aquel no has conseguit en la primieyra veguada entro al os.	And then pause the cautery over that sign with your hand having the cautery standing upright, and get that into the bone of the pelvis up to the middle of the duodenum; and repeat it in another way if you did not succeed in the first time getting into the bone.
E observa saviament del ysiment del budel en la hora de la tua cauterizacio, que no comburas aquel budel per so que sobre le malaute no vengua in mort o autre gran malicia.	And observe wisely the state of the navel at the time of your cautery, that you do not burn that navel so that it does not bring harm or great evil to the patient.
E sapias que quan tu am le cauteri no atenhas le os, no confereys la tua operacio.	And know that when you are using the cautery, do not touch the bone, nor confirm your operation.
E cove que·l cauteri dels enfants sia subtil segon le gran e la mesura de lor.	And it is good for children's cauteries to be subtle according to their great and small size.
E aprop cura le loc del cauteri per tres dias am boder entro que sia remauguda la scara del foc.	And then cure the location of the cautery for three days with borders, so that the scar of fire is renewed.
E aprop cura aquel am les autres enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with other ointments until it is healed.
E le malaute sia jasent sobre le sieu dos per xl dias entro que sia sigillat le loc e la plagua.	And the patient shall lie on his back for 40 days until the location and wound are sealed.
E cove que pauses le nutriment de lu segon la longitut del temps de la curacio de lu le qual le linesca le ventre de lu, e que le budel no yesca fora deves le esforsament de guerir.	And it is good that you pause the nourishment of him according to the length of time for his cure, which stretches his belly, and that the navel does not burst forth under the effort of healing.
E aprop quan se vol levar aprop xl dias, lahoras aministra liament decentment fayt, e tengua aquel per autres xl jorns.	And then when it is time to lift after 40 days, then administer gradually decreasing power, and keep him that way for another 40 days.
E sia mermat de trebalh e de replecio de vianda e de beure, e de votz vehementz, quar quan usa de aquest regiment de sanacio entiera sira sanat.	And he should be weakened by labor and replenishment of food and drink, and of loud voices, for when he uses this regimen of healing, then it will be whole.
E yeu diyre la curacio de las rupturas en las autras partidas del ventre, e so al comensament, e vols que no treguan, lahoras cauterisa la ruptura d’aquel am cauteri redon segon la quantitat de lu, e sia aquo que es exhurit de la codena ayssi cum la tersa partida de lu; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit, e no es ajustat.	And I will say the cure for ruptures in other parts of the belly, and at the beginning, and you want them not to stop, then cauterize the rupture with that round cautery according to the quantity of it, and this is what is exhausted from the cord as well as the third part of it; and then cure that with what we have said, and do not adjust.
E ja diyssero alcus primiers que ruptura sia cauterizada am cauteri triangular segon aquesta forma, pus que es senhada am tenta:	And already some first ones said that rupture should be cauterized with triangular cautery according to this form, since it is signified by attempt:
e es pausada linha que eys per la latitut en le latz pus sobira de la ruptura, e autra linha al desus; e depausa la tua ma am un cauteri clavilh, mays le primier cauteri es pus leugier e milhor.	and it is a paused line that goes through the latitude in the latz plus above the rupture, and another line above; and place your hand with a pointed cautery, but the first cautery is lighter and better.
Capitol .xlvi.	Chapter 46.
De cauterizacio de torcio.	On the Cauterization of Twist.
Quan endeve en alscus membres per cazement o per percussio dolor e persevera aquela dolor per lonc temps e no comfereys al u curacio am medicinas, lahoras cove que cauterizes am cauteri de punt.	When there is a pain in some members due to bruising or striking and the pain persists for a long time and does not conform to cure with medicines, then it is good that you cauterize with pointed cautery.
E sia le cauteri de tot membre segon la magnitut e la parvitat de lu, e vertut e develitat de lu, e locacio de torcio e dolor de lu.	And be the cautery of every member according to its magnitude and smallness, virtue and faultiness, location of twist and pain of it.
Donc si·s sanat per le primier cauteri, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera sobre lu le cauteri; quar de costuma de aquelas dolors es que sian punctatz de membre ad aquel membre le qual apropinque al u, per que cove que consieguas aquels am cauteri entro que·l malaute sia sanat.	Therefore, if it is healed by the first cautery, well; and otherwise, then repeat the cautery on him; for of those pains it is customary that they are punctured from one member to another which approaches it, so that you should achieve those with cautery until the patient is healed.
Capitol .xlvii.	Chapter 47.
De cauterizacio de lepra.	On the Cauterization of Leprosy.
Les lebros alcunas veguadas am cauteri per mot gran juvament, e magerment si la specia de lepra que es fayta per putrefaccio de flacma e de melencolia.	Some lepers are cured with cautery by a great amount of benefit, and especially if the type of leprosy is caused by the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
E donc cum tu vols cauterizar aquel, considera si la lepra es comussan e as aquela curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no deysen, ni esta, e temes sobre le malaute que la corrupcio comprehenda tot le cors de lu e tota la compleccio de lu, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le cap am v cauteris: am un en le mieg loc del cap, e am le segon pus dejos de lu, eves le front a la fi dels cabels; e amdos sobre dos corns; e am un detras, sobre la nuca o servitz.	And therefore, when you want to cauterize that person, consider if the leprosy is common and has been cured with what we have said in the division and not denied, nor stayed, and fear for the patient that the corruption may comprehend all his body and all his composition, then cauterize that on the head with many cauteries: one in the middle of the head, and a second one further away from it, up to the end of the hair; and both above the two horns; and one behind, on the nape or neck.
E ultima la tua ma am le cauteri un pauc entro que emprema en le os una petita empressio, e de lu sian deslocadas las scorsas, per so que la expiracio de grossas vapors sia alleujada de lu; e cauteriza sobre la melsa segon que es precesit.	And finally, your hand with the cautery a little bit to impress on the bone a small impression, and from there are dislocated the scabs, so that the exhalation of thick vapors is alleviated for him; and cauterize on the malleus according to what was previously said.
E si la lepra es ja expanduda sobre le malaute e apar manifestament, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas aquel am aquels cauteris les quals havem ditz en le cap; e am cauteri sobre la extremitat del nas, e am dos cauteris sobre las doas maysselas, e am dos cauteris sobre dos spondils del col, e am vi cauteris sobre les spondils del dos, e am un gran sobre les spondils prop de la coeta, e un sobre la cotea , e am dos sobre las anquas, e am un sobre quascuna anqua, e am dos sobre les donols e un sobre quascun donolh, e am dos sobre les coydes, e am dos sobre les muscles, e am dos las teneretutz del sieu pietz; e cauteriza aquel sobre totas las juncturas dels ditz de las mas e dels pes, e sobre quascun talon dels sieus pes, e sobre les foscils de las suas mas.	And if the leprosy is already spread out on the patient and appears manifestly, then it is good for you to cauterize him with those cauteries which we have said in the head; and with a cautery on the extremity of the nose, and two on both kneecaps, and two on both shoulder blades, and two on the vertebrae of the back, and six on the vertebrae of the neck, and two on each ankle, and two on each heel, and two on the tendons of his feet; and cauterize him on all the joints of his fingers and toes, and on every toe and heel, and on the phalanges of his fingers.
E guarda te dels nervis les quals so sobre le talo que no comburas aquels.	And beware of the nerves which are over the tendon that you do not burn those.
E alcunas veguadas es cauterizat am un cauteri sobre le os del pentenilh e am autre sobre la boca del stomac, e autre sobre le fietge.	And sometimes it is cauterized with a cautery on the bone of the pelvis and another on the mouth of the stomach, and another on the liver.
E sapias que quant mays ajustas cauteris, tant es mays juvatiu e mays conferent; e sapias que le malaute no ha en le cauteri dolor, ayssi cum han les sas, per so quar le cors de lu ja es stupefayt.	And know that the more you adjust the cauteries, the more beneficial and conforming it is; and know that the patient has no pain in the cautery, just as they have in their skin, because his body is already stupified.
E cove que les cauteris sian grans o paucs segon les membres e las juncturas segon que es precedit de las specias dels ferramentz.	And it is good that the cauteries are great or small according to the members and joints, as it is preceded by the species of instruments.
E aprop cura le cauteri am farina de errs coyta am mel e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the cautery with fine flour of ears coitus, mixed with honey and other remedy until it is healed.
Capitol .xlviii.	Chapter 48.
De cauterizacio de stupor.	On the Cauterization of Stupor.
Quan alcun membre es stabozit o adormit e es curat am medicinas, olis e emplastres, e no es sanat, lahoras tu cauteriza aquel membre stabozit am cauteris segon que merita la grandesa del membre o la parvitat de lu.	When some member is stupified or asleep and is cured with medicines, oils, and plasters, but does not heal, then you should cauterize that stupified member with cauteries according to the greatness of the member or its smallness.
E sia lo tieu cauteri intrant la ispicitut de la codena un pauc.	And be your cautery entering into the subtlety of the cord a little bit.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment until it is healed.
E alscunas veguadas es cauterizada alcuna stupor le qual endeve a las mas e als pes, e als spondils del dos e ves le eysiment dels nervis les quals mavon aquel membre, e es remauguda la stupor.	And sometimes it is cauterized some stupor which occurs in the hands and feet, and on the vertebrae of the back, and then the sensation of the nerves that move that member is restored, and the stupor is renewed.
Mays no prusuma sobre aquo sino aquel que es savi en la anotomia dels membre e de la egressio dels nervis tot le cors moventz.	But do not presume on this unless you are wise in the anatomy of the members and the exit of nerves throughout the entire moving body.
Capitol .xlix.	Chapter 49.
De cauterizacio de albaras que es morfea.	On the Cauterization of Moles that are Morpheas.
Quan albaras es antiqua e no comfereys a lu alcu dels enguentz de medicina, lahoras tu cauteriza sobre aquela am cauteri preon un pauc segon la quantitat de la specitut de la codena entro que sia remauguda la blancor e la color de lu, e la color de lu sia mudada.	When moles are old and do not conform to any of the ointments of medicine, then you should cauterize on them with a preconceived cautery a little bit according to the quantity of the subtlety of the cord until the whiteness and color of it are renewed, and the color of it is changed.
E aprop cura aquel am farina de errs e de lentilhas am oli rozat e am folhas de arnagrosa, e am sanc de colomba o am sanc de yronda, da cascuna sia una partida e totas sian mescladas, e aprop sia linit un drap e sus le loc sia pausat entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with fine flour of ears and lentils mixed with rose oil and leaves of arnagrosa, and the blood of dove or the blood of yronda, each being one part and all being mixed together; and then bind a cloth and place it on the location until it is healed.
Capitol .l.	Chapter 50.
De cauterizacio de cranc.	On the Cauterization of Crabs.
Quan canser es comensan e vols aquel ostar, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteri de cercle en le circuit de lu ayssi cum es revolgut.	When a crab is beginning and you want to remove it, then cauterize that with a circular cautery in the circle of it as it is turned.
E diysero les savis que sia cauterizat am lo derier cauteri en le mieg loc; mays a mi no es vist aquo, quar temi que sia ulcerat, e yeu ja e vist aquo alcunas veguadas.	And the wise men said that it should be cauterized with the last cautery in the middle location; but I have not seen this, because I fear that it will be ulcerated, and I have already seen this some times.
E es pus dreyturier que sia cauterizat en le circuit de lu am cercle ayssi cum avem dit, o am motz cauteris.	And it is better to be cauterized in the circle of it with a circle as we have said, or with many cauteries.
Capitol .li.	Chapter 51.
De cauterizacio de adubilati.	On the Cauterization of Adulteries.
Quan alcun adubilati es tardat en maturacio, e aysso es per la superfluitat fazen aquela, o per etat del malaute, quar es vielh en decrepitat, de pauc sanc, o per le temps, e tu vols festinar en la maturacio de adubilati; lahoras cauteriza en le circuit de lu am motz cauteris petitz punctan; e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela fastinara en maturacio.	When some adulteries are delayed in maturity, and thus it is because of the superfluity making that one, or because of the state of the patient, which is old in decrepitude, with little blood, or because of time, and you want to hasten in the maturity of adulteries; then cauterize in the circle of it with many small punctured cauteries; and then leave that which will fasten in maturity.
Mays si tu vols la perforacio de lu am cauteri, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu: e depausa aquel en le mieg loc de adubilati entro que penetre la codena.	But if you want the perforation of it with a cautery, then ignite the cautery which has this form; and place that in the middle location of the adulteries until it penetrates the cord.
E si le cauteri en aquel loc que es pus dejos, per so que le cors del brac sia alleujat; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if the cautery in that location is more distant, because the body of the arm is alleviated; and then cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .lii.	Chapter 52.
De cauterizacio de corrodent.	On the Cauterization of Corrosion.
Corrodent es corrupcio ambulant en le membre, la qual corrodeys aquel ayssi cum a foc comedent lenha secca.	Corrosion is corruption that walks in the member, which corrupts it as fire consumes dry wood.
Donc si vezes aquel corrodent en loc le qual sufferte cauteri am foc, lahoras tu igneys cauteris clavils motz paucs, e grans segon que es convenent en aquel loc en le qual es corrodent.	Therefore, if you find that corrosion in a location where it tolerates a cautery with fire, then ignite small and great cauteries according to what is convenient in that location where the corrosion is.
E aprop cauteriza aquel de tota partida entro que erradiques tota la corrosio e no romangua alcuna causa de lu.	And then cauterize all of it, from top to bottom, until you eradicate all the corrosion and there remains no cause of it.
E aprop leyssa aquel per tres dias, e pausa sobre les locs cauterizats solpre trissat am oli mesclat entro que las scaras sian totas eradicadas e tota la corrupcio.	And then leave that for three days, and pause over the locations cauterized with a gentle touch, mixed with oil, until all the scabs are eradicated and all corruption.
E aprop cura aquel am enguentz carn engendrantz.	And then cure that with ointments of flesh-generating things.
Mays si aprop tres dias vezes que la carn nasca sana en la qual no es corrupcio, bo es; mays sino, lahoras itera le cauteri sobre aquo que es romas en les locs corrumputz.	But if after three days the flesh grows healthy in which there is no corruption, well; but if not, then repeat the cautery on that which remains in the corrupted locations.
E corrodent es medicat alcunas vetz am medicina aguda, quar aquela es meza en loc de cauteri.	And corrosion is cured with some times of acute medicine, because it is a medium in place of cautery.
Mays empero cauteri am foc es de pus leugier juvament.	But nonetheless, a cautery with fire is of greater benefit.
E yeu ja e dit la curacio de lu am medicina aguda en la divisio, e donc pren aquela quan de lu auras endegencia.	And I have already said the cure for it with acute medicine in the division, and therefore take that when you will need it.
Capitol .liii.	Chapter 53.
De cauterizacio de claus e dels autres semblants.	On the Cauterization of Claws and other similar things.
Motas veguadas endeve a las partidas dejos del pe malautia que s’apela clau, e es causa grossa, fentrada, la qual ladeys le pe; e cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, so es cauteri am foc e cauteri am aygua cauda.	Sometimes there is a malady that appears as a claw, which is a great, inflamed cause that weighs down the foot; and cautery in those places is done according to two manners, either with fire or with hot water.
Mays cauteri am foc es que igniscas le cauteri concau semblant a pena de voltor, le qual sia feyt de ferr segon la quantitat la qual contengua le clau de tota partida, e sia de subtils marguas.	But the cautery with fire is to ignite the cautery, resembling a penitent's vulture, which is made of iron according to the quantity that contains the claw from all parts, and is of subtle edges.
E aprop pausa aquel ignit sobre le clau, e aprop revolveys la tua ma am le cauteri en le circuit del clau entro que·l cauteri pervengua a la profunditat del clau.	And then pause that which is ignited over the claw, and then revolve your hand with the cautery in the circle of the claw until the cautery reaches the depth of the claw.
E leyssa aquel per tres dias entro que comense getar brac.	And then leave that for three days until the arm begins to heal.
E aprop emplastre aquel am malvas salvatges trissadas am sal, e leyssa le emplastre sobre aquel per una nuoyt, quar aquel sira eradicat de las suas razitz.	And then apply an ointment to that with wild marshmallows crushed with salt, and leave the ointment on that for one night, because that will be eradicated from its roots.
E aprop cura le loc am enguent de carn generatiu entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the location with an ointment of flesh-generating things until it is healed.
E si so no-convertitz, e motas veguadas accideysso en la superficia del cors, majorment en las mas e les pes, lahoras cove que tu aministres en aquels cauteri am aygua, e es que prenguas una quannula de eram o de ferr o de pena de voltor, e pausa aquela sobre le clau; e aprop geta en la quanula de aygua cauda pauca cantitat, e rete la tua ma, e tu revolveys aquela am compressio de la tua ma de tot, e sia enpremut le marge de la canula en la razit del clau, e atrobara la aygua cauda via al preon de la razit del cau; e espera le malaute un pauc la mordicacio de l’aygua cauda per una hora, e aprop remau aquela, quar le clau am las suas razitz sira erredicat.	And if it does not convert, and many times accidents occur on the surface of the body, mostly in the hands and feet, then it is good that you administer with cauteries of water; and this is to take a cannula made of iron or of a penitent's vulture, and place it on the claw; and then pour into the cannula some cold water, and stretch your hand, and you revolve that with compression from top to bottom, and press the margin of the cannula against the root of the claw, and let the cold water flow back to the point of the root; and wait for the patient a little while the mordication of the cold water for an hour, and then remove it, because the claw with its roots will be eradicated.
E ayssi fe am aquels la i aprop l’autre entro que venguas sobre totz les quals de lor so en le cors.	And thus do it to those places and apply the other remedy until you come to all those parts of their own in the body.
E aprop cura aquels pus que las razitz dels claus so erradicadas am aquo dels enguentz les quals la carn ve engenran.	And then cure those places which are eradicated with the roots of the claws, with that of the ointments which make flesh grow.
Capitol .liiii.	Chapter 54.
De cauterizacio de tremor.	On the Cauterization of Trembling.
