And be the extremities of the two slits at two angles of the incision, which you have made until they converge, and be of their own made angle, so that when they come together, a figure is formed from them.
E aquesta figura es letra greca: la landa.	And this figure is the Greek letter: lambda (λ).
E aprop osta la carn aquela per la quantitat que es le latz de lu agut dejos de lu, aquo que siec la palpebra.	And then place the flesh so that it covers the quantity that is the edge of the eyelid below, which is the shape of the eyelid.
E aprop ajusta las partz seperadas e cos aquelas am le fil de lana; e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit de las medicinas mollificativas e de las calguas entro que sia sanat.	And then adjust the separated parts and sew them together with the thread of wool; and then cure those with what we have said about soothing medicines and poultices, until it is healed.
E si alxacrati endeve per fissura o sutura o cauteri, lahoras cove que tu fendas am fissura plana sobre les pels de la palpebra segon que es precedit.	And if the cataract develops through a fissure or suture or cauterization, then it is good that you make an incision with a flat opening on the hairs of the eyelid as it has preceded.
E aprop separa am la calgua entre doas labias segon que havem dit.	And then separate with a poultice between two lips, according to what we have said.
En la suma del sermo de la cura de alxacrati quan es desus o dejos, que corra en lu operacio, segon que es preparat de la forma de alxacrati, e aquela es en forma de motas diversitatz.	In the summary of the sermon on the cure for cataract when it is above or below, that runs in its operation, according to what is prepared in the form of cataract, and that is in a form of diverse variations.
E le artifexs savi totz temps prepara engen en quascuna manieyra la qual es possibla a lu entro que fassa retornar la figura a la forma natural, o prop de aquela, e aquel malaute segon que a lu conveneys de la operacio e dels strumentz en las majors disposicios.	And the skilled craftsmen always prepare art in any way possible for each operation to bring back the figure to its natural form or close to it, and that patient according to what is convenient for him with regard to the operation and instruments in the best dispositions.
Capitol .xv.	Chapter XV.
De la adherencia de la palpebra am la conjunctiva o am la cornea.	On the Adhesion of the Eyelid to the Conjunctiva or to the Cornea.
Quan accideys aquesta consolidacio a motz homes enayssi que sia solidada la palpebra pus desus am le album del huel, e sia prohibida de la facilitat del movement e de las suas obras naturals, donc cove que tu entrometas la extramitat del ray dejos la palpebra, e eleva en sus aquela, o exten aquela am le unci.	When this adhesion occurs in many men, it is necessary to solidify the eyelid above the white of the eye, and to prohibit its natural movements and works, therefore it is good that you insert the extremity of the thread below the eyelid, and lift it up or stretch it with the uncles.
E aprop tu inscideys la adherencia am spatum subtil, le qual no sia am acuitat de las inscisios, habantz obtus un petit per so que·l malaute no sia inquietat deves la operacio, e remau le spatum que no ledesca le huel am la sua acuitat.	And then you will insert the adhesion with a subtle instrument, which is not sharp as cuts, having obtuse a little so that the patient may not be disturbed during the operation, and leave the instrument so that it does not touch the eye with its sharpness.
E sia la tua inscizio quays excorjan aquela adherencia am facilitat entro que sia retornada la palpebra segon la sua forma natural e que sia sanada tota la adherencia.	And be your incision such that it excises that adhesion with ease, so that the eyelid may return to its natural form and all the adhesion may be healed.
E aprop tu met en le huel aygua salada am la qual tu laves; o distilla en lu de zunia dissolvut en l’aygua.	And then you put into the eye salty water with which you wash it, or distill in it a solution dissolved in water.
E aprop separa entre la palpebra e l’huel am calgua de li, e pausa sobre le huel lana infuza en album de huou, e aprop le tertz jorn usa de causas consolidativas entro que sia sanat.	And then separate between the eyelid and the eye with a poultice of linen, and place it over the eye infused in white of egg, and then use for three days causes that consolidate until it is healed.
Capitol .xvi.	Chapter XVI.
De inscizio de ungla e de eminencia de carn dels lacrimals.	On the Incision of the Eyelash and the Eminence of Flesh of the Lacrimal Glands.
Sapias que ungla es segon dos manieyras, quar o es nervosa, e es semblant a ciphac dur subtil; o es no-nervosa, semblant a humiditat blanca congilada, la qual quan ferr la toca, o es forsat aquela prendre am onci, es abscindida e le onci no es ficat en lu.	Know that the eyelash is according to two manners, because either it is nervous, and is similar to a hard, subtle cypress; or it is non-nervous, similar to white condensed humidity, which when it comes into contact with iron, takes on a dryness, and the eyelash is cut off and the needle is not fixed in place.
E amdos las specias no comensan sino del lacrimal major entro que va petit a petit que cobre la vista e prohibeys le lum e·l movement de huel.	And both species do not begin until the lacrimal gland, which gradually grows smaller as it covers the vision and prohibits the light and movement of the eye.
Mays la manieyra del obrar en la inscizio de lu es que·l malaute pause le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop obre les huels de lu, e eleva la palpebra am la tua ma, e aprop colligeys la ungla am onci de pauca duplicacio e exten aquela a las partidas desus.	But the manner of working in this incision is that the patient places his head on the bed, and then opens his eyes, lifts the eyelid with your hand, and carefully collects the eyelash with a needle of gentle doubling and stretches it to the upper parts.
E aprop pren una agula e entromet en aquela un pel de cavalh o de buou o de vaqua, o de semblantz, o de fiel fort, o duplica la extremitat de la agulha petit a petit e fica aquela en le mieg de la ungla, e penetra aquela am la agulha, e lia am fiel la ungla; e exten aquela a las partidas desus, e excorja am le pel le latz de la ungla lo qual siec la pupilla.	And then take a needle and insert into it a piece of horse or ox or cow hair, or something similar, or a strong thread, or double the extremity of the needle little by little and place it in the middle of the eyelash, and penetrate that with the needle, and tie the eyelash to the thread; and stretch that to the upper parts, and excise on the side of the eyelash which touches the pupil.
E ayssi tu sieguas aquela am le pel entro al derier de lu.	And then you will follow it with the hair until the end of it.
E aprop tu inscideys le romanent en la razitz del lacrimal am spatum subtil o am petitas forfexs, e leysa la carn del lacrimal natural per so que per inscizio de aquela no endevengua fluxs de lagremas continuabla.	And then you will insert the remaining part into the root of the lacrimal gland with a subtle instrument or small scissors, and loosen the natural flesh of the lacrimal gland so that through this incision there may not be continuous flows of tears.
E alscunas vetz la ungla am le sol onci estenduda o am fiel, ayssi co havem dit, e aprop sia excurjat am spatum leon del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And sometimes the eyelash with its extended or tied needle is thus, as we have said, and then it should be excised with a lion-shaped instrument, which has this form:
E guarda te que am le spatum no toques la tunica cornea e que avengua en lu ruptura, e que la pupilla sia perforada.	And beware that in the instrument you do not touch the tunic of the cornea and cause a rupture, and that the pupil is pierced.
Aprop la inscizio geta en le huel un pauc de sal trissa o di cief fayt de siniar, e leyssa aquel entro al autre dia; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove entro que sia sanat.	And then the incision should be left in the eye for a few days or until a white crust forms, and let that remain until the next day; and then cure it with water as is necessary, until it is healed.
E si la ungla no es nervoza e no podes metre la agulha, ni es ficada en aquela le onci, lahoras motas veguadas aquesta specia de ungla es curada am medicinas, e es sanada ayssi cum yeu e recomtat en la divisio.	And if the eyelash is not nervous and you cannot insert the needle, nor is it fixed in that place with the thread, then many times this species of eyelash is cured by medicines, and is healed just like yeast and recounted in the division.
E si tu vols inscindir aquela, lahoras tu obre le huel del malaute e pren spatum subtil leon de freul acuitat segon aquesta forma:	And if you want to excise it, then you will operate on the eye of the patient and take a subtle instrument, lion-shaped, with acute precision, according to this form:
am subtilitat.	with subtlety.
E si vezes que aquela es rarificada e es confugida e empren en aquela razit, lahoras distilla de la tua ora en le huel de cief fayt de siniar o am cief rog o am sal trissat, e opila le huel entro a l’autre dia.	And if sometimes it is rarefied and is confused and enters into the root, then you will distill from your eye a white crust or a grayish-gray crust or a crushed salt, and stop up the eye until the next day.
E aprop itera sobre aquela la operacio entro que sia remaugut tot aquo que es de lu, sino que·l contrari apostema caut sia en le huel, quar lahoras tu leyssa aquela, e cura al comensament la apostema entro que sia sanat.	And then repeat the operation on that until everything is removed from it, unless a contrary aposteme catches in the eye, because then you will leave it alone, and cure the aposteme at first until it is healed.
E aprop itera la tua operacio sobre aquela am razo entro que sia sanat.	And then repeat your operation on that with reason, until it is healed.
La emenencia de la carn lacrimal, si notz en le huel per gran nocument, sia suspendut am onci; e inscideys aquela de aquela una partida, e no ultimes la inscizio per so que no inscidesqua fluxs de lagremas.	The eminence of the lacrimal flesh, if noticed in the eye for great harm, should be suspended by thread; and excise that part from it, and do not finish the incision so that you may not cut off flows of tears.
E aprop distilla en le lacrimal cief rog e fayt de siniar entro que sia sanat.	And then distill into the lacrimal grayish-gray crust or white crust, until it is healed.
Capitol .xvii.	Chapter XVII.
De inscizio de alguazardenic e de aquo que es nascut de carn ajustada en le huel.	On the Incision of Algae and Water that is Born from Flesh Adjusted in the Eye.
Alcunas veguadas en les huels de alcus es nascuda carn roga, e es sobre-pausada entro que cobre la pupilla, o apropinqua o estrenh sobre las palpebras e fort leu comprem las palpebras a las partidas deforo e es assemblada a roza de balaustra.	Sometimes in some eyes is born red flesh, and it is superimposed until it covers the pupil, or approaches or stretches over the eyelids and strongly compresses the eyelids to the parts above and is assembled like the rose of a balcony.
Mays la operacio en lu es que·l malaute pausa le sieu cap en le tieu se; e aprop obre les huels de aquel e colligeys tota aquela carn am oncis convenientz ad aquo, e te aquo am una forcep o am cesti; e aprop inscindiys la carn el comensament entro que tot sia finit am le encisori, e guarda te del huel que no ledescas aquel deves la tua operacio.	But the operation in this case is that the patient places his head on the bed; and then opens the eyes of that place and collects all that flesh with suitable needles and threads; and then excises the flesh at the beginning until everything is finished with the scissors, and beware of the eye that you do not touch it with your operation.
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscides aquelas o am espatum le qual nos havem recomtat en la inscizio de la ungla, o am petitas forfexs am las quals es colligit ascebel segon que vindra la forma de lu aprop aquest capitol.	And be your incision with which you excise those or with the instrument which we have recounted in the incision of the eyelash, or with small scissors with which it is gathered in such a way that the form of it comes to this chapter.
Donc cum es complida la tua inscizio e es remauguda tota aquela carn, lahoras omple le huel de sal trissa, o destilla en lu polvera roga e semblantz a lu de las medicinas corrossivas, e pausa sobre le huel deforo coto am album de huou entro que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	Therefore, when your incision is complete and all that flesh is removed, then fill the eye with crushed salt, or distill into it red powder resembling it to the corrosive medicines, and place on the eye outside a cloth soaked in white of egg until you are assured that there will be no aposteme.
E si roman alcuna causa de alguardenici e es senhoragat sanc caut, e temes apostema caut, lahoras leyssa le huel e cura aquela apostema am aquo que ceda aquela apostema, e aprop itera sobre aquel am operacio entro que sia sanat, e semblantment fay en la carn ajustada la qual accideys en le huel de aquesta especia.	And if there remains any cause of algae and it is covered with a scar, and you fear an aposteme, then leave the eye alone and cure that aposteme with water which will heal that aposteme, and then repeat the operation on that until it is healed, and similarly do in the flesh adjusted which occurs in the eye of this species.
Mays empero tu cove que alienes tota curacio del huel freul per via natural o per via accidental, obran am ferr, e no metas la tua ma en alcuna de aquestas operacios entro que veges que aquel membre sia suffertant aquela operacio.	But still you must be careful to alienate all cure of the eye by natural or accidental means, working with iron, and not place your hand in any of these operations until you see that member is sufficient for that operation.
Capitol .xviii.	Chapter XVIII.
De colleccio de sabel en le huel.	On the Collection of Sabellum in the Eye.
Sabel so venas rogas las quals son testudas sobre le huel e prohibeysso al vesement la sua operacio, e develican le huel am longitut de dias.	Sabellum is a red vein which runs through the eye and prohibits its normal operation, and by its length it reveals the eye's days.
Donc necessari es al comensament que tu consideres si le huel en le qual es sabel es fort e en lu no es autra malautia que sabel, lahoras tu colligeys aquel sabel.	Therefore, it is necessary at the beginning that you consider whether the eye in which there is sabellum is strong and does not have another disease besides sabellum, then you will collect that sabellum.
E es que tu comandes al malaute que pause le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop suspen aquelas venas am un onci o am dos segon la tua prudencia; e sia aquel onci de subtil duplicacio segon aquesta forma:	And it is that you command the patient to place his head on the bed, and then suspend those veins with one thread or two according to your prudence; and let that thread be of subtle doubling according to this form:
o so dos oncis gradantment en un cos segon aquesta forma:	or two threads gradually in one case, according to this form:
E aprop sian colligidas aquelas venas am forses subtils, am subtilitat, e abstergeys le sanc hora aprop hora, entro que vegas aquelas venas esser remaugudas del huel e sian revolgudas.	And then are collected those veins with subtle forces, with subtlety, and wash away the blood hour by hour, until you see those veins to be removed from the eye and turned around.
E guarda te que tu no ledes le huel am las extremitatz del spatum; e si’ la tua operacio en le miegjorn denant le solelh, e sias mot ferm en la tua operacio que no inscidas sino aquelas venas.	And beware that you do not touch the eye with the extremities of the instrument; and if your operation is in the middle of the day before the sun, and be very firm in your operation that you only excise those veins.
E quan tu auras complitz, lahoras tu distilla en le huel cief vert o rog per que am sa acuitat corrodesca aquo que es remaugut del sabel.	And when you have completed, then you will distill into the eye green or red powder so that with its acute corrosion it may dissolve the water that is removed from the sabellum.
Mays si aquo no es a tu possible colligeys tot en aquela hora, e lahoras tu emplastra tot am aquo que cede la dolor de lu, e leyssa lu per alcus dias entro que sia sedada la dolor de lu e que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	But if it is not possible for you to collect all in that hour, then gather as much as you can and plaster the whole with water that relieves the pain of it, and leave it for a few days until the pain is assuaged and there is assurance of no aposteme.
E aprop itera sobre lu segon que la mateyssa manieyra entro que sia sanat.	And then repeat the operation on that according to the same manner until it is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de las forfexs:	And this is the form of the scissors:
Capitol .xix.	Chapter XIX.
De reduccio de arizati al nas.	On the Reduction of Swellings at the Nose.
Quan tu curas arisati am cauteri o am medicina aguda comburent segon que es precedida la narracio de lu e no es sanat, lahoras no es engen en lu sino que fendas sobre le apostema deves la maturitat de lu, e que extraguas tota la humiditat la qual es en lu e·l poyre entro que sia descubert le os.	When you cure swellings with cauterization or sharp medicine, and they do not heal as told, then there is no need for further intervention in that place, but rather you should cut into the aposteme until its maturity, and extract all the moisture which is in it and drain it so that the bone may be revealed.
E donc cum es descubert le os e vezes en lu corrupcio o negror, lahoras tu ratz lu am un sturment del qual aquesta es la forma:	And therefore, when the bone is revealed and corruption or blackness appears in it, then you will rasp it with an instrument of which this is the form:
E es nompnat de aspre cap, e sia feyt de fer indi, e sia le cap redon ayssi cum asir le qual sia fayt punctat per punctacio de lima o aliskalfati per punctacio subtil (ayssi cum es en la forma seguent).	And it is called "aspre cap", and it is made of iron, and its head is rounded like that which is made pointed by a file or an emery wheel in a subtle point (such as shown in the following form).
E pausa aquel sobre le loc corrumput del os, e aprop revolveys aquel entre les tieus ditz, e prem la tua ma petit a petit entro que sapias que aquela corropcio es rasa.	And place that on the corroded part of the bone, and then turn it between those two fingers, and press your hand gently, little by little, until you know that that corruption is removed.
E aquo sia fayt alcunas veguadas, e aprop restaura le loc am causas exsiccativas e stipticas.	And so it will be done some times, and then restore the place with causes of drying and tightening.
Donc si·l loc es consolidat e es en lu nascuda bona carn e es abscindit le cors de la sania e roman per xl dias, e no es renovat e no es apostemat e no accideys en lu accident, lahoras tu sapias que es sanat.	Therefore, if the place is consolidated and good flesh has grown in it, and the body of the sickness has been removed and remains for 40 days, and is not renewed or apostemated, nor does any accident occur there, then you will know that it is healed.
E sino, lahoras no es en lu engen sino reduzir la fissura a la forma del nas, e segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu descuebras de segon os am ferr o am medicina acuta, e cum sira descubert le os, lahoras tu pren tribo segon aquesta forma:	And if not, then it is not in that place to intervene, but rather to reduce the fissure to the form of the nose, and according to this manner: and it is that you uncover the second bone with iron or sharp medicine, and when the bone is uncovered, then you take a thread according to this form:
Sia la extramitat de lu ferr triangulada, e·l fust de lu sia prim extenuat entro a la extremitat ayssi cum vezes assi.	Be the extremity of the iron triangular, and the shaft of it be first thinned out to the extremity in such a way that it is as if it were worn away.
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le os, e sia aquel prop del lacrimal; e alongua la tua ma un pauc del huel, e aprop revol la tua ma am le tribo entro que penetre tot le os, e aquel sente le malaute per asso que atroba vent yssir per so quan te la sua ma.	And then place that on the bone, and it should be right next to the lacrimal; and stretch your hand a little bit from the eye, and then turn your hand with the thread in such a way that it penetrates all the bone, and he feels the patient by pushing with his hand as if he were looking out through that when he takes his hand away.
Donc lahoras restaura le loc am medicinas stipticas exsiccantz ayssi cum t’e eyssenhat.	Therefore, then restore the place with drying and tightening medicines in such a way that they will be suitable for your patient.
Donc cum nays la carn e·l loc es endurazit, lahoras la materia la qual effundia a las partidas deforo retorna al nas, donc aquo es pus leugier sobre le malaute.	Therefore, when the flesh and the place are hardened, then the material which was flowing to the parts above returns to the nose, therefore that is easier on the patient.
Capitol .xx.	Chapter XX.
De reduccio de la eminencia del huel.	On the Reduction of the Eminence of the Eye.
Quan le huel emineys am la sua totalitat e no accideys en le vezement nocument ni diminuacio, lahoras cove que laxas le malaute, e aprop que·l segues, e aprop que pausas ventozas en le cervitz ses scarificacio e succa per bona succaccio; e aprop pausa sobre le huel liniment le qual sia fayt de acatra e aloe e enses e sarcocolla, e aprop strenh le emplaustre sobre le huel am motz polvils.	When the eye protrudes entirely and does not cause harm or diminution in the vicinity, then you must loosen the patient, and then follow, and then pause for breaths in the neck without scarification and with good suction; and then place a poultice on the eye made of equal parts of safflower, aloe, and sarcocolla, and then strengthen the plaster over the eye with many powders.
E la manieyra dels polvils es que prenguas draps de li leons motz, e quascun drap sia duplicat en quatre plecs; e fay de aquels motz.	And the manner of the powders is that you take cloths of lion's mane many times, and each cloth be folded in four pieces; and make powder from those.
E aprop pausa aquels la un sobre le autre segon la quantitat de la qual ha le huel necessitat.	And then place those one on top of another according to the quantity that the eye needs.
E aprop strenh sobre aquels am drap dur am fort strictura; e itera las ventosas am succio ses scarificacio; e aprop osta las ventosas e leyssa le huel streyt le dia e la nueyt.	And then strengthen over those with a strong, tight cloth; and repeat the suction without scarification; and then stop the suction and leave the eye straight for a day and night.
Mays si entretant le liguament es mollificat, lahoras cove que sia mot streyt.	But if in the meantime the ligament is relaxed, then it is necessary to be very strict.
E aprop osta le liament aprop le dia e la nueyt ayssi cum havem dit.	And then stop the ligament for a day and night just as we have said.
E si vezes le huel ja esser redusit, bo es, e sino, lahoras itera le emplastre am les polvils e la strictura e las ventosas entro que sia sanat.	And if the eye has already been reduced, then it is good; and if not, then you must repeat the plaster with powders, tightness, and suction until it is healed.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De la inscizio de la eminencia de la tunica uvea.	On the Incision of the Eminence of the Uveal Tunic.
Quan endeve disrupcio en la tunica uvea, e aprop es eminent e procezeys fora las palpebras ayssi cum un gra de rasim, e es orrazada la forma de home per aquo, e vols aquo inscidir, lahoras la operacio en lu es ayssi cum havem recomtat, que tu entrometas la agula en la razitz de la uvea de la partida dejos en la partida desus, e aprop met la agula autra en la qual sia fil doble de la part del lacrimal, e fay aquela penetrar e leyssa la primieyra agula segon la sua disposicio; e aprop inscideys le loc del fiel doble e leva am aquel la partida de la uvea en le circuit de la agula, e strenh aquela mot.	When the uveal tunic becomes disrupted and there is an eminence that proceeds outside the eyelids like a grain of raisin, and it is rounded in shape like a human being by this, and you want to excise it, then the operation on it is as we have recounted, where you introduce the needle into the root of the uvea from the lower part and another needle into the double thread from the lacrimal side, and make that thread penetrate and leave the first needle according to its disposition; and then excise the location of the double thread and lift up with it the part of the uvea in the circuit of the needle, and strengthen that motion.
E aprop extratz la agula e pausa sobre le huel lana infusa en album de huou e leyssa entro que cayha le fil am la uva.	And then extract the needle and place on the eye wool infused in white of egg, and leave it until the thread comes out with the uvea.
E aprop cura le huel am aquo que conforte aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.	And then cure the eye with water that comforts it until the wound is healed.
E alcunas veguadas aduna de tota partida am cercle de drap entro le huel ajuste eminencia gran, e aprop sia perforat am le spatum subtil que vengua al preon del huel, e corra la humiditat albuginea, e descen le huel e intra tantost.	And sometimes gather all parts together with a circle of cloth into the eye, and then it is pierced with a subtle instrument that comes to the forepart of the eye, and flows the humor of the cornea, and descends the eye and enters soon.
E aprop strenh entro que sia sanat.	And then strengthen until it is healed.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXII.
De curacio de alconati.	On the Cure of Alconati.
Aquesta malautia que es apelada alconati no es sino sania la qual es ajustada en le huel semblant a aygua dessendent e no es aquela.	This disease which is called Alconati is nothing but a humor that is settled in the eye, similar to water descending and not that.
Mays la manieyra del obrar en ela es que fasses le malaute sezer sobre la sela aparelada e dreyta, e aprop pren le cap sieu en las tuas mas de doas partz e mau aquel entro que veias la sania pervenir a las partidas dejos, e aprop sia siccada e no descenda, e sia ostat le lum, e·l malaute veia las causas ayssi cum vezia.	But the manner of operating on it is that you make the patient sit on a prepared and straight bed, and then take his head in your hands on both sides, and lift him up until you see the humor coming out from the parts above, and then dry it and not let it flow down, and stop the light, and the patient sees the causes just as he sees.
E si no descendra en jos, sapias que es aygua.	And if it does not flow down below, you will know that it is water.
Mays si no es preparat le descendement a la sania am aquo que havem dit, lahoras fay le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e aprop pren spatum subtil e fen am aquel sobre le pannicol cernent un petit deves la continuacio de la conjunctiva am la tunica cornea en la corona (entro al loc vuet), entro que sia fora-getada la sania.	But if the descent of the humor is not prepared with the water as we have said, then make the patient sit between your hands and take a subtle instrument and find it on the panniculus cerning a little of the continuation of the conjunctiva with the tunic of the cornea in the crown (into that place where you see), until the humor is forgotten.
Donc cum es fora-getada, lahoras tu distilla en le huel aygua cauda en la qual has mesclat mel o aygua en la qual ja has bulit fenugrec e mel.	Therefore, when it is forgotten, then you will distill into the eye cold water in which you have mixed honey or water in which you have boiled fenugreek and honey.
E aprop sia curat am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	And then be cured by the other causes until it is healed.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXIII.
De la curacio de la aygua descendent del huel.	On the Cure of the Water Descending from the Eye.
Ja havem dit las specias de la aygua en la divisio e qual conveneys a perforar am sermo declarant, lahoras aquel segon la sanetat.	We have already said the species of water in the division and which is suitable to pierce with the instrument declaring the word, then that one according to health.
Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre un cayrat e lia le sieu huel sa, lu mot stringent.	Then it is necessary for you to make the patient sit between your hands on a chair and bind his head with a cloth, tight and strong.
E aprop pausa prop de la palpebra del sieu huel la tua ma senestra, si le huel en le qual es l’aygua es le huel senestra; o am la tua ma dreyta, si le huel es le dextre.	And then place your left hand near the eyelid of the patient's eye on which is the water, if it is the left eye; or with your right hand, if it is the right eye.
E aprop am la tua ma dextra pren almagda, si le huel es senestre; o am la tua ma senestra, si le huel es de dreyt.	And then with your right hand take almonds, if the eye is left; or with your left hand, if it is right.
E aprop pausa la extremitat de almagda prop de la corona per la grossesa del ray en le album del huel de part del mendre lacrimal, e aprop enpelleys almagda am vertut e revol la tua ma am aquel.	And then place the extremity of the almond near the crown for the thickness of the rim in the album of the eye from the smaller lacrimal part, and then press the almond with virtue and turn your hand with it.
E aprop penetre en le album del huel e sentas que almagda ja es pervenguda a causa vueda.	And then penetrate into the album of the eye and feel that the almond has already reached the seen cause.
E cove que sia la masura del cami de almagda al preon la mesura del spazi le qual es de la pupilla entro a la fi de la negror, e es la corona del huel; quar tu veyras am aquel pupilla am la visio de l’huel per la clartat de la tunica cornea.	And it is necessary that the measure of the path of the almond to the fore part be the measure of the space which is from the pupil to the end of the blackness, and it is the crown of the eye; for you will see with that pupil through the vision of the eye by the clarity of the tunic of the cornea.
E aprop pausa almagda entro al loc en le qual es l’aygua, e aprop tu la atira en jos una veguada aprop autra, e donc si la aygua descen tantost, lahoras vetz le malaute aquo sobre le qual huebre la sua vista tantost, e almagda en le sieu huel.	And then place the almond in the location where is the water, and then attract it down once or twice, and therefore if the water descends soon, then see the patient on which his vision will be restored soon, and the almond in his eye.
E aprop repausa se un pauc; donc si la aygua es descenduda, lahoras tu depausa aquela autre veguada abantz que almagda ne sia getada.	And then rest for a moment; therefore if the water has descended, then you will remove that other almond before it is thrown away.
E donc quan es sicada e no descen, lahoras tu extrat almagda am facilitat, e revol am aquel la tua ma pauc a pauc, e aprop dissolveys en l’aygua un petit de sal clara de gemma e am aquela lava le huel dedintz; e aprop pausa fora le huel coto o stopa o lana infusa en oli rozat e album de huou e ligua am aquo le huel sa.	And therefore when it is dry and does not descend, then you will extract the almond with ease, and turn your hand with it little by little, and then dissolve a small amount of clear gemstone salt in that water and wash the eye inward; and then pause outside the eye with a cloth or stopper or wool infused in rose oil and egg white, and bind the eye with water.
Mays nos e aquels que so de nostre temps pause sobre aquel comi trissat am album de huou.	But we will use those of our time that are passed on to us with an album of egg white.
E si no obezeys a tu almagda al intrament de l’huel per la sua duricia — quar es alcu dels homes del qual le huel es dur mot —, lahoras cove que prenguas le spatum le qual es nompnat alberid del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if it does not obey your almond at the instrument of the eye because of its hardness - for there are some men whose eyes are very hard - then you must take the instrument which is called "alberid" and this is its form:
E donc perfora am aquel aquela conjunctura, e no ultimes la tua ma en le trauc, e no es si no que fassas via ad almagda loc subtil.	And then pierce with that instrument the conjunctiva, and do not keep your hand in the wound, but rather make a way for the almond to reach a subtle location.
E aprop entromet almagda segon que havem dit.	And then insert the almond as we have said.
E deves le compliment de la tua obra, sia preparat al malaute dormitori descentment fayt en le qual dorma sobre le sieu dos en mayson tenebrosa, e sia prohibit de totz movementz .	And the completion of your work, prepare the patient for a sleeping descent made in the dark house where he will sleep on his back with no movements whatsoever.
E pausa en la natura de lu aquo per que sia linida la sua natura, e no maugua le sieu cap a la partida dreyta ni senestra de tot.	And pause in the nature of it so that his nature is aligned, and not move his head to the right or left at all.
E sia le liament segon la sua disposicio entro al tertz dia.	And let the ligature be according to its disposition within three days.
E aprop deslia aquel en aquela maysso tenebrosa e exproha la freol vista, e fay li vezer alcunas causas, e aprop retorna le liament entro al dia .vii.	And then loosen that in the dark house and uncover the fresh sight, and make it see some causes, and then return to the ligature within seven days.
E no cove que fassas aquo en la hora de las curacios o tantost aprop la infusio.	And do not need to do that at the hour of medications or soon after infusion.
Habantz cove que tu alienes aquo per so quar la aygua puega leugierament per gran e vehement de reguardament.	They had told you to abandon this because the water flows more lightly through great and fervent contemplation.
Mays si accideys apostema caut, lahoras cove que deslias le huel denant le vii dia, e rectifica aquel am aquo que ceda apostema.	But if an aposteme appears cautiously, then you must remove the eye before the seventh day and correct it with water that dissolves the aposteme.
Lahoras tu absol la vista de lu e pausa sobre la cara de lu oral per le qual sia regit le vezement de lu dejos lu per alcus dias, lu existent en la mayszo tenebrosa.	Then you absolve the sight of him and pause on his face near the orifice by which it is governed for some days, existing in the darkest darkness.
E aprop sia gitat de aquela mayzo gradantment e conversa8 en las suas causas.	And then be guided gradually from that darkness and converse with his own causes.
E sapias que in alchatea no es excusat le discipol de visio alcunas veguadas, e lahoras tu sias ardit sobre la operacio.	And know that in alchemy there is no excuse for the disciple to see some things at times, and then you will be bold on the operation.
E ja es pervengut a nos de alcu de aquels les quals so al Artach , e alcu disse que fayt foc en al Ayrac magdaam perforat am le qual es succada la aygua.	And already it has been passed on to us by some of those who are at the Artach, and some said that it makes fire in the Ayrrac, greatly perforated, through which the water is sucked.
Mays empero yeu non e vist degu en la nostra terra le qual haia perfeyt aquo, ni e aquo legit en alcu dels libres dels antics; e es possible que aquo sia novel.	But meanwhile, I have not seen this done in our land which has perfected that, nor read it in some of the books of the ancients; and it is possible that this is new.
E aquestas so las formas de las specias de magdaan per que sia sobre aquelas aquel le qual ignora aquelas:	And these are the forms of the species of magnesia, by which one is above those who do not know them:
E sian faytas de eram o de ferr propriament, e sian las extramitatz de lor am aquesta subtilitat triangulada, la extremitat aguda ayssi cum aquela es la forma.	And they are made of iron or bronze properly, and they are the extremities of their own magnesia with this subtlety triangularly, the sharp end thus as it is the form.
Capitol .xxiv.	Chapter XXIV.
De la curacio de carn nada en le nas.	On the Cure of Cured Meat in the Nose.
Quan en le nas so nascudas carns diversas ajustadas de las quals es alcuna causa la qual es assemblada a scorpio de motz pes, o a polip peys; e aquesta malautia es apelada polipus quar es a semblansa de aquel peys representat.	When in the nose there are born various meats diversified of which some cause is assembled to that of Scorpio's weight or to Polyp's flesh; and this disease is called Polypus because it resembles that flesh represented.
E de lu es carn cancrosa, lapadea, de fusca color; e de lu es que es carn leon no de color fusca.	And from there is a cancerous meat, pale and of a dark color; and then it is that the lion's flesh is not of a dark color.
Donc en aquela que es en aquestas carns leon no fraudulenta ni cancroza, cove que fassas le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e posat al solelh, e huebre las nars de lu, e picoys le tieu onci en aquelas carns.	Therefore, in that which is not fraudulent nor cancerous, it is necessary to make the patient sit between your hands and place him in the sun, and anoint his nose with that meat.
E aprop extrat aquela a las partidas deforo, e aprop inscindeys aquo que has comprehendut de aquelas am spatum agut subtil de la una partida entro que sapias que tota la carn ja es ostada; que si roman de lu deguna causa de la qual la abscisio es possibla, lahoras tu ratz aquo am la un dels estrumentz subtils am facilitat entro que de lu romangua denguna causa.	And then extract that to the parts above, and then incise it with the sharp instrument of one side into the part where you know that all the meat has been removed; if there remains any cause from which ablation is possible, then you must ratify that with one of the subtle instruments with ease until no cause remains.
Mays si senhoreja am sanc o accida apostema caut, lahoras tu pausa a lu aquo que cove; o es dels apostemas malignes, lahoras tu coyta e cauteriza aquel entro que sia abscindit sanc e sian ostadas las cavas totas.	But if the patient's wound is septic or an apostema appears cautiously, then you must pause and apply that which is necessary; or if it is one of the malignant apostemas, then you must cauterize and cut out that part until the wound is abscessed and all cavities are removed.
E aprop sia getatz en le nas aprop la inscizio vi agre e aygua o vi.	And then be guided in the nose, approaching the incision with water or oil.
Mays si le nas es ubert e de lu procezeys humiditat entro al palat, lahoras sapias que ja es sanat.	But if the nose is swollen and there is moisture proceeding from it into the palate, then you will know that it has already been cured.
Mays si la humiditat no penetra segon que cove, lahoras tu sapias que dedintz lu es carn nada en los pus sobiras osses de las nars als quals non es pervengut abscizio.	But if the moisture does not penetrate as it should, then you will know that there is no meat in the nose above the bones of the nostrils to which the ablation has not been performed.
Donc lahoras cove que entromitas fiel de li al qual sia alcuna grosseza, e nuza en lu motz nuzes, e pausa entre quascun nutz la quantitat del dit o mens, e engene le malaute e entromet una extremitat del fiel en le nars am lo ray o am autra causa la qual es a lu possibla.	Therefore, it is necessary that you insert the faithful one into the place where there is some thickening, and nuzzle in each notch the quantity of said or minus, and pause between each notch the quantity of said or minus, and guide the patient and insert one end of the faithful one into the nose with the ray or with another cause which is possible to it.
E pus que aquo aura fayt, que atire le sieu odorament entro que pervengua a las canals de las nars, e sia eyssit sobre le sieu golayro, quar tropas veguadas le semblant ad aquesta accio fan les enfantz a las scolas, e es leugiera causa ad aquel que ho vol far.	And after this has been done, that the patient's odorant is attracted into the canals of the nose, and be extracted on his gullet, because many times the same thing seems to happen at school, and it is a light cause for one who wants to do so.
E aprop pausa las dos extramitatz del fiel, una extremitat que iesca sobre le nas et l’autra que romangua en le nas, e aprop aministra serratura de carn am les nuzes que so en le fiel, e fay aquo entro que sapias que las carn ja so am les nuzes del fiel.	And then pause the two extremities of the faithful one, with one end coming out of the nose and the other remaining in the nose, and then administer a seal of meat to the notches that are on the faithful one, and do this until you know that the flesh is already at the notches of the faithful one.
E aprop extratz le fiel, e pausa en le nas aprop la abstraccio del sanc una calgua , e fay aquo per tres dias o mays entro que l’enguent corrodo tot aquo que es romas de las carns.	And then extract the faithful one, and pause in the nose near the abstraction of blood, one cup, and do this for three days or more until the encrustation is all consumed that remains from the flesh.
E aprop en la fi de la causa, pausa en le nas una canula de plom per alscus jorns entro que sia sanat.	And then pause in the nose with a lead cannula for several days until it is cured.
Mays si endigeys de curacio que exsique, usa de aquela.	But if you find a cure that exists, use that one.
E aquesta es la forma del instrument a capipurge fazedor am le qual son distillatz olis e medicinas en le nars:	And this is the form of the instrument for making capipurge, with which oils and medicines are distilled in the nose:
E fay aquo de argent o de eram, la qual sia semblant a una petita lampesa uberta, ayssi cum petita conqua, e le meat semblantment.	And make it of silver or bronze, which is like a small lantern open, just as a small shell, and the meat similarly.
E si vols, fay una canula clausa ayssi cum cana, e la cancula del estrument a capipurge fazedor e sia plana, descuberta; a la qual sia manubre en lo derier de lu, am le qual tenguas aquela quan escaufas en lu oli o aquo que tu vols dels sucs e de las causas suctiblas.	And if you wish, make a closed cannula like a reed, and the cannula of the instrument for making capipurge, and it shall be flat, open; at which will be a handle on the last part of it, with which you can hold that when you are extracting in oil or water that you want from the juices and causes susceptible.
E aquestz capipurgi es precios: recipe de enforbi de castor, de balayra blanc, de giengiebre, e piletre de safra, de pebre lonc, de escafragia, de epetum de spic ana unc. vi cumfizeys am suc de bleda e de caul, e sian faytas pillulas, e sia destemprada una pillula am aygua tebeza, e sia gitat en las nars del malaute jasent envers.	And these are the prices of capipurge: recipe of enforbi of castor, of white balayra, of gengibre, and saffron piletre, of long pepper, of escarole, of epetum spice an ounce. And thus you will make pills with the juice of bleda and caulis, and make them into pellets, and one pellet will be tempered with tea water, and inserted into the nostrils of the patient sitting upright.
Capitol .xxv.	Chapter XXV.
De theyls natz en las extramitatz del nas.	On the Worms that are in the Extremities of the Nose.
Motas veguadas es nat theyl en las extramitatz del nas, e es magnificat e omentat en alscus dias entro en que mot es leg le reguardament de lu.	Many times it is born a worm in the extremities of the nose, and it is magnified and increased in some days until the regard of it is seen.
E per aquo cove que tu inscidas aquel en le comensament de la apparissio de lu, e erediques tot aquel.	And therefore it is necessary that you incise it at the beginning of its appearance, and eradicate all of it.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc o cauteri o medicina comburent la qual estia en loc de lu.	And then pause over the place, or cauterize or apply medicine that is suitable for the location.
Mays si es tardada la sua inscizio entro que sia magnificat, lahoras considera si es lapificat, dur, de fusca color e de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr quar es apostema crancos; quar motas veguadas ad aquel que inscideys aquesta apostema endeve per lu granda malicia sobre aquel le qual aquel havia.	But if it is delayed in its incision until it is magnified, then consider whether it is softened, hard, of dark color and little sensation; then do not touch that with iron because it is a cancerous apostema; for many times those who incise this apostema incur great malice towards that which had been.
E si le apostema es de leon tocament e no es de fosca color, e vezes que inscizio es possibla en tot aquel, lahoras evacua le malaute e inscideys aquel senes temor, e cura le loc am aquo que exsique e costrenh entro que sia sanat.	And if the apostema is of lion's touch and not of dark color, and many times incision is possible in all that, then evacuate the patient and incise that without fear, and cure the place with what exists and constrains until it is healed.
Capitol .xxvi.	Chapter XXVI.
De sutura del nas e de las labias e de la aurelha quan la continuitat es dissolvuda per plagua o per semblantz.	On the Suture of the Nose and Lips and Ear when Continuity is Dissolved by Wound or Similarity.
Sapias que quan accideys solucio de continuitat en una de aquestas cartillages, pauc confereys en aquela operacio sino en alcus homes.	Know that when solution of continuity occurs in one of these cartilages, few confer in this operation except in certain men.
Donc cove, quan endeve ad alcu alcuna causa de aquelas, que consideres si es plagua fresca am le sieu sanc, e lahoras tu ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	Therefore, when you find that some cause of those is present, consider whether it is a fresh wound with its own blood, and then you should adjust the two lips of the wound with suture, and carefully cure that until it is healed.
E si las labias de solucio de continuitat so ja separadas, e quascuna es fayta sana, lahoras cove que tu excorjes quascuna partida de la sua codena apparent entro que n’iesca sanc.	And if the lips of solution of continuity are already separated, and each is made whole, then it is necessary that you excise each part of its own cord-like appearance until blood comes out.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias am sutura e strenh aquelas, e sobre aquelas pulveriza sanc de drago e enses trissat, e pausa sobre la polvera una pessa de emplaustra diafinicon, o de alcu autre dels emplastres consolidatius, e leyssa aquel liat per dos jorns o per tres, e aprop deslia aquel e permuta aquel emplaustre e leyssa aquel entro que·ls fiels per si sian abscinditz, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then adjust the two lips with suture and strengthen those, and over those sprinkle blood of dragon and powdered three times, and pause on the powder a compress of emplastrum diaphanic, or some other consolidating emplastre, and leave that bound for two days or three, and then remove that and replace it with another emplastre and leave that until the flesh is fully absorbed, and carefully cure with anointing until it is healed.
Mays la manieyra de la sutura es que tu agregues la solucio de continuitat o am agulhas ayssi cum havem recomtat en la sutura del ventre, o agregua la solucio de continuitat am fiel ayssi cum a tu e fayt saber.	But the manner of suture is that you add the solution of continuity or with needles as we have recounted in the suture of the abdomen, or add the solution of continuity with faithful thread as to your own and make it known.
Capitol .xxvii.	Chapter XXVII.
De extraccio de aquela causas que veno en las doas labias en las partidas dedintz.	On the Extraction of those Causes that come in the Two Lips in the Parts Behind.
Motas veguadas endeve a motz homes en las partidas dedintz de las suas labias alcus apostemas durs semblantz a gras de errs, e alscunas de lors son mendres e alcunas son majors.	Many times it happens to many men in the parts behind their lips certain hard and grainless apostemas, some smaller and some larger.
Donc cove que tu convertas las labias e fendas quascuna de aquelas duricias de tota part, e aprop la abscizio umpliscas le loc de sagi trissat entro que·l sanc sia restrengut, e aprop sia lavat am vi agre e sia curat le loc am aquo que es stipticitat, entro que sia sanat.	Therefore, it is necessary that you convert the lips and fissures into each of those hardnesses from all parts, and then fill the location with sagittated lint until the blood is restricted, and then be washed with hot water and be cured the location with what exists as a styptic, until it is healed.
Capitol .xxviii.	Chapter XXVIII.
De inscizio de la carn ajustada en las gengivas.	On the Incision of Adjusted Meat in the Gums.
Granre de veguadas nays sobre la gengiva carn ajustada la qual les antics apelero albulus, adonc cove que tu suspendas aquela am onci o que tenguas aquela am las forfecs e inscidas aquela deves la sua razit, e leyssas la sania correr o le sanc.	Great many times there is a growth of flesh above the gum adjusted meat which the ancients called albulus, therefore it is necessary that you suspend that with one or two threads, or that you hold that with forceps and incise that as it should be, and let the blood run or flow.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc sagi trissat o autra polveras stipticas o excicativas.	And then pause on the location with sagittated lint or other powders that are styptic or exciting.
E si aquela carn retorna, lahoras inscideys aquela segundariament, e cauterisa aquela, quar aprop le cauteri no retornara.	And if that flesh returns, then incise it secondarily, and cauterize it, because the cautery will not return.
Capitol .xxix.	Chapter XXIX.
De razo de dentz am ferr.	On the Reason of Teeth with Iron.
Quan en la superficia de las dentz de las partidas dedintz e de las de foro e entre las gingivas so ajustadas escorsas aspras, legas, e alcunas veguadas son de nigradas e son faytas citrinas o vertz entro que a la gingiva ve per aquo corrupcio e son faytas las dentz legas.	When in the surface of the teeth of the parts behind and those of the front and between the gums are adjusted rough, sharp, and some blackened, and some turned yellow or green until the gum is corrupted and the teeth become loose.
E donc cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas e pausar le cap de lu en le tieu se, e ratz las dents en las quals apareysso aquelas escorsas e causas semblantz arena entro que de lor no romangua deguna causa, e aquo fay de la negror e de la citrinitat e de las autras entro que sian mondificadas.	And then it is necessary that you make the patient sit between your hands and pause the top of him in your seat, and ratify the teeth in which those roughs and causes appear like sand until there remains no cause, and thus make the blackness and yellowness and other things disappear.
Donc si es ostat aquo que es en aquelas del comensament de la razio, bo es; e sino, lahoras tu itera la razio sobre aquelas al autra dia e al segon e al tertz entro que vengua al derier stament en aquo que tu vols.	Therefore, if this is the beginning of the reason, good it is; and otherwise, then you must iterate the reason over those on another day and on the second and third until it comes to the final statement in what you wish.
E sapias que las dentz han necessitat de motz rezoris de diversas formas e de motas figuras segon que es preparat a la tua operacio.	And know that teeth have required many remedies of diverse forms and figures according to how it is prepared for your operation.
E per so quar le razori am le qual la dent es raza de la partida dedintz es autre del razori am le qual es ras entre las dentz segon autras formas, e aquestas formas de razoris sian deves tu preparadas las quals veyras tantost:	And therefore the razors with which the tooth is razed from the part behind are another of the razors with which it is rasped between the teeth according to other forms, and these forms of razors should be prepared by you as you will see soon.
Capitol .xxx.	Chapter XXX.
D’eradicacio de dentz.	On the Eradication of Teeth.
Cove que tu cures la dent de la sua dolor am tot engen e tardes en tota eradicacio de lu, quar no es denguna causa que suplisqua la veguada de lu quan es eradicada, quar es sustancia sublima entro que es excusacio en la eradicacio de lu.	Necessary that you cure the tooth of its pain with all diligence and toil in its entire eradication from it, for there is no cause that can surpass its growth when it is eradicated, for it is a sublime substance into which it excites itself in its eradication from it.
Mays cove quan le malaute es forsat aquela dent eradicar, que fermament deves tu sia certificat quala es la dent dolent, quar motas veguadas la dolor descep le malaute e cuga que sia en dent sana, e tu eradicas aquela e aprop la dolor no cessa entro que la dent malauta e dolent sia eradicada, quar nos ja havem vist aquo per operacio dels barbies.	But it is necessary when the patient is forced to eradicate that tooth, that you firmly certify what is the aching tooth, for many times the pain deceives the patient and assumes it is in a healthy tooth, and you eradicate that one and then pause until the sick and aching tooth is eradicated, for we have already seen this through the operation of barbers.
Donc cum deves tu es sertificat qual es la dent dolent, e que o sabes be, lahoras cove que tu scarifiques en le circuit de la dent am spatum en le qual sia alcuna vertut, entro que sia dissolvut de la dent de la gingiva de tota partida, e aprop mau aquel am les tieus ditz, o am forfexs subtils al comensament petit a petit entro que aquela concucesquas.	Therefore, as you must be certified which is the aching tooth, and knowing well, it is necessary that you scarify in the circuit of the tooth with a spatula in which there is some virtue, until it is dissolved from the tooth to the gum of all parts, and then pause and let it settle with your own hands or with subtle forceps little by little until it conceives.
E aprop alogua en lu fortz tenalhas grans per bona loquacio o estuptura fort, e pausa le cap del malaute entre les tieus denolhs que be le tengues que no·s maugua, e aprop tratz la dent segon rectitut en manieyra que no trenques aquela, ni al malaute major dolor no dones.	And then pause in the strong hold with great force for good speaking or sudden power, and pause the head of the patient between your fingers that you will hold well so as not to harm, and then pull out the tooth according to rectitude in manner that you do not break it, nor give more major pain to the patient.
E donc si no es foro-getat, lahoras pren un de aquels instrumentz, e met aquel dejos lu de tota part am facilitat e esforsa la remocio de lu ayssi que es feyt al comensament.	And then if not forgotten, take one of those instruments, and put that at the disposal of all parts with facility and effort the removal of it thus as was done at the beginning.
Mays si la dent es trauquada o corrosa, lahoras cove que tu comples de drap aquel trauc e estrenguas aquel am la extremitat de ray subtil per so que no sia trinquada en la hora de la tua constriccio sobre aquela am tenalas.	But if the tooth is cracked or corroded, then it is necessary that you cover with cloth that crack and strengthen it with a thin thread at the extremity of a subtle ray so that it is not broken in the hour of your constriction upon it as you take hold.
E cove que tu obres exquesitament am scarificacio en le circuit de tota part de la gingiva e guarda mot la tua fortaleza que no trenques aquela e romangua partida de lu, e retorne sobre le malaute per la malicia que sia majo que la primieyra dolor de lu.	And it is necessary that you work with exquisite care through scarification in the circuit of all parts of the gum and guard well your strength so as not to break it and remain divided from it, and return upon the patient for the malice that will be greater than the first pain.
E guarda te que no fassas aquo que fan alscus ignorantz barbiers en lor fistinacio e audacia sobre la eradicacio de lor, ses que no aministran aquo que nos havem recomtat; quar motas veguadas fan venir sobre les homes malautias grans las quals son pus dificils que sian trinquadas, e las razitz de lor remaugudas totas, o alcunas de aquelas, o que extrayguas aquela am alcus osses de la mandigula ayssi cum motas veguadas havem testificat.	And beware that you do not do as some ignorant barbers do in their fistulation and audacity towards the eradication of their own, without administering what we have recounted; for many times they bring upon men great illnesses which are more difficult to be broken, and all or part of those teeth become disordered, or that tooth is extracted with some bones of the mandible as many times have testified.
E aprop la eradicacio de lu sia lavada la boca am vi caut o vi agre am sal.	And then the eradication of it should be washed away with hot water or warm water and salt.
E si endeve fluxs de sanc per aysso, ayssi cum motas veguadas endeve, lahoras trissa alcuna quantitat de zegi e aspergeys sobre la plagua, e si no confereys aquel zegi, cauteriza.	And if it is necessary to flow with blood in this way, just like many times it has been necessary, then take some quantity of egg white and sprinkle it over the wound, and if that egg white does not concur, then cauterize.
La forma de las forceps e tenalas subtils am las quals es mauguda la dent al comensament sia de longua extramitat, de breu manubre e gros, per so que no sian doblatz quan am aquels deves obrar.	The form of the forceps and subtle tongs with which the tooth is manipulated at the beginning should be of long extramital, short handle, and thick, so that they are not doubled when you must work with them.
E sian ayssi cum vezes de gros manubre entro que quan estrenhas am aquelas no sian dobladas, sian breus extramitatz.	And should be thus as times of thick handle, so that when you strain with them they are not doubled, but short extremities.
E sian faytas de ferr de India descentment faytas de dreytas extramitatz, e en las extramitatz de aquelas sian dentz de las quals las unas intron en las autras e estrenhan per constriccio descent fort, e alscunas veguadas las extramitatz de aquelas sian la forma del bec d’un auzel le qual ha nom ciconia, so es guanta, e son de fort constriccio.	And should be made of Indian iron, with curved extremities, and in the extremities of those, should be teeth which some enter into others and strain through constriction descending strongly, and sometimes those extremities are in the shape of a bird's beak, which is called ciconia, so it is guarded, and they have strong constriction.
Capitol .xxxi.	Chapter XXXI.
De erradicacio de dentz e d‘estraccio dels osses de las mandibulas trincadas.	On the Eradication of Teeth and Extraction of Bones from Mandibles Broken.
Quan deves la eradicacio de dent le qual es trinquat roman alcuna causa, lahoras cove que tu pauses sobre le loc coto am boder per un jorn o per dos entro que·l loc sia mollificat; e aprop entromet algesti o tenalhas las extramitatz de las quals so asembladas al bec de un auzel apelat ciconia o guanta, la forma de las forceps:	When you must eradicate a tooth that is broken for some reason, it is necessary that you pause over the location with a border for one day or two until the location is softened; and then insert gently or tongs the extremities of which are assembled to the beak of a bird called ciconia or guard, the shape of the forceps:
Las extramitatz de lor sian faytas dedintz ayssi cum lima o alfagi.	The extremities of theirs are made behind like lime or alfalfa.
E si no obediys a tu a eyssiment am aquestas forceps o tenalas, lahoras cove que tu caves sobre la razit e descrobas tota la carn e entrometas le instrument le qual ha nom atali, so es palanca petita del qual la forma es aquesta:	And if you do not obey your will with these forceps or tongs, then it is necessary that you hollow out the root and disarticulate all the flesh and insert the instrument which has no name, that is a small lever of which the shape is this:
E sia de breu extremitat grossa un petit, e no sia enbegut per so que no sia trinquat.	And it should be of short extremity, thick and small, and not be worn out for that reason that it will not break.
Donc si per aquo la razit es foro-getada, bo es; e sino, ajuda te am aquestz autres instrument dels quals aquestas son las formas: la forma del primier instrument es de triangulada extramitat en la qual sia alcuna grossesa:	Therefore, if the root is forgotten, good it is; and otherwise, help yourself with these other instruments of which these are the forms: the form of the first instrument is triangular extremity in which there should be some thickness:
La forma del segon instrument es que sia de triangulada e de pus subtil extremitat.	The form of the second instrument is that it should be triangular and with a more subtle extremity.
E ja so ajudatz am aquest instrument havent dos ramps del qual aquesta es la forma aprop la seguent:	And already you help yourself with this instrument having two ramps of which this is the form, approximately following:
e am autres instrumentz les quals precidero en rasura de dentz; quar juvament es fayt am aquest instrument le qual es asemblat a onci gran, e aquesta es la forma:	and with other instruments which precede in the rasping of teeth; for soon it is made with this instrument which is assembled to great once, and this is the form:
de la triangulada extremitat torta o curta, la qual sia alcuna grossesa, e no sia enbegut per so que no sia trinquat.	of the triangular extremity bent or short, which should have some thickness, and not be worn out for that reason that it will not break.
E otra sapias que·ls instrumentz de las dentz motz so e semblantment les autres instruments.	And therefore you know that the instruments of teeth are many and similar to each other, as well as the other instruments.
Mays le artifexs savi e subtil en l’art, atroba per si mateys segon aquo que a lu significa la operacio e las malautias diversas; quar son de las malautias a las quals les antics no diysero ni pausero propri instrument, per las formas de diversas specias.	But the artisans skilled and subtle in their art, find for themselves by their own means, according to what it signifies the operation and various diseases; for they are of the diseases to which the ancients did not decree nor pause proper instruments, due to the forms of diverse species.
Mays si es trinquat l’os de la mandibula o dels autres osses de la boca, o si poyreys, lahoras sia pes curat sobre aquel en son loc am aquo que es a lu convenient dels instrumentz e de las forceps las quals havem dit en la extraccio de las razitz de las dentz, e ajuda te am gesti del qual aquesta es la forma:	But if the bone of the mandible or of the other bones of the mouth is broken, or if it pines away, then be sure to place great care upon that in its location where it is suitable for the instruments and forceps which we have said in the extraction of tooth roots, and help yourself with gestures of which this is the form:
E sia en lu alcuna grosseza petit a petit, e sia instringida o tenguda am la boca per que no evasesca o fuga entro que l’os de tot sia foro-getat; e aprop restaura le loc am medicinas convenientz ad aquo.	And it should be in a place with some thickness, little by little, and be strung or held in the mouth so that it does not escape or flee until the bone of all is forgotten; and then restore the location with medicines suitable to this.
Mays si en l’os es petita poyredura, lahoras ratz aquel de aquela poyredura e de la sua negror, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	But if there is a small putridity in the bone, then pull out that from that putridity and its blackness, and cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxii.	Chapter XXXII.
De la cura de las dentz eminentz sobre las autras.	On the Cure of Teeth Elevated above Others.
Quan las dentz so eminentz no segon lor cors natural per aquelas la forma es laga, e majorment quan endeve a las femnas, e majorment a las piuselas venerablas; donc cove que tu consideras: si dent es nada aprop autra dent, e no es possibla sarradura ni linament de lu, lahoras radica aquela; mays que no sia annexa am autra dent, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am aquest instrument del qual aquesta es la forma; e es semblant a morr de porc, e sia feyt de ferr de India de extramitat mot aguda.	When teeth are elevated above their natural form and majorly so in women and especially venerable maidens; therefore it is necessary that you consider: if a tooth is not very close to another tooth, and there is no possibility of suture or binding of it, then pull out that one; but if it is annexed to another tooth, then you must incise that one with this instrument whose form is like this; it resembles a pig's tooth, and is made of Indian iron with an extremely sharp extremity.
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscideyses aquela en trops dias per la duricia de la dent, e que no sia comauguda autra de las dentz.	And then your incision should be with which you will incise that one in many days for the hardness of the tooth, and so that it is not confounded with other teeth.
E si es dent eminent expausat a limadura, lahoras lima aquel am lima de ferr de India del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if an elevated tooth is exposed to erosion, then remove that one with a file of Indian iron whose form is like this:
E sia tot de ferr de India e·l margua eysament; e sia de motz menutz puntz ayssi cum lima am la qual son faytas agulhas, am la qual la dent sia limada pauc a pauc en motz dias am fecilitat, per so que no sia autra dent comauguda e caga.	And it should be all of Indian iron and the edge slightly curved; and it should have many small points like a file with which are made needles, with which the tooth is filed gradually over several days with ease, so that there is no other tooth confounded and decayed.
E aprop lineys aquela en la fi, e ratz aquela am alscus razoris.	And then line it up in the end, and pull out that one with some rasors.
E si es dent del qual una partida es trinquada e lideys la lengua, lahoras cove que tu limescas aquel entro que l’aspretat de aquela fraccio sia ostada e engualhada, e sia aplenada per so que la lengua no ledesca ni la paraula no corrumpa.	And if a tooth is broken and the tongue lies against it, then it is necessary that you file it down until the sharpness of that fragment is removed and rounded off, and be filled in such a way that the tongue does not lie against it nor corrupt the word.
Capitol .xxxiii.	Chapter XXXIII.
De restauracio de dentz maugudas am fiel de aur o de argent.	On the Restoration of Damaged Teeth with Gold or Silver Wire.
Quan accideys a las dentz devant concussio e remossio per percussio o per cazament, e le malaute no pot strenher sobre aquo que manga, e tu has curat aquel am medicinas stipticas, e no ha valgut la tua curacio, lahoras per so que no cagan es engen en aquelas que sian strengudas am fiel de aur e no de argent, quar argent se fa vert e aprop se poyreys aprop alscus dias, mays aur nul temps no es mudat.	When accidents occur to teeth before concussion and removal by percussion or falling, and the patient cannot strengthen over that which is damaged, and you have treated that with stiptic medicines, but your treatment has not been effective, then for this reason, so that they do not decay, it is necessary to reinforce those with gold wire and not silver, because silver turns green and soon perishes within a few days, whereas gold never changes.
E sia le fiel en tal subtilitat e grocesa segon la quantitat que puesca entrar entre las dentz; e la forma de la reccio es que prenguas le fiel e pren lo doble de lu entre doas dentz sanas, e aprop que cresques am doas tortuositatz del fiel entre doas maugudas, o si’ una o motas, entro que pervengua la tela a la dent sana del autra partida.	And the wire should be in such subtlety and thickness according to the quantity that can fit between the teeth; and the form of the recipe is that you take the wire and double it within two healthy teeth, and then you increase by two bends of the wire between two damaged ones, or one or many, until the thread reaches the healthy tooth on the other side.
E aprop itera le teyssiment entro a la partida de la qual comenciest, e strenh la tua ma am facilitat e savieza entro que no sia mauguda.	And then repeat the thread within the part from which you began, and strengthen your work with ease and wisdom until it is not damaged.
E sia la tua striccio am la qual strenhas le fiel deves las razitz de las dentz que no evasesca.	And then tighten the thread with which you will bind the wire to the roots of the teeth that do not decay.
E aprop inscindeys las extramitatz del fiel superfluens am las forceps o tosoyras, e agregua aquelas en quascun loc am gesti, e converteys aquelas e las occulta entre la dent sana e la dent mauguda, per so que no fassa lesio a la lengua.	And then incise the excessive extremities of the wire with forceps or tongs, and add those in each place with gestures, and convert them and hide them between the healthy tooth and the damaged one, so that they do not cause injury to the tongue.
E aprop leyssa aquela ayssi streyta cum roman.	And then let go of it just as straight as possible.
Mays si es desliada o rumpuda, strenh aquela o aquelas am autra fiel en tal manieyra en tot son temps.	But if it is broken or separated, strengthen that one or those with another wire in such a way for all its time.
E aquesta es la forma de las dentz e la figura de la rectacio de doas dentz sanas e de doas maugudas, ayssi cum vezes aquestas liadas:	And this is the form of teeth and the figure of the restoration of two healthy teeth and two damaged ones, just like these linked together:
E quan se fa que retorno una dent o doas aprop le cazement de quascuna en lors locs, e sian recrescutz ayssi cum havem recomtat, e que remauguan.	And when one tooth or two returns to its place, and each remains in its own location, and are re-grown just as we have recounted, and remain.
E no fa aquo sino bo artifexs e savi.	And only skilled artisans and wise men can do this.
E alcunas veguadas es aptat alcuna causa dels osses de vaca, e es fayt de lor ayssi cum forma de dent, e es pausada en loc en le qual defayl la dent, e es strengit ayssi cum havem dit, e reman e serveys am aquel per lonc temps.	And sometimes it is suitable for some reason of cow bones, and is made from them in the shape of a tooth, and is placed in a location where the tooth has fallen out, and is strengthened just as we have said, and remains and serves that one for a long time.
Capitol .xxxiv.	Chapter XXXIV.
De inscizio del liament le qual ve en la lengua e prohibeys loquela.	On the Incision of the Ligament which is in the Tongue and Prohibits Speech.
Aquest liguament le qual ve dejos la lengua alcunas veguadas o es natural am le qual hom nays, o accidental e accideys per plagua la qual ja es consolidada.	This ligament which is found behind the tongue sometimes or is natural to it, or accidental and occurs through a wound that has already consolidated.
E la operacio en lu es que huobres la boca del malaute, le sieu cap existent en le tieu se; e eleva la sieua lengua, e aprop inscideys aquel liament nervos segon la latitut entro que sia solvuda la lengua de la sua recencio.	And the operation in this case is that you open the mouth of the patient, and the existing head of his tongue comes into view; and then elevate his tongue, and carefully incise that ligament according to its latitude, until the tongue is freed from its retraction.
Mays si en aquela es alcuna duricia o denodacio, e aquo es stat per consolidacio de plagua, lahoras tu gieta unci e scindeys aquel per la latitut entro que aias inscindit le liament e sia dissolvuda la nodacio.	But if in that case there is some hardness or stiffness, and this is due to the consolidation of the wound, then you should take care not to incise too deeply, but rather cut along the latitude until you have severed the ligament and dissolved the knot.
E guarda te que no sia fayta fissura en le preon de la carn e que scindas aqui arceria e vengua flux de sanc.	And beware that there is not a gaping wound in the flesh before the ligament, and that you do not cut too deeply and cause blood to flow.
E aprop sia lavat le vestigi de la inscisio am ayguaros o am vi agre o am aygua frega; e aprop pausa dejos la lengua licini; so es meca la qual tengua le malaute dejos la lengua en quascuna nuoyt per so que no sia consolidat autra veguada.	And then be sure to wash away the remains of the incision with warm water or vinegar, or with a cloth soaked in water; and then pause beside the tongue and let it lie down; thus is the method which will keep the patient's tongue from becoming stiff again every night so that another knot does not form.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, pausa sobre le loc vetriol trissat; mays si le sanc ventz, lahoras cauteriza le loc am cauteri lantiginos le qual conveneys ad aquo.	But if there is a flow of blood, pause over the location with a poultice; but if the bleeding ceases, then let the wound be cauterized with a caustic lanolin which is suitable for this purpose.
E aprop aquel cura am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	And then apply that cure to other causes until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	Chapter XXXV.
De extraccio de ranula dejos la lengua.	On the Extraction of a Ranula behind the Tongue.
Alcunas veguadas accideys dejos la lengua apostema asemblant a nomla petita prohibent la lengua de la sua operacio natural; e fort leu es magnificada entro que huempla la boca.	Sometimes, behind the tongue, an abscess forms similar to a small boil that prohibits the tongue from its natural operation; and very soon it is magnified until it fills the mouth.
E la operacio en lu es que huebras la boca del malaute sesent devant le solel e considera le apostema.	And the operation in this case is that you open the patient's mouth, seated before the sun, and consider the abscess.
E si tu le vezes de fusca color o de negra, dur, al qual le malaute no atroba sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel quar es cranc.	And if you see it of a dull red or black color, hard and dry, which the patient does not feel any sensation, then do not touch it because it is cancerous.
E si es declinat a blancor, en le qual es humiditat, lahoras tu met le onci en lu, e inscideys aquel am spatum subtil, e inscindeys le de tota partida; e si sanc te ventz en la hora de la tua operacio, lahoras tu pausa desus zegi trissat, so es vetriol, entro que sia restreyt le sanc.	And if it is turning white and has moisture, then you should insert a probe into it, and incise that part with a subtle spatula, and cut off the entire portion; and if blood flows in the hour of your operation, then you should pause above a poultice, so it is vetriol, until the bleeding ceases.
E aprop retorna a la obra tua entro que lo haias trayt am compliment de lu, entro que sia lavat am vi agre e sal; e cura aquel am l’autra curacio ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And then return to your work until you have completed it in accordance with the location, so that it is washed with warm water and salt; and cure that part with the other cure, just as it was done before, until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxvi.	Chapter XXXVI.
De extraccio de apostema de doas aurelhas e de aquel que es nada en le golayro e de las autras apostemas.	On the Extraction of an Abscess from Both Ears and that which is nothing in the Gullet and other Abscesses.
Quan endeveno en le golayro godat, so son glandulas las quals son asembladas algodat, las quals accideysso deforas e son nompnadas doas aurelhas, las quals quan tu las curas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no es sanat, lahoras tu considera si le apostema es dur, de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr.	When it occurs in the Gullet, so are the glands which are assembled together, which bulge out and are named two Ears, which when you cure them with what we have said in the division and they do not heal, then you should consider if the abscess is hard, of dull red color, and with little sensation, then do not touch it with iron.
E si es de roga color e la razic es grossa, lahoras no toques aquela am ferr per le flux del sanc; abantz layssa aquel entro sia madurat, e lahoras o tu trauqueras aquel, o sira romput per si.	And if it is of a red color and the root is large, then do not touch it with iron due to the flow of blood; rather leave it until it has matured, and either you will remove it or it will break apart on its own.
E si es de blanqua color, radon, e la razit de lu es subtil, lahoras aquel es que cove esser inscidit.	And if it is of a white color, rough, and the root of it is subtle, then that one needs to be incised.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras, denant la tua operacio, si ja ha repausat le apostema de lu caut am repaus complit o si es deminuit am alcuna deminucio; e lahoras fay sezer le malaute denant le soleyl, e·l cap de lu sia en le tieu se, e huebre la boca de lu, e le servidor prenent entre las suas mas prema la lengua de lu dejos am instrument mot noble del qual aquesta es la forma:	And the operation in this case is that you consider, before your operation, if the abscess has already subsided and repaid its debt or if it has diminished by some diminution; and then make the patient sit before the sun, and his head should be in its proper place, and open the mouth of him, and the servant takes hold between his own most prominent teeth the tongue of him behind with an instrument very noble, whose form is this:
E sia fayt de argent o de aram, e sia subtil cum cotel.	And it should be made of silver or iron, and it should be subtle like a knife.
Donc cum tu premes am aquel la lengua e es mostrat a tu la apostema, e catz sobre aquel le tieu vezement, lahoras pren onci e fica aquel en l’amenla, e tira aquel a las partidas defora tant quant podes.	Then, as you take hold of that tongue and it is shown to you the abscess, and you look at it with the skin around it, then take a probe and put that in the mouth, and pull that out as far as you can.
Otra aquo que tiras alcuna causa de las tunicas, e aprop incideys aquela am instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	Or other causes of the tunics, and then cut it with an instrument whose form is this:
e es asemblat a forceps, empero las extramitatz de lu son corvadas, ayssi que l’orrifici de quascuna de aquelas es en le endreyt del autra, mot agudas, le qual sia de ferr indi enbegut.	and is assembled to forceps, however the extremities of it are curved, so that the opening of each of those is in the end of the other, very sharp, made of Indian iron well ingrained.
