Mays si aquest instrument no es a tu present, lahoras inscideys aquel am spatum del qual aquesta es la forma de lu: E sia agut de la una part, no agut del autra part.	But if this instrument is not at your disposal, then incise it with a spatula whose form is this: And it should be sharp on one side and not sharp on the other side.
E pus que has inscidit una mella, inscideys l’autra segon aquesta meteyssa manieyra de inscizio, e aprop la inscizio le malaute guarguarise de aygua frega	And once you have incised one notch, incise the other following this same manner of incision, and then apply the incision to the patient's mouth with a cloth soaked in water.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, guarguarise aygua de decoccio de scorsa de milgrana o de fuelha de mirtra e semblantz ad aquel de las causas stiptiquas entro que·l flux del sanc sia restreyt, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	But if bleeding occurs, apply water from the decoction of scorsa of milgrana or of mirtra leaves and similar to that of caustic substances until the bleeding is stopped, and then cure it until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas naysso en le guolayro autras apostemas otra aquelas doas aurelhas, e inscideys aquelas segon que yeu e dit en la inscizio de doas mellas engualment.	And sometimes there are other abscesses in the gullet besides those two ears, and you should incise them according to what I have said about incising two notches together.
E yeu ja fu medicat una femna de apostema le qual era nat en le golayro de lu, le qual apostema tendia a color fusca, de pauc sentiment, le qual ja havia claus le golayro de lu, e la femna respirava am meat streyt, e ja havia prohibit a lu comestio e beure de aygua, e ja era pervenguda a la mort si mays agues stat per un dia o per dos.	And you had already treated a woman who had an abscess in her throat which was turning yellowish, with little sensation, and which had already closed up her throat, so that she was breathing very tight, and had been prohibited from eating and drinking water for a day or two, and it seemed to be on the verge of death if you hadn't acted within a day or two.
E l’apostema ja tant havia pugat que havia mezes dos ramps entro que eyssiro per dos traucs.	And the abscess had grown so large that it had taken two ribs between which it had pierced through two holes.
Donc yeu me cuytegui fisturalment e fiquegui en un de lor onci, e tiregui aquel, e atirada es de lu gran porcio, e aprop yeu incidigui aquela de on comprendegui del autre trau, e aprop yeu obrigui la boca de lu, e compremegui la sua lengua, e aprop yeu fiquegui le onci en aquela apostema.	So you carefully inserted your finger and stayed in one of them, and pulled it out, and pulled out a large portion of it, and then you incised the other notch of the other hole, and then you opened the patient's mouth, and compressed their tongue, and then you placed the probe in that abscess.
E aprop yeu abscizi gran partida de lu, e no corria de lu sino un pauc de sanc.	And then you cut out a large part of it, and there was only a little blood flowing from it.
Donc absolut es le guolayro de aquela femna, e comensec tantost beure aygua, e aprop presec vianda, donc yeu no cessegui inscidir de aquela apostema motas vetz per lonc temps, e succesia apostema en loc de aquel, le qual inscizia entro que es prolonguat aquel.	And thus the throat of that woman was completely cleared, and she began to drink water and eat food, and then you did not cease to incise that abscess many times over a long period, and subsequent abscesses occurred in its place, which you incised until it was prolonged.
Donc yeu engen agui e cauterizegui le guolayro de lu, donc astec de addicio; e aprop yeu perambulegui e no saubi que fec Dieus de aquela aprop mi.	And thus you went away and cauterized the throat of her, and afterwards there was no addition; and then you walked around and did not know what God had done to that patient through you.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Chapter XXXVII.
De inscizio de huvela quan es apostemada.	On the Incision of a Hernia when it is Abscessed.
Quan catarr deysen a la huvula, e es apostemada e es longa, lahoras ela es nompnada perpendicular; e si es en la partida dejos grossa e redonda, e lahoras ela es apelada buba.	When the hernia descends to the scrotum and is abscessed and is long, then it is called perpendicular; and if it is in the left side large and rounded, then it is called a bubo.
Mays quan es curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio, e no comfereys la tua curacio, e eyssament ja vezes que apostema caut ja es ostat de lu e es subtil, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquela que es agreguadas redonda; e si es ad aquela longitut, e es sanguina, de fusca color o de negre, e no es a lu centiment, lahoras cove que tu temtes la inscizio de lu, quar en aquela es temor sobre le malaute.	But when it is cured with what we have said in the division, and your cure does not concur, and it only happens that the abscess is left behind and is subtle, then you must incise that which is added roundly; and if it is to that length, and is bleeding, of a dull red or black color, and there is no sensation to him, then you must beware the incision of him, for in that case there is fear over the patient.
E quan tu vezes aquela segon la manieyra que yeu he dita de la sua blancor e longuesa, que tu fassas sezer le malaute e premas la lengua de lu am instrument del qual procesic la sua forma e aprop fica le onci en la nuva, e tira aquela en jos e inscideys aquela am un de dos instrumentz les quals e ditz en la inscizio de dos mellas.	And when you incise it according to the manner that I have said of its whiteness and length, then you should make the patient sit and take hold of his tongue with an instrument whose form is this: And place the probe in the new abscess, and pull it down and incise it with one of two instruments which are mentioned in the incision of two notches.
E cove que no inscidas aquela sino aquo que es ajustat sobre le terme natural ses addicio, quar si tu inscides de lu mays, lediyras le sieu parlar.	And beware that you do not incise it except at the point where it is adjusted to its natural term without addition, for if you incise too much, you will deprive him of his speech.
E aprop la inscizio, usa de aquo le qual havem recomtat en la inscizio de dos mellas, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And then use what we have recommended in the incision of two notches, and cure it until it is healed.
Mays si era le malaute espaventat per la inscizio de lu, cove que use de engen en la cauterizacio de lu ses temor, e la manieyra del cauteri en lu no es sino am aygua aguda, e es que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop prem la lengua de lu am le instrument le qual havem dit, e aprop pren de l’aygua la qual havem dita en le capitol de cauterizacio, e comfeys am aquela caus viva, e pausa aquela no spessa ni subtil, e de aquela omple la concavitat de l’estrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	But if the patient is terrified by the incision, beware that you use it in the cauterization of him without fear, and the manner of cauterizing in him is not but with sharp water, and you pause the patient's head in its proper place, and then take hold of his tongue with the instrument which we have said, and take some of the water which we have mentioned in the chapter on cauterization, and apply it to that living cause, and pause it neither thick nor thin, and fill the concavity of the instrument whose form is this:
Sia la extramitat de lu conquavitat en la qual sia pausada la medicina ayssi cum la conquavitat de culher de ray, e pausa le strument am la medicina sobre la vula, e·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu latz per so que corro saliva o musellage de la boca de aquel per la intrinscequa medicina, per so que no deyssenda de aquela deguna causa sobre le golayro de lu e que ledesca aquel.	So the extremity of it is in a concavity in which the medicine is paused just like the concavity of a spoon, and pause the instrument with the medicine on the abscess, and the patient will lie on his side so that his saliva or mucus from his mouth flows into the internal cavity of the abscess through the intrinsic medicine, so that it does not descend to any cause over his throat and trouble him.
E aprop te la tua ma am la medicina, e exprem aquela sobre la uvula per l’espazi de miega hora entro que vegas aquela esser denegrada e sedada per la mordicacio de la medicina.	And then take your hand and the medicine, and express it on the uvula for a space of about half an hour until you see that it is blackened and calmed by the biting action of the medicine.
E si vols, prengues coto e envolopes aquel sobre la extremitat del ray, e submergeys le coto en la medicina, e entrometas le ray am le coto en una canula de sobre entro que·l coto adheresca en aquela canula, e fay aquo tantas vetz entro que consiegues aquo que vols de la cauterizacio de la uva, e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela se seccara e cayra aprop tres dias o quatre.	And if you wish, take a cloth and wrap it around the extremity of the ray, and submerge the cloth in the medicine, and insert the ray with the cloth into a cannula above until the cloth adheres to that cannula, and do this many times until you achieve what you want from the cauterization of the uvula, and then leave it alone for three or four days.
E si indigeysses que iteras la medicina, itera aquela, e aprop la cauterizacio abstergeys en le circuit de la uva am coto enbegut en boder, e mondifica am aquel aquo que es en le circuit de lu de la medicina, e sia lavat am aygua frega, e sia curat deforo am embrocacio, e dedintz am guarguarismes entro que sia sanat.	And if you need to repeat the medicine, repeat it, and then cauterize it in the circuit of the uvula with a cloth wrapped around it in a border, and clarify it with that which is in the circuit of the medicine, and be washed with warm water, and be treated externally with an embrocation, and internally with poultices until it is healed.
E aquesta especia de curacio es pus salva que inscizio e pus long de temor.	And this kind of cure is more saved than incision and more free from fear.
Alcunas veguadas es curada la uvuola am aquo que es pus subtil que cauteri e inscizio, quar es curat am subfumigacio en aquesta manieyra: recipe calament, ysop, origua, ruda, scicados arabic, camamilla, broyda e semblant ad aquels de las erbas, e ajusta totas aquelas causas, o alcunas de lor, en una ola, e sian submergidas am vi agre, e bulhan; e la ola sia be lutada am lut decentment, e sia en le mieg loc de la ola un trauc, sobre le qual sia pausat un instrument conquau de aram segon aquesta manieyra; sia fayt de argent o de aram.	Sometimes the uvula is cured with this method which is more subtle than cauterization and incision, because it is cured through sublimation in this manner: take camphor, hyssop, origanum, rue, Arabic gum, chamomile, and similar herbs to those of the plants, and mix all these causes, or some of them, into a pot, and be submerged in warm water, and boil; and then stir the pot decently, and there should be a hole in the middle of the pot, above which is placed an iron instrument shaped like this: made of silver or iron.
E sia entromesa la extremitat en la boca del malaute entro que la vapor poge a la uvula sobre la quanula, entro que la uvula sia mot ofuscada.	And the extremity should be inserted into the mouth of the patient until the vapor reaches the uvula above the tonsils, so that the uvula is very much obscured.
E aprop itera sobre aquela motas veguadas entro qu’es secca, e guarda te que no fassas aquesta curacio al comesament de l’aveniment de apostemas, quar trop ajustaria en le apostema, e no cove que tu fassas aquo, sino deves la declaracio de apostema de lu caut.	And then repeat this many times until it is dry, and take care not to do this cure at the beginning of the appearance of abscesses, because too much would be absorbed into the abscess, and you should not do this, but rather declare the abscess to be so.
Mays si no es a tu present aquest instrument, lahoras pren una cana e compon en la extramitat de lu un clos de huou, per so que la boca del malaute sia comborida, quar le closc del huou prohibeys la vapor comburir la boca.	But if this instrument is not at your disposal, then take a reed and make a plug of wood in the extremity of it, so that the mouth of the patient may be stopped up, because the wooden plug prevents the vapor from burning the mouth.
E aquesta curacio es bona am salut.	And this cure is good for health.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Chapter XXXVIII.
De extraccio d’espinas e de aquo que adhereys en le golayro e de las autras causas.	On the Extraction of Thorns and what adheres to the throat and other causes.
Motas veguadas adhereys en le guolayro o spina de peys o alcuna autra causa.	Many times something sticks in the throat or thorn of a fish or some other cause.
Adonc cove que tu extraguas aquo que de aquels es apparent, sobre le qual catz la vista, pus que tu premes la lengua am instrument denant solelh, per so que a tu sia declarat aquo que es en la guola.	Then it is necessary that you extract what appears to be from those things, above which the sight sees, since you take hold of the tongue with an instrument in the sun, so that it may be declared to you what is in the throat.
E aquo que no apar e es a tu occultat en le guolayro, cove que tu fassas vomir le malaute denant que la vianda sia degerida en l’estomac, quar fort leu la causa annexsa le golayro sira foro-getada per vomit; o que deglusia le malaute una pessa de nap o de razit de laytuga o un boci de pa sec; o prengua una pessa de sponga marina sequa leon, e lia aquela fortment am fiel, e aprop le malaute transglussia aquela, quar cum perve al loc en le qual so spinas e es extrahuda, lahoras so foro-getatz.	And what does not appear and is hidden from you in the throat, it is necessary that you make the patient vomit before food is digested in the stomach, because very often the cause attached to the throat will be forgotten through vomiting; or that the patient drinks a glass of vinegar or essence of lettuce or a bottle of dry bread; or takes a piece of sea sponge, and binds it strongly with a thread, and then the patient swallows it, so that when it reaches the place where thorns are and is extracted, then they will be forgotten.
E mays pren una anguila e be am fiel liada, e sia dedintz mesa e soptament sia extrayta; o pren un porr e soptament le metas e soptament l’en tratz.	And instead take an eel and bind it with a thread, and let it be placed inside and then extracted; or take a tube and insert it and then pull it out.
Mays si no so foro-getatz am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas, lahoras husa de un instrument de plom segon aquesta forma:	But if those causes which we have said are not forgotten, then take a leaden instrument shaped like this:
E sia pus gros que ray un petit, e en la extramitat de lu sia conquavitat la qual tu entrometas en la sua guola am facilitat.	And it should be more thick than a ray a little bit, and in the extremity of it there should be a concavity which you insert into the patient's throat with ease.
E el aga le sieu cap elevat en sus, e guarda te que·l tocament del sieu os de la gola, per so que endevengua a lu cos e am aquela que enpellesca le os o la spina, o que aquel le metge am la sua ma.	And it should raise its head upwards and take care that the touch of its bone in the throat, so that it may enter into the body and with that which will compress the bone or the thorn, or that it will put itself under its own hand.
Mays empero que·l malaute aquel entrometa es miels, per la sua sciencia del loc de la causa annexa e enpellisca en jos, e tira la sua ma am le instrument en sus, tot aquo segon la quantitat la qual es a lu preparada entro que sia foro-getada.	But meanwhile the patient should insert it with ease, by his knowledge of the place where the attached cause is and compresses below, and pulls out his hand with the instrument upwards, all according to the quantity prepared to be forgotten.
Capitol .xxxix.	Chapter XXXIX.
De extraccio de sancguisugua annexsa al golayro.	On the Extraction of Blood-Clots Attached to the Throat.
Quan es medicada sanguisugua am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la curacio am medicinas e no comfereys, considera lahoras en le guolayro del malaute al solelh, pus que tu aias compremuda la lengua de lu am instrument le qual a tu havem recomtat.	When it is medicated with blood-clots with what we have said in the division of the cure with medicines and does not concur, consider then that in the throat of the patient there is sunlight, because you have compressed his tongue with an instrument which we have recommended.
Donc si tu vezes la sancguisugua, extratz aquela am onci petit o am gesti subtils decentment.	Then if you find the blood-clot, extract it with a small probe or subtle gestures decently.
E si no es a tu possible estrayre am aquel, lahoras pren una canula concava e entromet aquela en lo guolayro del malaute, e aprop pausa en la concavitat de la canula un ferr ignit, e fay aquo tantas vetz (entro que la sancguisugua sia morta e se osta del guolayro) e abstengua se le malaute tot lo jorn de aygua.	And if it is not possible to extract it with that, then take a concave cannula and insert it into the throat of the patient, and then pause in the concavity of the cannula a hot iron, and do this many times (until the blood-clot is dead and falls out of the throat) and abstain from giving water to the patient all day.
E aprop prengua una veyria plena de aygua frega, e obra la boca de lu en aquela, e lava la boca am aquela; e no trasglucia de aquela alcuna causa e maugua l’aygua una hora aprop autra am la sua ma, quar la sancguisugua tantost cum sent l’aygua catz.	And then take a full vial of warm water, and open the mouth of the patient with it, and wash the mouth with it; and do not let any cause pass through it and spoil the water for an hour afterwards by his own hand, because the blood-clot soon as it feels the water takes fright.
Mays si no es foro-getada am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras subfumigua le malaute am cimetz o am assafetida per le instrument le qual havem recomtat en la sufumiguacio de uvula.	But if it is not forgotten as we have recommended, then sublimate the patient with cinnamon or asafoetida using the instrument which we have recommended in the sublimation of the uvula.
Fay aquo, so en quar cayra.	And do this, so that it will fall.
E es un’autra manieyra de operacio en sufumiguacio de aquela, es que tu prenguas una ola en la qual sian carbos ignitz e la ola sia cuberta am una cobertora en le mieg de la qual sia un trauc, e sia compausat en aquel trauc la extremitat del instrument; e aprop dega desus la subfumigacio; e pause le malaute la sua boca en la extremitat de la canula, e claugua la sua boca per que la subfumiguacio no sia foro-getada entro que sapias que la subfumigacio es pervenguda a la sancguisugua, quar la sancguisugua tantost cayra.	And there is another way of operation in the sublimation of it, that you take a pot in which are burning coals and the pot is covered with a cover in the middle of which is a hole, and the extremity of the instrument is placed in that hole; and then bring down the sublimation; and pause the patient's mouth at the end of the cannula, and close his mouth so that the sublimation is not forgotten until you know that the sublimation has reached the blood-clot, for the blood-clot will soon fall.
E si no catz, lahoras tu itera la subfumiguacio motas vetz, e abstengua le malaute de beure, e mange causas saladas e alhs, e no begua aygua, e ayssi necessari es que am aquest regiment sia fora-getada.	And if it doesn't work, then you repeat the sublimation many times, and abstain from giving water to the patient, and give him salty and bitter causes, and not fresh water, and thus it is necessary that with this regimen be forgotten.
E aquesta es la forma del instrument am le qual es trayta sancguisugua del guolayro quan es vista; e es semblant a forceps ayssi cum vezes, sino quar es en lu alcuna curvitat:	And this is the shape of the instrument with which blood-clots are extracted from the throat when seen; and it resembles forceps thus, except that there is some curvature.
le qual sia mesa al guolayro, e la extremitat de lu es semblant a bec de ciconia, que es guanta, en la qual es aspretat de lima, per so quar, quan comprem alcuna causa, aquela no leyssa.	The one that is placed in the throat, and the extremity of it resembles the beak of a heron, which is grasping, with a lime that is sharpened, so that when you compress some cause, it will not let go.
Capitol .xl.	Chapter XL.
En le qual es la suma del sermo en apercio de apostemas e en seccio de lor.	In which is the summary of the sermon in warning against abscesses and their treatment.
Les apostemas so motas specias, de motas manieyras, segon que ve rememoracio de lor, de quascuna en aquest libre.	Abscesses are many species, of many methods, according to the remembrance of their kind, each one described in this book.
E so diversas en perforacio e seccio de lor per doas manieyras, de las quals la una es per la specia de apostemas en si meteys; e per aquo que comprem de las humiditatz.	And thus diverse in perforation and section of them through two methods, one of which is by the species of abscesses themselves; and therefore, according to the humors.
E la segonda manieyra es prop les locs en les quals accideys del cos, quar le apostema accident en le cap es autra de la apostema accident en le cul; e le apostema en le loc carnos accident es autra del apostema accident en junctura; e a quascun de lor es son juguament per operacio.	And the second method is according to the places in which they occur in the body, for the abscess that occurs in the head is different from the abscess that occurs in the buttocks; and the abscess that occurs in a bony place is different from the abscess that occurs at a joint; and each one has its own judgment by operation.
E mays de apostemas so alcunas las quals cove que no sian perforadas sino aprop maturacio de la sania en aquels o compliment de lor.	And some abscesses are such that they should not be punctured, but rather allowed to mature with the pus in those places or completed as they are.
So autras apostemas les quals cove que sian traucatz quan son cruzes, e no son maturatz segon lor compliment, ayssi cum apostemas que son propdas a las juncturas, quar apostema quan ve prop junctura, lo esser de lu es prolonguat entro que·s poyreys aquo que es en le circuit de lu, e fort leu son corromputz les liamentz o les nervis de aquela junctura, per que es fayta causa de contraccio de aquel membre; o es apostema prop de membre principal, e si tu tardas la perforacio de lu entro sia madurat nosira al membre principal; o es prop le cul, donc perfora aque no-madurat; e no cove que·l perforas cru, de no-complida degestio, sino aquel que es prop del cul, per so que no poyresca le preon de lu e sia elonguat a las partidas dedintz del cul, e sia fayta fistula, o que sia fayt en le terme de lu que no sia sanat.	And other abscesses are such that they should be pierced when they are crossed, and not allowed to mature according to their completion, just like those abscesses that are proper to joints. When an abscess occurs near a joint, it prolongs itself within the circuit of the joint, and very often corrupts the ligaments or nerves of that joint, causing contraction of that member; or is an abscess near a main limb, and if you delay piercing it until it has matured too late for the main limb; or is an abscess in the buttocks, then pierce it unripe; and do not make it cross, but rather the one that is proper to the buttocks, so that the prepuce of it is not putrefied and elongated outside the buttocks, and a fistula is formed, or it becomes inflamed in its term and does not heal.
Mays cove que tu sapias la hora de la perforacio de la apostema, e aysso es quan es maturat.	But it is necessary that you know the hour of piercing the abscess, and thus it is when it is matured.
E sapias que es madurat quan es la cedacio de la dolor e la cessacio de la febre, e aprop la diminucio de la rogor e de la pulsacio, e la acuitat del cap del apostema, e les autres senhals.	And know that it is matured when there is the cessation of pain and fever, and a decrease in the swelling and pulse, and a sharpness at the top of the abscess, and other signs.
E quar cove que sapias la perforacio cazer en le loc pus dejos del apostema e de pus venient de curacio de la eminencia.	And where it is necessary to know that the piercing should be done in the place most distant from the abscess and coming from the cure of the elevation.
E perforacio tostemps sia per le lonc de la carn o del cors, si las apostemas son en las partidas de las mas o dels pes, e en loc dels lacertz, de las cordas dels nervis, de las arcerias; e, al derier, en totz locs enguals en les quals no es reflecio; quar en aquels que so reflectitz, usa de perforacio segon aquel membre.	And piercing should be done through the length of the flesh or body if the abscesses are in the parts of the arms or legs, and in places of the lacertae, tendons, nerves, and arteries; and, finally, in all places where there is no reflection; for in those that are reflected, use piercing according to that member.
Mays quan le apostema es en loc carnos, lahoras miels es que leysses la perforacio de lu entro que sia confermada la digestio de lu segon compliment, ayssi quo havem dit; quar si tu perforas aquel denant aquo, es prolonguat le cors del poyre de lu e de mota sordicia, e fort leu las labias de lu so enduradas e la profunditat de lu.	But when the abscess is in a bony place, then it is better that you delay piercing it until you are confirmed of its digestion according to completion, as we have said; for if you pierce it too early, it will prolong the body's putrefaction and many foul humors, and very often the lips of it will be hardened and the depth of it.
Mays alcus apostemas so perforatz segon la latitut de la carn o del cos deves la necessitat, o segon aquo del qual lo membre indigeys.	But some abscesses should be pierced according to the latitude of the flesh or body if it is necessary, or according to what the member requires.
E cove que administres petita perforacio , e·n les apostemas grans gran perforacio e ampla o motas seccios segon la diversitat de la grandesa dels apostemas.	And it is necessary that you administer a small piercing, and in large abscesses a great piercing and a wide or many sections according to the diversity of the size of the abscesses.
E autras so dels apostemas en les quals cove que la codena sia conquavada e sia encidida, quan es fayta ayssi quo pan e fayta es en terme que ja stigua, ayssi cum aquel que accideys en trops de dubelec e de bubos.	And others are the abscesses in which it is necessary that the cord is concaved and is incised, when it becomes thus as if pan and made are in term, as with those that occur in many parts of the duodenum and of boils.
E de aquels so que so insciditz am seccio havent tres angles; e de aquels es en le qual es inscidit ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirtra, ayssi cum las apostemas dels angonars.	And of those that are incised with a section having three angles; and of those it is in which it is incised as if it were a figure of a myrtle leaf, as with the abscesses of the groin.
E de lor so en les quals es administrada seccio redonda e seccio lunar, e semblantz ad aquels.	And of those that are incised with a round section and a lunar section, and resemble those.
Mays aquel al qual no es cap ayssi cum son apostemas leons superficials, cove que tu perforas aquel am perforacio superficial, o plana tant solament.	But that one to which there is no such abscess as those of the lions, superficially, it is necessary that you pierce it with a superficial or flat piercing only.
E cove quant le apostema es gros e ya ha colligit mota sania, que perfores aquel e no te coytes que extraguas tot le poyre en aquela hora; habantz extratz de aquel una partida, e aprop opila le apostema entro al autre dia, e aprop extratz una partida major, e aprop fa aquo motas veguadas segon graduacio entro que sia foro-getat.	And it is necessary that when the abscess is large and has already collected much pus, you pierce it and do not hesitate to extract all the pus at that moment; having extracted one part of it, and then plug the abscess until the next day, and then extract a larger part, and then repeat this many times according to gradation until it is forgotten.
E majorment si·l malaute es de freol vertut, o femna prens, o enfant petit, o viel en decrepitut, quar l’esperit animal motas vetz es resolvut am la egressio de la sania, e fort leu mor le malaute, e tu operte les.	And especially if the patient is of frail virtue, or a woman in childbed, or a small child, or an old person in decrepitude, for the animal spirit many times is resolved with the exit of the pus, and very often the patient dies, and you open them.
Don guarda aquest capitol am gran cautela, e aprop la tua perforacio en la qual perforas aquestz apostemas, cove que abstergescas las plagues e consideras donc si la plagua del apostema es pauca, o es una seccio plana, lahoras tu aministra las qualguas de li o de coto antic; e si le apostema es gran, e las fissuras de la perforacio son motas, lahoras cove que tu pauses meca en quascun trauc entro que pervenguan ensemps.	So guard this chapter with great caution, and accordingly administer your piercing in which you pierce these abscesses, so that you wash away the plagues and consider whether the plague of the abscess is small, or is a flat section; then you should administer those things of old or new patch; and if the abscess is large, and the fissures of the perforation are many, then it is necessary that you pause in each hole until they come together.
E si en le apostema es abscindit una partida de la codena o has concavada aquela en le circuit, lahoras cove que tu la complescas de coto viel o de fil fayt de drap de li, ayssi cum quan has traytz pans o razizos, ses humiditat; e strenh aquel entro al tertz dia; e aprop proceseys aquel e cura le am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if in the abscess is separated a part of the cord or has concavated that in the circuit, then it is necessary that you complete it with an old patch or with a thread made from linen cloth, as when you treat bread or raisins, without moisture; and strengthen that within three days; and accordingly process it and cure it with water as needed for the dressings until it is healed.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc en la hora de la operacio tua, lahoras tu aministra aygua frega e vi agre en les quals mules un drap de li, e pausa aquel sobre le loc del fluxs del sanc motas veguadas.	But if bleeding occurs during the hour of your operation, then you should administer warm water and vinegar to the mules where a linen cloth is wrapped, and pause that over the location of the blood flow many times.
Mays si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras cove que tu aministres regiment e curacio e polveras las quals he recomtadas en motz locs de aquest nostre libre e de divisio.	But if the bleeding persists, then it is necessary that you administer a remedy and cure, and powder those which I have recommended in many places of this our book and division.
Mays si es en temps de hivern, e·l loc de la apostema es loc de motz nervis, lahoras cove que tu enfundas pulvils en vi e oli caut, e pauses aquels sobre les locs.	But if it is in the time of winter, and the location of the abscess is a place of many nerves, then it is necessary that you apply poultices in wine and oil, and pause those over the locations.
E si es en estiu, e les locs son carnoses, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils enbeguts am aygua e oli o am vi e oli, e tot aquo sia freg entro que sia le ters dia, ayssi cum havem dit, e lahoras cove que tu deslies le apostema e abstergescas aquel e aministres en la curacio de lu aquo que a lu conveneys entro que sia sanat.	And if it is in the summer, and the locations are fleshy, then it is necessary that you apply poultices wrapped in water and oil or wine and oil, and let it be warm for three days, as we have said, and then remove the abscess and wash it with water as needed until it is healed.
E aysso es aquo que es necessari de la cognicio de la curacio de apostemas universalment, mays segon la via de distinccio ja he dit de tot apostema en qual manieyra es via de la cura de lu per capitols singularment.	And thus is what is necessary for the knowledge of the cure of abscesses universally, but according to the method of distinction that I have said of all abscesses in which way is the path of its cure by chapters individually.
Capitol .xli.	Chapter XLII.
De seccio de apostemas les quals veno en la codena del cap.	Of the section on abscesses that occur in the cord of the head.
En la codena del cap petitz apostemas, e so de specias de nodes les quals conteno tunicas que so a lor factz ; e las specias de lor so motas.	In the cord of the head, small abscesses, and some species of nodes that contain tunics which are their own facts; and the species of them are many.
E de lor son pingas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditat semblant a lima.	And among them are pustules, and those that contain humidity similar to lime.
E de aquelas so las quals conteno humiditat semblant a pols, et asemblantz a lor; e de aquelas so que son lapideas, durs.	And among them are those that contain humidity similar to powder, and resembling their own kind; and those that are lapideous, hard.
E en la seccio de totz, e en la extraccio de aquels no es temor, cum deves la exteccio de aquels no fa contrariat arceria.	And in the section of all and in the extraction of those there is no fear, as you should not cause tension in the arteries.
E la operacio en seccio de aquels es que tu esproes aquels am instrument la forma del qual ve aprop aysso, le qual es apelat entromes, entro que sapias que contengua.	And the operation in this section is that you apply them with an instrument of the form which resembles it, which is called "entromes", until you know what they contain.
Quar si aquo que conte es humiditat, lahoras scindeys aquel am seccio segon la longitut per seccio superficial segon aquesta forma:	Therefore, if what it contains is humidity, then you should divide it with a section according to its length, in a superficial section, following this form:
E comensa en la seccio de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G. Donc cum la humiditat es evacuada, lahoras tu excoria aquela pel que conte aquela humiditat, e no leysses de aquela alcuna causa de tot, quar tropas veguadas retorna, si roman de aquela alcuna causa.	And begins in the section of the line of .B. up to the line of .G. Then, as the humidity is evacuated, you should excoriate that skin which contains that humidity, and do not leave any cause from it, for many times it returns if some cause remains.
E aprop submergeys coto en enguent egipciach, si es present, e sino, en aygua e sal; e umpleys am aquel la plagua e layssa aquel entro ad autra dia, quar am aquo corrodeys tot so que es romas de aquela pellicula.	And accordingly submerge a patch in Egyptian ointment, if present, and if not, in water and salt; and fill it with that the wound and leave it until the next day, for by this means you corrode all that remains of that skin.
E aprop itera sobre aquel coto am enguent egipciach segondament e tersament si indigeyses de lu, entro que·t comfides que no y haia romas alcuna causa de aquela pellicula; lahoras cura la plagua am enguent entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly iterate over that patch with Egyptian ointment secondarily and tertiary times, if it is needed, until you are confident that there is no remaining cause of that skin; then cure the wound with ointment until it is healed.
E si apostema conte nodi gras, lahoras tu inscideys aquel segon aquesta forma:	And if the abscess contains fatty nodes, then you should incise it according to this form:
am seccio havent forma de crotz, e geta oncis entre doas labias de la seccio e scorsa aquel de tota partida, e esforsa la tua vertut en extraccio de la tunica la qual conte aquel.	with a section having the shape of a cross, and cut once between two lips of the section, and scrape off all that part, and exert your skill in extracting the tunic which contains that.
Mays si a tu arceria fa contrarieta, lahoras fay aquo que yeu t’e recontat primieyrament.	But if it causes tension in your arteries, then do as I have recounted to you first.
E semblantment fay en le apostema lapificat de seccio e de curacio segon que a tu havem dit; e seccio sobre apostema lapificat es pus leugiera, quar es de pauc sanc e de pauca humiditat.	And similarly do with the abscess that is hardened by section and cure according to what I have said; and section on a hardened abscess is easier, for it has little blood and little humidity.
E alcunas vetz so alcus de aquestz apostemas les quals so en le cap en alcus homes am los quals de tot no es humiditat; la qual causa es quar yeu inscindigui sobre un apostema en le cap de una femna vielha e atrobegui le apostema ayssi cum peyra sorda, aspra, blanqua, la qual no podia esser trinquada, e si a alcu fos am aquela percussit, plaguera aquel.	And some times there are such cases of these abscesses that are in the head of certain men, with whom there is no humidity; and this cause is because you incised over an abscess on the head of an old woman who was so deaf, harsh, white, and numb, that it could not be touched, and if someone had touched it with that percussion, it would have hurt him.
Mays en les autres apostemas accidentz en le cap otra aquest no es aquest capitol, ayssi cum les apostemas que veno als caps dels enfantz e deves las razitz de las aurelhas, mays la seccio de aquestz totz sia seccio superficial.	But in other abscesses that occur on the head, this is not the same chapter, such as those that come to the heads of children and are filled with wax, but the section of these all is superficial.
E pausa la perforacio de aquels de la partida pus bassa de lor per so que sia alleujat le cos de la sania a las partidas pus bassas.	And pause the piercing of those at the lower part of them, so that the body of the pus may be relieved in the lower parts.
E aprop cura aquelas am aquo que conveneys ad aquel de curacio.	And accordingly cure those with what is needed for their cure.
Capitol .xlii.	Chapter XLII.
De seccio de scrophulas las quals accideyso en le col.	Of the section on scrofulas that occur in the neck.
Motas veguadas endeveno aquestas apostemas en le colh e en las aysselhas e en les angonars; e alcunas veguadas accideyso en las autras partidas del cos.	Many times these abscesses occur in the neck and armpits and groin; and sometimes they occur in other parts of the body.
E so aquelas que accideysso en le colh, e so motas que so engendradas entre lor, e tota scrofula de aquelas es dintz la sua tunica propria, e ayssi cum en les nodis e apostema del cap, ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And those that occur in the neck, and many that are generated between them, and all scrofula of these is within its own tunic proper, and as with the nodes and abscesses of the head, as we have recounted.
E las specias de aquestas scrophulas son motas, quar de aquelas so alcunas lapideas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditatz, e de aquelas so malignas las quals no obeseysso a curacio.	And the species of these scrofulas are many, for some are lapideous, and some contain humidity, and some are malignant which do not submit to cure.
Donc en aquela la qual tu vezes de bona disposicio en le Tocament, de la qual la color de aquo que es manifest es propda a la color de la codena, e es mauguda a tota partida, e no es annexsa am le nervi del colh, ni am las venas, ni am la arceria, e no es preonda, cove que tu inscidiscas aquela am siccio superficial de la partida desus a la partida dejos del cos de la linha de .G. entro la linha de .B., e scorja aquela de tota partida, e exten dos labias de la codena am onci, o am motz oncis si has necessitat de aquels, ayssi cum havem dit en las apostemas del cap, e extratz aquela petit a petit.	Therefore, in that one which you find to have good disposition in the Touchment, of which the color is manifestly related to the color of the cord, and is bad at all parts, and is not annexed to the nerve of the neck, nor to the veins, nor to the arteries, and is not swollen, it is necessary that you incise it with a superficial section from above to below along the line of .G. up to the line of .B., and scrape off all that part, and extend two lips of the cord with one cut, or with many cuts if you need them, just as we have said in the abscesses of the head, and extract it little by little.
E es mays cautela que no sia inscidida la vena o nervi.	And it is even more caution that the vein or nerve should not be incised.
E sia le spatum no mot agut, que no ajuste a tu la tua ma am inscizio, o que enquiete le malaute, e que inscidas aquo que no es necessari inscidir; quar si inscideysses vena o arceria e prohibeys tu de la tua operacio, lahoras pausa en la plagua vetriol trissat o autras polveras las quals ostan fluxs de sanc, e estrenh la plagua, e layssa aquel entro que·s repausa la acuitat de la apostema e sia mollificada la plagua e comense esser poyrida.	And it is more caution that the spatula not be very sharp, so that it does not adjust to your hand and incise, or that you disturb the patient, and that you incise what is not necessary to incise; for if you incise a vein or artery and prohibit yourself from your operation, then pause in the wound until it becomes dry and rough, or other powders which stop the flow of blood, and strengthen the wound, and leave it until the acuteness of the abscess subsides and the wound becomes softened and begins to heal.
Quan le sanc es abscindit.	When the blood is separated.
Donc retorna a la tua operacio entro que l’aias complida.	Therefore, return to your operation until you have completed it.
E aprop inquireys am le tieu dit indic si es romas alcuna causa de las autras petitas scrophulas, donc inscideys aquelas e munda aquelas.	And accordingly, inquire about the sign your teacher has indicated if there remains any cause of other small scrofulas, then incise those and clean them.
E si es en la razit de la scrophula gran vena, cove lahoras que no inscidas aquela scrophula de la sua razitz.	And if it is in the root of a large scrofula, then it is necessary that you do not incise that scrofula from its roots.
Abantz cove que lies aquela am fiel doblat fort e que leysses aquela entro que caia per si ses nocument.	And accordingly, tie up that with a double thread and let it rest until it falls by itself without causing harm.
E aprop omple la plagua de coto vielh le qual tu has ja submirgit en enguent egipciac, e aprop cura aquel.	And accordingly, fill the wound with an old patch which you have already submerged in Egyptian ointment, and accordingly cure it.
E si inscides aquela scrophula tota, lahoras cove que tu ajustes las doas labias de la plagua e cuzas2 tantost pus que no y ha romasa deguna superfluitat.	And if you incise that scrofula entirely, then it is necessary that you adjust the two lips of the wound and sew them together as soon as possible so that there is no remaining superfluity.
Mays si tu vezes que haia romasa superfluitat per la grandeza de la scrofula, cove que tu entendas a inscidir la razit de aquela, e astrayra aquela e aministra sutura e aquo que es dit.	But if you find that there is remaining superfluity due to the greatness of the scrofula, then it is necessary that you understand how to incise its root, and extract it and administer suturing and what is said.
E aquela de las scrophulas que conteno humiditatz, perfora aquela am perforacio superficial aqui la on appar a tu le loc de maturacio de lu, e pausa perforacio de aquo que siec le pus bas del cos, ayssi cum havem dit.	And that of the scrofulas which contain humidity, pierce it with a superficial incision at the place where it appears to you as the location of maturity, and pause the incision so that it reaches the pus base of the body, just as we have said.
E aprop aministra perforacio, calguas am enguent e semblantz ad aquels, per so que corroda aquo que es romas de la corropcio.	And accordingly, administer the incision with ointment and similar substances to those, so that it corrodes what remains of the corruption.
E aprop quan tu vezes la plagua ja esser mundada, lahoras tu cura aquela am enguent de carn generatiu entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, when you see the wound already cleansed, then cure it with ointment of generating flesh until it is healed.
Capitol .xliii.	Chapter XLIII.
De seccio del pilhot del apostema accident dintz le guolayro.	Of the section on the pilling of the abscess which occurs in the groin.
Diyssero les antics aquesta seccio en le epilhot, e no vist alcu hom en nostra terra que aquela aia fayta.	They called this section in the old days "epilhot", and we have not seen anyone in our land who has done it.
E aquesta es la inscriptura del sermo de aquels.	And this is the inscription of the sermon of those.
Mays en les homes haventz esquinencia, cove que sia esquivada la extraccio del epilhot, cum per aquo no sia fayt juvament per so quar totas las venas e las majors del malaute so aqui.	But in men who have syphilis, it is necessary to avoid the extraction of the epilhot, because through this there would be no help, for all the veins and major vessels of the patient are here.
Mays en aquels que han apostemas cautz en la boca o guolayro o dos aurelhas, quan la malautia no es en la cana, cove husar de la seccio de epilhot a fugir la perdicio la qual es fayta per perfocacio.	But in those who have abscesses that are cauterized in the mouth or groin or both ears, when the disease is not in the canal, it is necessary to use the section of epilhot to avoid the destruction which is caused by perforation.
Donc cove quan volem aquo, que inscidam le epilhot dejos tres cercles dels cercles del epilhot, o quatre am petita seccio per la latitut en aquel que es entre dos cercles per quantitat, que la seccio sia en ciphac, no en la cartillage, e aquest loc es convenent a seccio, quar es privat de carn e les vayselhs de sanc de lu son luhen.	Therefore, when we want to do this, it is necessary that we incise the epilhot below three circles of the epilhot, or four with a small section in latitude between two circles for quantity, so that the section is in cartilage, not in bone, and this location is suitable for section, because it is privy of flesh and the vessels of blood from there are distant.
E si le metge es pauruc, cove lahoras que extenda la codena del golayro am onci, e aprop fenda la codena entro que pervengua a la canal, mays evite les vaysels de sanc si vetz de aquelas alcuna causa.	And if the doctor is cautious, it is necessary that he extends the cord of the groin with one cut, and accordingly cuts through the cord until it reaches the canal, but avoid the vessels of blood if you see any cause.
E aprop inscida li ciplach segon que havem recomtat; e es significat sobre la seccio de la canal per le flacma le qual es de aquela eyssit am aquo que es de lu disromput e per la abscizio de la votz.	And accordingly, incise the ciplach according to what we have recounted; and it is signified on the section of the canal by the flame which is from that side and is disordered and broken off due to the abscission of the voice.
E layssa la plagua uberta per alcun temps.	And leave the wound open for some time.
Donc cum la hora es remauguda en la qual perforacio es temuda, agregua doas labias de la codena de la plagua, e cus aquela sola ses la cartillage.	Therefore, when the hour is ripe in which perforation is to be feared, add two lips of the cord of the wound, and sew it up alone, except for the cartilage.
E aprop administra medicinas que fan naysser la carn entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, administer medicines that make the flesh new until it is healed.
E diyssec Albucasis que la summa del sermo le qual havem recomtat, exposicio no es sino que veias que alcus de aquetz apostemas ja han opilat lo guolayro del malaute, e le malaute es vengut entro a mort, e le ale de lu es entresecat, e alcus van a inscidir le epiglos per so que respire le malaute sobre le loc de la plagua per alcuna respiracio, e sia salvat de mort.	And Albucasis says that the summary of this sermon which we have recounted is an exposition not to show that some of these abscesses have already filled up the groin of the patient, and the patient has come close to death, and his soul is exhausted, and some go to incise the epiglottis so that the patient may breathe over the location of the wound through some respiration, and be saved from death.
E per aquo comandero layssar la plagua uberta entro que sia consumida la malicia de la malautia; e es la malicia de lu per tres dias; e donc lahoras comandero cosi la plagua, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And therefore, I command to leave the wound open until the malice of the disease is consumed; and it is the malice of that place for three days; and then I command to close the wound, and cure it until it is healed.
E aquo que yeu he vist per mi meteys, es que una sirventa pres un cotel e mesec le en le sieu golayro e inscidic am aquel una partida de la cana del pulmo, e yeu fu apelat a la curacio de lu, e atrobegui la mugen ayssi cum es mugit del moridos, e descubrigui la plagua e atrobegui le sanc le qual era yssit de la plagua petit.	And what I have seen through my eyes is that a servant took a cauterizing iron and applied it to his groin, and incised a part of the canal of the lung, and you were called to the cure of him, and he began to groan as if groaning from the dying, and discovered the wound and extracted the blood which was situated in the little wound.
Donc yeu fo confessat que aquela no havia inscidit vena ni guidegi, e le vent yssia de la plagua, e curegui aquela entro que foc sanada.	Therefore, you were confessed that he had not incised a vein nor an artery, and the breath was coming from the wound, and cured it until it was healed.
E no accidic a la sirventa si no rauquiera en la votz, e aprop alcus dias retornec ad miloracio de las suas dispozicios.	And he did not suffer any harm except for some roughness in his voice, and accordingly, after several days, he returned to an improvement of his physical condition.
E ara dic yeu que en la seccio del epilhot no ha temor.	And now I say to you that there is no fear in the section of the epilhot.
Capitol .xliv.	Chapter XLIV.
De seccio sobre apostema le qual accideys en le golayro defora, e es apelat hernia del golayro.	Of the section on abscess that occurs in the groin outside, and is called a hernia of the groin.
Aquest apostema nompnat hernia del golayro es apostema gran segon la color del cors, e es mot en las femnas.	This abscess is called a hernia of the groin, which is a great abscess according to the color of the body, and it occurs more in women.
E es segon dos manieyras, quar o es natural o accidental.	And it is according to two manners, either it is natural or accidental.
E en le natural no es engen de curar.	And in the natural one there is no need for cure.
E l’accidental es segon dos manieyras del qual la un es semblant a nodes grasses, e l’autra manieyra es semblant apostema le qual es fayt per nodacio de arteria, e en aquel es temor.	And the accidental one is according to two manners, of which one is similar to grassy nodes, and the other manner is similar to abscess which is caused by a constriction of an artery, and in that there is fear.
E no cove que·s fassa presumpcio a lu cum ferr sino en aquel que es petit.	And it is not necessary to make presumption about it unless it is small.
E tu proha aquel e investigua aquel am le dit, e si atrobas lu semblant a nodi gras, e no es suspendut am alcuna de las venas, lahoras tu inscideys aquel ayssi cum les nodes, e extratz aquel am aquo que conte lu de la pel e bursiclam; e sino, lahoras es perscrutat tot le sieu esser, e aprop cura le loc am aquo que cove de curacio entro que sia sanat.	And you should proceed with that and investigate it according to what is said, and if you find it similar to grassy nodes, and not suspended from any of the veins, then you incise it as with the nodes, and extract it with water that contains the peel and bursiclam; and otherwise, then thoroughly examine the entire being, and accordingly cure the location where healing is needed until it is healed.
Capitol .xlv.	Chapter XLV.
De seccio de las specias de nodes.	Of the section on the species of nodes.
Dels nodes so motas specias e yeu ja he dit totas las specias de lor en la divisio.	Of the nodes many species and I have already said all the species of theirs in the division.
E cove que yeu recomte assi la diferencia entre node e exitura cum fassa dubitacio.	And it is necessary that you recount thus the difference between a node and an exitra, so as to dispel doubt.
Donc yeu dic que am exitura es caliditat e febre e dolors vehementz entro que es sedada la ebullicio de la superfluitat; e es complida putrefaccio que lahora cessa la febre, la dolor e la calor.	Therefore, I say that with exitra there is heat and fever and violent pains until the ebullition of the superfluity is sedated; and it is completed putrefaction which then ceases the fever, pain, and heat.
Mays am node no es caliditat ni febre ni dolor, e conte aquel ciphac leon le qual es al u sac propri.	But with a node there is no heat nor fever nor pain, and it contains that cartilage-like substance which is in its own sac.
E es segon la color del cors, e le comensament de lu es cum un ceze e es fayt ayssi cum vace, sia major o minor, e son segon dos specias, quar o so grassas e conteno humiditat, e las colors de la humiditat son motas, segon que yeu diyssi en la divisio.	And it is according to the color of the body, and its beginning is like a cheese and it is made thus like a pouch, whether greater or lesser, and they are according to two species, either they are grassy and contain humidity, and the colors of the humidity are many, as I said in the division.
Donc cove, quan pervenas a la curacio de node, que exprohes aquel e inquiras aquel al comensament am sturment le qual es apelat intromes, segon que vindra la sua forma en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	Therefore, when you come to the cure of a node, that you expose it and inquire into it at the beginning with a instrument which is called an intro-mes, according to what its form will appear in the chapter which is next to this one.
E es manieyra de inquisicio de apostemas e de totz nodes, e es que tu prenguas aquest sturment e entromet aquel en le loc pus humit le qual atrobas en le apostema, e tu revolveras les tieus ditz am aquel petit a petit entro que sapias que·l sturment ja ha penetrat la codena.	And it is the manner of inquiry into abscesses and all nodes, which is that you take this instrument and introduce it into the most humid part of the abscess, and you turn the handle thus little by little until you know that the instrument has penetrated to the cord.
E aprop ultima la tua ma segon la mesura de la grandeza del apostema, e aprop extratz le entromes e considera aquo que es yssit en le vestigi de lu.	And accordingly, finally, your hand according to the measure of the greatness of the abscess, and accordingly extract the intro-mes and consider what is situated in its place.
E si es fora-getada la humiditat corrent, de qualque color sia, lahoras tu le inscideys am seccio superficial segon que he dit en les autres apostemas.	And if the moisture which flows is forgotten, of whatever color it may be, then you incise it with a superficial section according to what I have said in other abscesses.
E si del vestigi de l’intromes no hieys humiditat, lahoras sapias que es gras.	And if from the place of the intro-mes there is no moisture, then you know that it is grass.
E secca sobre lu am seccio havent forma de crotz segon aquesta forma:	And dry on it with a section having the shape of a cross according to this form:
ayssi cum t’e ensenhat, e suspen aquel am oncis, e excorja la codena de tota part am facilitat, e guarda la pel o sac, si podes, sobre aquel e extraguas aquela sania am le node.	just as I have taught you, and suspend it with a needle, and excise the cord from all parts with ease, and preserve the skin or sack, if possible, over that and extract that pus from the node.
Mays si es romput en la operacio, no es possible extrayre aquela sana, e motas veguadas endeve aquo, e lahoras tu la extratz a pessas entro que de lu no romangua denguna causa.	But if it is broken in the operation, it is not possible to extract that pus, and often times end up with this, and accordingly you extract it by pieces until there is no longer any cause from there.
Quar si de lu roman denguna causa, pauc o trop, le node retorne segon le mays.	For if from there remains no cause, a little or too much, the node will return as before.
E si tu vezes que de lu roman alcuna part petita, lahoras comple la plagua de alcunas polveras corrosivas agudas e strenh la plagua, e pausa sobre aquela que sede apostema caut, e cura aquel del autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And if you find that from there remains a small part, then complete the wound with some sharp and corrosive powders and strengthen the wound, and pause over it which has abscessed cautiously, and cure that other way until it is healed.
E si es node gran, lahoras tu cus las doas labias de lu e cura aquel am aquo que encarna.	And if it is a great node, then you sew the two lips of it and cure that with water which nourishes.
Mays si vena pulsatil es a lu contraria, o no-pulsatil, lahoras tu coyta e huemple le loc de zegi trissat que es vetriol e leyssa aquel streyt per dos dias o per tres entro que·s poyresca la plagua e que repause la ebullicio del sanc; e aprop retorna a inscindir aquo que es romas del node.	But if the pulsating vein is on the opposite side, or non-pulsating, then you compress and apply a wet compress to the location of the gauze, which is vitriol, and leave it so for two days or three until the wound becomes firm and the ebullition of blood subsides; and accordingly return to incise that which remains of the node.
Capitol .xlvi.	Chapter XLVI.
De las formas del sturmentz necessaris en seccio e perforacio.	Of the forms of the instruments necessary for section and perforation.
De aquels so las formas dels intromesas, e so de tres specias, que de aquels es alcu gran, e de lor es migier, e de lor es petit.	Of those, the forms of intro-meses, and of three species, that of which is great, and of which is medium-sized, and of which is small.
La forma de intromes gran es aquesta:	The form of the great intro-mes is this:
La forma de intromes migier es aquesta:	The form of the medium-sized intro-mes is this:
La forma de intromes petit es aquesta:	The form of the small intro-mes is this:
Sian faytz de ferr, de alfulud, de extremitatz cayradas decentment, per so que festino le intrament en les apostemas.	They are made of iron, with a pointed end, and curved extremities that descend in a gentle slope, for the purpose of fixing the instrument in abscesses.
E aquestas so las formas dels experientz, e son nompnatz albered, e un de aquels es apelat berid.	And these are the forms of the experiments, and they are called "albered", and one of them is called "berid".
E so de tres especias, quar de lor es gran, migier e pauc.	And there are three species, that of which is great, medium-sized, and small.
La forma de experient gran, forma de lu:	The form of the great experiment, shape of it:
La forma de experient migier, forma de lu:	The form of the medium-sized experiment, shape of it:
La forma de experient pauc, forma de lu:	The form of the small experiment, shape of it:
Conveneysso que sian per aquels apostemas e exituras e fistulas e bubos per so que entre aquelas so dels osses e de autras causas.	Conveniently so that they are for those abscesses, exitrae, fistulae, and bubae, and also for the bones and other causes.
E so faytz redontz, grosses, leons, ayssi cum grans agulhas am las quals son cosidas las selhas, e son faytas de eram citri, o de eram o de ferr, o de argent, E las milhors so quan so faytas de eram citri.	And thus they are made round, thick, and long, like great needles with which the stitches are sewn together, and they are made of earthenware citron, or of iron, or of silver, And the best ones are when they are made of earthenware citron.
E son faytz les experient de plum negre, les quals se acordan que per aquels sian ubertas las fistulas en la conquavitat de las quals so reflexios, que sian reflectidas am la sua levitat am aquelas refleccios.	And they are made of black plums, which are adapted to those that are plentiful the fistulae in the concavity of which there are reflections, which are reflected in their lightness with those reflections.
E so de tres specias, quar alcus de lor so loncs, e dels autres migiers, e dels autres breus, segon la quantitat del ample de la fistula e de la strictura de lu.	And there are three species, that one of them is long, and the others medium-sized, and the others short, according to the quantity of the width of the fistula and its constriction.
Forma del experient gran de plom:	Form of the great experiment of lead:
Forma del experient migier de plom:	Form of the medium-sized experiment of lead:
Forma del experient petit de plom:	Form of the small experiment of lead:
Las formas dels oncis so de motas specias, quar de aquels so alcus simples, als quals es una curvitat solament, e so de tres specias: grans, paucs e migiers.	The forms of the needles are of many species, that one of them is simple, with only a single curvature, and there are three species: great, small, and medium-sized.
E de lor so uncis orps, e so de tres specias.	And among them there are iron needles, and there are three species.
E de aquels so uncis haventz doas curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among those, there are needles with two curvatures, and there are three species.
E de lor so haventz tres curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among those, there are needles with three curvatures, and there are three species.
E totz aquetz so necessaris en lor loc.	And all these are necessary in their place.
Forma de unci simple gran, forma de lu:	Form of a large simple needle, shape of it:
Forma de unci simple migier:	Form of a medium-sized simple needle:
Forma de unci simple pauc, forma de lu:	Form of a small simple needle, shape of it:
Forma de unci orp gran:	Form of an iron needle great one:
Forma de unci orp migier, forma de lu:	Form of an iron needle medium-sized one, shape of it:
Forma de unci orp pauc, forma de lu:	Form of an iron needle small one, shape of it:
Forma de unci gran havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a large needle having two curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent dos curvatas:	Form of a medium-sized needle having two curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a small needle having two curvatures:
Forma de unci gran havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a large needle having three curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a medium-sized needle having three curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a small needle having three curvatures:
E aquestas so las formas dels scalpels am les quals son seccatz e scorjatz les nodes e le apostemas, e so de tres specias, quar de aquels es gran, migier, e pauc.	And these are the forms of scalpels with which one cuts and scores nodes and abscesses, and there are three species, that one of them is great, medium-sized, and small.
Forma de scapel gran:	Form of a large scalpel:
Forma del scapel migier:	Form of a medium-sized scalpel:
Forma de scapel pauc:	Form of a small scalpel:
Las extramitatz de aquels am les quals es fayta seccio so agudas e las autres extramitatz so no-agudas, e no so pausadas en tal manieyra, sino per que sia fayt juvament en la excorjacio dels nodes la temor de inscizio de vena o de nervi, e per aquels sia sanat le malaute e atrobe tranquilitat un petit per la adustio la qual atroba deves la excoriacio del apostema.	The extremities of those with which section is made are sharp and the other extremities are not sharp, and they are not paused in such a manner, but rather so that it may be done gently in the excision of nodes to avoid the danger of incising a vein or nerve, and for this reason the patient is cured and afterwards tranquility is found a little due to the adaptation which is obtained from the excision of the abscess.
E aquestas son las formas de almagidas, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc, ayssi cum veyras.	And these are the forms of ligatures, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small, just like threads.
La forma de magda gran:	The form of a large ligature:
Forma de magda migier:	Form of a medium-sized ligature:
Forma de magda pauc:	Form of a small ligature:
Sian faytas de eram e so semblantz de ray am le qual e fayt alcofol.	They are made of earthenware and resemble rays, with which one makes alcohol.
E es en la extramitat lada punctada am spatum occultada e en aquela corr a las partidas dedintz e defora, quan tu vols, ayssi cum veses.	And it is in the lateral extremity that one makes a small puncture with a hidden spatula and in that corner runs the partitions inwardly and outwardly, whenever you want, just as you see.
Las formas de spatimis, les quals so amaguatz entre los ditz deves la perforacio dels apostemas e no les percebo les malautes, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc.	The forms of spatulas, which are hidden between the fingers when one performs the puncture of abscesses and do not touch the patients, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small.
E aquestas so las formas de aquels:	And these are the forms of those:
Las formas de ventozas am las quals es abscindit le flux del sanc, e so de tres specias; gran, migiera e pauca; las formas de lu:	The forms of absorbents with which one absorbs the flow of blood, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small; their forms are:
Sian faytas de eram citri, redondas am alcuna longitut , e sian subtils.	They are made of earthenware citron, rounded with some length, and are subtle.
E cove que sian aquestas specias de ventosas deves tu grans, migieras e paucas, per so que per aquelas abscindas flux de sanc am velocitat en necessitat, e lahoras quan a tu primieyrament no es medicina.	And it is necessary that these species of absorbents are great, medium-sized, and small, for the purpose of absorbing the flow of blood with velocity when needed, and accordingly when first aid is not medicine.
Enpero no uses de aquelas ad abscidir sanc en tot loc del cors, e non uses sino en locs carnoses, ayssi cum en les lacertis de las cambas e de las coyssas, e en les lacertz dels brasses, e de las mamillas e del ventre e dels engonars, e semblantz a lor dels lacertz carnoses humitz.	However, one does not use those to absorb blood in all parts of the body, and one uses them only in fleshy areas, such as in the crevices of the hips and buttocks, and in the creases of the arms, and breasts, and belly, and groin areas, and similar to their fleshly counterparts.
E alcunas veguadas son faytz de aquels strumentz autres petitz semblantz scorsas de fisacs segon aquesta forma; per les quals lo sanc es abscindit quan es fayt per fleubotomia, o deves inscizio de vena o de arceria.	And sometimes they are made of those small instruments resembling scissors according to this form; by which blood is absorbed when it is done through phlebotomy, or incision of a vein or artery.
E alcunas veguadas son faytas redondas segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes they are made round according to this form:
Capitol .xlvii.	Chapter XLVII.
De la cura de las mamillas dels homes las quals so asembladas de femnas.	Of the cure of men's breasts which are similar to those of women.
Alcunas veguadas so infladas las mamillas de alcus homes deves le compliment del dormir cum comensan esser pellutz, e aprop so infladas las mamillas, e so asembladas las mamillas de las femnas, e romano apostemosas, lejas.	Sometimes the breasts of certain men become inflamed due to the excess of sleeping when they start getting older, and accordingly, the breasts are swollen, and similar to those of women, and abscesses form at a distance.
E ad aquel que avoreys aquo, cove que inscidisca aquelas am seccio lunar segon aquesta forma, de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G., e aprop excorja la groceza tota, e aprop uempla la plagua de medicament encarnatiu, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am cosidura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And to the one who is afflicted with this, it is necessary to incise those with a lunar section according to this form, from the line of B to the line of G, and accordingly excise all the gangrene, and accordingly fill the wound with an incarnate medicine, and accordingly adjust the two lips of the wound with sewing, and cure that until it is healed.
Mays si la mamilla declina a las partidas dejos e es mollificada per la sua magnitut ayssi cum endeve a las femnas, lahoras sia fendut en dos latz sieus pus sobiras, am dos seccios semblantz a figura lunar, de las quals quascuna sia contenguda en l’autra deves la fi de quascuna, entro que sia que la linha major contengua la menor segon aquesta forma de la linha de .B. e la linha de .G. E aprop excorja la codena la qual es entre dos labias de la plagua, e osta la pingueza, e aministra aquo que havem dit de la sutura e de las polveras aquo que es necessari en la curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the breast sinks into the partitions and is softened by its magnitude just like in women, then it should be cut in two parts from top to bottom, with two sections resembling a lunar figure, of which each one is contained within the other, until the major line contains the minor one according to this form of the line of B and the line of G. And accordingly excise the cord that is between the two lips of the wound, and remove the swelling, and administer the liquid we have said about suturing and the powders which are necessary for healing until it is healed.
E si tu non conpleysses la inscizio de aquo que cove inscidir per la inquietut del malaute, e per flux de sanc, lahoras cove que huemplas la plagua de coto submergit en enguent corrosiu e layssa aquel entro que aquo corroda que es romas de la grayssa, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if you do not complete the incision of that which is necessary to be cut due to the unease of the patient and the flow of blood, then it is necessary to fill the wound with a submergent poultice in corrosive gauze and leave it until the corroded part that remains of the grayish color is gone, and accordingly cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .xlviii.	Chapter XLVIII.
De perforacio de apostemas que veno dejos le titillic.	Of the puncturing of abscesses that come left behind the titillate.
Aquetz apostemas que veno dejos le titillic so de las specias de scrophulas, durs, las quals conte una pel que es sac.	Those abscesses that come left behind the titillate are of the species of scrofulae, hard ones, which contain a sack.
E de aquelas so alcunas que conteno humiditatz; e aquelas que conteno humiditatz cove que sian inscididas am seccio lunar segon aquesta figura: de la linha de .G. a la linha de .B. E cum es tot evacuat aquo que es en le apostema de la sania, lahoras tu le comple de coto viel e leysa le entro al autra dia.	And among those, some contain moisture; and those that contain moisture should be incised with a lunar section according to this figure: from the line of G to the line of B. And when all the fluid that is in the abscess has been evacuated, then you should fill it with a warm compress and leave it until the next day.
E aprop le coto sia ostat e sia curat am enguent convenient ad aquo, entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, the compress should be applied and the wound should be cured with a suitable poultice until it is healed.
E si le apostema de las specias dels nodes es, e de las scrophulas, lahoras tu scindeys sobre aquel ayssi cum havem dit en la seccio sobre las scrophulas engualment.	And if the abscess is of the species of nodes and scrofulae, then you should cut it open just as we have said in the section on scrofulae equally.
May si la plagua es extenduda en aysso que yesca poyredura, lahoras administra en lu cauteri segon que en aquo havem denant dit.	And if the wound is extended in such a way that it appears to be inflamed, then you should apply a cautery to it just as we have said before.
Capitol .xlix.	Chapter XLIX.
De seccio de apostemas que accideysso per arceria o per vena.	Of the section of abscesses that occur through artery or vein.
Quan arceria es rompuda, e la codena es consolidada la qual es sobre aquela, lahoras motas veguadas accideys apostema E les senhals per les quals es conoguda que imflamacio e apostema sian per la arteria o per vena: quar quan apostema es per arceria es lonc agreguat en le preon del cors; e que quan inpelleysses le apostema am les tieus ditz, sentes en lu quays sia stridor.	When an artery is ruptured and the cord that is consolidated on top of it has become inflamed and an abscess has formed, then many times these signs are observed: for when an abscess is caused by an artery, it becomes long and aggregated in the forepart of the body; and when you press the abscess with those said fingers, you will feel a stridor.
E aquel que es per vena es redon al manifest del cors.	And that which is caused by a vein is rounded to the visible part of the body.
E seccio sobre aquest apostema es error, e majorment en aquel que es dejos las aysselhas, e en les angonars, e en le col, e en motz locs del cors; e es mot gran, donc cove que la sua curacio am ferr sia esquivada, e aquel que es en las extramitatz, o al cap, cove que sia evitat.	And the section on this abscess is in error, and more so in those that are left behind in the armpits, and in the neck, and in many places of the body; and it is very great, therefore it is necessary to avoid its cure with iron, and that which is in the extremities or at the head should be avoided.
Mays sobre aquel que es de lor per imflacio de l’orrifici de la arceria, scindeys en la codena seccio en le lonc; e aprop huebre la seccio am uncis e aprop la arceria, e deliura de las tunicas entro que sia descuberta.	But over that which is caused by them through inflammation of the orifice of the artery, you should cut open the cord section in the long way; and accordingly, you will find the section with scissors and accordingly, you will tie off the artery, and deliver from the tunics until it is uncovered.
E aprop met sobre aquel agulha e fay aquela penetrar entro al autre latz, e estrenh la arceria am fiel doble en dos locs, — la qual causa yeu a tu eyssenhegui en extraccio de doas arcerias les quals so en les templars.	And accordingly, you will make a stitch on that with an needle and make it penetrate into the other side, and strengthen the artery with a double thread in two places, — which causes you to see your own eyes in the extraction of two arteries which are in the temples.
E aprop punh le loc le qual es entre dos liamentz am spatum entro que yesca le sanc tot que es en lu, e sia dissolvut le apostema.	And accordingly, you will push the place between two ligatures with a spatula until all the blood that is in it is drained and the abscess is dissolved.
E aprop administra curacio en la qual es engendrat poyre entro que caian les liamentz; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz convenientz ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, you will administer care in which fire is generated until the ligatures fall away; and accordingly, you will cure that with suitable poultices to it until it is healed.
E si es apostema per seccio de vena, lahoras cove que tu tenguas am la tua ma aquo que es a tu possible del apostema am la codena, e aprop intromet la agulha dejos le loc le qual tu has tengut dejos la tua ma, e fay aquela penetrar; e sia en aquela fil doble entro que tu extraguas aquel del autre latz, e aprop ligua le apostema am bo liament segon que yeu he dit a tu en le liament de uva4 de doas partz am doas extremitatz del fil.	And if the abscess is caused by an incision of a vein, then it is necessary for you to take with your hand as much water as is possible from the abscess and the cord, and accordingly, you will insert the needle left behind the place which you have taken with your hand, and make it penetrate; and be in that double thread until you extract that from the other side, and accordingly, you will tie off the abscess with a single ligament as I have said to you earlier about the ligature of two parts at two extremities of the thread.
Mays si temes que extraguam le fil, lahoras entromet le fiel am aquela agula dejos tot le apostema deves la inscizio de la agulha primieyra, e strenh les tieus fiels en quatre locs.	But if you fear that the thread will be extracted, then accordingly, you will insert a double thread with the needle left behind all the abscess, through the incision of the first needle, and strengthen those threads in four places.
Aprop secca le apostema en le mieg loc de lu entro que quan es yssit aquo que es en lu, lahoras tu inscideys la superfluitat de la codena, e layssa aquo que de lu es liat.	And accordingly, you will cut off the abscess in the middle of it, until when what is left is in it, then you will incise the superfluity of the cord, and leave that which is tied to it.
E aprop pausa sobre lu pulvil le qual has submergit en vi e oli, e aprop administra la curacio la qual es fayta am calguas e enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, you will pause over the poultice which you have submerged in vinegar and oil, and accordingly, you will administer care which is made with some and powders until it is healed.
Capitol l del apostema le qual accideys per torcio de nervis.	Chapter 1 on the abscess that occurs due to twisting of nerves.
Ayssi cum accideys apostema en arceria e en vena, e semblantment accideys apostema en les nervis quan accideys en lor percussio o accideys per trebal superfluable, e per semblantz.	Just as an abscess occurs in the artery and vein, and similarly an abscess occurs in the nerves when it occurs through percussion or due to excessive strain, and by similar causes.
E es fayt le mays de lu en les locs dels adjutoris o del talo, o en tot loc en le qual so maugudas las juncturas.	And it is made in the most part of it in the places of the assistants or the heel, or in any place where the joints are damaged.
E es apostema greu, e es asemblat a la color del autre cors, e es en las majors de lu disposicios ses de lor e quan es streyt am vehementia, sent en lu le malaute semblant stupor.	And it is a severe abscess, and is akin to the color of another body, and is in the major part of it disposed to its own kind, when it is stretched with vehemence, then in it the patient appears as if in a stupor.
E no es apostema agreguat en le preon del cors, e per so es dejos la codena, e el es maugut a tota partida e no va a las partidas denant ni detras.
