And it is not an abscess aggregated in the forepart of the body, and therefore it is left behind the cord, and it is damaged to all parts and does not go to the parts before or behind.
Donc aquo de aquels que es en las juncturas no cove que sia envasit am ferr, quar fort leu endevenguera contracio.	Therefore, that which is in the joints should not be incised with iron, for very lightly it would result in contraction.
Mays aquel que es en le cap o en le front fen la codena am spatum.	But that which is in the head or forehead should have the cord cut open with a spatula.
Mays si es apostema pauc, lahoras te aquel am les forfecs e abscindeys aquel de razitz.	But if it's a small abscess, then take that with forceps and cut it open with razors.
E si es gran, lahoras tu le suspen am unci, e excorja aquel, e aprop osta aquel; e ajusta la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if it's large, then you should suspend that with threads, and excise that, and accordingly remove that; and adjust the wound with a suture, and cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .li.	Chapter LI.
De seccio de apostema le qual accideys de cheil que accideys al ventre.	Of the section of abscess which occurs due to inflammation that occurs in the belly.
Endeveno ad alcus homes motas veguadas en les ventres de aquels e en las autras partidas del cors de aquels theils les quals son apelatz funguals per similitut de aquels am funges, dels quals la razitz es subtil e·l cap de aquel es gros; e ja las labias de aquels so conversas, e es de aquels que es petit, e es de aquels que es mot magnificat.	I have observed in some men that many times in their bellies and in other parts of their body those things which are called fungi by similarity to those with fungi, whose roots are subtle and the head of that is thick; and already the lips of those are conversed, and it is of those who is small, and it is of those who is very magnified.
E yeu ja e vist un, e en le ventre de lu eran dos theils les quals eran mays a funges semblantz, e no era diferencia entre aquels blancs, de menuda razitz.	And I have already seen one, and in the belly of it were two things which resembled fungi, and there was no difference between those white ones, with a subtle root.
E ja las labias de aquels eran enversadas e se fendian, e humiditat corria de aquel tot temps.	And already the lips of those were turned inwards and split open, and moisture flowed from that at all times.
Donc yeu inscidegui aquels e atrobegui en la un en pes quays xviii unc. e l’autre quays vi unc.	Therefore you should incise those and insert them into the one in a weight of 18 ounces. and the other, weighs 6 ounces.
E la operacio en la inscizio de lor es que consideres lahoras si·l malaute es humit, e la color de atheil es blanca, humit, de subtil razitz; lahoras tu le inscideys am spatum lat, e sian en la presencia tua cauteris en le foc, quar motas veguadas deves la seccio de lu es expellit mot sanc; e si te ventz le sanc, cauteriza aquel.	And the operation in the incision of theirs is that you consider whether the patient is humid, and the color of the thing is white, humid, with a subtle root; then you should incise it with a spatula, and be present when you have cauterized it over fire, because many times the section of it must expel much blood; and if you see the blood, cauterize that.
E si vezes le malaute pauruc e temeros, guarda te de inscizio am ferr; mays lahoras pren fiel de plom recent fayt, e strenh am aquel atheil, la manieyra del qual es aquela que havem dita; e leyssa aquel per dos dias.	And if the patient is weak and fearful, be careful not to incise with iron; but rather take a lead thread of recent making, and strengthen that thing, in the manner which we have said; and leave it for two days.
E aprop ajusta en la strictura del fil de plom; donc, no cesses strenher le plom granre devetz en theil, entro que sia abscindit e cayha per se ses trebalh.	And accordingly, adjust it in the constriction of the lead thread; therefore, do not cease to strengthen the lead greatly on that thing, until it is cut off and falls away by its own weight.
Mays si theil es de grossa razitz, lahoras en la inscizio de lu es alcuna causa de temor e de paor, e majorment en aquel que es en le ventre.	But if that thing is of great root, then in the incision of it there is some cause for fear and terror, and most especially in that which is in the belly.
Mays possibla es que tu inscindas la maytat de lu , e aprop cauteriza aquel per que no retorne.	But possible is that you incise the greatest part of it, and accordingly cauterize that so that it does not return.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanada la plagua.	And accordingly, cure that until the wound is healed.
E guarda te que tu no presumas inscidir theil le qual es de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, de leg reguardament, quar aquel es absi cancros.	And be careful not to incise that thing which is of a dark color, with little sensation, and with little regard, for that is absolutely cancerous.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio de cranc aprop aysso.	And you will find it to be a memory of cancer accordingly.
Capitol .lii.	Chapter LII.
De curacio de eminencia del umbilic.	Of the care of the navel prominence.
Eminencia del umbilic es fayta per motas causas; o per fissuras del ciphac le qual es sobre le ventre, e yeys de lu la tela o budel segon que endeve en las autras rupturas; o per sanc le qual flueys de vena o de arceria segon que es denant dit, o per ventositat coarctada en lu.	The navel prominence is caused by many reasons; or by fissures of the cicatrix which is on the belly, and you see that it is torn away or bundled up according to what is seen in other ruptures; or by blood which flows from a vein or artery, as has been said before, or by coarctation of the ventricle in it.
Mays si es per fissura del ciphac e per yssiment de la tela, lahoras la color del apostema es semblant a la color del cors; e es leon ses dolor, e aprop appar de divers situament.	But if it is due to a fissure of the cicatrix and the bursting forth of the navel string, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body; and there is no pain, and accordingly, it appears in different situations.
E si es per egressio del budel, lahoras le situament de aquel am lu de aquo que havem recontat, de mays vehement diversitat, e cum tu premes aquel am les tieus ditz es occultat, e aprop retorna; e fort leu es am lu so, e es magnificat mot deves le introt de banh e vehement trebalh.	And if it is due to the bursting forth of the navel string, then the situation of that with water as we have recounted, is with a more violent diversity; and when you press that with the threads I mentioned, it is hidden, and accordingly returns; and very quickly it becomes so, and is magnified much by the introduction of bath and violent labor.
Mays si per humiditat, lahoras es leon e no es occultat quan premes am la tua ma, ni es constrengut, ni es cregut.	But if due to humidity, then it is not so, and does not hide when you press with your hand, nor is it constricted or believed.
E si es per sanc, lahoras am aquestz senhals apareys le apostema a negror declinant.	And if due to blood, then accordingly, the abscess appears with these signs declining towards blackness.
Mays si es per carn nada, lahoras es apostema greu, gros e dur, e es ficat segon una quantitat.	But if it is due to nothing but flesh, then accordingly the abscess is a severe one, large and hard, and is situated according to a quantity.
Mays si es per ventositat, lahoras le tocament de lu es leon.	But if it is due to coarctation, then accordingly the touch of it is like nothing.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras lahoras si la eminencia de l’umbilic es per sanc de arceria, o de vena, o per ventositat; lahoras cove que sias prohibit de la curacio de lu, quar en aquela es temor e paor ayssi cum t’e ensenhat en le capitol en le qual he dit les apostemas per arceria e per vena.	And the operation in this case is that you consider whether the prominence of the navel is due to blood from an artery, or a vein, or coarctation; accordingly, it is necessary for you to be prohibited from treating it, because in that there is fear and terror just as I have taught you in the chapter where I described abscesses caused by arteries and veins.
E si la eminencia del umbilic es per le budel o per la tela, lahoras cove que comandes al malaute que tengua le ale sieu, e sia stant extendut; e aprop senha am tenta en le circuit de tot le umbilic, e aprop comanda a lu que stia envers entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e aprop circunda am spatum lat en le circuit del umbilic sobre le loc le qual has senhat am la tenta; e aprop exten la maytat del apostema a las partidas desus am unci gran; e aprop lia en le circuit am fiel fort o am ceda e la manieyra del liar decent.	And if the prominence of the navel is due to the navel string or the cord, then accordingly you should command the patient to take hold of his own navel and be standing upright; and accordingly, sign with a tent in the circuit of all the navel, and accordingly, command him to stay between your hands on both sides of his navel, and accordingly, surround it with a spatula in the circuit of the navel over the place which you have marked with the tent; and accordingly, extend most of the abscess above into the upper parts with threads; and accordingly, tie it off in the circuit with strong thread or with cord, and the manner of tying should be decent.
E aprop huebre le mieg del apostema extendut sobre le liament e intromet le dit tieu en aquel indic e quereys le budel; e si tu l’as atrobat ni guardat per le liament, lahoras tu extratz alxorati e impelleys le budel a las partidas dedintz del ventre.	And accordingly, take the middle of the abscess, which is extended over the ligature, and insert the said thread into it and seek out the navel string; and if you have found or guarded it by the ligature, then accordingly, extract the abscess and push the navel string down to the lower parts of the belly.
E si has atrobada la tela, lahoras pren aquel am unci; e inscideys las superfluitatz de lu.	And if you have found the cord, then accordingly take that with threads; and incise the superfluities of it.
Mays si es contraria a tu arceria o vena, lahoras circunda aquel mot, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio; e pren dos agulhas e met en aquelas dos fiels fortz e entromet dos agulhas en le circuit le qual has feyt entorn le apostema en manieyra de crotz, las quals fassas penetrar; e aprop strenh le apostema en quatre partidas sobre las agulhas.	But if it is contrary to your artery or vein, then accordingly circle that place, and accordingly return to your operation; and take two needles and put them in those two strong threads, and insert the two needles into the circuit which you have made around the abscess in a cross-like manner, so that they will penetrate; and accordingly strengthen the abscess in four parts above the needles.
E si tu vols, osta las agulhas e leyssa le loc entro que poyresca la carn extenduda e caia per si; o inscideys aquel quan es subtiliat e se poyreys, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if you wish, remove the needles and leave the place until the flesh extends and falls away by itself; or incise that when it is subtlety and becomes soft, and accordingly cure that with water as needed until it is healed.
E si la eminencia del ombilic es de carn nada en lu o per humiditat, lahoras cove que tu conquaves le apostema ayssi cum havem dit e estraguas le sanc o la humiditat, la qual atrobas en lu, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove e que consolide le loc.	And if the prominence of the navel is due to nothing but flesh or humidity in it, then accordingly you should conquer the abscess as we have said and remove the blood or humidity which you find there, and accordingly cure that with water as needed and consolidate the place.
Capitol .liii.	Chapter LIII.
De curacio de cranc.	Of the care of cancer.
Ja havem dit, en la divisio, de specia de cranc e en qual manieyra es via a la curacio de lu am medicinas, e que es squivador en lu la curacio am ferr per so que no sia ulcerat; e havem dit cranc engendrat en la mayra e cautela de la curacio de lu.	We have already said in the division, about the species of cancer and how it is treated with medicines, and what is to be avoided in treating it with iron so that it is not ulcerated; and we have said that cancer is generated through excessive care and caution in treating it.
E diyssero les antics que alcunas veguadas cranc es en loc on es possibla la eradicacio de lu, ayssi cum de cran le qual es en las mamillas o en la coyssa e a lor semblantz dels membres allocat a estrayre tot aquel, e majorment quan es comensant petit.	And the ancients said that sometimes cancer is in a place where its eradication is possible, just like breast cancer or abdominal cancer and their similarities to the members allocated to remove all of it, and most especially when it starts small.
Mays quan es antiquat e es gra, no cove que te propries a lu, quar yeu non pogui sanar de aquel alcu ni no he vist autre, ni que sia pervengut ad aquo.	But when it is old and great, you should not attempt to treat it, because you will not be able to heal it at all nor have I seen anyone else do so, nor that it has been brought to a good outcome.
E la operacio en lu es quan es allocat ayssi cum havem dit, es que tu precedescas e laysses le malaute e purgues de colera negra alcunas veguadas, e aprop sagna aquel, si es atrobada replecio manifesta.	And the operation in this case is when it is allocated as we have said, that you precede and leave the patient and purge him of black cholera some times, and accordingly apply a poultice to that place if a manifest repletion has been found.
E aprop prepara le malaute am preparacio en le qual sia locat am operacio, e aprop prohiceys en le trauc uncis les quals cove ad aquel; e aprop concava de tota part am la codena sego bona perexcrutacio entro que no romangua alcuna causa de las razitz de lu.	And accordingly, prepare the patient with preparation for the operation in which the place is located, and accordingly prohibit in the thread threads that are necessary for that; and accordingly concave all parts of the cord so that it is good excision until there remains no cause of the roots of it.
E layssa correr le sanc, e no abscidas aquel leugierament, e exprem les locs, e abstergeys le sanc gros tot am la tua ma o am instrument am le qual es a tu possible dels instruments.	And accordingly, let the blood flow, and do not incise it slightly, and express the places, and wipe away the thick blood with your hand or with an instrument that is at your disposal from among the instruments.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat de sanc gros inscizio de vena o de arceria, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que·l flux del sanc sia cessat, e aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if you find that the thick blood incision of the vein or artery causes contrariety to it, then accordingly cauterize that place until the flow of blood is stopped, and accordingly cure that with another cure until it is healed.
Capitol .liv.	Chapter LIV.
De curacio de ydropici.	Of the care of hydropsis.
Nos ja havem recomtat, en la divisio, de las specias de ydropici de l’aygua, e les senhals de quascuna especia, de la curacio de lu am medicinas.	We have already recounted, in the division, about the species of hydropsis caused by water, and the signs of each species, as well as its treatment with medicines.
E aquela la qual es curada am ferr no es sino la specia de althitas sola, e no es aproximat am ferr a la specia de timpanistres ni a la especia de yposarcha, quar aquo es mortal.	And that one which is cured with iron is only the species of Althita alone, and it is not approached with iron to the species of Timpanister nor to the species of Yposarca, because this is mortal.
E quan tu ja has medicat aquesta especia de ydropici timpanistre am medicinas e no comfereys la tua medicacio, lahoras considera, quar si al malaute ja es conseguida debelitat, o es am aquel autra malautia otra ydropici, ayssi cum si es en lu tos o cos de ventre e semblant ad aquels, lahoras guarda te que no le mediques am ferr, quar temor es sobre aquo.	And when you have already medicated this species of hydropsis timpanister with medicines and it has not been confirmed by your medicine, then accordingly consider whether the patient is already weakened or has another disease, just like if it is in the lungs or belly and similar to those, then accordingly beware that you do not treat it with iron, because fear is above this.
Mays si tu vezes le malaute de vertut exuberant, e am lu no es autra malautia sino ydropici tant solament, e no enfant ni vielh, lahoras la manieyra de la operacio de lu es que tu eleves le malaute entre las tuas mas, e le ministre aprop lu exprema le ventre de lu am la sua ma, enpellen la aygua a la partida dejos del pentenilh, e aprop pren spatum spinos segon aquesta forma:	But if you find the patient to be of robust virtue, and there is no other disease but hydropsis alone, and it is not an infant or an old person, then accordingly the manner of the operation for that is that you lift the patient between your hands, and give them proper care, expelling the water from the belly with their own hand, filling the water at the part left of the pentenilh, and accordingly take a pointed spatula in this form:
sia de dos partz agudas lonc, de aguda extremitat ayssi cum spatum; mays empero sia en lu alcuna brevitat petit a petit, per so que en la operacio am aquel no passes entro al budel, e que ledas aquel.	with two sharp parts long, with a sharp extremity just like a spatula; but however, be in it some smallness little by little, so that in the operation with that you do not enter into the navel string, and lead those to.
E aprop considera si la generacio de ydropici es de part dels budels, quar lahoras cove que tu am la seccio te alonhes del ombelic per la quantitat de tres ditz a las partidas dejos, en le dreyt de lu sobre le pentenilh.	And accordingly consider if the generation of hydropsis is from one of the navel strings, because then you should have the section move away from the navel by the quantity of three said parts to the left over, on the right side of it above the pentenilh.
Mays si la generacio de hydropici es per malautia del fietge, lahoras la tua seccio sia sinistra del ombilic per tres ditz.	But if the generation of hydropsis is due to disease of the liver, then accordingly your section should be left of the navel by three said parts.
E si la generacio de lu es per la melsa, lahoras la tua seccio sia en le las dreyt.	And if the generation of it is due to melancholy, then accordingly your section should be in the right side.
E no cove que la tua seccio sia sobre le costat sobre le qual vol jaser le malaute per que no corron las superfluitatz ad aquel loc freul.	And it is not necessary for your section to be on the side on which the patient wishes to lie down, so that the superfluities do not flow to that place freely.
E aprop perfora am le instrument tota la codena, e aprop entromet en aquela seccio, e eleva la tua ma am le spatum entre la codena e·l siphac, e tu excorja aquel; e si’ la quantitat de una ungla o enviro.	And accordingly pierce the entire cord with an instrument and accordingly insert it into that section, and lift your hand with a spatula between the cord and the siphac, and you will excise that; and if it is the quantity of one fingernail or thereabout.
E aprop perforo le ciphac entro que pervengua le spatum al loc vuoyt, e es loc de l’aygua.	And accordingly pierce the cicatrix until the spatula reaches the location where you want it to be, and that is the location of the water.
E aprop extratz aquel e entromet un instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	And accordingly extract that and insert an instrument which has this shape:
e es semblant a canula de argent subtil; es fayt de argent o de eram o de lato leon, al qual en la partida pus bassa de lu es un petit trauc, e en les costatz de lu so tres traucs: dos de una partida e un del autra partida; e fayta es la extremitat de lu insciza segon la manieyra de pluma, ayssi cum vezes:	and it is similar to a silver canula; it is made of silver or of iron or of lead, and at the bottom part of it there is a small hole, and on both sides of it there are three holes: two from one side and one from the other side; and the end of it is incised according to the manner of a feather, just like when you:
E en la extramitat de lu pus sobirana es armilla, quar quan le instrument perve al aygua, lahoras aquela tantost deysen sobre le instrument, donc evacua de l’aygua en la ora miega quantitat, quar si tu evacuas de aquela mes que no cove en la hora, fort leu mor le malaute per resolucio del sieu spirit animal, o accideys a lu cincopi que es appropinquada la mort.	And on the top of it is a ring, because when the instrument reaches the water, then that ring will soon descend upon the instrument, and accordingly evacuate from the water in a moderate quantity; for if you evacuate more than necessary at that hour, very quickly the patient will die due to resolution of their animal spirit, or you will cause injury to them which is close to death.
Mays evacua de aquela segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu e segon que significan a tu las disposicios del malaute de la vertut del pols de lu e de la bontat de lu.	But evacuate from that according to the quantity of the virtue of it and according to what your observations indicate about the patient's disposition, the virtue of their pulse, and the good or bad nature of them.
E aprop extrats le instrument, e rete l’aygua la qual causa es quar tantost es retenguda per la codena la qual rete le trauc que es sobre le ciphac del qual e recomtat a tu que perfores aquel segon aquela manieyra.	And accordingly extract the instrument, and retain the water which is retained because it is held back by the cord which holds the hole that is on the cicatrix of which I have told you to pierce it according to this manner.
E aprop itera le instrument al autra dia si vezes le malaute tollerant aquo, e extratz de la aygua petita quantitat, e fay aquo per alcus jorns sobre temor, e guarda te de error entro que no romangua de l’aygua sino pauc.	And accordingly repeat the instrument on another day if you find that the patient is able to tolerate this, and extract a small quantity of water, and do this for some days with caution, and beware of error until there remains only a little water.
Mays si tu temes sobre le malaute, e leyssas de l’aygua gran quantitat, lahoras cura aquel am sepultura en arena cauda, e mota suzor en banh, e al solelh espere per lonc temps; e cura aquel am medicinas dessicativas entro que sia sanat.	But if you fear for the patient, and let a large quantity of water flow, then accordingly cure that with burial in hot sand, and mix it with warm mud, and wait under the sun for a long time; and cure that with desiccative medicines until they are healed.
E cauteriza sobre le stomac, e la melsa e·l fitge aprop la extraccio de l’aygua, segon que yeu he recontat en aquo que es precedit.	And cauterize on the stomach, and the melancholy and liver accordingly with the extraction of water, according to what I have recounted previously in this which has preceded.
Capitol .lv.	Chapter LV.
De la curacio dels enfants les quals so natz les locs de la urina no-perforatz.	Of the cure of children who are born with undescended testicles not perforated.
Alcunas veguadas alcun dels enfantz es eyssi del ventre de la sua mayre e·l cap de la sua mixtio no es perforat (o es trauc streyt o no es en son loc).	Sometimes one of the children is thus born from the belly of its mother and the head of its mixture is not perforated (or has a very narrow hole or is not in its place).
Donc cove coytar am perforacio de lu tantost que es nascut am spatum mot subtil segon aquesta forma:	Therefore it is necessary to pierce that with a perforation as soon as it is born with a fine spatula according to this shape:
E aprop pausa en le trauc un clavil subtil de plom e ligua aquel, e te per tres jorns o per .iiii.tre.	And accordingly pause in the hole a small clasp made of lead and tie that one on, and leave it there for three days or four.
E quant vol urinar sia remaugut e hurine; e aprop retorne aquel.	And when it is time to urinate, be renewed and flow; and accordingly return that.
E si tu no pauses le plom, ja es possible que la urina la qual va sobre le loc, no leysa aquest claure.	And if you do not pause the lead, it is possible that the urine which flows over the place will not allow this to close.
Mays aquel del qual le trauc es streyt sia medicat am clavil de Plom, ayssi cum havem dit, per trops dias entro que sia amplificat.	But that which has a narrow hole should be treated with a leaden clamp, just as we have said, for many days until it is widened.
Mays aquels en les quals es le trauc no en son loc, so leditz, la qual causa es quar de aquels, aquel que es nat e·l trau es deves la fi del cap de la vergua per que no pot urinar a las partidas dedintz, entro que eleva la vergua am la sua ma a las partidas desus; e no es a lu generacio, per so quar le sperma no pot pervenir a la mayre segon rectitut, e es malautia mot laga.	But those in which the hole is not in its place are led astray, and this is because of those who are born with the trait that is at the end of the penis, so that it cannot urinate downwards, but instead lifts the penis with its own hand upwards; and it is not a natural generation, therefore the sperm cannot reach the mother according to rectitude, and it is a miserable illness.
E la manieyra de la operacio en lu es que·l malaute sia envessat sobre le sieu dos, e aprop exten le cap de la vergua de lu am la tua ma sinistra am vehement extraccio, e inscideys le cap del cap de la vergua del loc del perpucii am spatum agut, ayssi cum es inscizio de pluma, o que tu ne razas alcuna partida, per so que·l mieg de lu vengua semblant al cap de la vergua e que le trauc caia en le mieg loc segon que cove.	And the manner of the operation in this case is that the patient should be placed on their back, and accordingly stretch the head of the penis with your left hand with a vehement extraction, and incise the head of the head of the penis at the location of the perineum with a sharp spatula, just like when you make an incision with a feather, or that you remove some part, so that the middle of it resembles the head of the penis and the hole falls into the middle place according to what is necessary.
E guarda te que en la tua operacio de flux de sanc, quar motas vetz accideys aquo; e pausa te a lu am aquo que abscindeys le sanc, e cura la plagua entro que si’ sanada.	And beware that in your operation of blood flow, because often this happens; and pause at the place where you will incise the blood, and cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lvi.	Chapter LVI.
De albater le qual accideys en le prepucii en le cap de la vergua e de corropcio e negror e adherencia del prepucii del cap de la vergua.	Of the affliction which occurs in the foreskin of the penis and its corruption, blackness, and adhesion to the head of the penis.
Motas veguadas accideys aquest albater en la vergua e es eminencia de carn laga.	Many times this affliction occurs on the penis and is an excess of soft flesh.
E de aquela una es maligna e autra es no-maligna.	And one of them is malignant and the other is non-malignant.
No-maligna, cove que suspendas am unci subtil e abscindas aquela entro que aquela mondes tota; e aprop pausa sobre aquela coto submirgit en enguent egipciac; e aprop aquel, cura le am enguent diafinicon entro que sia sanat.	Non-malignant, requires that you suspend with a fine thread and incise it so that all the excess flesh is removed; and accordingly pause over the cut submerging it in Egyptian ointment; and accordingly cure it with diaphanous ointment until it is healed.
E si albater es maligna, de lega color, lahoras cove que tu aministres cauteri aprop la inscizio de lu e la razio de lu.	And if the affliction is malignant, of a bad color, then accordingly you must administer cauterization at the incision and the reason for it.
Mays si albater es en le prepuci del cap de la vergua no-circumcis, e la una partida de albater es dedintz le prepucii e l’autra partida es defora, lahoras cove que tu ostes albater le qual es dedintz al comensament entro que es consolidat; e lahora tu cura aquel deforo, quar quan tu curas aquel ensemps le prepuci, no es asegurat que no sia trinquat.	But if the affliction is in the foreskin of the uncircumcised penis and one part of it is inwardly towards the foreskin and the other part is outwardly, then accordingly you should remove the afflicted part that is inwardly towards the beginning until it is consolidated; and then you will cure that which is outside, for when you cure that simultaneously with the foreskin, there is no guarantee that it will not become tangled.
E ja eysamen accideys en les genetius e en le prepuci negror e corruccio, adonc cove que tu conquavas tot aquo que ja es denigrat e que ja se vol corrompre o que ja es corrumput; e aprop lineys sobre aquel aprop aquo am mel, le qual es contusit am farina de scorsa de milgrana e de errs trissatz e crivellatz.	And often it happens in the genitals and foreskin of blackness and corruption, therefore it is necessary that you scrape away all that which has already been denigrated and which already wants to corrupt or has already corrupted; and accordingly line that over with a mixture made with honey, which is mixed with flour of scoria of millet grain and with crushed and sifted errors.
E aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sana.	And accordingly cure that with another treatment until it is healed.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, lahoras aministra cauteri lunar segon aquesta forma:	But if there is an excessive flow of blood, then accordingly administer lunar cauterization in this form:
quar cauteri juvatiu es a dos disposicios ensemps, so es a flux de sanc e a la plagua quan es corrumpuda.	for cauterization is beneficial at two dispositions together, namely the flow of blood and the wound when it is corrupted.
E si le cap de la vergua es corrodut e es destruit tot en la hora, lahoras cove que tu intrometas en lo meat del prepucii una canula de plom per so que le malaute urina per aquela.	And if the head of the penis is corroded and destroyed completely in an instant, then accordingly it is necessary that you insert into the opening of the foreskin a leaden catheter so that the patient may urinate through it.
En la adherencia del prepucii am le cap de la vergua (et aquesta adherencia no accideys sino en aquel del qual le prepucii es sa, e sobre lu no es exhigida circumcizio; e quan accideys adherencia per plagua o per apostema) cove que excorjas am spatum obtus entro que sia dissolvut le liament e sia deliurat le cap de la vergua de tota partida.	In the adhesion of the foreskin to the head of the penis (and this adhesion only occurs in those whose foreskin is intact and has not been circumcised; and when adhesion occurs due to wound or abscess) it is necessary that you excise with an obtuse spatula until the bond is dissolved and the head of the penis is completely freed from all parts.
E si es dificil desirnir aquelas exquisidament, lahoras cove que tu excorjes am spatum alcuna causa del cap de la vergua e del prepucii, e aysso es quar le prepucii, quan es subtil, fort leu es perforat per la sua subtilitat leugierament.	And if it is difficult to excise those parts exactly, then accordingly you should excise with an instrument some cause at the head of the penis and foreskin, and thus it is because the foreskin, when it is subtle, can be easily perforated by its own subtlety slightly.
E aprop separa entre·l prepucii e·l cap de la vergua am dra7 de li subtil, le qual ja es mulhat en l’aygua frega per que no adherescan autra veguada.	And accordingly separate between the foreskin and the head of the penis with a thread of fine silk, which has already been moistened in water so that they will not adhere again.
E aprop sia curat am vi stiptic entro que sia consolidat.	And accordingly it should be treated with a strong medicine until it is consolidated.
Capitol .lvii.	Chapter LVII.
De mundificacio dels enfants e de la curacio de aquo que accideys ad aquels de circumcisio.	Of the purification of children and the cure of that which occurs to them due to circumcision.
Circumcisio no es solucio de continuitat ayssi cum las autras plaguas: mays empero cum sia de la nostra operacio e de nostra voluntat, e lus de aquela sia propriament en les enfants, es necessari que asignem en aquela milhor operacio e via pus leugiera perdusent a salut.	Circumcision is not a solution to continuity in the same way as other wounds: but rather it is of our operation and our will, and that which occurs in it is properly in children, it is necessary that we assign in it a better operation and path more easily leading to health.
Donc dic que les antics no diyssero circumcisio en alcu dels lors libres, quar no n’usan en las suas leys, e no es sino quar havem aquisit per speriment, la qual causa es que yeu he atrobat la major partida dels artifexs e dels barbies usar circumcisir e mundificacio am novacula e am torores; e usan de liament am fiel e de inscizio am la ungla.	Therefore I say that the ancients did not write about circumcision in any of their books, because they did not use it in their laws, and it is only because we have acquired through experience, which is why many artists and barbers have found out to circumcise and purify with a razor and with torments; and they use ligatures with thread and incisions with the nail.
E yeu ja he prohadas totas aquestas manieras e no atrobegui milhor mondificacio am forfexs, am liament am fiel que en mondificacio cum la ungla, quar motas vetz efugeys la codena pus desus, quar la codena del prepucii a dos tunicas, e roman la tonica pus dejos, e fort leu es forsat ad autra inscizio e dolor sicura.	And you have already condemned all these methods and did not find better purification with razors, with ligatures with thread that in purification like the nail, because many times you have escaped the cord above, because the foreskin has two tunics, and the lower tone remains below, and it is soon forced to another incision and sure pain.
E am mundificacio le qual es fayta per alphecati, e es digital, del qual usan les sabatiers, no es segurada la inscizio de la extremitat del membre viril, quar fort leu intra en le trau de lu.	And the purification which is made by alalfa, and is delicate, of which barbers use, is not guaranteed to be a secure incision at the extremity of the male member, because it soon enters into the wound itself.
Mays en la operacio am ungla, fort leu obazeys ferr e corromp la tua operacio.	But in the operation with nail, iron soon obstructs and corrupts your operation.
E la codena del enfant es breu per natura, e motas veguadas nays en tal manieyra que no ha necessitat de mondificacio, e yeu he vist aquel.	And the cord of the child is short by nature, and many times they are so made that they do not need purification, and I have seen those.
Mays de la mondificacio que·s fa am forfexs e liamentz am fiel, la bontat, experiment descrobic a mi, quar las forfexs so de proporcional inscizio, per aquo quar la acuitat que es desus es ayssi cum la acuitat que es dejos; e donc cum tu premes la tua ma so proporcionadas dos acuitatz, e inscideysso segon una comperacio en un temps; e es fayta compressio del fiel am figura contenent la codena de la vergua de tota partida, am le qual no catz error de tot.	But from the purification that is made with razors and ligatures with thread, I have discovered by experience that there is a flaw, because the razors are of proportional incision, therefore the acuity above is as much as the acuity below; and thus when you press your hand so proportionally on two acuities, and inscribe them according to one measurement in time; and it is made compression of the thread with a figure containing the cord of the penis from all parts, with which there is no error at all.
E la manieyra de la operacio primeyra es que tu fassas estar le enfant majorment si es de aquels que entendo un petit, que no fassas sino que tu lies le fiel en la sua vergua tant solament, e que leysses aquel entro al autra dia.	And the manner of the first operation is that you should make the child lie down as much as possible if it is one of those who understand a little, and not make anything except to tie the thread in its penis so only, and let it be for another day.
E aprop fay aquel alegrar en tota aquela manieyra que es a tu possibla de aquo que recep la sua intelligencia.	And accordingly make that child happy in all that manner which is possible to you according to the intelligence it receives.
E aprop fa aquel estar entre las tuas mas estatuir preparadament, e no sia ges cezent; e occulta las forfexs en la tua ma o dejos le tieu pe, que l’enfant no veia aquelas ni degun autre dels instruments.	And accordingly make that child be between your arms most carefully prepared, and not at all anxious; and conceal the razors in your hand or leave them behind so that the child does not see those nor anyone else of the instruments.
E aprop entremet la tua ma a la vergua de lu e suffla en la codena, e tira aquela entro que sia eyssit le cap de la vergua, e aprop mondifica aquel de aquo que es agregat en ela de sordicia.	And accordingly insert your hand into the penis of him and blow into the cord, and pull that in until it is out at the head of the penis, and accordingly purify that which is accumulated therefrom, from sordid things.
E aprop lia le loc signat am fiel dobla, e aprop ligua pus bas de aquel un petit le segon liament, e aprop te am le dit pous e endic tieu le loc del liament dejos am bona retencio, e inscideys entre dos liaments.	And accordingly tie the marked place with double thread, and accordingly ligate lower down on that a little bit, and accordingly bind it with the said thread, leaving the location of the ligature below with good retention, and inscribe between two ligatures.
E aprop eleva la codena sus leugierament e estratz le cap de la vergua; e aprop leyssa le sanc corre petit e petit, quar es milhor ; e pausa polvera desus e sobre la polvera pausa drap en le qual es spandut mugol de huou coyt en ayguaros concosit am oli rozat recent bo; e layssa aquel sobre aquel entro al autra dia; e cura aquel am curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly lift the cord slightly and extract the head of the penis; and accordingly let the blood flow little by little, for it is better; and pause powder above and on top of the powder, pause a cloth in which is spread a mixture of honey cooked with water and rose oil recently boiled; and lay that over it until the next day; and cure that with treatment until it is healed.
La forma de las forfexs a mondificacio, aquesta es la forma:	The form of the razors for purification, this is the form:
Sian las unas extramitatz no-talhantz e las autras sian talhant, que non sia yssit le ram del clau, e sia la longitut de las doas acuitatz ayssi cum la longitut de dos manubres engualment.	Be the extra tips not cutting and the others cutting, so that the ram of the key is not left, and the length of both edges be as much as the length of two equal hands.
Mays la error en mundificacio es quar fort leu efugeys la codena intrinseca tota, o partida de lu deves la inscizio.	But the error in purification is that soon you flee the internal cord entirely, or a part of it becomes detached from the incision.
Donc cove que tu extendas aquela de la tua hora am la tua ungla denant la apostemacio del loc e que inscidas aquela segon equalitat.	Therefore, it is necessary that you stretch that of your hour with your nail in front of the apostema of the location and incise according to equality.
E si no la podes tenir am la tua ungla, lahoras extratz aquela am unci e inscideys aquela.	And if you cannot hold it with your nail, then accordingly extract that with a thread and incise it.
Mays si son passatz tres dias, e roman aquo que es imflat dejos la vergua apostemat, lahoras tu leyssa aquo entro que sia cedat le apostema caut, e excorja aquel am fecilitat, e inscidex aquel segon que a tu es preparat.	But if three days have passed and that which is inflamed below the penis has not subsided, then accordingly you should let it be until the apostema becomes calm, and excise that with facility, and incise that according to what is prepared for you.
E guarda te del cap de la vergua, quar no nosera a lu aquo.	And beware of the head of the penis, because it will not be at ease with this.
E donc cura aquel am aquo que la plagua consolida de las polveras las quals havem recomtadas en le tractat de las polveras.	And accordingly cure that with the powder which consolidates wounds, as we have recounted in the treatise on powders.
E si es inscidit de la codena sobre mesura, e obezeys a las partidas desus, aquo no notz a lu.	And if it is incised with the cord according to measure, and obeys the parts above, then this will not be noticed by him.
E mays cura aquel am aquo que havem dit entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly cure that with what we have said until it is healed.
Capitol .lviii.	Chapter LVIII.
De curacio de urina retenguda en la vesiqua.	Of the cure of retained urine in the bladder.
Retencio de urina en la vesica es fayta per oppulacio fayta per peyra o per sanc congilat, o per poyre o per carnada, e semblantz ad aquels de aquo que havem dit de las manieyras de curacio en la divisio.	Retention of urine in the bladder is caused by oppression made by pain or by blood congested, or by a poultice or by flesh, and resembles those things that we have said about the ways of cure in the division.
E si no es dissolvuda la urina, e veses retencio de lu esser per peyra le qual ja es en le col de la vesica, lahoras cove que le malaute sia encorbat sobre les sieus denolhs.	And if the urine is not dissolved and retention of it is seen to be caused by pain which is already in the neck of the bladder, then accordingly the patient should be supported on his own pillows.
E aprop conponeys les pes de aquel sobre le sieu dos e extendas le sieu ventre de la partida pus desus del sieu dos, e le malaute estrengua le sieu ale tant quant es a lu possible.	And accordingly place the weights of that on his own back and stretch his belly from the part above his back, and the patient should strain his arm as much as is possible to him.
Donc lahoras le col de la vesica es costreyt ha espulsio de la peyra a las partidas detras, per que la urina es absolta.	Therefore, accordingly the neck of the bladder is strained to expulsion of the pain in the parts behind, so that the urine may be evacuated.
E si no es dissolvuda am aquo que havem dit he vehement es fayta la causa sobre le malaute, lahoras cove que aministres extraccio de lu am instrument le qual es apelat siringua, del qual aquesta es la forma: Sia de argent e sia subtil leon conquau, ayssi cum canula de pena de ausel am subtilitat de ray lonc en similitut d’un palm e mig, al qual sia cana subtil en le cap de lu.	And if it is not dissolved with what we have said, then the cause of the disease is violent and requires a strong treatment, accordingly it is necessary to administer an extraction from him with an instrument which is called syringe, the form of which is as follows: It should be made of silver and very fine thread, like a needle with a subtle tip in the shape of a palm and a half, with a thin cane at its head.
E la manieyra del eyssiment de la urina per aquel es que prenguas le fiel doblat e lies en la extramitat de lu lana o coto per bona liadura; e entrometas las extramitatz del fiel en la partida dejos de la ciringua, e inscideys am las forfexs si superflueys alcuna causa de la lana, mays intromet la en la canula am vehemencia E aprop enongeys la ciringua am boder e am album de huou.	And the manner of extracting urine with this is that you take double thread and tie it in the extremity of the thread or cloth for good binding; and insert the extremities of the thread into the part below the ring, and inscribe with razors if there is any superfluous cause of the thread, but insert it into the needle with vehemence And accordingly, fill the ring with border and album of honey.
E fay cezer le malaute sobre la selha, e embroca la vesiqua de lu e la vergua am olis umitz, e oli de oliva e ayguaros.	And make the patient sit on a stool, and envelop the bladder of him with warm oil, olive oil, and honey.
E aprop entromet la ciringua am facilitat entro que pervengua a la razit de la vergua; e aprop dobla la vergua desus a la partida del embelic; e aprop empelleys la ciringua dintz aquela; e aprop empelleys aquela entro que pervengua a la vesica, e aquela centa le malaute esser pervenguda a la causa vuoda, e no es fayt asso segon aquest orde, sino le meat en le qual va a tortuositat.	And accordingly insert the ring with facility until it reaches the root of the penis; and accordingly double the penis above to the part of the belly; and accordingly push the ring into that part; and accordingly push that part into the bladder, so that the patient is brought to the desired cure, and not made in the same way as this order, but rather in a manner that goes against tortuosity.
E aprop exten le fiel am la lana petit a petit, quar la urina siec la lana.	And accordingly stretch the thread with the cloth little by little, because the urine is eating away at the cloth.
Aprop extratz aquela e fay per curacio urina, e usa ciringua, no cesses fer aquo e usa ciringua entro que sia evacuada la vesica e le malaute atrobe alleviacio.	And accordingly extract that and make it for urine cure, and use the ring, do not stop doing this and use the ring until the bladder is evacuated and the patient receives relief.
Capitol .lix.	Chapter LIX.
De qualitat de clisterizacio de la vezica am clampcedra e am semblantz instrumentz les quals sian acordants ad aquo.	Of the quality of catharticization of the bladder with clysteredra and similar instruments which are in accord with that.
Quan accideys en la vesica ulceracio o apostema, o sanc congilat en aquela, o es coartat poyredura, e vols en aquela destillar ayguas e medicinas, lahoras sia fayt am instrument le qual es apelat clampcedra, e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When ulceration or apostema occurs in the bladder, or blood is congested in it, or the skin is constricted with poultice, and you want to make it distill waters and medicines in that place, then accordingly it should be done with an instrument which is called clampcedra, and this is its form:
sino que en la extramitat de lu es sorda, so es clausa.	except that at the extremity of it is deaf, so it is closed.
Et en aquela so tres traucs: dos de la una partida , ayssi quo vezes.	And in that there are three holes: two from one side, like so many times.
En le comensament es loc concau, en le qual es aquo que es enpellit, e sia segon quantitat que oppile aquel, ses addicio, entro que quan alcuna causa es ab aquel tirada de las humiditatz, sia atirada, e quan es expellida, am aquo sia atirada, e quan es expellit lonc, segon que fa clampcedra am la qual es phicat naphta en las batalhas de mar.	In the beginning it is a concave space, in which is poured water that fills it up to the quantity needed, plus addition, until when any cause is drawn out of the humidities with it, and then it is drawn back, and when it is expelled long, according to how clampcedra acts, as is written naphta in the battles of the sea.
Donc cum tu vols prohicir humiditatz en la vesica, entromet la extremitat de clapcedra en la humiditat, e atira am aquel aquo que es empellit a las partidas desus, quar la humiditat es atirada en la conquavitat de clapcedra.	Therefore, when you want to extract humidities from the bladder, insert the extremity of clampcedra into the humidity, and draw out with it the water that is poured into the parts above, because the humidity is drawn into the concavity of clampcedra.
E aprop entromet la extramitat de clapcedra en la vergua segon que havem recomtat en la ciringua; e aprop empelleys la humiditat am aquo que empelleys, quar aquela humiditat perve a la vesica tantost, e le malaute cent aquela.	And accordingly insert the extremity of clampcedra into the penis according to what we have recounted in the ciringua; and accordingly pour out the humidity with water that pours it out, because that humidity comes to the bladder shortly, and the patient is cured thereby.
Forma del cristeri subtil am le qual la vesica es cristerizada, e es aquela la forma:	The form of the subtle clyster which is used to catheterize the bladder, and this is its form:
E sia fayta de argent o de lato, de la qual le cap pus aut sia semblant a petita pluma, e dejos lu cana dedintz liament.	And it should be made of silver or lead, with the head being like a small feather, and below it a thin cane attached.
E aprop pren vesica de moto, e pausa en aquela la humiditat que vols cristirizar en la vesica, e aprop lia aquela entre dos am fort liguatura am fiel doble, e escalfa aquela humiditat sobre le foc.	And accordingly take the bladder of a moving animal, and pause in it the humidity that you want to catheterize in the bladder, and accordingly tie it between two with a strong binding made of double thread, and heat that humidity over the fire.
E aprop entromet la extremitat del cristeri en la vergua.	And accordingly insert the extremity of the clyster into the penis.
E aprop estrenh la tua ma sobre la vesica am la humiditat am strectura descent entro que·l malaute centa que aquela humiditat ja es pervenguda a la vesica.	And accordingly press your hand upon the bladder with the humidity, stretching downwards until the patient feels that that humidity has reached the bladder.
Mays si a tu no es present vesica, lahoras tu pren una pessa de parguames e fay de aquel cercle; e perfora aquel de tota la sua retonditat; e aprop entromet fiel fort en aquels traucs, ayssi quo so revolgut; e aprop agregua le cercle ayssi quo es agreguat alsofatur, pus que tu pausas en aquel aquo que tu vols de las humiditatz, e olis e ayguas.	But if you do not have the bladder present, then accordingly take a bag of parchment and make from it a circle; and perforate that entirely around its circumference; and accordingly insert a strong thread into those holes, turning them over; and accordingly add the circle just as it is added also in such a way that you pause on that which you want from the humidities, and oils and waters.
E aprop tu lia aquel en le instrument e fay am aquel ayssi cum has fayt am la vesica, e exprescio am la tua ma entro que la humiditat pervengua a la vesica.	And accordingly you tie that in the instrument and make it as you made for the bladder, and express with your hand until the humidity reaches the bladder.
Capitol .lx.	Chapter LX.
De extraccio de peyra.	Of the Extraction of Pain.
Nos ja havem dit en la divisio las specias de peyra e curacio de lu am medicinas, e la diferencia entre peyra engendrada en los ronhos e peyra engendrada en la vesica, e les senhals de aquela.	We have already said in the division the species of pain and cure of it with medicines, and the difference between pain generated in the lungs and pain generated in the bladder, and the signs of that.
E havem dit la peyra en la qual catz operacio am ma, e seccio.	And we have said the pain in which catches operation with hand and section.
E la peyra engendrada en la vesica propriament es aquela que es ficada en la vesica.	And the pain generated in the bladder properly is that which is placed in the bladder.
E yeu so narrant aquel am exposicio manifesta e abreviacio.	And you will narrate that with manifest exposition and abbreviation.
Donc dic que peyra engendrada en la vesica majorment ve als enfantz; e dels senhals de lu es que la urina que es eyssida de la vesica es semblant a aygua en la sua subtilitat, e apar en aquela arena; e le malaute fregua la sua vergua, e motas veguadas pen, e aprop es dressada; e am aquo yeys foro le cul en motz de aquels.	So I say that the pain generated in the bladder mostly appears to children; and among its signs is that the urine which flows from the bladder is like water in its subtlety, and appears in that sand; and the patient frequently rubs his penis, and many times takes a step back, and accordingly it is dressed; and with this you will find the anus in the shape of those.
E es laugiera la sanacio dels enfants de aquela entro que han conseguitz xiiii ans; e es dificil curacio en les viels.	And it is more difficult to cure children of that until they have reached the age of 14 years; and it is a hard cure in old people.
Mays en les joves es migiera per aquo quar es entre aquels.	But in young people it is easier because it is between those.
E de aquel del qual la peyra es major e la curacio es pus leugiera; E si es pauca, es contraria ad aquela.	And from that of which the pain is greater and the cure is lighter; And if it is little, it is contrary to that.
Donc cum pervenem a la curacio de aquela, cove al comensament de aquela que mondifiquem le malaute am cristeri le qual extragua tota la fenda la qual es en les sieus budels; quar aquela fenda alcunas veguadas prohibeys la envencio de la peyra deves la inquisicio de lu.	So, when we come to the cure of that, it is necessary at the beginning to purify the patient with a clyster which extracts all the fissure that is in his intestines; for that fissure sometimes prevents the evacuation of the pain from its inquiry.
E aprop sia pres le malaute am les sieus pes e sia contosit e maugut enjos per so que la peyra descenda al preon de la vesica, o que saute de loc aut alcunas veguadas.	And accordingly be pressed the patient with his own weights and be constricted and narrowed in his joints so that the pain descends to the root of the bladder, or jumps from one place to another occasionally.
E aprop fay aquel cezer entre las tuas mas preparat, e las mas de lu sian dejos las coysas de lu, per so que la vesica tota sia fayta declinant a las partidas dejos.	And accordingly make that patient sit between your most prepared hands and those of him be left the things of his, so that the bladder is made to decline entirely to the parts below.
E aprop perquier aquela e tota aquela deforo.	And accordingly cover all that with a covering.
Donc si sentes la peyra en l’espazi, lahoras tu te coyta tantost am seccio sobre lu.	So, if you feel the pain in space, then immediately cut yourself off from it with section upon it.
E si no catz de tot dejos le tieu tocament, lahoras cove que tu untes am oli le tieu dit indic de la ma sinistra, si malaute es enfant, o le dit miga si es jove complit, e entrometas aquel en le sieu cul.	And if you do not feel completely the pressure of your touch, then it is necessary that you anoint with oil the indicated spot on your left hand, if the patient is a child, or the middle spot if he is a young adult, and insert that into his anus.
E perquier de la peyra entro que stia dejos le tieu dit.	And cover with oil of the pain until it remains below your said spot.
E converteys aquela petit a petit entro al col de la vesica.	And convert that little by little into the neck of the bladder.
E aprop prem sobre aquel am lo tieu dit, e expelleys aquel a las partidas defora ves le loc del qual vos la seccio.	And accordingly press upon that with your said spot, and expel it into the parts outside of the bladder at the location from which you made the section.
E comanda al ministra que prema la vesica am la sua ma; e comanda a un autra ministra que am la sua ma dextra extenda les genetius a las partidas desus, e am la sua autra ma remaugua la codena la qual es dejos les genetius, en partida del loc en le qual se fa la seccio.	And command the servant to press the bladder with his right hand; and command another servant to stretch out her left arm towards the parts above, and with her other arm to relax the cord which is below the genitals, in the part of the location where the section is being made.
E aprop entromet espatum be inscident del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And accordingly insert an spatula which is incident, and this is its form:
e scindeys en lu aquo que es entre·l cul e·ls genetius, no en le mieg loc, abantz al latz de la coyssa sinistra; e sia la seccio sobre aquela peyra e·l tieu dit sia en le cul, e sia fayta seccio transversa, per que la seccio defora sia ampla e dedintz streyta segon la quantitat que egrecio de la peyra sia a lu possibla, e no major, quar fort leu comprem le tieu dit le qual es en le cul la peyra deves la seccio, e es foro-getada ses defacultat.	and cut through the flesh between the anus and genitals, not in the middle location, but above the left flank; and let the section be upon that pain and your said spot be on the anus, and let it be a transverse section, so that the section outside is wide and thin below according to the quantity of pain that has been evacuated, and no greater, for then little by little the flesh will compress your said spot which is in the anus, and forgets its defect.
E sapias que de la peyra es alcuna a la qual so angle e margers, per que le eyssiment de lu es fayt deficil per aquo.	And know that of the pain is some which has an angle and corners, for which the evacuation of it is made difficult by this.
E de aquela aquo es leon semblant a glan, e es redonda, e es fayt de lu leugier eyssiment.	And from that pain, there appears a node similar to a gland, and it is rounded, and it makes the evacuation of it lighter.
Donc si es aquela al qual so angles e marger, ajusta en la fissura.	So, if it is that which has angles and corners, adjust it in the fissure.
E si no es ayssi foro-getada, lahoras cove que tu engenes sobre aquel, o que strenguas sobre aquel am gesti decentment, la extremitat del qual sia ayssi cum lima am le qual strenguas sobre la peyra, e no evasesca de lu; o que entrometas dejos lu instrument subtil de curvada extremitat.	And if it is not so forgotten, then accordingly you must gently press upon that, or strengthen upon that with decent gestures, the extremity of which should be as a file on which you would strengthen upon the pain, and not escape from it; or that you would insert below it a subtle instrument of curved extremity.
Mays si tu no podes sobre aquel, lahoras tu amplifica le trauc un petit, e si tu veus flux de sanc, abscindeys en strenh aquel am vitriol trissat.	But if you cannot press upon that, then accordingly you must amplify the hole a little, and if you see a flow of blood, cut it off with strength using a vitriolated thread.
Mays si la peyra es mays de una, lahoras al comensament tu impelleys la ma a la boca de la vesica, e aprop inscideys sobre lu; e aprop impelleys un petit aprop aquo; e semblantment fay si son motas mays de doas.	But if the pain is more than one, then at the beginning you will push your hand to the mouth of the bladder, and accordingly inscribe upon it; and accordingly push a little further on; and similarly do so if there are many more than two.
E si es peyra mot gran, lahoras ignorancia es que tu inscidas aquel am gran seccio, quar accideys al malaute una de doas causas: o que mora o que endevengua a lu destillacio de urina continuabla, per aquo quar le loc no es de tot consolidat.	And if it is great pain, then ignorance is that you inscribe upon it with great section, for it happens to the patient one of two causes: either he dies or endures the continuous evaporation of urine, because of which the location is not entirely consolidated.
Mays aministra expulcio de lu entro que sia fora-getada, o engenia en la fractura de lu am las forfexs entro que extragua aquela en pessas.	But administer expulsion from there until it is forgotten, or engineer in the fracture of it with razors until that comes out in pieces.
Donc cum tu auras cumplit la tua opperacio, lahoras omple la plagua de enses de aloe e de sanc de drago, e strenh aquel.	So, when you have completed your operation, then accordingly fill the wound with the juice of aloe and the blood of dragon, and strengthen that.
E pausa sobre aquel drap enfus en oli e vi, o en oli rozat e aygua frega, per so que apostema caut sia cedat.	And pause upon that cloth dipped in oil and vinegar, or in rough oil and cold water, so that the apostema may be cooled.
E aprop resupina le malaute sobre le sieu col, e no deslias le liament entro al tertz dia.	And accordingly repose the patient on his own pillow, and do not loosen the bond for three days.
E cum aquel auras desliat, embroca le loc am aygua e mot oli, e aprop cura aquel am enguent diafinicon e am enguent diabazilicon entro que sia sanat.	And when that has been loosened, envelop the location with water and hot oil, and accordingly cure it with divine ointment and devilish ointment until it is healed.
Mays si en la plagua accideys apostema caut, adhust e corrosiu, e de aquel semblantz ayssi cum si le sanc es en la vesica congelat, e per lu es la hurina prohibida (e aquo es conogut per la egressio del sanc am urina), a donc entromet lo tieu dit en la plagua e extratz aquel sanc, quar si roman provoca la vesica a corropcio de la vesica e de lu putrefaccio.	But if in the wound there occurs an apostema that is cautious, adjusted and corrosive, and from it appears as if the blood is frozen in the bladder, and because of this the urine is prohibited (and this is known by the excretion of blood with urine), then accordingly insert your said spot into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will provoke the bladder to corruption of the bladder and putrefaction.
E aprop lava la plagua am vi agre, aygua e sal, e am opposicio a tota specia, am aquo que conveneys a lu de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly wash the wound with vinegar, water and salt, and with opposition to all species, as is necessary for the cure, until it is healed.
E cove en las horas de tota la curacio que tu lies amdos las coyssas e ajustes las medicinas las quals so pausadas sobre le loc.	And accordingly note in all the hours of the entire cure that you have laid and adjusted the medicines which are paused upon the location.
E si la peyra es petita e es en le meat de la vergua, e es ficat en lu, e eyssement de urina es prohibit, lahoras cura aquel am aquo que yeu recomti denant que pervenguas a seccio, quar tropas veguadas per aquesta curacio yest acusat de seccio; e ja yeu e esproat aquo, e es que tu prenguas un perforador de ferr alfelut, del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And if the pain is small and is in the head of the penis, and is stuck there, and the emission of urine is prohibited, then accordingly cure that with what I have recommended before you come to the section, for too many times by this cure you are accused of section; and now I have already tried this, and it is that you take a perforator of iron like an alfalfa, the form of which is as follows:
de triangulada extramitat, agut, ficat en fust.	of triangular extremity, pointed, fixed in a wooden handle.
E aprop pren fiel, e lia am aquel la vergua dejos la peyra per so que no retorne a la vesica.	And accordingly take a thread, and tie it around the penis below the pain so that it does not return to the bladder.
E aprop entromet le ferr en la vergua, perforant am fecilitat entro que·l perforador vengua ad aquela peyra.	And accordingly insert the iron into the penis, perforating with facility until the perforator comes to that pain.
E revolveys le perforador am la tua ma en aquela peyra petit a petit, e tu perforsa la perforacio de lu entro que fassas aquel del autra part penetrar; quar la urina tantost es absolta.	And accordingly revolve the perforator with your hand in that pain little by little, and you perforate the perforation of it until you make that from the other side penetrate; for the urine is soon abolished.
E aprop prem la tua ma sobre aquo que es romas de la peyra de la partida deforo de la vergua, quar aquela es trinquada, e es foro-getada am la urina, e le malaute es sanat.	And accordingly press your hand upon that which is remaining of the pain from the departure outside of the penis, because it is torn, and it is forgotten with the urine, and the patient is healed.
Mays si aquesta curacio no es a tu aparelhada per alcuna causa la qual prohibeys de aquela, lahoras lia un fiel dejos la peyra, e autra fiel desus la peyra.	But if this cure is not adapted to your equipment for any reason which prohibits it, then accordingly tie a thread below the pain, and another thread above the pain.
E aprop encideys sobre la peyra en aquela vergua entre doas liaduras.	And accordingly inscribe upon the pain in that penis between two ligatures.
E aprop extratz aquela.	And accordingly extract that.
E aprop deslia le liament e mondifica le sanc congilat, le qual es fayt en la plagua.	And accordingly loosen the bond and purify the congealed blood which is formed in the wound.
E no es necessari liament de fiel dejos la peyra, sino per que no retorne a la vesica, e l’autre liament desus sino, quar quan es desliat le fiel aprop la egrecio de la peyra, la codena retorna a son loc e cobra la plagua.	And it is not necessary to tie the thread below the pain, but only so that it does not return to the bladder, and the other thread above, only because when the thread is loosened and approaches the evacuation of the pain, the cord returns to its place and closes the wound.
E per aquo es a tu necessari quan lias le fiel desus, que tu eleves la codena a las partidas desus, o que retorne deves le tieu compliment, e cobra la plagua ayssi co havem dit.	And therefore it is necessary for you when you tie the thread above, that you raise the cord to the parts above, or that you complete your said action, and close the wound as we have said.
Capitol .lxi.	Chapter LXI.
De extraccio de peyra de las femnas.	Of the Extraction of Pain from Women.
Peyra en las femnas pauc es engendrada.	Pain in women is rarely generated.
Mays si ve peyra ad alcuna de aquelas, lahoras dificil es la curacio de lu, e es prohibida per tropas manieyras.	But if there is pain in some of those (women), then it is difficult to cure it, and it is prohibited by many ways.
La una de lor es quar la femna fort leu es verges.	One of them is that the woman is too proud.
E la segonda es quar tu no trobas femna be scient que descroba si meteyssa al metge quan es casta, o es de las femnas haventz maritz.	And the second one is that you do not find a woman well instructed that can recognize if she has been touched by a doctor when she is chaste, or is of women without husbands.
La tersa es quar tu no hatrobas femna be sabent aquesta art, majorment la operacio am ma.	The third one is that you do not find a woman who knows this art, especially the operation with hand.
E la quarta es que·l loc de la seccio sobre peyra en las femnas es longinc del loc de la peyra, per que indigeys de seccio preonda, e en aquela es temor.	And the fourth one is that the location of the section on pain in women is too far from the location of the pain, so you need a deep section, and there is fear.
Mays si necessitat provoca a tu ad aquo, lahoras cove que tu prenguas una femna metga be scient, e pauc es atrobada.	But if necessity prompts you to this, then accordingly take a woman who is well instructed, and not easily startled.
Mays si tu es privat de aquela, lahoras cerca metga quast e subtil, o presenta una femna matrona be esenhada en le feyt de las femnas, o femna que en aquesta art ennueys partida del art.	But if you are deprived of that, then accordingly seek out one who is quiet and subtle, or present a matronal woman well experienced in the nature of women, or a woman who has parted from this art.
Donc fay aquela present, e comanda a lu que fassa tot aquo que tu li mandaras, de la enquisicio sobre la peyra al comensament; la qual causa es que reguarde si la femna es verges, lahoras cove que meta lo sieu dit en le cul de lu e quiera la peyra.	So make her present and command him to do everything that you will tell him, from the inquiry about the pain to the beginning; which cause is that he looks if the woman is chaste, then accordingly put his said thing into her anus and ask for the pain.
Donc si atroba aquela, coarte aquela dejos le sieu dit, e lahoras comanda a lu que inscida sobre aquela.	So if you find that, cut it below his said thing, and then command him to inscribe upon it.
Mays si no es verge, lahoras comanda a la matrona que entrometa lo sieu dit en le conh de la malauta e enquiera sobre la peyra, pus que pausa la sua ma sinistra sobre la vesica, e comprem aquela am bona comprecio.	But if she is not chaste, then command the matron to insert his said thing into the anus of the patient and inquire about the pain, since he places his left hand on the bladder, and compresses it with a good compression.
Donc si atroba aquela, lahoras cove que gradantment maugua aquela de l’orrifici de la vesica a las partidas dejos am somman de la sua vertut entro que pervengua am aquel a la razit de la coyssa.	So if you find that, then accordingly gradually relax it from the orifice of the bladder to the parts below with the sum of its virtue until it reaches the root of the canal.
E aprop inscida sobre aquela apposicio de la maytat del conh deves la razit de la coyssa de qualque part sia a lu parada e cent la peyra en aquela partida, e·l dit de lu no sia remaugut de la peyra coartan dejos lu.	And accordingly inscribe upon it the opposition of the middle of the anus to the root of the canal from which some part is brought to an end and centred in that part, and his said thing is not relaxed from the pain cut below.
E la seccio sia pauca al comensament; e aprop entrometa lo ray sobre aquela seccio, e si sent la peyra, lahoras ajuste en seccio segon la quantitat la qual sap que la peyra sira getada de aquela.	And the section should be small at first; and accordingly insert the ray upon that section, and if you feel the pain, then adjust in section according to the quantity which you know will cause the pain to be removed from there.
E sapias que las specias de peyra son motas: quar de aquelas es pauca e gran, e leon e aspra, e longua e redonda, e havent ramps.	And know that the types of pain are many: for some are small and great, and sharp and rough, and long and rounded, and with nodules.
Donc tu sapias quantas specias so de lu per aquo que tu signifiques sobre aquo que vols.	So you know how many species there are of that for which you signify upon that which you will.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, ajusta en le loc vetriol trissat e te aquela per una hora entro que sia abscindit le sanc, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio entro que la peyra sia fora-getada.	And if you see a flow of blood, adjust to the location with vitriol thread and tie it there for an hour until the blood is cut off, and then return to your operation so that the pain is forgotten.
E fay que prepares am tu dels instrumentz les quals e ditz en la extraccio de peyra en les homes, per so que sias ajudat per aquels en la tua operacio.	And make sure you prepare with your own the instruments which are said in the extraction of pain in men, for so that you may be helped by them in your operation.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, e sabes que la expulcio del sanc es de la arceria que es insciza, lahoras tu pausa polvera sobre le loc e estrenh aquel am pulvils e strictura descent, e no iteras aquo; e layssa la peyra e no extraguas aquela, quar fort leu morira la malauta.	And if you see a flow of blood, and know that the expulsion of blood is from the wound that is inscribed, then you pause powder on the location and strengthen it with powder and strict descent, and do not iterate this; and leave the pain and do not extract it, for very soon the patient will die.
E aprop cura la plagua.	And accordingly cure the wound.
Donc cum es cedada la acuitat del sanc aprop alcus jorns, e·l loc se poyreys, lahoras tu retorna a la tua operacio entro que la peyra sia fora-getada.	And then when the sharpness of the blood has ceased after some days, and the location is healed, accordingly you return to your operation so that the pain is forgotten.
Capitol lxii.	Chapter LXII.
De seccio sobre ernia acoza.	Of the Section on Hernia Acuta.
Hernia ayguoza no es sino agregacio de humiditat en le ciphac blanc lo qual es dejos la codena dels genetius contenent le huou, e es nompnat ciphac.	Hernia aquosa is nothing but an aggregation of moisture in the white pouch which is below the cord of the genitals containing the fluid, and it is called a pouch.
E alcunas veguadas es en le propri pannicol le qual a lu preparec natura en la partida del huou, entro que sia cuyat que ja es autre huou; e es la codena del genetiu entre le ciphac blanc le qual havem dit, e no es aquo sino tart.	And sometimes it is in the proper sac which nature has prepared for it in the part of the fluid, until another fluid is born; and it is the cord of the genitals between the white pouch which we have said, and it is not this but rather a tumor.
E la generacio de aquest hernia es per debelitat la qual accideys als genetius, per que ad aquels es efundunda aquesta materia, e alcunas vetz accideys per percuscio fayta sobre les genetius.	And the generation of this hernia is due to debility which occurs in the genitals, for it flows into them this material, and sometimes it happens through a blow made on the genitals.
E aquesta humiditat es havent motas colors, quar la color de lu o es declinant a citrina o a sanguinent, o rog, o es negra feculenta, o es ayguosa blanqua, e es aquo que es mays.	And this humidity has many colors, for the color of it either declines to citrine or blood-red, or red, or is blackish-feculent, or white as water, and it is this which is most.
E les senhals per les quals es saubut on es aquesta agreguacio de aygua so aquestz: quar si es en le ciphac blanc le qual havem dit, lahoras le apostema es redon declinant un pauc a longitut ayssi cum figura de huou, e appar le genetiu, quar la humiditat conte aquel de tota part.	And the signs by which it is known where this accumulation of water is are these: for if it is in the white pouch which we have said, then the apostema is rounded and declining a little towards length, thus like the figure of a fluid, and appears the genitals, because the humidity contains that from all part.
E si la humiditat es en le propri pannicol, lahoras le apostema es redon am partida del huou e per aysso hom estima que es autre huou.	And if the humidity is in the proper sac, then the apostema is rounded with the part of the fluid and therefore one estimates that it is another fluid.
E si la humiditat es entre la codena dels genetius e·l ciphac blanc, lahoras catz dejos le centiment.	And if the humidity is between the cord of the genitals and the white pouch, then cats are born below the sensation.
E cum tu vols la cognicio de la color de la humiditat, lahoras tu esproa la color de la humiditat en le apostema am entromes cayrat del qual la forma es precedida; e segon aquo que es eyssit en le vestigi del entromes, jutga de aquo que es dedintz lu.	And when you want to know the nature of the color of the humidity, then accordingly you test the color of the humidity in the apostema with entromes which precede its form; and according to what is found in the vestige of the entromes, judge from that what is below it.
Donc quan nos vinem a la curacio de lu am ferr, lahoras cove que comandem al malaute que sia fleubotomat si aquo es a tu possibla, e vezes le cos de lu ple.	And then when we come to the cure of it with iron, accordingly command the patient to be flaccid if this is possible for you, and sometimes let his body please.
E aprop sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos sobre alcuna causa un pauc auta, e pausa dejos lu motz draps.	And accordingly it should be raised on the patient's back for some reason a little above, and pause below him many cloths.
E aprop setz tu sobre la part sinistra de lu, e comanda al ministra que segua a la dextra de lu, le qual extenda la sua vergua a hun de dos latz a la codena dels genetius e a la partida del mirac del ventre.	And accordingly set yourself on the left side of him, and command the servant to follow on the right side of him, which stretches his arm to one of two sides to the cord of the genitals and to the part of the miracle of the belly.
E aprop pren spatum lat e scindeys la codena dels genetius del mieg loc per la longitut entro prop le pentenilh.	And accordingly take a spatula and cut the cord of the genitals from the middle location by its length to the proximity of the pubic hairs.
E sia fayta la seccio segon rectetut engualment distant de la linha que deveseys la pel dels genetius, entro que pervengua al ciphac blanc comprehendent.	And the section should be made according to right proportion, equally distant from the line that you must draw on the skin of the genitals, until it reaches the white pouch including.
E excorja aquel, e observa, e guarda te per aysso que tu no inscidas aquel; e la tua excoriacio am la qual aquel excorjas per partida jassia que sia suspenduda am le huou mays e subtilment escruta am la excoriacio segon la quantitat a tu possibla.	And excavate that, and observe, and be careful for yourself so that you do not inscribe that; and your excavation with which you excavate by part below as it is suspended in the fluid most and subtly scrutinize the excavation according to the quantity as possible for you.
E aprop perfora le ciphac ple de aygua am perforacio ampla, e extratz tota l’aygua.	And accordingly pierce the white pouch full of water with a broad perforation, and extract all the water.
E aprop separa entre doas labias de la seccio am uncis, e exten le ciphac a las partidas desus; e no toques la codena les genetius comprehendent, e inscideys le ciphac en aquela manieyra que es a tu possible.	And accordingly separate between the two lips of the section with an incision, and extend the white pouch to the parts above; and do not touch the cord of the genitals including, and inscribe the white pouch in that manner which is possible for you.
E inscideys aquel am la sua totalitat o en pessas, e majorment le sieu latz subtil, quar si tu no perscrutas exquisidament la inscizio de lu, no es fayta segurtat que la aygua no retorne.	And accordingly inscribe that with its totality or in pieces, and mostly the subtle side, for if you do not scrutinize the inscription of it exquisitely, there is no certain guarantee that the water will not return.
Mays si le huou procezeys de aquela defora de la sua codena en la ora de la tua operacio, lahoras quan tu auras complida la seccio del ciphac, retorna dedintz aquel, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la codena dels genetius am sutura, e aprop cura aquel ayssi cum las autras plagua, entro que sia sanat.	But if the fluid proceeds from that outside of its cord in the time of your operation, then when you have completed the section of the white pouch, return to that and accordingly adjust the two lips of the cord of the genitals with suture, and accordingly cure that just as with other wounds, until it is healed.
E si atrobas le huou corromput per autra malautia, lahoras cove que tu lies les vayssels les quals so sore le suspensori, e extrat le huou, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit.
