And if you find the fluid corrupted by another disease, then accordingly you should ligate the vessels which are sore the suspensori, and extract the fluid, and accordingly cure that with what we have said.
Mays si l’aygua es agreguada en doas partidas esemps, lahoras sapias que doas son las ernias; donc inscideys aquela partida segon que has feyt en l’autra engualment; e si es a tu vist que sia una opera, lahoras tu la fay.	But if the fluid is aggregated in two separate parts, then you should know that there are two hernias; therefore inscribe that part according to what you have done on the other in equal manner; and if it appears to be one operation, then you do it.
E aprop tu abstergiys le sanc, e entramet en las seccios lana submersa en oli o en oli rozat; e pausa deforo autra lana la qual tu as submersa en vi e oli, e expandeys aquela sobre dos genetius e·l mirac del ventre; e pausa desobre draps doblatz e pulvils, e lia aquels desobre am liament le qual es segon aquesta forma:	And accordingly you should wash the wound, and insert into the sections wool submerged in oil or rose-colored oil; and pause before another wool which you have submerged in wine and oil, and spread that over two genitals and the miracle of the belly; and pause above folded cloths and powder, and tie those above with a thread which is according to this form:
e aprop sian preses dos draps e sian humplitz de lana carmenada segon aquesta semblansa; e sian faytas las extremitatz am les quals es premut de coto o de lana humida, e sian agreguatz am strectura en le braguier de las braguas, e la una de las extremitatz prengua del cul entro al dos, e la segonda prengua a la partida del pantenilh, e dos extramitatz sobre dos coyssas dejos e dos extramitatz autras sobre dos angonars, e tota extrictura sia ajustada en le braguier de las braguas.	and accordingly be pressed two cloths and be filled with cuminated wool according to this likeness; and be made the extremities at which it is necessary to be cut off or moistened with wool, and be added to structure in the waistband of the breeches, and one of the extremities take from the backside to the back, and the other takes to the part of the pubic hairs, and two extremities above two canals below and two other extremities above two gonads, and all structure shall be adjusted in the waistband of the breeches.
E alcunas veguadas aquesta hernia es medicada artificialment am cauteri en loc de seccio am ferr; e es que tu prenguas cauteri cutellar subtil e que inscidas am aquel la codena dels ginitius, e es ignit segon que havem recomtat entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc contenent la aygua, e lahoras tu pren cauteri segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes this hernia is medicated artificially with a cauter in place of section with iron; and it is that you take a cauter cutlery subtle and inscribe on it the cord of the genitals, and ignite it according to what we have recommended until the white pouch containing water is revealed, and then you take the cauter in this form:
e es asemblat a letra greca.	and it is assembled into Greek letter.
E aprop perfora am aquel ciphac, e es ignit entro que tota la humiditat sia fora-gitada.	And accordingly pierce through that white pouch, and ignite until all the moisture has been drained out.
E aprop exten le ciphac am uncis, e excorja am uncis, e excorja am cauteri subtil ignit; e inscideys aquel segon que es a tu possible entro que eradiques tot lu; e guarda te del huou que·l foc no·l toque.	And accordingly extend the white pouch with an incision, and excavate with an incision, and excavate with a subtle cauter ignited; and inscribe that according to what is possible for you until you eradicate all of it; and be careful of the fluid so that the fire does not touch it.
E sapias que aquesta operacio es pus salva e pus longinqua de flux de sanc, e milhor que operacio am seccio.	And know that this operation is more saved and more distant from bleeding flux, and better than an operation with section.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat apostema caut en la hora de seccio o en hora de cauteri, o flux de sanc, lahoras cove que tu cures qual contrarietat fa a tu per aquo, am curacio la qual conveneys a lu segon que es dit.	But if you encounter an apostema contradiction in the hour of section or in the hour of cauterization, or bleeding flux, then accordingly you should cure which contradiction comes to you through this, with a cure which is suitable for him according to what is said.
Mays si le malaute es pauruc, e no spera la segonda operacio per la sua horribilitat, lahoras administra perforacio segon que yeu recomti aquo; e es quan es certificat deves tu, per aquo que havem dit de las significacios, que aquela hernia es ayguosa.	But if the patient is poor and does not hope for a second operation due to its horribleness, then accordingly administer a perforation according to what we have recommended here; and it is when you are certified by that which we have said about the significations, that this hernia is watery.
Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute sobre alcuna cezelha elevada, aprop perfora le apostema en la partida pus bassa de lu am spatum lat, e pausa la perforacio segon la longitut del cos.	And accordingly it is necessary that you should make the patient lie on some elevated stone, and then pierce the apostema in the lowest part of him with a spatula, and pause the perforation according to the length of his body.
E sia la apercio ampla entro que corro tota l‘aygua.	And make the perforation broad so that it drains out all the water.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc coto e lia aquel e layssa aquel, per so que corro le romanent de l’aygua.	And accordingly pause on the location cut and tie it and leave it, so that it drains out the remaining water.
E aprop cura aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.	And accordingly cure that until the wound is healed.
Mays si contrarietat es a la egrecio de l’aygua en aquela hora tu perforas aquela: e aquo no es fayt sino per aquo quar le pannicol blanc en le orrifici de la plagua fa contrarietat e prohibeys le eyssiment de l’aygua, lahoras cove que tu metas en la plagua pena o instrument am la qual es extrayta l’aygua dels ydropitz, la forma del qual es precedida; o ajusta en la opprecio de la plagua un petit.	But if there is opposition to the evacuation of water at that hour you pierce it: and this is not done except for the reason that the white sac in the orifice of the wound makes opposition and prohibits the emission of water, then accordingly you should put into the wound a probe or instrument with which the water is extracted from the hydrocele, the form of which is preceded; or adjust on the surface of the wound a small one.
E sapias que l’aygua retorna, e es agueguada aprop vi meses o enaviro aquels; e cum es agreguada, lahoras sia perforat segon aquela meteyssa manieyra, quar le malaute ayssi passara les sieus dias.	And know that the water returns, and is added accordingly about 6 months or thereabouts; and when it is aggregated, then accordingly it should be pierced in the same manner, so that the patient thus will pass his days.
Capitol .lxiii.	Chapter LXIII.
De seccio sobre hernia carnosa e la curacio de lu.	Of the Section on Fatty Hernia and its Cure.
Sapias que en la seccio sobre aquesta hernia es temor perdusent a pernicia en las majors disposicios; per que a mi es vista la dimissio de lu e esser salvat per aquela milhor.	Know that in the section on this hernia there is fear of being lost to destruction in the greater dispositions; for which I have seen the departure from it and being saved through that better.
E yeu so rememorant la operacio en aquela e las specias dels apostemas.	And you should remember the operation on this and the species of the apostemes.
Donc, dic que l‘apostemas natz en les cos dels quals les genetius so conponutz e es fayt aquo per motas causas: o per superfluitat aguda agra, la qual es efundida als genetius, o per percuscio.	Therefore I say that the apostemes are born in the bodies of those whose genitals are composed and it is done so for many reasons: or because of acute and bitter superfluity which is poured into the genitals, or because of a blow.
E es la color de la apostema segon la color del cos, e no es atrobat en lu dolor, e es apostema greu.	And it is the color of the apostema according to the color of the body, and not found in it pain, and it is a grave apostema.
E fort leu es apostema lapificada, del qual la color es fosca, e no es centiment a lu.	And very often it is a fatty apostema, the color of which is dark, and there is no sensation to it.
E alcunas veguadas es fayt per nodacio de las arcerias, e per imflacio de aquelas ayssi quo ja es perceubut la rememoracio de lu, o per imflacio de venas.	And sometimes it is done through constriction of the vessels, and through inflammation of those things so that already the memory of it is perceived, or through inflammation of veins.
Mays aquo que es per imflacio de arcerias es conogut per la dispercio de la apostema quan compremas aquela am les tieus ditz; e no cove que aquel toques.	But this which is due to inflammation of vessels is known through the dissemination of the apostema when you compress it with those things said above; and it does not need that it touches.
Mays aquel que es fayt per imflacio de vena no es dispergut de lu alcuna causa deves la compressio am les ditz.	But this which is due to inflammation of vein is not disseminated from it by any cause through compression with those things.
E ja es possible que sobre aquesta specia sia fayta seccio e sobre les autres carns; e es que tu inscida la codena dels genetius, e aprop esten le huou a las partidas desus, e extratz aquel del ciphac blanc, e deliura le suspensori dels vaysels, e ligua les, e inscideys le suspensori pus que tu deliuras aquel de tota partida de las partidas del huou.	And it is possible that on this species a section may be made and on the other fleshes; and it is that you inscribe the cord of the genitals, and accordingly stretch the fluid to the upper parts, and extract it from the white pouch, and deliver the suspensori of the vessels, and tie them, and inscribe the suspensori more than what you deliver from all part of the fluids of the womb.
Donc si l’huou ja es am aquelas carnadas consolida, lahoras cove que tu extraguas le huou e inscidas aquel.	Therefore if the fluid is already consolidated in those fleshy parts, then accordingly you should extract the fluid and inscribe it.
E si es adherencia entro alcuna causa del ciphac, o entre aquo que es entre les bayssels, lahoras cove que tu deliures tota aquela adherencia e inscidas aquela per inscizio redonda.	And if there is adhesion due to some cause of the white pouch or between what is between the vessels, then accordingly you should deliver all that adhesion and inscribe it with a rounded inscription.
Mays si es nativitat de carn en le loc de la adherencia la qual es detras, lahoras cove que tu inscidas tot aquo que es de lu, e extraguas le huou ayssi cum havem dit.	But if there is a natural growth of flesh in the location of the adhesion which is behind, then accordingly you should inscribe all that is from it and extract the fluid as we have said.
Donc cum es complida la tua operacio, lahoras omple la plagua de lana imfuza en oli rozat e vi; e aprop cura aquela am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	Therefore when your operation is completed, then accordingly fill the wound with wool impregnated in rose-colored oil and wine; and then cure it with another cure until it is healed.
Capitol .lxiv.	Chapter LXIV.
De la curacio de hernia que es de vitz.	Of the Cure of Hernia which is of Vine.
Vit es apostema envolut per alcuna envolucio semblant a broto am mollificacio dels testiculs, e es fayt dificil movement exercitiu e deambulacio sobre le malaute.	Vine is an aposteme enveloped by some kind of wrapping similar to a bud in the softening of the testicles, and it is done with difficult movements exercised and walking about the patient.
E en la curacio de aquesta malautia es per temor per aquo del qual es precedida rememoracio.	And in the cure of this illness, it is due to fear because of that which is preceded by remembrance.
Empero cove que diguam opperacio en aquela segon que fero les primiers.	However, it is necessary to say operation on that according to what the first ones did.
E dic que cove que fassas sezer le malaute sobre una cezelha elevada; e aprop enpelleys le suspensori dels testiculs a las partidas dejos; e aprop te la codena dels genetius am les tieus ditz am les baysels que so probdas a la vergua; e tengua aquels autre ministre que tu, e extenda aquels am extencio vehement.	And I say that it is necessary to make the patient lie on an elevated stone; and accordingly impale the suspensori of the testicles at the parts below; and accordingly tie the cord of the genitals with those things said above, which are proved by the rod; and have another minister with you, and extend those things with vehement extension.
E aprop inscideys am spatum lat agut per seccio traversa en le dreyt dels vaysels entro que sian les vayssels descubertz.	And accordingly inscribe with a spatula broad and straight for a transverse section in the right of the vessels, until the vessels are uncovered.
E aprop excorja de tota partida ayssi quo a tu havem dit en extraccio de arceria las quals so en las templas.	And accordingly excavate from all part as we have said above in extraction of artery which are in the temples.
E aprop fica en aquelas un’agulha en la qual sia fiel doble, e lia aquel en le primier del locs en les quals accideys vit, e lia aquel autra veguada en le derier de lor.	And accordingly put an needle in those which is faithful double, and tie it at the first place of the places where it happens to be vine, and tie it another time at the last place of theirs.
E aprop inscideys aquels en le mieg loc per seccio dreyta segon la longuesa del cos, e extratz aquo que es agreguat de las humiditatz fetulentas e corruptas.	And accordingly inscribe those in the middle location with a straight section according to the length of the body, and extract that which is added from the putrid and corrupted humors.
E aprop cura la plagua am curacio de las autras plaguas en las quals vols sania esser engendrada per so que caian les vaysels les quals noyreysso un de dos genetius, quar no es mal per aquo.	And accordingly cure the wound with a cure of other wounds in which you want to be generated for that reason that the vessels which nourish one of two genitals may not fall, because it is not evil for that.
Mays si accideys vit a totz les bayssels, lahoras cove que·ls testicols sian extragutz o que les testicols per aquo se cequo am les vayssels, per que sia privat de tot nutriment per la inscizio dels vayssels, e que sian estaborits, o que cequo per so que no sia juvament am aquels.	But if the vine affects all the vessels, then accordingly it is necessary to remove the testicles or for the testicles to be severed from the vessels, in order that it may be deprived of all nourishment through the constriction of the vessels, and that they may become atrophied, or that it becomes so that there is no longer sustenance with them.
Capitol .lxv.	Chapter LXV.
De la cura de hernia entestinal.	Of the Cure of Intestinal Hernia.
Le adveniment de aquesta hernia es per seccio que endeve en le ciphac extendut sobre le ventre de part dels angunars del mirac del ventre, per que deysendo les budels de aquela ruptura ad alcu dels budels.	The advent of this hernia is by a section that enfolds in the white pouch extended over the belly from the parts of the gonads of the miraculous womb, so that those bags of rupture fall into some of the bags.
E aquesta ruptura es o del ciphac o de excencio de lu, e accideysso aquestas doas specias per motas causas: o percussio, o per sautz, o per clamor, o per elevacio de alcuna causa greu, o per semblantz.	And this rupture is either of the white pouch or of excess of fluid, and it occurs in these two species for many reasons: or because of a blow, or because of sound, or because of noise, or because of elevation of some grave cause, or because of likenesses.
E·l senhal de aquo, quan es per extencio del ciphac, es que accideys pauc a pauc en lonc temps, e no accideys soptament, e es apostema engual entro ves le preon per so quar le ciphac comprem le budel.	And the sign of this is when it occurs gradually over a long time, and does not occur suddenly, and it is an aposteme which grows evenly into the preceding part because the white pouch compresses the bag.
E le senhal de lu es quan es per seccio del ciphac, quar al comensament fa accidir dolor vehement sobtament; e es apostema divers aparent dejos la codena propdana aparent, e aquo es per eyssiment del budel, e·l cos de lu a las partidas deforo del ciphac.	And the sign of it is when it occurs by section of the white pouch, because at first it makes sudden and vehement pain; and it is an aposteme which appears different from what was previously apparent, and this is due to the emission of the bag, and the body of it towards the parts above the white pouch.
E alcunas veguadas es fora-getat am le budel la tela, e es apelada aquesta hernia entestinal zirbal.	And sometimes it is forgotten with the bag, and it is called this intestinal hernia, also known as zirbal.
E alcunas veguadas es fayta am ventositat, e alcunas veguadas corr en le budel fenda, e aqui es retenguda, e es am aquo gran pernitia3 del malaute, e alcunas veguadas fa endevenir dolor malvada e majorment quan es premut.	And sometimes it is made with ventosity, and sometimes it runs in the bag's cleft, and stays there, and that is where great peril lies for the patient, and sometimes it causes a wicked and more intense pain when it is pressed.
E en la curacio de las especias de aquesta malautia am ferr es temor, per que cove que sia esquivat le cazament en aquela.	And in the cure of the species of this illness with iron, there is fear, because it is necessary to avoid the caustic agent in that.
E la manieyra de la operacio de aquela es que comandes al malaute que redugua le budel am la sua ma a las partidas dedintz de la sua conquavitat si obezeys al sieu retornament, e aprop sia envessat sobre le sieu col entre las tuas mas, e eleva las cambas de lu.	And the manner of the operation of that is that you command the patient to relax the bag with their own hand towards the parts inside their conquest if they obey your returnment, and accordingly be placed on top of his shoulder between your thighs, and raise the knees of him.
E aprop sten la codena la qual siec la codena dels testicols a las partidas desus, e inscideys la codena dels testicols tota per le lonc; e aprop fiqua en doas labias de la seccio uncis segon que indigeysses a hubrir la seccio am aquels.	And accordingly tie the cord which joins the cord of the testicles to the parts above, and inscribe the cord of the testicles all along; and accordingly place it in two lips of the section incision as you need to irrigate the section with those.
E si’ la seccio segon la quantitat que a tu sia possible que de aquela le huou sia foro-getat.	And if the section is according to the quantity that is possible for you, so that all the fluid is forgotten from that.
E aprop excorja aquela ciphaqueth les quals so dejos la codena dels testicols, entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc dur de quascuna partida.	And accordingly excavate those pouches which are below the cord of the testicles, until the white pouch is uncovered from every part.
Lahoras tu entromet le tieu dit en aquo que siec le testicol, en aquo que es entre ciphac blanc, le qual es dejos la codena del huou, e entre le ciphac segon, e absolve am aquel’adherencia que es en la partida detras del huou.	And accordingly, you should intervene with your own hand in that which is said to be the testicle, between the white pouch and the one which is below the cord of fluid, and between the white pouch and the second one, and absolve from that adhesion which is in the part behind the fluid.
E aprop mau am la ma la codena dels testicols a las partidas deforo, e am aysso exten le ciphac blanc en sus am la ma sinestra, e eleva le huou am le ciphac a la partida de la seccio; e comanda al ministre que extenda le huou ensus e tu dissolveys la adherencia que es detras am solucio complida.	And accordingly, you should take hold of the cord of the testicles with your hand and extend the white pouch in its own direction with your left hand, and raise the fluid with the white pouch to the part of the section; and command the minister to extend the fluid upwards and you dissolve the adhesion that is behind with complete solution.
E cerqua am les tieus ditz que lay no sia alcuna causa del budel envelopat en le ciphac blanc dur.	And accordingly, I say that there should be no cause for the bag to be enveloped in the white pouch hard.
Mays si tu atrobas de lu alcuna causa, lahoras tu enpelleys aquel al ventre dejos.	But if you find any cause from it, then accordingly you should impale that into the belly below.
E aprop tu pren una agulha en la qual sia fiel gros fayt de x fiels, e entromet aquel deves le derier del ciphac, le qual es jos la codena dels testicols, la qual siec seccio; e aprop inscideys las extremitatz las quals emineysso del fiel entro que sian quatre fiels, e aprop compausa alcus de lor sobre alcuna figura en manieyra de crotz; e lia am aquel le ciphac del qual havem dit que es dejos la codena dels testicols am fort liament de dos partz.	And accordingly, you should take a needle with a thick thread of 6 threads, and enter that into the last part of the white pouch, which is below the cord of the testicles, where there is the section; and accordingly inscribe the extremities which emerge from the thread until they are four threads, and accordingly compose some of them into a figure in the manner of a cross; and tie it with that white pouch of which we have said that it is below the cord of the testicles with strong binding of two parts.
E aprop envolveys las extremitatz dels fiels e lia aquelas am liament vehement entro que alcu dels vayssels que noyrrisso aquels no puscan trametre alcuna causa per so que de aqui no accida apostema caut.	And accordingly, you should envelop the extremities of the threads and tie them with a strong binding into the white pouch, so that some of the vessels which nourish those may not be able to transmit any cause for an aposteme to occur.
E pausa autra veguada liament segon foro le primier liament, lonh de lu mens tres ditz; e aprop aquestz dos liaments layssa del ciphac le qual es dejos la codena dels testicols la quantitat de la grandeza del dit, e inscideys tot le romanent segon redondeza, e osta de lu le huou.	And accordingly, you should pause another time for a binding, after the first binding, at least three times; and accordingly, leave those two bindings on the white pouch which is below the cord of the testicles, in the quantity of the greatness of that, and inscribe all the remaining part according to roundness, and stop from there the fluid.
E aprop inscideys en la partida dejos de la codena dels testicols per seccio de la qual corra sanc e sania ayssi cum havem recomtat en aquo que havem dit.	And accordingly, you should inscribe in the part below the cord of the testicles with a section from which blood and pus may flow as we have recommended above.
E aprop aministra lana submersa en oli, e pausa en la plagua; e aministra le liament le qual havem recomtat (e alcunas veguadas le ciphac blanc es cauterizat, le qual havem dit aprop la inscizio de lu temen de flux de sanc, quar motas veguadas accideys aquels) e leyssa le liament entro que per si caia.	And accordingly, you should administer wool immersed in oil and stop at the wound; and administer the binding which we have recommended (and sometimes the white pouch is cauterized, which we have said to be inscribed with caution against bleeding flux, because many times it occurs) and leave the binding until it falls by itself.
Mays si le cazement de lu es tardat, lahoras de aygua cauda sia embrocat, e pausa sobre aquel entro que caia segon que havem dit.	But if the bleeding is delayed, then accordingly cold water should be poured on it, and pause over that until it falls as we have said.
E aprop cura la plagua am l’autra curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, cure the wound with another cure of wounds until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvi.	Chapter LXVI.
De hernia ventosa.	Of Hernia Ventosa.
En aquesta hernia no e vist alcu que sia estat ardit sus la curacio de lu am ferr.	In this hernia, there is no one who has been bold in the cure of it with iron.
E les primiers diyssero que es fayta ayssi cum havem recomtat en la hernia que es am vi; la qual es que tu lies les vayssels aprop la seccio sobre aquela am fecilitat de lu; e aprop secca en le mieg loc en enviro le apostema am aquo que obro aquel, entro que caian les vayssels.	And the first ones said that it is made as we have recommended in the hernia which is with wine; which is that you lay the vessels accordingly above the section on that with facilitation of the fluid; and accordingly, cut off the middle part around the aposteme with water that opens up to those vessels.
E cura la plagua segon que havem dit entro que sia sanada.	And cure the wound according to what we have said until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvii.	Chapter LXVII.
De la disropcio que es fayta en les anguonars.	Of the Disproportion which is made in the Gonads.
Alcunas veguadas endeve ruptura en les angonars ayssi cum havem dit, e emineys le loc.	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the gonads as we have said, and emerges the location.
E no deyssen als genetius alcuna causa dels budels al genetius; e si deyssen, aquo es pauc; e retorna s’en en totas horas.	And there is no cause for the genitals of the bags to be affected by the testicles; and if there is, it is little; and returns again in all hours.
Mays si es prolonguat le temps am aquo, es ajustada fissura en le ciphac entro que deysenda le budel en le ciphac; e accideys aquo per la extencio del ciphac le qual es en le angonars ayssi cum havem dit, la qual causa es quar le ciphac es estendut, e aprop es mollificat e·l loc es apostemat e emineys.	But if the time is prolonged with this, there is a fissure adjusted in the white pouch so that it descends into the white pouch; and this occurs because of the extension of the white pouch which is in the gonads as we have said, which cause is that the white pouch is stretched and becomes softened and the location becomes apostematized and emerges.
E la cura de lu es am cauteri ayssi quo es precedida la narracio de lu.	And the cure for this is with a cauterization as we have previously described.
E alcunas veguadas es curada am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: e es que·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu dos entre las tuas mas, e aprop secca le loc de la ruptura dels apostemas emineys am seccio per la latitut segon la quantitat de tres ditz.	And sometimes it is cured with iron according to this manner: and that the patient lies on his back between your thighs, and accordingly cuts off the location of the rupture of the apostemes which emerges by section along the latitude according to the quantity of three threads.
E aprop strenh le ciphac blanc que es jos la codena entro que sia descubert.	And accordingly, strengthen the white pouch that is below the cord until it is uncovered.
E aprop pren le ray e pausa aquel sobre le loc eminent del ciphac, e prem aquel al preon del ventre.	And accordingly, take a needle and pause it over the elevated location of the white pouch, and press that onto the abdomen.
E aprop cus le dos locs eminentz sobre la extremitat del ray del ciphac, e ajusta am la sutura un de aquels am l’autre.	And accordingly, close the two elevated locations on the extremity of the needle of the white pouch, and adjust with the suture one to the other.
E aprop extratz la extremitat del ray, e no inscidas del ciphac de tot, ni no extenda le huou, ni autra causa ayssi cum yeu te fi saber en la curacio de hernia entestinal.	And accordingly, extract the extremity of the needle, and do not inscribe the entire white pouch, nor extend the fluid, nor any other cause as you have learned in the cure of intestinal hernia.
E aprop cura aquela am la curacio de las plaguas, e cum inscideyses les fiels, mundifica aquela e restaura la plagua entro que sia consolidada; quar le ciphac es contrayt e no es ajustada la eminencia de ruptura.	And accordingly, cure that with the cure of wounds, and as you inscribe the threads, cleanse it and restore the wound until it is consolidated; for the white pouch is contracted and the prominence of rupture is not adjusted.
E cauteri es milhor en aquest loc, quar es pus propda a salut.	And cauterization is better in this location, since it is more conducive to health.
Capitol .lxviii.	Chapter LXVIII.
De mollificacio de la codena dels testiculs.	Of the Softening of the Cord of the Testicles.
Motas veguadas la codena dels testiculs en alcus homes es mollificada per aysso quar las carns que so entre aquela son mollificadas, e es fedat le reguardament de lu.	Many times the cord of the testicles in some men is softened because the flesh that is between it is softened, and it becomes fat for consideration.
Adonc necessari es ad aquel que es preguat en la curacio de lu que fassa jazer le malaute segon le sieu dos, e enscida tota la codena la qual es mollificada sobre la codena natural; e aprop que ajuste doas labias am la sutura.	Therefore it is necessary for the one who is treating this to make the patient lie on his back and inscribe all the cord which is softened onto the natural cord; and accordingly, adjust two lips with the suture.
E si vols, cus en le comensament la superfluitat de la codena mollificada am tres cozeduras o quatre e am ferma sutura.	And if you wish, cut off in the beginning the superfluity of the softened cord with three or four cauterizations and a firm suture.
E aprop inscideys entre las suturas; e aprop cura per curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat e caian les fiels.	And accordingly, inscribe between the sutures; and accordingly, cure by the cure of other wounds until it is healed and the threads fall.
Capitol .lxix.	Chapter LXIX.
De castracio.	Of Castration.
Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias.	Know that castration in our law is excommunicated, but by reason it is written to me that I remember of it in this book; and it is not necessary to recall it except for two methods, one of which is because of the science of the doctor when he is inquired about it, who knows the cure of it which occurs; and the other method is that we many times have needed castration of other beasts for our uses from those, such as horses, and oxen, and pigs, and similar to animals.
E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.	And therefore I say that castration is done in two ways: either by ablation or by incision at section.
Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan.	But in that which is done by ablation, the way of the operation is that we make the beast lie down in cold water until its testicles are softened and relaxed and hang.
E aprop pren aquels am la tua ma entro que sian resols e no apparescan dejos le tocament.	And accordingly, take those with your hand into the water so that they are resolved and do not appear below the touch.
Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra.	But in castration done by incision and section, you must have the beast and press the cord of the testicles with your left hand.
E aprop lia le suspensori, e inscideys sobre quascun huou am una seccio entro que dos huous proceseysso.	And accordingly, tie the suspenders and inscribe on each fluid with one section so that two fluids proceed.
E aprop inscideys aquels pus que auras quascu excorjat.	And accordingly, inscribe those more than you will excise.
E no leysses sobre aquels del ciphac alcuna causa, sino le ciphac subtil le qual es sobre les vazes.	And do not leave any cause on those of the white pouch, except for the subtle white pouch which is above the vessels.
E aquesta manieyra de castracio es milhor la qual es fayta per atrissio, quar atrissio fort leu layssa alcuna causa dels testicols per que la bestia desira coyt.	And this manner of castration is better which is done by ablation, for ablation leaves very little cause of the testicles so that the beast does not desire to copulate.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lxx.	Chapter LXX.
De la cura de hermafrodozia.	Of the Cure of Hermaphrodites.
Hermafrodozia en les homes es segon dos manieyras: la una es quar o appar en aquo que siec l’espazi en la codena de testiculs, en aquel que es entre dos testiculs figura quar cunh de femna en la qual so pels.	Hermaphrodites in men are according to two manners: one is when it appears in what space there is between the cord of the testicles, where a female figure is formed as if it were a womb, and this has a male and female part.
E alcunas veguadas de aquel corr urina le qual es en la codena dels testiculs.	And sometimes from that there flows urine which is in the cord of the testicles.
Mays en las femnas es una specia: e es que·l conh de la femna sobre le pentenilh es ayssi cum dos testiculs de home un pauc de tot yminiheys a la partida deforo ayssi cum le perpucii de home e dos testicols.	But in women, there is one species: and it is that the womb of the woman over the pubis is as if two testicles of a man are joined together in a little less than half the part above, like the perineum of a man and two testicles.
E la curacio es de tres specias: de dos dels homes e de una specia de las femnas.	And the cure is of three species: one from the men and two from the women.
E es que cove que tu inscidas aquelas carns ajustadas entro que efuga la emprecio de aquela, e aprop que cures aquelas am curacio de las autras plaguas.	And it is that you must inscribe those adjusted flesh parts so that the fear of that is removed, and accordingly cure those with the cure of other wounds.
E en la segonda specia dels homes de la qual yeys urina la qual es en la codena dels testiculs, no es curacio ni opperacio en lu.	And in the second species of men from which urine flows which is in the cord of the testicles, there is no cure or operation for that.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De lentinge e de carn eminent per causas de las femnas.	Of Linting and Eminence of Flesh due to Causes of Women.
Lentige fort leu es ajustada sobre causas naturals entro que es etressat e es fayt leg le reguardament; e alcunas veguadas es magnificada en alcunas femnas en tant entro que es spandit ayssi cum en les homes e perve entro al coito.	Linting is very little adjusted on natural causes until it is stretched and made firm the consideration; and sometimes it is magnified in some women to such an extent that it spreads like in men and pours into copulation.
Adonc cove que tu tenguas la superfluitat de lentinge am la tua ma o am unci e inscidas.	Therefore, you must have the superfluity of linting with your hand or with an instrument and inscribe it.
E no ultimes en inscizio, majorment en le preon de la razit, per so que no endevengua flux de sanc.	And do not leave any inscription, especially in the region of the rectum, so that the flow of blood is not interrupted.
E aprop cura aquela am curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, cure that with the cure of wounds until it is healed.
Mays carn nascuda es carn que nays en le horrifici de la mayre entro que umple aquel, e fort leu es eyssit a las partidas deforo segon semblansa de coa (e per aquo alscus primiers appelero aquo “malautia caudada”); donc cove que nos inscidam ayssi cum inscidem lentinge, e curem aquela entro que sia sanada.	But born flesh is flesh that comes from the loins of the mother until it fills up, and very little is issued to the parts above according to the semblance of a hen (and for this reason we also call this “diseased generation”); therefore, you must inscribe it as I inscribe linting, and cure it until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxii.	Chapter LXXII.
De curacio de alratica.	Of the Cure of Hysteria.
Alratica es que le conh de la femna no sia perforat, o sia le trauc petit.	Hysteria is when the womb of the woman is not perforated or is only slightly pierced.
E es o natural o accidental.	And it is either natural or accidental.
Accidental es per malautia la qual ha precedit, e aquela es fayta o per carn nada ajustada o per ciphac subtil o espes.	Accidental is due to disease that has preceded, and it is caused by flesh not well adjusted or by a subtle white pouch or thickening.
E es fayt o en le preon de la mayre, o en les costatz de lu, o en le pus sobira de lu, o en le pus bas de lu, e prohibeys de cuoyt e de enprenguacio e de enfantament, e fort leu prohibeys las mestruas.	And it is caused in the lower back of the mother, or in the sides of her, or in the upper part of her womb, or in the lower part of her womb, and it prohibits coition and pregnancy and childbirth, and very little permits menstruation.
E la cognicio de aquela es fayta per reguardament de la metrona, si la oppilacio es apparent, propdana; mays si no es apparent, lahoras tu cerqua aquela am les tieus ditz o am le ray.	And the knowledge of this is done by consideration of the meter, if the oppression is apparent, propounded; but if it is not apparent, you must search for it with the said threads or with a needle.
Mays si oppilacio es per ciphac subtil, e es propda a las doas labias, lahoras tu coyta e disromp aquela.	But if oppression is due to a subtle white pouch and it is propounded on the two lips, you must cut and break that.
E es que pauses sobre las doas labias pulvils, e aprop pausa les tieus ditz indicz de amdoas las mas encemps.	And it is that you pause above the two lips of dust, and accordingly pause the said threads indicating both the upper and lower masses.
E la femna sia sobre le sieu dos, las sieuas coyssas extendudas, e aprop exten las doas labias am forsa entro que aquel ciphac subtil sia romput e la oppilacio sia uberta.	And the woman should be on her back, her legs extended, and accordingly extend the two lips with force until that subtle white pouch is broken and the oppression is opened.
E aprop pren lana e enbeu le4 en oli e pausa aquela sobre·l loc, e jagua am home le dia per so que·l loc inscis no sia consolidat.	And accordingly, take wool and dip it in oil and pause it on the location, and make the patient lie down at home that day so that the location is not consolidated.
Mays si le ciphac es gros e espes, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquel am spatum lat o am fuelha de mirta.	But if the white pouch is thick and dense, you must inscribe it with a spatula or with myrtle leaves.
Mays si la oppilacio es per carnada, lahoras suspen aquela am unci, e inscideys aquela.	But if the oppression is due to inflammation, you must suspend that with an instrument, and inscribe it.
E sian am tu las medicinas que fan cessar flux de sanc ses mordicacio, ayssi cum ahacatia, e sanc de drago, e enses, ajustat am album de huou.	And take the medicines that make cease the flow of blood without scratching, such as aconitum, and blood of dragon, and gallbladder, adjusted with album of hen.
E aprop aministra una canulha de plom ampla per so que la plagua no sia consolidada leugierament.	And accordingly, administer a leaden cannula widely so that the wound is not slightly consolidated.
E tengua aquela per alcus jorns e aministra calgua de li sec.	And keep it for some days and administer cold water of lily.
E aprop sia curada am l’autra curacio de consolidacio entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly, be cured with the other cure of consolidation until it is healed.
E alcunas vetz accideys en la mayre nativitat de autres carns, e lahoras cove que inscidas segon aquesta manieyra.	And sometimes it happens in the natural birth of other flesh, and you must inscribe according to this manner.
Mays si aysso es per apostema crancos, a l’apostema crancos le qual es en la mayre no sia fayta contrarietat am ferr en deguna manieyra.	But if it is due to gangrenous aposteme, there should be no contradiction with iron in any manner.
Capitol .lxxiii.	Chapter LXXIII.
De la cura de emorroydas e de tayl e de botor roja que accideysso en le conh de las femnas.	Of the Cure of Hemorrhoids and Tail and Red Bottom that occur in the Womb of Women.
Emorroydas so apprecio dels orificis de motas venas entro que de aquelas corro mot sanc continuadament; e cum so antiquadas emorroydas e son fayts theyls.	Hemorrhoids are a prolapse of many veins until those flow blood continuously; and when old hemorrhoids are formed, they become hardened.
E ja yeu he dit en la divisio las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e diyre ayssi aquelas que recebo curacio e aquelas que no recebo curacio.	And I have said in the division the species of those and their signs, and will also say which receive cure and which do not receive cure.
Donc dic que emorroydas e theyls quan so en le preon de la mayre e no apparo al sentiment, lahoras en aquelas no sia fayta curacio am ferr.	Therefore I say that hemorrhoids and hardened veins when they are in the lower back of the mother and do not appear to the sense, therefore in those there is no cure with iron.
Mays aquelas las quals so en le orrifici de la mayre sobre las quals catz sentiment, so aquelas que so curadas.	But those that are in the opening of the mother above which one senses, are those that can be cured.
E cove que tu metas la femna en mayso frega e aprop exten atheyl am les forfexs, o am drap aspre, e inscideys aquelas am las razitz.	And you must put the woman in a warm place and accordingly extend the hardened veins with forceps or with rough cloth and inscribe them with the roots.
E aprop pulveriza sobre aquelas deves le fluxs del sanc de una de las polveras insciscivas ses mordicacio, ayssi cum acassia e semblant ad aquels.	And accordingly, powderize on those the flow of blood with one of the inscribable powders without scratching, such as aconitum and similar to those.
E aprop enpellesca les sieus pes per una hora, e aprop pausa aquela en aygua freja.	And accordingly, press the patient's feet for an hour, and accordingly pause that in cold water.
E si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras fay aquela sezer en decoccio de sumat e de scorsas de milgranas e de gualas e de semblantz.	And if the flow of blood persists, then make that person drink a decoction of samarang and scorched millet and mallows and similar things.
E aprop pren farina de ordi e comfiys aquela am miel e vi agre e fay emplastre am aquo sobre le dos de lu.	And accordingly, take oat flour and comfort that with honey and vinegar and make an ointment with water on the back of him.
E si le sanc es abscindit, bo es; e sino, fay adherir am dos ventozas, e a las mamilhas ses escarificatio.	And if the blood is absorbed, it is good; and otherwise, make adhere to two blisters, and to the nipples with scarification.
E aprop pren lana e submergeys aquela am suc de coliandre o am suc de arnagloza o am suc de guarravier am vi pentit e fay adherir al loc; e aprop cura le loc am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, take wool and submerge it in the juice of colocynth or in the juice of argemone or in the juice of guaiacum with vinegar and make adhere to the place; and accordingly, cure the place with poultices until it is healed.
Mays athyl rog le qual es de aspre reguardament, cove que tu inscidas aquo que a tu appar de aquel segon que he dit en theyl engualment.	But harden the vein which is of rough observation, you must inscribe this as it appears to you according to what I have said in the equal measure.
E cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxiv.	Chapter LXXIV.
De perforacio de eyssedura accident en la mayre.	Of the Perforation of Accidental Bleeding in the Womb.
Motas specias de apostemas accideysso en la mayre, ayssi cum cranc e apostema lapident e ulceracios e adhubelat e erpetromens e fistulas emorroyas e raguarrias e thyl e autres apostemas.	Many species of accidental apostemes occur in the womb, such as gangrenous and lapidated aposteme, ulcers, adhesion, erpetromen, fistula hemorrhoids, red bottoms, hardened veins, and other apostemes.
E yeu ja he dit aquestas malautias e las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e las curacios de lor en la divisio.	And I have said these illnesses and their species and signs, and the cures for them in the division.
E cove que yeu digua en aquest tractat de apostema caut le qual ve en la mayre quan es dels apostemas que collegeysso sania, e si vols saber en qual manieyra se fa la opperacio de lu am ferr.	And it is fitting that you say in this treatise of aposteme caustic which appears in the womb when it is one of the apostemes that college together to heal, and if you wish to know in what manner the operation is done with iron.
Adonc cove que tu consideres si la dolor de la apostema en le sieu comensament es aguda am percussio e flecma e febre, e vezes aquel enrogezir e si catz sobre aquel le sentiment, lahoras no·t coytes am perforacio de lu, e cura aquel am aquo que ajuda sobre la maturacio entro que cesse la acuitat dels accidentz.	Therefore it is fitting that you consider if the pain of the aposteme in its beginning is acute with percussion and flux and fever, and sometimes blenches and if one senses above that a sensation, then do not cut with perforation of iron, and cure that with water which helps on maturity until the acuity of accidents ceases.
E lahoras cove que tu fassas cezer la femna sobre una cezelha que aia doas cezelhas; e recline sobre le sieu dos e ajusta les sieus pes a la partida pus dejos del ventre, e las sieus coyssas sian expandudas, e pausa les sieus brasses dejos les sieus denols, e lia quascus am liament ad aquo convenient.	And accordingly it is fitting that you make the woman lie on a bed which has two mattresses; and recline her on her back and adjust her feet to the part most distant from the womb, and have her legs expanded, and pause her arms below her nails, and tie each one with a ligament to water suitable.
E aprop la matrona segua del latz dreyt e aministre le instrument am le qual es ubert le orrifici de la mayre, la forma del qual vindra en aquelas causas que·s faran aprop.	And accordingly the midwife follows the right path and administers the instrument with which the opening of the womb is opened, the form of which will come in those causes that are made to follow.
E cove quan vols ministrar aquest instrument que tu fiques am lo ray le preon de la mayre de la femna, e aquo que del instrument es intrat en la mayre no sia mays que·l preon de la mayre e leda le malaute.	And accordingly when you wish to administer this instrument, you must make it with the ray of the back of the woman's womb, and that which is entered into the womb from the instrument should not be more than the back of the womb and lead the patient.
Mays si l’estrument es major que·l preon de la mayre, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils sobre la textura del preon de la mayre per sso que sia prohibit l’intrament de tot instrument en le preon de la mayre.	But if the instrument is greater than the back of the womb, then it is fitting that you powderize on the texture of the back of the womb so that the introduction of any instrument into the back of the womb is prohibited.
E cove que tu pauses le vertitge que corr en le strument del latz pus desus e que le ministre tengua le strument e revolva le vertitge entro que sia ubert le orrifici de la mayre.	And accordingly you must powderize the vertex that runs on the instrument from above and down, and the minister should hold the instrument and turn the vertex until the opening of the womb is opened.
E cum appar la excitura, e es tocada am la ma e es leon e molh, lahoras cove que tu secces aquela deves le cap de lu am spatum lat.	And when the excitement appears, and it is touched with the hand and is warm and moist, then you must cut that with a spatula at the head of him.
E cum la sania es evacuada, lahoras cove que tu pauses en la plagua una meca submersa en oli rozat o oli vert en le qual sia alcuna stiptisitat; e pausa la calca7 en la seccio en le preon de la mayre.	And when the discharge is evacuated, then you must powderize on the wound a compress soaked in rose oil or green oil which has some stimulating quality; and pause the pressure in the section on the back of the womb.
E pause deforo la mayre e sobre le pentenilh lana munda submersa en aygua en la qual sian bulidas malvas.	And accordingly, pause above the mother and on the pubic hair a clean wool soaked in water in which mulberries have been boiled.
E aprop sia curada aprop dos dias am enguent le qual conveneys ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, be cured after two days with poultice which is suitable for that until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas es lavada la mayre e la plagua enayssi que es cristerisat am aygua e mel, e aprop am aygua en la qual es bulhida razit de liri o de aristologia longua, e aprop retorna al enguent.	And sometimes the mother is washed and the wound similarly as it is anointed with water and honey, and accordingly anointed with water in which the root of lily or aristolochia longa has been boiled, and accordingly returns to the poultice.
E si la plagua es dedintz en la mayre ameguada, lahoras cove que tu sias prohibit de la curacio de lu am ferr, habantz cura aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio.	And if the wound is deep in the mother's womb, then it is fitting that you are prohibited from the cure of him with iron, having cured that with water as we have said in the division.
Capitol .lxxv.	Chapter LXXV.
A ensenhar las matronas en qual manieyre les enbrios bius sian medicatz quan yeysso segon figura no-natural.	To teach midwives how to medicate children when they are born with a non-natural figure.
Necessaria causa es que la matrona conogua en le comensament la figura del enfantament natural per senhals de lu, e es que quan tu vezas la femna expremar a las partidas dejos e desira odorar le ayre, e sobre aquo es enleujada per aquo que sobre ela es del part, e festina le eyssiment del enbrio, lahoras sapias que aquest part es segon figura natural, e es l’eyssiment de lu sobre le sieu cap, e la segondina am aquel o suspensa o pendent del ombelic.	A necessary cause is that the midwife knows at the beginning the figure of natural childbirth by signs from her, and it is that when you see the woman expel at the parts below and desire to smell the air, and above it is inclined due to what is on her part, and hasten the extraction of the child, then you will know that this part is according to natural figure, and it is the extraction of him over his head, and the second birth with that or suspended or pendulous from the umbilicus.
Donc cum tu vezes aquels senhals, lahoras cove que·l ventre de lu sia compremut per so que l’embrio deysenda leugerament quar quan deyssen sobre le sieu cap, deysen a lu la segondina, e es mondada de aquelas superfluitatz am bona mondificacio.	Therefore, when you see those signs, then it is fitting that the belly of him be compressed so that the child descends slightly because when they descend upon his head, they give to him the second birth, and it is cleansed from those superfluities with good cleansing.
Mays aquel que es otra aquest part es no-natural e no-lausable, quar quan le enbrio es eyssit sobre sos pes e·l cos de lu es eyssit devant le cap de lu e·ls pes de lu, e la ma de lu una, o al pe de lu .i., o es eyssit le cap de lu e la ma de lu, o al ventre de lu, e fort leu es convertit sobre le sieu col, e semblant de las figuras de lu no-lausablas.	But that which is another this part is non-natural and not to be approved, because when the child is born with his feet and the body of him is born before his head and his feet, and one hand or at the foot. i.e. or is born with his head and one hand or at the belly of him, and very little is converted on his back, and similar to the figures that are not to be approved.
Don necessaria causa es a la matrona que sia savia e subtil en totas aquelas causas, e que·s guarde de error e de decepcio.	Therefore, it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in all those causes, and to guard against error and deception.
E yeu so mostrant tota figura de aquelas, e qual engen es en aquelas per so que sia significat per aquo e sia stat sobre aquo.	And I am showing the whole figure of those, and what sign is in those so that it may be signified by this and has been on top.
Quan le feyt es eyssit sobre le sieu cap per egrecio natural, e aquel es vehement sobre la femna e es fayt a lu part dificil, e vezes la vertut de lu ja debelitada, lahoras fay aquela sezer , o que las femnas tenguan lu, e evapora le conh de lu am fenugrec coyt e am olis humitz.	When the child is born on top of its head through natural eccentricity, and it is vehement upon the woman and has made a difficult part for him, and sometimes the virtue of him is already debilitated, then make that person drink, or have women give to him, and evaporate the womb with henbane and humus oil.
E aprop entrometa la metrona entre les sieus ditz espatum petit e fenda am aquel la segondina, o secce aquela am la sua ungla entro que corro aquo que es en ela de humiditat.	And accordingly introduce the midwife between the said spatula small and a fissure with that second birth, or cut that with her own fingernail until it runs with water which is in it of humidity.
E preme le ventre de la femna entro que deyssenda le fet.	And press the belly of the woman until it gives birth to the child.
Mays si no deyssen, lahoras cove que la femna sia cristirizada de mucellage de ptilli e mucellage de fenugrec am cizami.	But if it does not give birth, then it is fitting that the woman be anointed with a poultice of pimpernel and a poultice of fenugreek with camomile.
E aprop comanda a lu, aprop le cristeri, que sia compremuda e fay aquela stornudar am condisi; e te la boca de lu e·l nas de lu per huna hora, quar le fet sira foro-getat tantost.	And accordingly command him to you, and command the anointing, that it be compressed and make her sneeze with conditions; and tie the mouth of him and his nose for one hour, because the child will soon be forgotten.
E si las doas mas del fet so foro-getadas al comensament, lahoras cove que tu redusiscas aquelas am fecilitat petit a petit.	And if the two arms of the child are forgotten at the beginning, then it is fitting that you reduce them with little ease little by little.
Mays si no obezeys al intrament, lahoras pausa la femna sobre una cezelha e leva les pes de lu sus, e aprop concuceys la cezelha sobre la terra; e la femna sia tenguda que no caia deves la concussio.	But if it does not obey the instrument, then you must pause the woman on a bed and lift her feet up, and accordingly conceive the bed on the earth; and the woman is to be held so that she does not fall under the concussion.
E si las mas no son dedintz tornadas e morr le fet, lahoras inscideys aquelas e extratz le romament del fet o lia le cors a la ma de lu am drap e extratz aquel am equalitat, quar aquel sira foro-getat.	And if the arms are not returned and the child dies, then you must inscribe those and extract the remains of the child or tie the body to the hand with cloth and extract that with equality, because it will soon be forgotten.
De eyssiment del embrio sobre les sieus pes.	The Extraction of the Child from its Feet.
Quan le fet yeys sobre les sieus pes, lahoras cove que tu impelliscas aquels en sus, e aprop convertas le fet petit, e aprop que engualhes aquel, e aprop que prenguas un pe de lu e extendas aquels petit a petit.	When the child is born on its feet, then it is fitting that you push them inwards, and accordingly convert the child little by little, and accordingly make equal that part, and accordingly take one foot of him and stretch those little by little.
Mays cum son eyssit entro a las coyssas, lahoras tu comanda a lu que se exprema, e fay aquela extornudar am condizi, quar sira foro-getat si Deus lo vol.	But when they are born into the thighs, then you must command him to come out, and make her sneeze with conditions, because it will soon be forgotten if God so wills.
E si no es foro-getat am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras tu retorna le fet petit a petit entro que pauses aquel segon figura natural, quar aquel sira lahoras foro-getat am leugier eyssiment.	And if it is not forgotten as we have recounted, then you must return the child little by little until it comes to the second birth according to natural figure, because it will soon be forgotten with easier extraction.
E si es prohibit am tot aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras pren de musellage de altea e de goma dissolvuda, e percuteys tot en le mortier per bona percussio, e aprop linieys am aquo le conh de la femna, el pus bas del ventre de lu.	And if it is prohibited according to all that we have recounted, then you must take musellage of althea and dissolved gum, and beat everything in the mortar for good beating, and accordingly line with water the womb of the woman, as far down as the belly of her.
E aprop fay aquela cezer en aygua tebeza, entro que consegua les ypocondias.	And accordingly make that person drink in tepid water until they achieve the hips.
E cum vezes que las partidas dejos de lu so lenificadas, lahoras fay a lu subfumiguacio de mirta e sub-pausa aquela a lu.	And when the parts below of him are softened, then make him inhale the vapor of myrtle and pause that for him.
E quan te la sub-fumiguacio per una hora, lahoras tu la fay sezer sobre una cezelha, e aprop fay aquela stornudar e extrenh la boca de lu, e levas de aquela, e prem la partida pus bassa del ventre de lu am leugiera compressio, quar le fet sira tantost foro-getat.	And when the sub-fumigation has lasted for an hour, then make her lie on a bed, and accordingly make her sneeze and stretch her mouth, and lift that away from her, and press the lower part of the belly of her with gentle compression, because the child will soon be forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre les sieus denols e las suas mas.	The Birth of the Child on its Fingernails and Arms.
Quan le fet eyssira segon aquesta forma, lahoras tu engenies en entrometen las suas mas petit a petit; e aprop la femna stia evessada sobre le sieu col, e les pes de lu pengo en jos, e aquelas sia jasent sobre le lieyt, e complegua las suas mas.	When the child is born in this form, then you must guide its arms little by little; and accordingly, have the woman lie on her back, and her feet hanging down, and those [arms] be placed on the light, and complete its arms.
E aprop prem sobre le ventre de lu petit a petit, e aprop extratz aquo que es dejos les pes de lu de las aurelhas entro que sia preparada en la partida pus dejos.	And accordingly press on the belly of her little by little, and accordingly extract that which is behind the feet from the ears until it is prepared in the lower part.
E si le fet no es fora-getat, lahoras pren les pes de lu e mau aquels am movement vehement, e aprop prem aquo que es sobre les ypocondres petit a petit entro que le fet puege a las partidas desus.	And if the child is not forgotten, then take her feet and move them with violent motion, and accordingly press that which is above the hips little by little until the child can pass through the upper parts.
E aprop entrometa las suas mas e engualhe le fet petit a petit, e comanda a la femna que se exprema entro que le fet sia foro-getat.	And accordingly introduce its arms and equalize the child little by little, and command the woman to come out until the child is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet latutidinalment pendent una de las suas mas.	The Birth of the Child Lateral to One of Its Arms.
Sia engeniat en reduccio de la ma de lu, mays si no podes aquela reduzir, lahoras eleva la femna e fe aquela anar.	Be guided in the reduction of her arm, but if you cannot reduce that, then lift the woman and make her walk.
E si anar no pot, lahoras fay la jazer sobre le lieyt, e concuteys las coyssas de lu am concussio vehement, e aprop aministra liamentz les quals yeu e recomtatz de mucillages.	And if she cannot walk, then make her lie on the light, and conceive the thighs of her with strong concussion, and accordingly administer those which you have recounted of poultices.
E si es vengut le enfantament, lahoras fay aquela sezer sobre cezelha, e aprop studia sobre la reduccio de la ma, e enguala le fet segon figura natural, e fay stornudar la femna e comanda a lu que comprema a si entro que sia foro-getat.	And if the childbirth is over, then make her lie on a bed, and accordingly study the reduction of the arm, and equalize the child according to natural figure, and make her sneeze and command him to compress himself until it is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre·l col expandudas las suas mas e la fassia de lu es al dos de la sua mayre.	The Birth of the Child with its arms expanded and the flesh of him at the two sides of his right side.
Cove que la matrona tengua la ma del fet e aprop revolva aquel petit a petit, e eque aquel am facilitat.	It is fitting that the midwife hold the arm of the child and accordingly rotate it little by little, and equalize that with ease.
E cum es e quant so es engualhat, e lahoras pausa sobre le conh de lu aquo que havem recomtat de oli e de mucellages.	And when it is and as much as is equalized, then pause over the womb of her that which we have recounted of oil and poultices.
E aprop comandas a lu que·s maugua petit a petit, e quan auras feyt aquo, lahoras fay aquela cezer sobre una cezelha e comanda li que sia inclinada sobre le latz dreyt, e aprop comanda a lu que sia compremuda; e fay aquela stornudar am condizi.	And accordingly command him to sneeze little by little, and when you have done that, then make her lie on a bed and command him to be inclined over the right side, and accordingly command him to compress himself; and make her sneeze with conditions.
Exitus foetus praeparati super latus.	The Exit of the Prepared Foetus from the Right Side.
Quan deyssen a horrifici de la mayre segon aquesta manieyra, considera, e lahoras tu inscideys la segondina am la tua ungla entro que sia evacuada de la humiditat.	When it comes to the horror of the right side according to this manner, consider, and accordingly you must inscribe the second birth with your own fingernail until it is evacuated from humidity.
E si le fet es suspendut sobre la cara e·l col de lu, lahoras tu inscideys aquela del embelic, per so que no sia retengut e mora.	And if the child is suspended over the face and neck of her, then you must inscribe that from the navel, in order that it may not be retained and die.
E aprop empelleys le fet a las partidas dedintz entro que pauses aquel segon que cove, e manda a la femna que comprema a si alcunas veguadas, e el sira fora-getat am eyssiment leugier, si Dieus o vol.	And accordingly push the child into the lower parts until it comes out according to what is fitting, and command the woman to compress herself sometimes, and if God so wills, it will soon be forgotten with easier extraction.
Exitus geminorum aut foetuum multorum.	The Exit of Twins or Multiple Foetuses.
Sapias que gemels motas veguadas so natz, e alcunas vetz naysso tres o quatre , mays aquo es estranh e tart s’endeve; mays v so causas foro natura, e no vivo.	Know that sometimes twins are born, and occasionally three or four, but this is rare and not to be wondered at; however there are causes that are natural, and not living.
E conte aquelas, ja sia que sian montiplicatz, una segondina, e son seperatz per ciphac, distingen aquels enter le liguament en l’ombilic de cascun de aquels E alcunas veguadas so foro-getatz ayssi cum es un fet per eyssiment natural leugier, e so eysitz alcunas veguadas per eyssiment no-lausabla ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And contain those, whether they are multiple or not, one second birth, and separate them by caesarean section, distinguish those from the bond in the umbilical cord of each of them; and sometimes some are forgotten thus as is one child for easier natural extraction, and some are extracted sometimes through non-natural extraction just as we have recounted.
E si son dificils alcus de lor deves le enfantament e perveno ad aquo que havem dit de las figuras no-naturals, lahoras tu cura aquels ayssi cum havem recontat.	And if some of them are difficult to deliver and come to what we have said about non-natural figures, then you must cure those just as we have recounted.
E si’ la matrona subtil e fassa aquo que fa am facilitat e subtilitat, e am tarditat, e sia ingeniat segon tota figura segon que es a lu preparat de l’engen amenant a salut.	And if the midwife is subtle and does that which facilitates and subtlety, and with delay, and is guided according to all figure as it is prepared by the ingenuity leading to salvation.
Rememoratio eius quod formatur in matrice ex embrionibus et Abortiuntur.	Recollection of that which is formed in the womb from embryos and is aborted.
Alcunas veguadas son formatz en la mayre un, e dos, e tres, e quatre, e v, e vi, e vii, e mays x, e ja es deves mi verificat que una femna abortem ne getet vi, e una autra x totz formatz, la qual causa fo fayta per mensuracio dels glorios savis.	Some women are found to be fertile in one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, and even up to ten months, and you should verify that a woman aborts at the sixth month, while another conceives again with all the numbers, which is caused by measurement of the wise sages.
E tot aysso cove que sia en la sciencia de la matrona quar fort leu ad aquela parve semblant de aquo, e donc opause se ad aquo am so que cove.	And all this is to be in the science of the midwife because it is very similar to that, and therefore pause at that with what is fitting.
Capitol .lxxvi.	Chapter LXXVI.
De extraccio del fet quan es mort.	On the Extraction of the Child when it is Dead.
Quan tu curas le fet mort am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la medicacio e no es defora eyssit, e tu yest forsat usar de opperacio am ma, lahoras cove que consideras si la femna es de sana vertut e no es am alcu dels accidentz per les quals sobre ela es temuda perdicio.	When you cure the dead child with what we have said in the division of medicine and it is not otherwise extracted, and you are forced to use operation with force, then it is fitting that you consider whether the woman is of good virtue and not affected by any of the accidents by which perilous loss may occur upon her.
Lahoras cove que la femna sia envessada sobre le lieyt sobre le sieu dos, e sia le cap de lu enclinat enjos e las coyssas de lu sian elevadas.	Then it is fitting that the woman be inclined over a bed on her back, and her head lowered down and her thighs raised.
E·l ministre tengua aquela de doas partz o sia liada en le lieyt per so que·l cos de lu no se extenda deves la extraccio del fet.	And the minister must hold that in two parts or tie it in a bed for so that her body does not stretch out during the extraction of the child.
E aprop tu humecta la boca de la mayre de lu am olis humitz e am mucellage de altea e de fenugrec e de semensa de li.	And accordingly moisten the mouth of her with oil and with humus oil and with poultice of althea and fenugreek and with seed of lily.
E aprop unte la matrona la sua ma am aquels olis e mucellages, e aprop entrometa la sua ma am fecilitat en la mayre, e aprop cerque am la ma loc en le qual fique les uncis en le fet.	And accordingly anoint the midwife's hand with those oils and poultices, and accordingly introduce her hand with ease into the mother, and accordingly search for the exact location where the fingers should be placed on the child.
E locs convenient en aquo: adonc tu considera si le fet es preparat que deysenda sobre le sieu cap, e lahoras tu fique les uncis en les huels de lu, o en le col, o en la boca, o en le palat, o dejos la barba, o en la furcula de lu, o en les locs propdas de las costas, o dejos les ypocondres.	And when the location is convenient: then you consider whether the child is prepared to come out over its head, and accordingly place your fingers in the holes of it, or on the neck, or mouth, or palate, or below the chin, or at the furcula, or in the places proper to the chest, or below the hips.
Mays si le deysendiment es sobre les pes de lu, lahoras en le pentenilh, o en le mieg de las costas.	But if the delivery is over the feet, then in the navel, or in the middle of the chest.
E cove que tengua le unci am la ma dreyta, e pausa la curvitat de lu en aquel loc le qual es entre les ditz de la ma senestra, e entrometa la ma am facilitat e fique le unci en alcu de aquels locs les quals havem ditz, entro que pervengua a la causa boyda.	And it is fitting that you have the finger on the right hand, and pause the curvature of it at that location which is between the fingers of the left hand, and introduce the hand with ease and place the finger in one of those locations which we have said, until you arrive at the cause of birth.
E aprop pause e fique en la apposicio de lu un autre unci, o le tertz si es necessitat, per so que sia atraccio engual, e no sia extencio segon la sua rectetut tant solament.	And accordingly pause and place another finger, or the third if necessary, in order that there may be equal attraction, and not extension only according to its straightness.
Ans sia maugut a tota partida, per so que l’eyssiment de lu sia alleujat ayssi cum es fayt en dent deves la eradicacio de lu.	And thus it is good at all parts, in order that the extraction of him may be facilitated just as it is done in a tooth for the eradication of it.
E cove en lu aquo que es entre lor que la extencio sia mollificada; e si alcuna partida de lu es retenguda, lahoras cove que la matrona unte alcus sieus ditz am oli e entrometa aquels espertament e revolva am aquels aquo que es retengut.	And it is fitting in that which is between them that the extension be softened; and if some part of him is retained, then it is fitting that the midwife anoint some of her fingers with oil and introduce those expertly and revolve around what is retained.
Donc si la partida del fet es fora-getada, lahoras les uncis sian permudatz entra loc le qual sia pus aut; e fay aysso entro que tot le fet sia fora-getat.	Therefore, if the part of the child is forgotten, then it is fitting that the fingers be permeated into the place where it is more high; and make thus until the whole child is forgotten.
Mays si la ma es eyssida denant l’autra, e no es possible reduzir aquela per la coartacio de lu, lahoras cove que drap sia envolopat sobre aquela; e aprop extratz aquela entro que tota sia fora-getada, e inscideys aquela o en la junctura de la ma o en le coyde.	But if the hand is extracted before the other, and it is not possible to reduce that by the contraction of him, then it is fitting that a cloth be wrapped around that; and accordingly extract that until all is forgotten, and inscribe that either in the junction of the hand or in the thigh.
E ayssi cove que fassas en l’autra ma e en les dos pes.	And thus it is fitting to do so in the other hand and in both feet.
Mays si le cap del fet es gran, o accideys a lu coartacio en le eyssiment, o es en le cap de lu aygua ajustada, lahoras cove que entrometa entre les ditz espatum spinos e fenda le cap e extragua la aygua, o que discroba aquel am un instrument le qual es nompnat “alundat”, la forma del qual vindra am las formas dels autres instruments en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	But if the head of the child is large, or there occurs contraction in the extraction, or the water is adjusted in the head of it, then it is fitting that you insert between the fingers the spatula with spines and split the head and drain the water, or displace that with one instrument which is called "alundat", whose form will come from the forms of other instruments in the chapter which is apropos to this.
E semblantment fassa si·l fet es de gran cap per natura: e lahoras cove que inscida aquel am algematu, o que prengua aquel am alunda ayssi cum havem dit; e aprop extra les osses am les forceps.	And similarly do so if the child is naturally large-headed: and it is fitting that you inscribe that with an instrument called "algemat", or take that with an "alundat" just as we have said; and accordingly extract the bones with forceps.
E si le cap es eyssit e es coartat deves la furcula, lahoras sia fendut entro que la humiditat la qual es en le pietz sia efunduda.	And if the head is extracted and is contracted at the furcula, then it is fitting that it be split into so that the humidity which is in the pelvis may be poured out.
Mays si no es complicat, ni obezeys a eyssiment, lahoras tu inscideys le cap tantost segon que a tu sira possible.	But if it is not complicated, nor obedient to extraction, then it is fitting that you inscribe the head at once according as it will be possible for you.
E si le dejos del ventre es apostemat o es en lu ydropici, lahoras cove que tu perfores aquel entro que corro la humiditat que es en lu.	And if the remains of the womb are apostemated or are in a state of dropsy, then it is fitting that you perforate it until the humidity which is in it runs out.
Mays si le fet es sobre les sieus pes, lahoras la atraccio de lu es leugiera e la direccio de lu a la boca de la mayre es leugiera.	But if the child is on its feet, then it is fitting that the attraction of it be light and the direction of it to the mouth of the mother be light.
Mays si es coartat deves le ventre e·l pietz, lahoras cove que tu extraguas aquel am drap le qual auras envolopat sobre la tua ma, e que fendes le ventre e·l pietz entro que corra aquo que es en aquels.	But if it is contracted in the womb and pelvis, then it is fitting that you extract it with cloth which you will wrap around your hand, and that you split the womb and pelvis into so that the water which is in them may flow out.
Mays si les autres membres so ostatz e torna le cap, lahoras la metrona entrometa la ma senestra; mays si la boca de la mayre es huberta, lahoras intrometa la ma en le preon de layre, e cerque am aquela le cap, e atira aquel am les ditz entro a la boca de la mayre, e aprop entrometa en lu un unci, o dos uncis, e atire lu am aquels.	But if the other members are still and turn back the head, then it is fitting that you insert your left hand; but if the mouth of the mother is swollen, then insert your right hand into the prepuce of layre, and search for that head, and draw it towards those fingers into the mouth of the mother, and accordingly introduce one finger, or two fingers, and attract him with those.
E si la boca de la mayre es coartada per apostema caut le qual accideys a l’u, lahoras cove que no sia trebelhat sobre lu; abantz cove lahoras aministrar efusio de causas humidas grassas.	And if the mouth of the mother is contracted by apostema and it causes trouble to you, then it is fitting that you do not trouble yourself about it; before it is fitting to administer an effusion of humid and greasy causes.
E aministre emplastres; e segua le pacient en ayguas que mollifican e humectan.	And administer poultices; and follow the patient with waters that soften and moisten.
E si le fet es sobre le sieu costat, lahoras si possible es, sia agulat: e sia aministrat aquo que havem dit en le fet viu.	And if the child is on its own chest, then it is fitting that it be pierced: and anointed with water as we have said in the living child.
E si aquo no es possible, lahoras sia inscidit en pessas, e sia extrayt.	And if this is not possible, then it is fitting that it be inserted into a pot and extracted.
E cove que non layssas alcuna causa dedintz de la segondina.	And it is fitting that you leave no cause behind the second birth.
E cum tu auras complida tota la tua opperacio, lahoras aministra aquo que havem dit de la curacio en les apostemas cautz les quals accideysso de la mayre.	And when you have completed all your operation, then administer the water as we have said for the cure of apostemes which occur in the mother.
E si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras deyssendas en ayguas stipticas e aministra l’autra curacio.	And if there occurs a flow of blood, then you should induce it into astringent waters and administer the other cure.
E yeu ja e vist una femna en le ventre de la qual era fet mort, e aprop sobre aquel foc autra veguada emprenhada, e aprop foc mort es le fet autre.	And you have already seen a woman in whose womb was a dead child, and accordingly on that same spot another pregnancy had begun, and accordingly the dead child is the other.
Accidit al u aprop lonc temps apostema en le sieu embelic; e inflat es entro que foc ubert, e comensec a getar brac.	It happened to him that a long time ago an apostema occurred in his navel; and it swelled up into a hot inflammation, and began to discharge pus.
E yeu fu appelhat a la cura de lu, e medicat a lu per lonc temps, e la plagua no es consolidada.	And you were called upon to cure him, and treated him for a long time, and the wound was not consolidated.
Adonc yeu pausegui sobre lu de alscunas causas emplastra de forta atraccio, e eyssic de lu un os, e aprop passero alcus jorns, e eyssic un autre os; e yeu fu trop meravilhat, cum en le ventre no sia os.	Then I placed over him some poultices of strong attraction, and extracted from him a bone, and accordingly after some days, another bone was extracted; and I was very astonished, since in the womb there is no bone.
E adonc yeu cogitegui que eran dels osses del fet mort.	And then I thought that they were the bones of the dead child.
Donc yeu enguisigui la plagua, e extrayssi de lu motz osses , la femna existent en las sieuas milhos disposicios, e ja visquec en tal manieyra per lonc temps, correc de lu un petit de brac.	Therefore I bandaged the wound, and extracted from him many bones, the woman existing in her usual dispositions, and already living in such a manner for a long time, bore a small child.
E yeu no afermegui asso esser stranh, sino quar en aquo es sciensa e ajutori ad aquo que le metge artifec am la ma per curacio aministra.	And I did not marvel at this being strange, but because in this is science and aid to that which the physician by art and skill administers with his hands for healing.
De las formas dels instrumentz que so necessaris a extrayre le fet.	Of the forms of the instruments that are necessary to extract the child.
Forma de vertitge am la qual es uberta la mayre:	The shape of the uterus, which is opened up in the mother:
