Aquesta es la forma de strenhedor en le qual so engualhatz les libres, al qual engualhament sian dos virtitges en doas extremitatz de dos futz.	This is the shape of a strengthener in which are joined the liberties, at which joining there are two uteruses in two extremities of two feet.
May empero aquesta virtitge cove que sia pus subtil de strictori, e sia fayt o de eba o de fust de boys.	But this uterus must be made more subtle than the strictor, and made of ebony or boxwood.
E sia la latitut de quascun fust quays dos ditz e le marge de quascu amdos quays un dit, e la longitut de quascu es un palm e mig; e en le mieg loc de dos fustz so dos ajustaments de aquel meteys fustz les quals ja son fermatz, dels quals la longitut es la maytat de un palm e un pauc mes, e la latitut de quascu es quay dos ditz, o un pauc mes.	And the latitude of each stick is two fingers and a margin on both sides, one finger, and in the middle part of two sticks are two adjustments made by those sticks which are already fixed, of which the length is half a palm and a little more, and the latitude of each is two fingers or a little more.
E aquestz dos additamentz sian entromeses en la boca de la mayre per que sia uberta am aquels quan tu revolves las doas prescriptas virtigges.	And these two adjustments are inserted in the mouth of the mother so that it is opened up with them when you revolve the two prescribed uteruses.
Forma autra semblant de aquela pus subtil e pus leugiera:	Another shape similar to that, more subtle and lighter:
Sia fayta de fustz de eba o de boys segon la semblansa de forceps.	Is made of ebony or boxwood sticks according to the likeness of forceps.
Mays empero en la extremitat de lu so dos additament ayssi cum vezes, e la longitut de aquels additament es quays un palm, e la latitut de quascu es dos ditz.	But in the extremity of it there are two additions like that, and the length of those additions is one palm, and the latitude of each is two fingers.
E cum tu vols am aquels ubrir la mayre, lahoras tu fay cezer la femna sobre le lieyt les pes pendentz, ubert aquo que es entre las coyssas de lu.	And when you want to open the mother with those, then you must place the woman on a bed, her feet hanging down, and open up what is between her thighs.
E aprop obre la tua ma am le instrument ayssi cum fas am forfexs engualment segon la quantitat que vols de la aprecio de la boca de la mayre entro que la metrona fassa so que vols.	And accordingly place your hand on the instrument, as you would with forceps, in equal measure according to the quantity you want of the appreciation of the mouth of the mother until she does what you want.
La forma de vertitge la qual diysero les antics:	The shape of the uterus which they called the "ancients":
Forma de impellent am le qual es empellit le fet:	The shape of a prompter, with which the child is prompted:
Forma de amisidat2 am le qual es conterit le cap gran	The shape of a reducer, with which the large head is reduced:
E es asemblat a forceps al qual so dentz en la extremitat, ayssi cum vezes, e alcunas veguadas es fayt lonc ayssi cum forceps segon aquesta forma, ayssi cum vezes, al qual so dentz ayssi cum dentz de ressegua am le qual es inscidit e conterit.	And it is assembled to forceps, with which there are teeth at the extremity, like times, and some times it is made long like forceps according to this shape, like times, with which there are teeth like the teeth of a saw, into which it is inserted and reduced.
Forma de amesidat pauc:	The shape of a reducer little:
Forma de unci havent una spina:	The shape of a finger with one spine:
Forma de unci havent doas spinas:	The shape of a finger with two spines:
Forma de forceps a la qual so dentz de cerra am le qual le cap del fet sia conterit:	The shape of forceps to which there are teeth like a saw, with which the head of the child is reduced.
Forma de spatum havent dos extremitatz am le qual le cap es abscindit:	The shape of a spatula having two extremities, with which the head is split:
Forma de dos espatums latz:	The shape of two broad spatulas:
Totz aquels instrumentz so excersitatz, e quan mes so multiplicadas las specias de aquel e so preparadas deves le artifexs, quant es pus leugier a la sua opperacio e pus aut deves les homes per la sua quantitat.	All those instruments are exercised, and when more species of that and prepared by the artists, as much is easier for their operation and higher than what men can do by their quantity.
E no obres de aquels instrumentz ja sia qua sia deves tu aparalhat, quar la necessitat de aquels no es excusabla.	And you must not omit to use those instruments in any case, for the necessity of them is not excusable.
De extraccio de la segondina.	Of the extraction of the second birth.
Quan la segondina es retenguda deves le enfantament, lahoras cove que tu comandes a la malautae que retengua le sieu ale, e aprop fay aquela stornudar am condizi, e strenh la tua ma sobre la boca de lu e sobre las nars de lu, e si per aysso es defora eyssit, bo es.	When the second birth is retained, then it is fitting that you command the woman to retain her breath, and accordingly make her cough, and strengthen your hand on the mouth of her and on her nose, and if by this means it is brought out, well it is.
E sino, lahoras tu pren una ola e perfora en la cuberta un trauc e pausa en aquela erbas ubrent la boca de la mayre, ayssi cum calament e ruda e anet e camamilla e scicados arabic e cassia lignea e santaurea.	And if not, then take a cloth and perforate it in the lid of a casket and pause on that herb which burns the mouth of the mother, like calamus and rue and anise and camomile and Arabic scordium and cassia wood and saint-honorius.
Totas aquestas erbas o alcunas de lor sian submersas en aygua en la ola, e pausa aquela sobre le foc.	All these herbs or some of them are submerged in water in the cloth, and pause it on the fire.
E aprop pausa una canula de canaviera en la boca de la mayre, e tengua aquela entro que la evapor vengua a la concavitat de la mayre.	And accordingly place a cane made of hemp in the mouth of the mother, and hold it until the vapor comes to the concavity of the mother.
E aprop fay aquela stornudar ayssi cum havem dit, e la segondina sira fora-getada am velocitat.	And accordingly make her cough as we have said, and the second birth is brought out quickly.
Mays si roman aprop aquesta curacio e no es eyssida, lahoras tu comanda a la matrona que submerge la sua ma sinistra en oli sizami o en micellage de altea, e aprop entrometa aquela en le conh e queresca am aquela la segondina, e cum aquela auras trobada, lahoras pren la e exten aquela pauc a pauc Mays si es annexsa en le preon de la mayre, lahoras entrometa la sua ma segon que havem recomtat, e quan aura trobat la segondina, extragua aquela petit a petit segon rectetut per so que la mayre no caja deves la atraccio vehement.	But if this cure does not work and the second birth is not brought out, then you command the midwife to immerse her left hand in sassafras oil or in a mixture of altaica, and accordingly insert it into the womb and seek out the second birth, and when you have found it, then take it and extend it little by little. But if it is annexed in the prepuce of the mother, then insert your hand according to what we have recounted, and when you have found the second birth, extract it gradually, according to rectitude, so that the mother does not faint from the vehement attraction.
Abantz cove que sia permudada als costatz dreyt e sinestre am facilitat.	Beforehand, it is fitting that it be permeated into the right and left sides with ease.
E aprop sia ajustat en la quantitat de atraccio, quar ela obedira e evasira de adhirencia.	And accordingly it should be adjusted in the quantity of attraction, for it will obey and depart from adhering.
E si la boca de la mayre es coartada, nos ja havem recomtat la curacio am sturnutacio e am medicacio de la ola am erbas.	And if the mouth of the mother is contracted, we have already recounted the cure with coughing and medication with the cloth and herbs.
Mays si no es fora-getada am totas las causas las quals havem recomtadas, lahoras guarda te que no fetigues sobre aquela en iteracio de abstracio, mays empero cove que aquo que es eyssit de lu a la boca de la mayre lies a la coyssa de la femna, e aprop cristeriza aquela am enguent e tetrafarmacon; quar aquel fara poyrir aquela aprop alcus dias e sira dissolvuda e sira fora-getada.	But if it is not brought out by all the causes which we have recounted, then beware that you do not fatigue yourself in iteration of abstraction, but rather it is fitting that what has issued from there to the mouth of the mother lies at the side of the woman, and accordingly anoint it with enguent and tetra-pharmaceutical; for this will make it rot after a few days and be dissolved and brought out.
Mays quan se poyreys, es de lu elevada mala audor al cap, e al estomac, e aquo ledeys la malauta; e adonc cove que sian aministradas sub-fumiguacios e convenientz ad aquo.	But when it rots, it rises to the bad authority of the head and stomach, and this leads the patient; and then it is fitting that sub- fumigations and conveniences should be administered according to what.
Mays alcus dels Antics ja so esproatz sub-fumigacio de nazitort e de figuas seccas.	But some of the Ancients have already been proven to use sub-fumigation with Nazitor and dried figs.
Forma de instrument am le qual la femna es sub-fumiguada deves la retentio de mestruas e de la segondina:	The shape of an instrument by which the woman is sub-fumigated for the retention of menses and second birth:
Sia fayta de veyre o de eram.	Is made of beaver or earthenware.
E sia pausada la extremitat subtil en le conh e la extremitat ampla sobre le foc, e la sub-fumiguacio sia pausada sobre las brazas del foc.	And is placed the subtle extremity in the womb and the wide extremity over the fire, and the sub-fumigation is placed over the arms of the fire.
E tengua aquela entro que sia consumida aquela sub-fumiguacio e itera·n autra.	And hold it until that sub-fumigation is consumed and another iteration occurs.
De curacio del cul del enfant no-perforat.	Of the cure for the child's unperforated navel.
Motz enfantz naysso e les culs de lu no so perforatz, les quals ya ciphac subtil e opilat.	Many children are born with navels that are not perforated, which are covered with a subtle and opaque film.
Adonc cove a la matrona que perfore am le sieu dit aquel ciphac; e sino, perfora aquel am spatum agut, e guarda se que no toque le lacert.	Then it is fitting for the midwife to pierce with her finger that film; and if not, pierce it with a sharp spatula, and take care not to touch the navel.
E aprop pause sobre aquel lana enfusa en vi e oli; e aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia senat.	And accordingly apply some lanolin infused in wine and oil; and accordingly cure that with unguent until it is clean.
Mays si temes que sia opilat, lahoras pausa en le trauc una canula per motz dias, e osta la quan le enfant voldra degerir.	But if you fear that it may be obstructed, then place a tube in the wound for many days, and remove it when the child will desire to evacuate.
E ja accideys oppilacio del cul per consolidacio de plagua o de apostema; adonc cove que aquela consolidacio sia inscidida, e aprop sia curada am aquo que avem dit de la curacio e del plom.	And if there is obstruction of the navel due to consolidation of wound or aposteme; then it is fitting that this consolidation be pierced, and accordingly cured with water as we have said for the cure and with lead.
De curacio de las fistulas que endeveno dejos.	Of the cure for the fistulas which are left behind.
Las fistulas que endeveno en la partida dejos pus bassa so nodacio e grossetut las quals endeveno prop del cul defora o en l’espazi de la una partida.	The fistulas that are left behind in the departure, which are lower down and thicker, and those that are located near the navel outside or in the space of one part.
E es una fistula o motas.	And it is a single fistula or multiple ones.
E cum aquela nodacio es antiquada e corr de la humiditat aygosa blanca o poyridura subtil, e alcunas veguadas so de aquestas fistulas alcunas penetrantz.	And when that swelling is antiquated and flows with white or subtle pus, and some of these fistulas are penetrating.
E aquelas penetrantz so conogudas per aquo que es eyssit de aquelas per la egressio e per ventosetat; e alcunas vetz use le malaute de egressio, e fort leu es eyssit de aquelas verm.	And those that are penetrating are known by what is issued from them through the egress and ventilation; and sometimes the patient uses the egress, and then a little blood is issued from them.
E so de aquelas fistulas alcunas veguadas en l’espazi penetrantz entro a la vesica, e entro al meat de la vergua; e so de aquelas penetrantz entro la junctura de la coyssa e entro al notz de la coeta.	And some of those fistulas penetrate into the space and enter the bladder, and into the urethra of the penis; and some of those that are penetrating enter the juncture of the thigh and into the notch of the hip.
E aquo en que es conoguda fistula penetrant entro al cul e no-penetrant, es que tu metas le tieu dit endic en le cul, e entrometas tenta subtil de eram o de ferr en la fistula quan no y es turtuositat.	And the way to know whether a penetrating fistula enters the navel and does not penetrate is that you place your finger inside the navel, and then carefully introduce a thin probe made of earthenware or iron into the fistula when there is no resistance.
Mays si en aquela es turtuositat, lahoras entromet en aquela tenta subtil de plom o de pels de caval entro que tu sentas la tenta o le pel en le tieu dit.	But if there is resistance in that, then insert into it a subtle probe made of lead or the fur of a horse until you feel the probe or the fur on your finger.
E si no sentas aquela de tot ni no procezeys del trauc alcuna causa de egestio ni verm ni ventositat, ayssi cum havem dit, lahoras sapias que es no-penetrant, e lahoras coyta te a la curacio.	And if you do not feel it at all or there is no passage of the tube from any cause of emission, blood, or ventilation, just as we have said, then you will know that it is non-penetrating, and accordingly, consult with the cure.
E quan la fistula es penetrant entro a la vesica o entro al meat de la vergua, lahoras la significacio de lu es eyssiment de urina de aquela e prohibicio de lu ad aysso que·l loc am medicina sia consolidat.	And when the fistula is penetrating into the bladder or into the urethra of the penis, then the significance of it is issuing forth with urine from that place and prohibition of it to such an extent that the location where medicine is consolidated.
Mays si es penetrant entro la junctura de la coyssa o entro al os e envencio de dolor en le circuit, lahoras senhal de lu es que la tenta perve entro aqui si en lu no es turtuositat entro al os, e envencio de dolor en le circuit de la partida; e que de lu yeys poyredura tostemps; e que no val en aquela medicacio, ni es consolidada am enguent.	But if it is penetrating into the juncture of the thigh or into the bone and causing intense pain in the circuit, then the sign of it is that the probe will enter here if there is no resistance in the bone, and intense pain in the circuit of the departure; and that from there pus will flow constantly; and that it does not take with that medication, nor is consolidated with unguent.
E en totas aquelas fistulas penetrant no es curacio de tot, e la curacio de aquelas es trebalh e vanetat dels folyls metges sobre·l qual so fermatz.	And in all those penetrating fistulas there is not complete cure, and the cure of them is the toil and vexation of the learned physicians on which we have fixed.
Mays en aquela que no es penetrant e no antiqua, sanacio am ferr es sperada segon que yeu a tu recomtare, e aquo que ja yeu e proat.	But in that which is not penetrating and does not decay, the healing with iron is expected according to what I have recounted and proved.
E es que le malaute jagua entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos e eleva las cambas de lu entro sus, las coyssas sian enclinadas al ventre de lu, e aprop entromet tenta de plom, o de eram si es en la fistula turtuositat, entro que sapias le loc on perve la tenta.	And it is that the patient lies down between your knees above his or her back and raises their legs up to yours, with the thighs sloping towards the belly of the patient, and accordingly inserts a probe made of lead or earthenware into the fistula if there is resistance, until you know the location where the probe fits.
E si aquela sent le malaute entorn le cuol, lahora cove que tu entrometas le tieu dit endic en le cuol.	And if the patient feels pain around the navel, then it is fitting that you insert your finger into the navel.
E si sentas en le tieu dit la tenta ja per si meteyssa descuberta penetrar, otra aquo que sentas entre le tieu dit e aquela siphac o carn, lahoras sapias certanament que aquela es penetrant; e adonc no trebalhes en aquela, quar no es en aquela sanacio, ayssi cum havem dit.	And if you feel the probe already having gone in and penetrating, or if you feel between your finger and that siphac or flesh, then you will certainly know that it is penetrating; and accordingly, do not trouble yourself with it, as we have said.
Mays empero diyssero alcus que es sana en alcus homes tart.	But however, some people may say that it cures in some cases, although it may not always be so.
E de la medicacio per la qual es sperat juvament en lu es que tu ignes cauteri subtil segon le ample de la fistula, ayssi cum es precedit, e intrometas aquel ignit en la fistula entro que pervengua entorn le cuol; e aprop itera aquel doas o tres vetz entro que sapias que ja son adhustas totas aquelas carns ajustadas fistuladas que so semblantz a cana de pluma de ausel.	And the medicine by which one hopes for improvement in that is that you make a subtle cauterization according to the size of the fistula, just as has been preceded, and then insert that ignited substance into the fistula until it pervades around the navel; and accordingly repeat this process two or three times until you know that all those adjusted fleshy parts that are resembling the quill of an eagle have been adjusted.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder entro que en yescan totas aquelas carns que so adhustas, e aprop cura aquela am medicinas la carn engendrantz e consolidantz, e si es sanada, bo es; e sino, lahoras no es sana en degun temps per autra curacio.	And accordingly cure that with calques wrapped in parchment until all those adjusted fleshy parts are cooked; and accordingly cure that with medicines that generate and consolidate flesh, and if it is cured, well it is; and if not, then it will not be cured in any time through another cure.
E si la tenta intra, e no penetra entro·l tieu dit le qual es en le cul, e entre aquel e la tenta que es velament spes de carn o de ciphac, e vezes la fistula en aquo que siec la superficia de la codena, lahoras secca la codena del comensament de la fistula, e tu ve seccan am la tenta, e sia en la fistula entro que la seccio pervengua al loc en le qual perve la extremitat de la tenta, e per la tenta es liberat e catz.	And if the probe goes in and does not penetrate into the navel which is in the navel, and between that and the probe which is a subtle specer of flesh or film, and the fistula is opened on that surface where the codon is, then dry the codon from the beginning of the fistula, and you see drying with the probe, and it is in the fistula until the drying reaches the location where the extremity of the probe emerges, and by the probe is freed and cut.
E aprop mundifiqua aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so asembladas a canula de pena de ausel e no romangua de aquelas alcuna causa.	And accordingly, cleanse those fleshy parts that are gathered like the quill of an eagle and do not remain from any cause.
Mays si flux de sanc vezes que vengua entre tu e la tua opperacio quan ensideysses aquelas carns, lahoras le milh que sia e del pus leugier instrument es cauterizar am foc o am medicina acuta, quar cauteri am foc ajusta bonas doas habitutz: so es adhustio de aquelas carns ajustadas, e abscizio del sanc exseccacio de las humiditatz.	But if the flow of blood comes and goes between you and your operation when you are cleansing those fleshy parts, then take a mile that is and use the least painful instrument to cauterize with fire or sharp medicine, for cauterization with fire adjusts two good habits: it adjusts the adjustment of those adjusted fleshy parts, and abscizes the blood excess of humidities.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder o en caus trissat entro que·l loc geta brac, e aprop lahoras cura la plagua am enguentz carn dura engendran e consolidan.	And accordingly, cure that with calques wrapped in parchment or in three-fold cloth until the wound gets its breadth, and accordingly, cure the wound with unguents of hard flesh that generate and consolidate.
E so medicinas en las quals so stipticitat e exseccio; quan lahoras es restaurada ja es sanada e no temes iteracio.	And such medicines which have astringency and excess; when it is restored, then it is healed and you do not fear relapse.
Mays si la fistula ja perve entro al preon del cul e es elonguada de lu superficia del cos, lahoras entromet le tieu dit en le cul e inquireys am aquel.	But if the fistula has penetrated into the perineum of the navel and is elongated from its surface on the body, then insert your finger into the navel and investigate with that.
E donc si centes la tenta e entre tu e ela es velament de ciphac o de carn, e es propda a la penetracio, lahora no es operacio en lu sino segon via di fiducia e de speransa.	And therefore, if you find the probe and it is subtly of film or flesh, and is propitious to penetration, then there is no operation in that place except according to the way of faith and hope.
La qual causa es aministrar en lu una de tres manieyras: o que cauterize aquela ayssi cum havem dit; o que secces aquela entro que consieguas la conquavitat de lu per que sia a tu possible entrometre las qualcas e la curacio propdana; e no procesiscas mot am seccio per so que no inscidas le lacert contenent le cuol, e que accidisque sobre le malaute eyssiment de la egistio ses voluntat; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit quar fort leu sira sanat; o que elongues aquel velament e mondes aquel pus que seccas aquel entro prop le cul, ayssi cum havem dit, o am tenta o am autre instrument de aguda extremitat, e aprop mondifique aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so en la seccio entro la on podes am percrustacio; e aprop esforsa te a far la restauracio de tota la plagua am seccio, e si le orrifici pus desus no es consolidat, e romangua la fistula uberta en la partida del cul, e sira pus leugier per le malaute.	The cause is to administer in that place one of three ways: either to cauterize it as we have said; or to dry it out until you achieve the conquest of that place so that it is possible for you to insert some and apply the propitious cure; and do not proceed with drying because you do not want to insert the navel containing the belly, and what happens is that the patient's will is expressed; and accordingly, cure that with water as we have said, because very soon it will be healed; or elongate that film and cleanse that pus that dries out there into the propitious place, just as we have said, either with a probe or another instrument of sharp extremity, and accordingly cleanse those fleshy parts fistulated which are in the drying process until you can perform percrustation; and accordingly, strive to achieve the restoration of all the wound with drying, and if the upper opening is not consolidated, and the fistula remains open on the side of the navel, it will be easier for the patient.
E alscunas veguadas la fistula es finida segon aquesta manieyra: es quan tu entrometas la tenta en la fistula, e es en le latz del cul entorn la superficia del cos am la codena e en le marge del cul, lahoras pren tenta de perforada extremitat, que es ayssi cum agulha de preparantz les coers segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes the fistula is closed in this way: when you insert the probe into the fistula, and it is in the navel area around the surface of the body with the coden and on the margin of the navel, then take a tentative perforation that is like an awl preparing the hearts according to this form:
e entromet en aquela fiel envolopat de v fiels o entorn aquels; e aprop entromet tenta am fiel en la fistula entro que consiegua la conquavitat de lu.	and insert it into that faithful wrapping of five faithful ones or around those; and accordingly, insert the probe with faith in the fistula until you achieve the conquest of that place.
Mays si es penetrant en le marge del cul prop dedintz, lahoras tu extratz le fiel de aquel trauc ayssi que tu intrometas le tieu dit en le cul; e extraguas la extremitat del fiel e ajustes las duas extremitatz essemps, e estrenh cascuna, e leyssa aquo per un dia o per dos, e quan mays inscideys le fiel en la carn, estrenh be aquel entro que aquelas carns sian inscididas las quals so entre doas extremitatz del fiel e que cajan.	But if it is penetrating in the margin of the navel proper to the backside, then you extract the thread from that channel and insert your finger into the navel; and extract the extremity of the thread and adjust the two extremities together, and strengthen each one, and leave it like that for a day or two, and when you have inserted the thread into the flesh, strengthen it well so that those fleshy parts are stitched which are between the two extremities of the thread and fall.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia consolidada e sanada.	And accordingly, cure the wound until it is consolidated and healed.
Mays si le orrifici de la fistula no es penetrant, lahoras fay aquel penetrar, en qualque manieyre sia a tu preparat, sino que sia mot en le preon, quar no es a tu que fassas aquo per que no inscidas le lacert; e aprop fay am aquela entro que sia sanada.	But if the opening of the fistula is not penetrating, then make it penetrate in whatever way you are prepared, but not in the navel, for it is not your place to do so; and accordingly, do that until it is healed.
La forma de spatum spinos am lo qual es fenduda la fistula: la curvitat del qual es mot aguda e l’autra partida es no-aguda, per so que no inscidas aquo que no es necessari, ayssi cum vezes.	The shape of the spatulum with which the fistula is divided: its curvature is very sharp on one side and not sharp on the other, so that you do not insert what is unnecessary, just as sometimes.
De sutura de emorroydas en las quals corra sanc en la inscizio de aquelas.	Of the suturing of hemorrhoids in which blood flows during the insertion of those.
Emorroydas so segon dos manieyras, quar o so entre le cul semblantz aysi que es de carbos, o quays aquelas sian cum a gras de rasim.	Hemorrhoids are according to two ways, for either they are between the navel like coal, or those that are like grass on a rye field.
E de aquelas so petitas e grans, e que le sanc corr de aquelas tostemps e es una, e so motas, e so fora·l cul, e en las extremitatz de lu.	And of those that are small and large, and that the blood flows from them constantly and is one, or many, and that they are outside the navel, and in the extremities thereof.
Mays empero aquelas que so foro le cul so segon las mes de pauca humiditat, de las quals corr aygua citrina o un petit de sanc am cos continuabla, e so segon la color del cos.	But however, those that are outside the navel are according to the degrees of little humidity, from which clear water or a small amount of blood flows with continuous flow, and according to the color of the skin.
E la curacio de aquela que es dedintz le cuol es que comandes al malaute que se assela e que se exprema entro que le cuol yesca e las emoroydas apparescan a tu.	And the cure for that which is behind the navel is that you command the patient to settle and to be quiet until the navel is cleansed and the hemorrhoids appear to you.
Adonc tu te coyte e suspen am uncis o que tenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, e aprop incideys aquelas deves las suas razitz.	Then take hold of them with your nails or what you have, and accordingly cut off those roots.
Mays si les uncis no so tengutz en aquelas per la humiditat de lor e mollificacio de aquelas, lahoras pren aquelas am drap aspre o am coto o am flassada de lana, e extratz aquelas am les tieus ditz, e aprop inscideys aquelas e polveriza sobre lor alcunas polveras caudas aprop la inscizio, per que sian ad aquelas en loc de cauteri; o cauteriza aquelas segon que es precedit en le capitol de cauterizar.	But if the nails are not caught in those due to their moisture and softening, then take those with a rough cloth or with a thread or with a woolen floss, and extract those with your fingers, and accordingly cut off those roots and powder some powders suitable for cauterization near the incision, so that they are applied to those places in place of cauterization; or cauterize them according to what has been preceded in the chapter on cauterizing.
E aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And accordingly, cure those with the other cure until they are healed.
E si le cul no obezeys a egressio, lahoras cristerisa le malaute am cristeri en le qual sia mordicacio petita, e sia lavat am aquel aquo que es en le cuol e que obezesca a egressio leugierament quan le malaute s’esprem.	And if the navel does not obey emission, then anoint the patient with a little mordicating ointment on the navel area, and wash it with that water which is in the navel and which will obey emission slightly when the patient is pressed.
Mays si las emorroydas so defora le cul, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiera, e es que tu prenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, o que prenguas aquelas am unci, e inscidas aquelas, e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit entro que sian sanadas.	But if the hemorrhoids are outside the navel, then the cause of theirs is light, and it is that you take them with your fingernail or with a small knife, and cut off those roots, and accordingly cure those with water as we have said until they are healed.
E aquel que avoreys inscizio, cove que aministres sutura de lor segon aquesta manieyra: pren fiel envolopat e entromet aquel en agulha e aprop extratz las emorroydas a las partidas dessus, e fay aquel penetrar am la agulha en la razit del autra part, e envolveys las doas extramitatz del fiel en la partida pus dejos de la agulha, e so latitudinalment; e estrenh la emorroyda am strectura fort, e aprop noza le fiel e extratz la agulha.	And he who has an incision, must minister the suturing of them according to this way: take a thread wrapped around and insert that into the needle and accordingly extract the hemorrhoids from the upper parts, and make it penetrate into the root of the other part, and wrap the two extremities of the thread in the more distant part of the needle, and so latitudinally; and strengthen the hemorrhoid with strong traction, and accordingly remove the thread and needle.
E fay aquo a totas, e layssa de aquelas una e no la cozes, per so que la superfluitat del sanc corra de aquela.	And do this to all of them, and leave one alone and don't cauterize it, so that the superfluity of blood flows from that one.
E aprop pausa sobre le cul drap enfus en oli rozat o en cerot; e pausa aquel sobre·l cuol e comanda al malaute que·s repause.	And accordingly, press a cloth soaked in rose oil or cerate onto the navel area, and press that onto the navel and command the patient to rest.
E aprop layssa aquela entro que caja; e quan es casuda, cura aquelas am enguentz o am autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And accordingly, leave that alone until it forms a scab; and when it is scabbed over, cure those with unguents or other remedies until it is healed.
De curacio de fistulas.	The Cure of Fistulas.
Motas veguadas accideys per exseccacio de fenda o per costriccio de natura.	Many times accidents happen due to excess of fissure or constriction of nature.
E cum so antiquadas e no val en aquela medicina, lahoras cove que tu razas aquelas am la puncta de spatum o am la tua ungla entro que sian faytas humidas e sia hostada de aquelas la escorsa pus desus, la qual prohibeys aquelas de consolidacio; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian consolidadas.	And since they are ancient and do not work with that medicine, then it is necessary to cut them off at the point of spatula or with your fingernail until they become moist and host the scab above, which prevents consolidation; and accordingly, cure those until they are consolidated.
Lahoras tu osta aquelas am razio pus vehement que la primieyra entro que mot sancno e sian excoriadas; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian sanadas.	Then you must cut those off at the root, more fiercely than the first time, until they bleed much and are excoriated; and accordingly, cure those until they are healed.
De curacio de almesamir, so es clau.	The Cure of Almesamir, is key.
Sapias que alamermar, so es clau, e no es si no notz redon segon la color del cors semblant a cap de claviel, e es fayt en tot le cors e majorment en las partidas dejos les pes e als ditz, e endeve per aquels dolor deves le anament.	Know that Almesamir is key, and it is not so unless the notes are red on the color of the skin resembling a cap of clover, and it is made throughout the body and especially in the parts left behind by the feet and hands, and it involves through those pains the desire for love.
E adonc cove que sia inscidit aquo que es en le circuit del clau, e sia tengut am les forfexs o am unci, e sia eradicat de la sua razit; e aprop cura aquel.	And then it is necessary to cut out what is in the circle of the key, and to hold it with forceps or small knives, and to eradicate its root; and accordingly cure that.
E si vols, cauteriza le segont que es precedit en le sieu capitol.	And if you wish, cauterize according to what is preceded in the chapter on cauterizing.
Mays de veruca es eminencia petita aspre fistulada redonda sobre la superficia del cos, e motas veguadas veno en las mas dels enfantz.	But of verucca, it is a small, hard, fistulous prominence on the surface of the body, and many times appears in the majority of children.
E curacio de lu es que estendas e inscidas aquela, o que estrenhas aquela am fiel o am pel entro que caja.	And the cure for it is to stretch and cut it off, or to strengthen it with a thread or a piece of cloth until it forms a scab.
E si vols, cauteriza aquo, segon que havem dit, am foc o am medicina acuta.	And if you wish, cauterize that according to what we have said, with fire or sharp medicine.
E ja so eradicadas enversas e no-enversas am le instrument le qual yeu diyre.	And already removed inwards and outwards with the instrument which you will say.
Mays formica es eminencia petita feutrada o fistulada grossa sobre la superficia del cos anant mot en le preon, e quan le freg atroba aquela es centit en lu semblant de mordificacio de formigua, e es fayta entorn le cos.	But formica is a small, fatty or fistulous prominence on the surface of the body approaching the navel, and when it is touched by the finger, it seems to be bitten by an ant, and is made around the body.
E curacio de lu es que prenguas una canula de pena de auca o de pena de voltor, e sia fort, e pausa aquela sobre la formigua entro que la contengua le cercle de la canula de las partidas de lu; e aprop revolveys la tua ma am la canula entro que inscidas aquo que es en le circuit de la formigua, e pauses aquela en le preon de la carn, e que eradiques la formigua de la sua razit.	And the cure for it is that you take a reed pen or a votar pen, and it should be strong, and press that on the formica until it contains the circle of the pen in its parts; and accordingly revolve your hand with the pen until you cut out what is in the circuit of the formica, and then pause that in the navel of the flesh, and that eradicates the formica from its root.
E si vols, fay aquo am canula de eram o de ferr segon aquesta forma:	And if you wish, do it with a reed pen or an iron pen according to this form:
Sia la partida desus de la canulha trahent a subtilitat, sorda (so es no-perforada), envolopada per so que sobre le dit la aprencio de lu sia ablaviada e la revolucio de aquela.	Be the upper part of the pen tip slightly sharp, not perforated, wrapped in order that on the said part of the skin, the ablution of it may be performed and the revolution of that.
E si vols cauteriza la formiga segon que es denant dit en la cauterizacio de atheyl en le capitol de cauteri.	And if you wish, cauterize the formica according to what is said before in the chapter on cauterizing.
De forma dels instrumentz que so aministratz a dar cristeri.	The Form of the Instruments that are Administered to Give Cautery.
Alcunas veguadas es fayt cristeri de argent o de lato o de eram fondut o malleat; e alcunas veguadas es fayt de aquels instrumentz petit e gran segon aquels als quals so aministratz, quar aquel que es aministrat en la curacio dels petitz enfants sia petit; e de aquel dels quals los culs son freuls o doloyrozes, les cristeris de aquels sian petitz.	Sometimes it is made cauterization of silver or lead or melted iron or hammered; and sometimes it is made with those small and large instruments according to what is administered, for that which is administered in the cure of little children is small; and of those whose buttocks are rough or sore, their cauterizations shall be small.
La forma de cristeri gran e pauc:	The Form of Great Cautery.
Le cap de la canula de lu desus en le qual es liada la borsa sia ampla segon aquesta manieyra; e sia a lu distinacio la on la borsa es liada ayssi cum vezes.	The head of the reed pen above, in which the bag is tied, should be broad according to this way; and there should be a distinction at the point where the bag is tied, just as sometimes.
E la extremitat de lu pus dejus, la qual es entromesa en le cul, sia sorda (so es no-uberta) mot leon, atrasent a subtilita; e en la un del latz de lu sian dos traucs, e en l’autre costat un trauc, e sia la amplesa del trauc segon la groseza dels rays e pus gros un petit.	And the extremity of it, which is inserted into the navel, should be blunt (not open) like a lion's tooth, with subtlety; and on one side of it there are two holes, and on the other side one hole, and the width of the hole should be according to the thickness of the rays and slightly thicker than small.
E sia la borsa en la qual sian pausadas las medicinas de vesica de bestia o de pel de ovelha, e la razit de lu sia un palm.	And it should be a bag in which medicines from the bladder of an animal or sheep's wool are placed, and the root of it should be one palm.
E sia perforada per motz traucs ayssi cum es revolvuda; e si l’espazi le qual es entre les traucs la grossetut del dit.	And it should be pierced with many small holes just as it is rolled up; and if the space between the holes is the thickness of the said.
E aprop entromet en aquels traucs fiel fort de fiel cru le qual sia de detz fiels, o enviro aquels; e ajusta am aquel la borsa; e quan es pausada en lu la borsa, sia streyt en le cap del cristeri entre dos distingentz am fort costriccio, e aprop cristeriza am aquel quascun trauc: Mays la qualitat de cristerizar am aquel es que tu omples la borsa de la medicina, que sia escalfada segon la quantitat de la tolleransa del malaute; e guarda te que no sia trop cauda ni trop freja.	And accordingly insert the needle into those holes, a strong thread of raw thread which is made from ten threads, or surround them; and adjust that bag to it; and when the bag is placed in it, be tight in the head of the cauterizer between two distinct ones with strong constriction, and accordingly cauterize each hole: But the quality of cauterizing is that you fill the bag with medicine, which should be warmed according to the quantity of the tolerance of the patient; and take care that it is not too hot nor too cold.
E aprop le malaute sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos, e eleva las suas cambas en sus e pausa dejos lu un cuer sobre le qual ja so les homes o un lansol; e aprop unta la extramitat del cauteri am oli o am album de huou o am mucellage de fenugrec o de semblantz; e aprop entromet aquel en le cul am facilitat, e aprop le ministre prengua la borsa e exprema aquel am doas mas e essemps am vehemencia entro que sia evacuat en le budelh tot aquo que es en le cristeri; e aprop extra le cristeri e le malaute leva las suas cambas a la paret.	And accordingly the patient should be laid on his back, and raise his knees towards himself, and pause there until one cup is left above which men or lansol; and accordingly apply a small amount of oil or album of honey or mucilage of fenugreek or similar substances to the extremity of the cauterizer; and accordingly insert that into the navel with ease, and accordingly the minister should take the bag and express all that is in the cauterizer into the bucket with two hands and sometimes with great vigor until everything is evacuated from the cauterizer; and accordingly extricate the cauterizer and the patient will lift his knees to the wall.
E si la medicina forsa aquel a eyssiment, tengua le tant quant poyra; e si dorm am aquel per tota una nueyt, es mays derier en juvament.	And if the medicine forces him to sleep similarly, hold it as long as he can; and if he sleeps with that for a whole night, it is more likely to lead to good results.
Mays si tu cristerizas aquel en las malautias de solucio de ventre e l’eyssiment de lu le coyta, lahoras tu itera le cauteri entro que sia sanat.	But if you cauterize that in the diseases of belly flux and navel inflammation, then you must iterate the cauterizer until it is healed.
E si en le cul so emorroydas o apostemas ledens, lahoras sia le cristeri mot subtil e leon, dels cristeris am les quals les enfantz so criterisatz.	And if in the navel there are hemorrhoids or apostemas, then it should be a cauterizer very subtle and lion-like, of those cauterizers with which children are cured.
De curacio de las plaguas.	The Cure of Sores.
Yeu ja e dit en la divisio de la curacio de las plaguas aquo que convenia al libre, e yeu dic assi la curacio de aquelas am ma e am medicinas segon le conpliment.	And thus I have said in the division of the cure of sores above what is fitting for a free person, and I say thus: the cure of those with me and with medicines according to the complement.
Donc dic que las plaguas son diversificadas segon aquo en que son faytas las plaguas e segon le loc sobre le qual cazo las plaquas.	Therefore I say that sores are diversified according to how they are made and according to the place on which the sores occur.
E las causas per que motas vetz son faytas las plaguas so ayssi cum getament de peyra, o inscisio d’espaza o de cotel, o percussio am lansa, o am fustz, o am sageta, o semblantz ad aquels de motas causas.	And the causes by which many times sores are made are just as if from a blow of peyra, or incision with space or cotelet, or striking with lance, or with fist, or with arrow, or similar to those of many causes.
Mays las plaguas que so en les locz del cos so ayssi cum plagua la qual catz sobre le cap, o·l col, o·l pietz, o·l ventre, o·l fitge, e semblantz ad aquels dels membres.	But the sores that are on the parts of the body are like a sore which appears on the head, or on the neck, or on the feet, or on the belly, or on the thigh, and similar to those of the limbs.
E yeu so recomtant la curacio de alcunas plaguas per que pauses aquela ratiocinacio e regla sobre las autras plaguas.	And I recommend the cure for some sores by which you pause that rationalization and rule on other sores.
E yeu comensare de las plaguas del cap simplas, quar la rememoracio de las compostas vindra al comensament del tertz capitol.	And I begin with the sores of the head, simple ones, for the remembrance of the composed ones will come at the beginning of the third capital.
Donc dic que quan accideys en le cap plagua simpla e no es fractura, lahoras considera: si es per getament de peyra o de semblant, e ja ha trinquada la codena tant solament e es gran plagla e temes sobre aquel malaute havinement de apostema caut, lahoras tu te coyta e fleubotoma la cephalica tantost, e no tardas aquo; e extrats ad aquel del sanc segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu si no mes alcuna causa prohibent de fleubotomia, majorment si·l sanc que es eyssit de la plagua es pauc.	Therefore I say: when a simple sore occurs on the head and it is not a fracture, then consider this: if it is due to a blow from a peyra or similar, and already the wound has opened so slightly that it is a large sore and you fear about that patient having an apostema or cauterization, then you must immediately take hold of the cephalic vein and bleed, but not too much; and extract as much blood as necessary according to the quantity of the virtue of the patient's blood, unless there be some other cause prohibiting bleeding, especially if the blood that has issued from the wound is little.
E sia la flaubotomia del contrari de la partida plaguada; e guardase le malaute de replecio e de vi e de viandas grossas.	And be the bleeding on the opposite side of the wounded part; and watch out for the patient's replenishment, and their diet, and their hearty food.
Mays si de la minuicio prohibeys alcuna causa, lahoras sia aminorat de la vianda e no apropinque a carn ni a vi.	But if some cause prohibits from the beginning, then it is advisable to minimize food and not approach meat or wine.
E pausa sobre la plagua, si a lu accideys apostema caut, coto enfus en oli rozat solet o en vi en le qual es stipticat.	And pause on the sore, if an apostema cauterization occurs, cut in with rose oil or wine that is stipticated.
Mays si est segur de apostema caut, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua, si es recent am le sieu sanc e le ayre no ha mudat aquela la polvera la qual yeu recomtare aprop petit.	But if it is sure of apostema cauterization, then pause on the sore, if it is recent with its own blood and the air has not changed that powder which I recommend as proper little.
E si le ayre ja ha mudada aquela, lahoras pausa sobre alscus enguentz entro que sia sanada.	And if the air has already changed that one, then pause on some other unguent until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua es gran o es per inscizio d’espaza e de semblantz, e no so ajustadas las labias de lu per puvils, lahoras ajusta aquelas am sutura segon que yeu recomtare de la sutura de lor.	But if the sore is large or is due to incision with space and similar things, and the lips of it are not adjusted for pus, then adjust those with suture according to what I recommend for their suture.
Mays si la plagua ja es discuberta del os e pen, e no es retencio de lu sino un petit suspensori, lahoras inscideys aquela e aprop cura la plagua am medicinas e restaura la carn aprop en loc de codena, e comanda al malaute que sia pescut de viandas en las quals es groceza: caps e formen coyt e semblantz a lor, entro que sia compost.	But if the sore is already uncovered of bone and flesh, and there is no retention of it but a small suspender, then cut into that and accordingly cure the sore with medicines and restore the flesh according to its location, and command the patient to eat food in which there is grossness: caps and forms of meat and similar things until it is composed.
E si atrobas en la codena putrefaccio e no adhereys al os, lahoras tu inscideys tot aquo poyrit e geta aquo, e aprop cura aquo.	And if you find in the wound putrefaction and it does not adhere to the bone, then cut out all that is putrid and rotten, and accordingly cure it.
Mays si en aquestas plaguas es arteria o vena de la qual fluxs de sanc pot evenir, e no es abscindida per medicinas, lahoras tu inquier sobre la arteria, e si atrobas aquela no-inscidida, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am spatum, o lia aquela; e si necessitat te provoca que aquo que havem dit no comfereys, lahoras tu cauteriza entro que·l sanc sia abscidit.	But if in these sores there is an artery or vein from which blood flux can occur, and it is not abscessed by medicines, then you must inquire about the artery, and if you find that one not incised, then cut into it with spatula, or tie it; and if necessary, it will cause what we have said not to conform, then you must cauterize until the blood is absorbed.
E si aquestas plaguas son simplas e petitas, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiere; enayssi que tu polverizas sobre aquelas aquesta polvera, quar consolidada aquela denant que l’ayre mude aquelas.	And if these sores are simple and small, then the cause of them is light; therefore you must powderize on those this powder, because it will consolidate before the air changes those.
E la manieyra de la polvera es aquesta: recipe oli de enses partida una, de sanc de drago partida doas, de caus no-extincta partidas tres; sia tot mot trissat e crivellat, e de lu sia la plagua omplida, e sia constrengida per bona constriccio entro que be sobre aquela aderesca, e sia coagulada am le sanc.	And the method of the powder is this: take one part of oil of enses, two parts of blood of dragon, and three parts of non-extinct cause; mix it well and crush it thoroughly, and fill the sore with that powder, and constrict it with good constriction until it adheres to the sore, and coagulates with the blood.
E aprop strengeys aquela desus am pulvils e leyssa aquela, e no la deslias mentre esta ayssi que no es apostemada, quar no es eredicada de lu la medicina entro que sia sanada.	And accordingly stretch that powder above with powders and loosen it, and do not remove it while it is like this, so that the medicine is not eradicated from it until it is healed.
E alcuna vetz fa aquo sola cautz, quan no es a tu en present enses e sanc de drago.	And sometimes one makes this alone with caustics, when it is not present to you in the same place as the oil of enses and blood of dragon.
E ja fa aquesta meteyssa operacio en las grans plaguas quan conveneys que sia pausada sobre aquelas e sian streytas, e so plaguas recentz am le lor sanc, las quals le ayre no ha alteradas.	And already this method of operation is done in large sores when it is necessary to pause on those and be stretched, and these sores are recent with their own blood, which the air has not altered.
E si le ayre las ha alteradas, e majorment quan es en temps d’estiu, lahoras no es entencio a la posicio de aquesta polvera, mays adonc cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit, enayssi que tu pauses sobre aquelas alcus enguents degistius, o que pauses sobre aquelas pols de la farina del ordi am aygua e mel entro que getan poyredura; e aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And if the air has altered them, and especially when it is in the time of summer, then do not take thought about the position of this powder, but instead cure those with what we have said, namely by applying some ointments that are dissolved, or by applying powders made from barley flour mixed with water and honey until they produce a poultice; and accordingly cure those with another remedy until they are healed.
Mays si accideys am la plagua fractura en os, e es petita, lahoras tu extratz aquo am gesti.	But if there is a fracture in the bone near the sore, and it is small, then you must extract that with gestures.
E yeu diyre la cura de las fracturas del cap en aquo que es envenidor.	And I will say: the cure for fractures of the head in this way that is venomous.
De las plaguas del col.	The Sores of the Neck.
Mays si la plagua accideys en le col, lahoras no es en lu differencia en medicacio, e entre la plagua del cap quan es simpla.	But if the sore occurs in the neck, then there is no difference in treatment between it and a simple sore of the head.
Mays si ja le nervi del col es inscis o arteria, lahoras si es nervi, no es en lu engen sino que sia evitada curacio de lu am aquo que fa vehement stipticitat, ayssi cum ziniar e zegi que es vetriol e semblantz a lor quar nozo als nervis e contrazo aquel.	But if the nerves of the neck are cut or arteries, then if it is a nerve, do not apply a caustic to it, but rather avoid applying a remedy that causes strong stipticity, such as vinegar and eggs, which are like vitriol and similar things that harm nerves and contract them.
E no pauses sobre la plagua alcuna causa de tot freja, quar la sustancia dels nervis es freja e la continuacio de lu es am le cervel, le qual es le pus aut de totz les membres.	And do not apply any cause to the sore that is completely cold, because the substance of the nerves is cold and their continuation is in the brain, which is the most noble of all the members.
E si’ aquo am que es curat de medicinas leugieras, ayssi cum es caus lavada am aygua dousa, alcuna veguada enfusa en oli rozat o no-rozat, e thucia quan es lavada am aygua dousa e las autras peyras minarantz segon aquesta manieyra, e enguentz humitz.	And if that which is cured by medicines is light, just as it is washed with lukewarm water, some day infused in rose oil or un-rose oil, and thucia when it is washed with lukewarm water and the other minor wounds are treated according to this method, and ointments moist.
Mays si la plagua es gran, lahoras aministra sutura, o coarta las labias de lu, e aprop cura aquela am pulvils entro que sia sanada.	But if the sore is large, then you must apply suture, or compress the lips of it, and accordingly cure that with powders until it is healed.
Mays si a la plagua es profunditat o accideys en lu a la pus bassa partida poyredura, lahoras perfora aquela en le loc mays depremegut.	But if the sore is deep or occurs in the lowest part of the poultice, then you must pierce that in the most depressed location.
Mays si en la plagua ja es inscisa arteria e es conseguit flux de sanc, lahoras separa o secca aquela, o lia aquela, o cauteriza aquela si necessitat te provoca ad aquo.	But if the sore already has an incised artery and there is a flux of blood, then you must separate or dry that, or tie that, or cauterize that if necessity requires it to happen.
Mays si ja ha insciditz les spondils del golayro o tot, e so salvadas las venas del col, lahoras tu ajusta las labias de la codena am sutura sobre la cana del golayro e no toques aquel; abantz egala aquel e reduzeys aquel sobre la sua figura natural, e aprop strenh aquel am strectura decent, e leyssa aquela per alcus jorns; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz en les quals es stipticitat e excitacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the vertebrae of the neck or all have been incised, and the veins of the neck are saved, then you must adjust the lips of the spine with suture over the canal of the neck and do not touch that; before equalizing it and reducing it to its natural shape, and accordingly strengthen it with decent tension, and loosen it for some days; and accordingly cure that with ointments in which there is stipticity and excitement until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua ja en le os a fayta enprecio, lahoras percuireys aquela, e lahoras si en lu ha fragmentz de hos, extratz totz aquels que podes de lor; e aquo que a tu no es apparelhat, leyssa aquo entro que la plagua se poyrisca, e sia separat e la egrecio de lu sia alleujada.	But if the sore has made a impression in the bone, then you must pierce it, and if there are fragments of bone in it, extract all those that you can from them; and as for what is not attached to you, loosen it until the sore subsides, and be separated, and the excrescence of it be alleviated.
E si la plagua es recent lahoras polveriza sobre aquela polvera la qual t’e recomtada.	And if the sore is recent, then powderize on it the powder which I have recommended to you.
Mays si en la plagua es fayta fistula, lahoras cura aquela am aquo del qual la rememoracio vindra aprop en le sieu capitol.	But if the sore has made a fistula, then cure that with what will come to mind in its own capital.
De las plaguas del col o de semblantz quan fayta entre las spallas e es fayta am spaza o am cotel o am lansa o am semblantz.	The Sores of the Neck or Similar Ones when Made Between the Shoulders and is Made with Space or with Cotelet or with Lance or with Similar Things.
Si es percussio de lansa o de cotel, e vezes de lu la profunditat, lahoras considera mays si de la plagua yeys ventositat quan le malaute elena; lahoras sapias que la plagua es mortal.	If it is a blow from a lance or cotelet, and the depth of it is great, then consider more whether the sore is ventilated when the patient complains; know that the sore is mortal.
E si en lu no es profunditat e la plagua es recent am le sieu sanc, lahoras tu pauses en lu de la primieyra horo polvera, e no strenhas aquel per que no sia le sanc retengut en la profunditat de lu e que retorne al cor e que aucigua le malaute, mays pausa en lu enguent atractiu, e deslia aquela doas veguadas le dia.	And if there is no great depth and the sore is recent with its own blood, then pause in it on the first hour powder, and do not strengthen that so that the blood is not retained in the depth of it and does not return to the heart and does not harm the patient; but pause in it attractive ointment, and remove it twice a day.
E si l’enguent no es a tu present, lahoras tu pausa en le orrifici de la plagua coto viel per que sucque aquo que yeys de las humiditatz; e fay que le malaute dorma sobre la plagua per que corra aquo que es en lu ajustat.	And if the ointment is not present, then pause in the orifice of the sore a little bit so that it sucks up what you have from the humidities; and make sure the patient sleeps over the sore so that water flows in it adjusted.
Mays si ja de la plagua son passatz tres dias o mays e no accideys al malaute spasme ni tremor de cor mal ni strictura de ale, e vezes las autras dispozicios bonas de lu, lahoras sapias que plagua es salva; e adonc cura aquela am calguas e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanada.	But if three days or more have passed since the sore occurred and the patient does not experience spasms, nor trembling of the heart, nor constriction of the bile, and other good dispositions are present in them, then know that the sore is saved; and then cure it with calques and with another remedy until it is healed.
Mays si la sanacio de lu es excusada, e ja tot temps es uberta, lahoras sapias que ja es fayta fistula; cura donc aquela per le sieu capitol.	But if the healing of it is excluded, and all time has been opened, then know that already a fistula has been made; cure therefore that according to its own capital.
E si la plagua es per inscisio de spaza o de cotel, e es simpla en la superficia del pietz o del dos, lahoras cura aquela am aquo que es precedit de sutura, si es gran, o am polvera, si es petita.	And if the sore is due to incision with space or cotelet, and it is simple on the surface of the foot or hand, then cure that with what precedes suture, if it is great, or with powder, if it is small.
Mays si ja ha fayta enprecio en le os, e so ja de lu inscizas pessas, lahoras tu torqua la plagua e coyta ad extrayre aquelas pessas, si so separadas.	But if the sore has made an impression in the bone, and there are pieces of bone that are separated from it, then you must twist the sore and pull to extract those pieces, if they are separate.
Mays si no so separadas, lahoras leyssa las entro que se poyresca la plagua, que la extraccio de lor es alleujada.	But if they are not separated, then loosen them until the sore subsides, which will alleviate the extraction of them.
E de las autras plaguas accidentz en les autres membres le juvament en curacio es le juvament de aquo que havem dit.	And for other sores that occur in other members, the judgment in cure is the judgment of what we have said.
De las plaguas del ventre.	The Sores of the Belly.
L’indisposicio la qual accideys en le ventre es o gran, o pauc, o migiera.	The indisposition which occurs in the belly is either great, small, or medium-sized.
De la gran alcunas veguadas yeys le budel o nervi del budel, per que es fayta intromissio de lor e la sutura de lor esser pus vehement e pus subtil.	Of the great ones, some times you will see the belly or nerves of the belly, which is made with an introduction of theirs and the suture of theirs being more violent and more subtle.
E disrupcio petita es fayta dificil per autra manieyra, e siec se que la reduccio de lor es pus dificil, si no te coytes de la intromissio de lor al sieu loc tantost, quar se ubre e es engrossat per que le intrament de lu es fayt difficil.	And small disruption is made difficult by another way, and it is known that the reduction of theirs is more difficult, if you do not take care to introduce them into their place as soon as possible, for it opens up and becomes swollen, making the instrument of them difficult.
E donc la milhor disrupcio es migiera, quar en aquela no es dificil la reduccio del budel, ayssi cum es dificil en las doas specias denant ditas.	And therefore the best disruption is medium-sized, for in that one there is not difficult the reduction of the belly, just as it is difficult in the two species mentioned earlier.
E sapias que sutura del ventre es segon quatre manieyras, mays doas suturas son comunas que conveneysso en suturas de las autras plaguas del cors.	And know that the suture of the belly is according to four methods, but two sutures are common ones that are necessary in sutures of other sores of the body.
E duas autras suturas proprias comunican a las autras plaguas, mays empero so mays proprias en la sutura del ventre.	And two other sutures are proper ones that communicate with other sores, but however they are more proper in the suture of the belly.
E yeu recomti a tu quascuna am exposicio e declaracio.	And I recommend to you whatever explanation and declaration.
Donc dic que quan la plagua es petita e es eyssit alcuna causa del budel per aquela, e es fayt dificil a reduzir aquel, lahoras aquo es en una de doas manieyras: o per parvitat de la disrupcio ayssi cum havem dit, o quan al budel es venguda inflacio per la frigiditat de l’ayre.	Therefore I say that when the sore is small and there is some cause from the belly for it, and it is made difficult to reduce that, then this is in one of two ways: either by the smallness of the disruption as we have said, or when the belly has become inflamed due to the coldness of the air.
E donc quan aquo es ayssi, lahora cove que tu scalfes aquel enayssi que tu submerges una sponga ho drap humit en aygua tebeza sola, o que coguas en aygua squinant, e cyperum, e spic, e embroques am aquela le budel entro que la imflacio sia resolvuda.	And therefore when that is so, you must then scrape it in such a way that you submerge a sponge or wet cloth in tepid water, or that you gather sanguinary, cypress, and spike, and embrocate with that on the belly until the inflammation is resolved.
E alcunas veguadas fa aquo vi en le qual ha stipticitat, e es milhor que la aygua sola en resolucio de la imflacio.	And sometimes I have found that this [treatment] has a certain sharpness, and it is better than just water alone in resolving the inflammation.
E donc cum tu vezes la imflacio esser resolvuda, lahoras tu humecta le budel am aygua en la qual es coyta altea e malvas, quar per aquo es alleujat le intrament de lu am pauca causa.	And therefore when the inflammation is resolved, then you must moisten the belly with water in which is cooked aloe and mulva, for by this it is alleviated the instrument of it with little cause.
Mays si es escusat le intrament de lu aprop aquesta curacio, lahoras scindeys la disrupcio un petit am strument am le qual so inscididas emorroydas.	But if the instrument of it is excused from this cure, then you must divide the disruption into small pieces with an instrument in which are incised emoryddos.
E la curacio primieyra es milhor, quan es propriada que no es seccio, e no sia occupacio a seccar aprop necessitat e defaliment.	And the first cure is better when it is proper and not necessary to cut, and there is no occupation to cut at the time of necessity and faintness.
Del instrument, sec se la forma de lu:	Of the instrument, it is necessary to know its shape.
La una partida de lu torta aguda, e l’autra partida no-acuta, e la extremitat subtil, e no sia am la subtilitat de spatum, abantz sia obtusa un pauc.	One part of it is bent acutely, and the other part is not acute, and the extremity is subtle, and it should not be too fine, but rather a little obtuse.
E donc cum la plagua es amplificada e yeys fora le budel, lahoras cove que la sua reduccio sia segon la forma de lu natural, en le sieu loc propri, si es possible sobre aquo, quar milhor es.	And therefore when the sore is enlarged and protrudes from the belly, then it is necessary that its reduction be according to its natural shape, in its proper place, if possible above that, for it is better.
Mays quan la disrupcio es ampla, e es en la partida pu bassa del ventre, lahoras cove que tu fassas jazer le malaute sobre le sieu dos, e pausa las suas cambas pus autas que·l sieu cap; e si es en la partida pus desus del ventre, lahoras tu pause le cap de lu e·l pietz pus autz que las partidas dejos.	But when the disruption is large and is in the lower part of the belly, then it is necessary that you make the patient lie on their back, and place their knees higher than their head; and if it is in the upper part of the belly, then you should support the head and feet so that they are higher than the remaining parts.
E semblantment si la disrupcio es en una de las doas partz del ventre, lahoras pausa la tua entencio e la tua consideracio tostemps en aysso per que la partida en la qual es la plagua sia pus auta que l’autra.	And similarly, if the disruption is in one of the two parts of the belly, then pause your attention and consideration always for that part where the sore is, so that it may be higher than the other.
E ayssi cove que tu aministres aquo en las plaguas grans e en las plaguas migieras.	And thus it is necessary that you administer this in great sores and in medium-sized sores.
E en las plaguas petitas, pausa aquo que es a tu preparat, e aprop fay que·l ministre sia entre las tuas mas pyatados, le qual tengua la disrupcio tota am la sua ma e ajusta las labias de lu, e aprop descuebre de aquela ad aquel que siec la sutura alcuna causa aprop autra.	And in small sores, pause this which is according to your preparation, and make sure that the one who administers it is among those most skilled, who has the disruption entirely with his hand and adjusts the lips of it, and makes sure to uncover from this to another, for which there is some reason.
E aquesta es la manieyra de sutura comuna: una que prenguas la agula, o comte de agula segon la cantitat de la amplitut de la plagua; e aprop layssa de la extremitat de la disrupcio del dit anular, e strenh la agula una, otre que tu no metas fiel en las doas extremitatz de la codena, am doas extremitatz del ciphac que es dejos la codena de las partidas dedintz, entro que fassas aquela penetrar de aquela partida; e tu ja has agreguadas doas extremitatz de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, e so faytas quatre ordes.	And this is the common method of suturing: take the needle, or count the needle according to the amount of amplitude of the sore; and then leave from the extremity of the disruption of the ring finger, and strengthen the needle once, or twice, so that you do not put faith in the two extremities of the cord, with the two extremities of the ciphac that is left behind the cord of the parts inside, until you make it penetrate from that part; and you have already added two extremities of the cord and two extremities of the ciphac, and so there are four orders.
E aprop strenh am fiel doble en le circuit de la agula, e alcunas veguadas de doas partz ensemps, e aprop agregua las doas labias e la plagua per agreguacio decent; e aprop layssa la grossitut del dit e fiqua una autra agulha en aquela, e aprop lia aquela am fiel ayssi cum fiest am la primieyra agulha; e no cesses far aquo si es necessitat am las agulhas entro que ajas complida tota la contriccio de la plagua.	And then strengthen the double thread with the needle, and sometimes on two parts together, and then add the two lips and the sore by decent addition; and then leave the thickness of the finger and put another needle in it, and then bind that with thread just like the first needle; and do not stop doing this if it is necessary with needles until you have completed all the contraction of the sore.
E sian las agulhas migieras entre groceza e subtilitat, quar las agulhas subtils mot leugierament insciden la carn; e las grossas so de dificil intrament en la codena, e donc per aquo cove que sian migieras en subtilitat e grosseza.	And the needles should be medium-sized between thickness and subtlety, for the thin needles only slightly cut into the flesh; and the thick ones are difficult to manipulate in the cord, and therefore it is necessary that they be medium-sized in subtlety and thickness.
E no cove que la agulha sia ficada en doas extremitatz de la codena propdana mot, per so que la carn no sia inscidida leugierament e que la plagua se huebra devant la sua consolidacio.	And it is not necessary to have the needle inserted in two extremities of the cord proper immediately, for fear that the flesh will be cut too little and the sore will be exacerbated before its consolidation.
E no sian prolonguadas de sutura per que la plagua no sia prohibida de consolidacio.	And the sutures should not be prolonged for fear that the sore will not be allowed to consolidate.
E aprop inscideys las extremitatz de las agulhas per so que no ledescan le malaute deves le sieu dormier; e pausaras sobre la sutura pulvils expanduts de tota partida, les quals tenguan las extremitatz de las agulhas; e layssa aquelas entro que sapias que la plagua ja es consolidada.	And then insert the extremities of the needles so that they do not disturb the patient's rest while sleeping; and place poultices spread out on all sides, which have the extremities of the needles; and leave those until you know that the sore is consolidated.
E aquestas specias de sutura am agulhas en cal manieyra es pus convenient en las plaguas petitas, quar habasta en la sutura de lor una agulha o doas o entorn aquelas.	And these types of suture with needles in this manner are more suitable for small sores, for they can be completed with one needle or two or around that.
Mays la segonda sutura es cominal: e es que tu aministres am sutura las quatre extremitatz, de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, en una veguada, am agulha en la qual sia fiel envolopat engual en subtilitat e grosseza.	But the second suture is common: and it is that you administer with a suture the four extremities, of the cord and two extremities of the ciphac, at once, with a needle in which there is thread wrapped around in subtlety and thickness.
E aprop quan am la agulha auras penetrat aquestas quatre extremitatz, reduzeys la agulha de aquela meteyssa partida de la qual comensest, per so que le fiel retrayt caja de la pus subirana partida a la plagua, per so que la sutura sia segon sutura de drap am la qual les draps so strengutz.	And then, when the needle has penetrated these four extremities, reduce it to that middle part where you started, so that the thread will retreat from the highest point of the sore and return to the wound, so that the suture is like a cloth suture with which the cloths are strengthened.
E pausa entre quascuna sutura la quantitat del gros del dit mendre.	And pause between each suture the amount of thickness of the finger.
E aquesta sutura sabo les homes.	And this suture is known to men.
E am tal sutura yeu cozegui la plagua la qual era accidida a un home en le sieu ventre le qual era stat plaguat am un cotel, e era la disrrumpcio de la plagua major de un palm, e era eyssit dels budels entorn dos palms del budel del mieg loc e era la disrupcio en le mieg del membre; e adonc yeu reduzegui aquel depus que le budel havia stat foro la plagua per xxiiii horas.	And with such a suture, I have closed the wound which had been inflicted on a man in his belly, which had been wounded with a knife, and was the disruption of a wound that was greater than one palm, and was situated around two palms from the navel, and was the disruption in the middle of the member; and then I reduced it after the belly had been opened for 24 hours.
E la plagua fo consolidada en le spazi de xv dias o entorn, e curegui aquel e es sanat; e aprop aquo visquec per motz ans, e es conversat en las suas disposicios.	And the wound was consolidated in the space of 15 days or around, and cured him; and then I watched over him for some months, and he converted to his former dispositions.
E les autres metges havian jutgat que no fora sanat; e per miracle foc, quar yeu no curegui aquel am enguent, quar era en loc en le qual enguent no era atrobat ni deguna medicina, mays pausegui sobre la plagua coto viel dos veguadas lo dia e ablucio assiduo am aygua de mel entro que foc sanat.	And other doctors had judged that he would not be cured; and by miracle, it was so, for you did not treat him with ointment, for there was no medicine or balm found in the place where the wound was, but instead you poured water from a honeycomb twice a day and performed frequent ablutions with water of honey until he was healed.
Mays yeu diyre dos specias de sutura proprias segon narracio de Paraula.	But you said two species of suture proper according to the narration of Paraula.
E es que tu comenses am sutura de la codena, e entrometas agulha de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz.	And then you began with the suture of the cord, and inserted the needle from the outer part to the inner part.
E donc cum la agulha penetra en la codena e en aquel meteys lacertz segon rectetut e en longetut de tot le cos, e layssa la extremita del ciphac en le qual has entromesa la agulha; e fay penetrar en la autra extremitat la agulha de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo en l’autra extremitat del mihat.	And then, as the needle pierces the cord and meets the lacertus in straightness and length along the entire body, and leaves the extremity of the ciphac where you have inserted the needle; and make it penetrate into the other extremity from the inner part to the outer part, in the other extremity of the mihat.
E don cum tu auras fayta aquela penetrar, lahoras tu fay aquela penetrar autra veguada en aquela meteyssa extremitat del mihat de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz; e leyssa la extramitat del ciphac que es en aquest latz, e fay penetrar la agulha en l’autra extremitat de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo.	And then, when you have made it penetrate, pause and make it penetrate again in that same extremity of the mihat from the outer part to the inner part; and leave the extremity of the ciphac that is in this place, and make the needle penetrate into the other extremity from the inner part to the outer part.
E fay penetrar am aquela la tua penetracio am la qual fas aquela penetrar en le ciphac en la extremitat del mirat la qual es en la partida de lu entro que tot aquel penetre.	And make it penetrate with that same penetration which you make it penetrate into the ciphac in the extremity of the mihat, and which is in the part of you until all that penetrates.
E aprop comensa de aquest meteys costat e cus aquel am la extremitat que es del ciphac en l’autra latz, e extratz la agulha de la codena la qual penetrec, e aprop redutz aquela en aquela codena e cos la extremitat del ciphac que es en l’autra costat am aquesta extramitat del mirat; e extratz aquela de la codena la qual es de part de lu.	And then, starting from this side, sew it with that same thread and attach the extremity of the ciphac to the other side, and remove the needle from the cord which was penetrated, and then reduce it into that same cord and sew the extremity of the ciphac that is on the other side to this extremity of the mihat; and remove it from the cord which is part of you.
E fay aquo una veguada e autra, e fay aquo una veguada aprop autre veguada entro que tu cozes tot aquo que es deforo segon aquel eysemple.	And do it once and then again, and do it once more in a similar way until you have sewn all that is outside according to this example.
E la suma de aquesta manieyra de sutura es que tu cozes am sutura de pellicies am la qual cozo las pels, enayssi que tu cozes le ciphac una veguada de la part de la extremitat de la codena, e que leysses aquela autra veguada entro que la ajas complida.	And the sum of this suture method is that you sew with a suture of pellicies in which you sew the skins, and thus you sew the ciphac once from the part of the extremity of the cord, and then leave it for another time until it is complete.
Mays la segonda specia de sutura propria la qual dieys eyssament Gualia , e aquest es de sermo de lu e per lu recomtat, es que tu cozas aquela segon semilitut am la qual alcus medicantz cozo aquela, enayssi que agreguan tota partida a la sua compar partida a lu convenient per natura; e aplican la extremitat de autre de lu e la extremitat del mirat al autra extremitat de lu, e aquo es fayt segon que yeu a tu recomti.	But the second species of suture proper which you say is called Gualia, and this is from Sermo de Lu and per Lu recommended, is that you sew according to semilitut with which some medicants sew it, and thus they add all parts to their corresponding part according to nature; and they apply the extremity of one side to the other side, and the extremity of the mirror to another extremity, and this is done as I recommend to you.
Cove que tu fiques la agulha en la extremitat del mirat a tu propdana de la partida deforo, e fassas aquela penetrar a la partida dedintz en aquel sol, e leysses dos extremitatz del ciphac; e aprop revolveys la agulha e fay aquela penetrar de foro a la dedintz en dos extremitatz del ciphac.	It is necessary that you place the needle in the extremity of the mirror at your own proper part from the outer part, and make it penetrate to the inner part in that same sole, and leave two extremities of the ciphac; and then turn back the needle and make it penetrate from outside to inside in two extremities of the ciphac.
E aprop revolveys aquelas cascunas, e fay penetrar quascunas de la partida dededintz entro a la partida deforo en dos extremitatz del mirat autras que so en le latz contrari.	And then turn back those two parts, and make each one penetrate from the inner part to the outer part in two other extremities of the mirror on the opposite side.
E aquesta manieyra de sutura es milhor de la sutura comuna leugiera, e es sutura de la qual precedic rememoracio.	And this method of suture is better than the common light suture, and it is the suture which I previously recommended.
Aquest es le sermo de Gualia	This is the sermon of Gualia.
E mays le diyssero alcus, sutura del ventre es rectificada am dos agulhas, so es que tu entrometas en aquestas a quascunas un fiel, e comensa am intromiccio de agulha de aquo que es deves tu, e fay aquela penetrar entro al autra latz segon sutura de aquels les quals cozo les cuers engualment.
