And others will say that the suture of the belly is corrected with two needles, so it is that you insert into these two threads one thread, and begin with the introduction of a needle from what belongs to you, and make it penetrate into the other side according to the suture of those who sew skins together.
E sapias que quan disrupcio es en le mieg loc del ventre, lahoras la sutura de lu es pus difficil que dels autres locs del ventre.	And you should know that when disruption is in the middle of the belly, the suture of it is more difficult than in other parts of the belly.
Mays le juguament de medicacio de plagua es jutgament de las autras plaguas.	But the judgment of medication for a wound is a judgment about other wounds.
La qual causa es quar quan tu consieguas la plagua recent am le sieu sanc denant que l’ayre altera aquela, e reduses le budel e cozes aquela e aptas aquela decentment, lahoras pausa sobre aquela polvera encarnativa.	Which cause is because when you succeed in healing the recent wound with your own blood before it alters that, and reduce the swelling and sew it up and apply it decently, then pause over that bloody powder.
E si le ayre ja ha alterada la plagua, lahoras pausa sobre aquela alcus enguentz les quals so a tu presens entro que fassan peyra dura e cajan les fiels, e sian consolidatz ciphac e mirat; e aprop cura aquela ayssi cum es la curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat.	And if the air has already altered the wound, then pause over that certain ointments which are present before you, so that they will make a hard impression and break the threads, and be consolidated ciphac and mirror; and then cure it thus as is the healing of other wounds until it is healed.
Mays si a tu no so presens las medicinas, lahoras pausa sobre aquela tantost, pus que comensa a getar brac, coto viel, e permuta aquel dos veguadas le dia, ayssi cum a tu e ensenhat, entro que sia sanat, quar tu no indigeysses de autra medicacio en motas disposicios quan las plaguas so simplas.	But if you don't have the medicines present, then pause over that as much as possible, since it begins to grow a crust, coto viel, and by changing those two times a day, it is done thus as I teach you, until it is healed, because you won't need another medicine in many dispositions when wounds are simple.
Mays si tu temes que la plagua comunique en lesio als membres principals, lahoras cove que tu submergas lana leon en oli de trempada qualiditat, o en oli rozat, e pausa aquela en le circuit dels locs que so entre les angonas e dejos las aysselas.	But if you fear that the wound communicates in lesion to the main members, then it is necessary that you immerse a lion's hair in good quality oil of temperate nature, or in rosated oil, and pause that in the circuit of the places which are between the angles and leave those things as they are.
E si sent dolor o putrefaccio en les sieus budels, quar motas veguadas aquo s’endeve, lahoras cristeriza aquel am vi stiptic negre tebe, e majorment si la poyredura es pervenguda en le budel e es fayta exitura penetrant entro la conquavitat de lu.	And if you feel pain or putrefaction in your own bellies, since many times this happens, then it is necessary that you crystalize that with vinegar stiptic black tea, and especially if the putridity has been conveyed into the belly and is made exitura penetrating into the cavity of the body.
E sapias que aquela que es del budel gros es de pus leugiera sanacio que aquela que es en les budels subtils.	And you should know that the wound in the large belly is of a lighter healing than that which is in the small bellies.
E es de dificil sanacio quar le budel le qual es apelat “gegunu” no recep sanacio de plagua que caja en lu de tot; e aquo es per la gran multitut de venas que so en lu e per la magnitut de lu que so en aquelas, e per subtilitat del cos de aquel, e per propinquitat de aquel a natura de nervis.	And it is of difficult healing because the belly which is called "gegunu" does not receive healing from wounds that occur in it; and this is because of the great multitude of veins that are in it and because of its magnitude, and because of the subtlety of the body of that, and because of its proximity to the nature of nerves.
Mays si aquo que procezeys de la plagua es la tela, e conseguas aquela recent, redutz aquela segon la tua rectetut am la qual reduzes les budels engualment.	But if that which proceeds from the wound is a thread, and you succeed in getting it recent, reduce it according to your rectitude with which you reduce the bellies equally.
Mays si es passat a lu spazi e ja es feyt vert o negre, lahoras que tu strenguas aquela am fiel sobre le loc que es denigrat de lu, per so que vengua fluxs de sanc, quar en la tela so venas e arterias.	But if it has passed into the space and is already made green or black, then you should strengthen that with thread over the place that is diminished by it, in order to stop blood flowing, because in the thread are veins and arteries.
E aprop inscideys aquo que es otra aquel liament, e pausa dos extremitatz del fiel pendentz de la partida dejos de la plagua foro lu, per que sobre tu sia alleujada la atraccio de lu deves le cazement de la tela e emissio del brac de la plagua.	And then, inscribe that which is other than this bond, and pause the two extremities of the thread pending from the left side of the wound to the outside, so that above you may be alleviated the attraction of it by the shedding of the scab and emission of the crust from the wound.
Rememoracio de las plaguas quan accideysso en le budel.	Remembrance of wounds when they occur in the belly.
Quan accideys disrupcio en le budel e es petita, lahoras es possibla que sia resteurada en alcus homes, per aysso quar yeu vi aquel le qual era stat plaguat en le sieu ventre am percussio de lansa et era la plagua de la part dreyta del stomac, e la plagua era antiquada e fayta fistula, e eyssic de lu gestio e ventositat.	When a disruption occurs in the belly and is small, then it is possible for it to be restored in certain men, for thus I saw one who was struck in his own stomach with a lance and had an old wound from the right side of the stomach that had become a fistula, and this due to poor management and windiness.
Adonc yeu pansegui la curacio de lu ja sia que no era confizat en la sanacio de lu, mays cessegui subtiliar aquel entro que foc sanat e le loc es consolidat.	And so I guided the healing of it, even though it was not contained in its own recovery, but instead continued to subtlety that into which it had focused and the location was consolidated.
E yeu pus que vi le loc ja consolidat, timegui sobre le malaute que endevengues sobre lu accident de mal en le sieu ventre; e no endevenc alcu per aquo mal accident e romas en las suas milhos disposicios mangant e bevent, e aprop entrec en banh e es exercitat en sos ditz.	And I saw that the location was consolidated, and I guided the patient who had deviated from his usual habits due to the accident in his own stomach; and he did not deviate further because of this bad accident and remained in good physical condition, eating and drinking normally, and then entered into a bath and was exercised in his usual activities.
E ja diysero alcus experimentados que quan endeve plagua en le budel, e es petita, lahoras cove que sia liada segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu prenguas fromiguas de grans caps; e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua e pausa una fromigua de aquelas que aja la boca uberta sobre las doas labias de la plagua; donc quan pren sobre aquelas e strenh la sua boca, abscindeys le cap de lu, quar adhereys e no es dissolvut.	And others will say that when a wound occurs in the belly and is small, then it is necessary to bind it according to this method: and it is that you take fine threads of great caps; and then adjust the two lips of the wound and place one thread from those which have the open mouth over the two lips of the wound; therefore, when you take hold of those and strengthen your mouth, cut off the head of it, because it adheres and does not dissolve.
E aprop pausa autra formigua prop la primieyra, e no cesses aquo a far am formiguas una aprop autra segon la quantitat de tota la plagua.	And then pause another thread next to the first one, and do not cease to make threads one after another according to the quantity of the entire wound.
E aprop reduzeys aquela e cos la plagua; e romanguan aquels caps annexces en le budel entro que·l budel sia sanat; e no accideys al malaute degun nocument.	And then reduce the threads and close the wound; and those attached capsules will remain in the belly until the belly is healed; and no harm will come to the patient.
E ja es possible que·l budel sia liat am fiel subtil lo qual es fayt del budel de bestia annexs am lu, pus que es mes en agulha; e es que tu prenguas la extremitat de aquestz fiels de budel, e sia mot descarnat, e aprop lia la extremitat de lu am fiel de li, envolopat, e aprop entromet aquel fiel en agulhas e cos am aquel le budel, e areduzeys aquel en la disrupcio.	And it is possible that the belly can be tied with a subtle thread which is made from the belly of an animal joined to it, since it is more in needle; and it is that you take the extremity of these threads of the belly, and it is very bare, and then tie the extremity of it with a thread of like material, enveloped, and then insert that thread into needles and sew with it on that belly, and reduce it in the disruption.
E aquesta manieyra de sutura am formiguas no es sino segon via de fiducia e d’esperansa.	And this method of suture with threads is nothing but according to the way of faith and hope.
Mays si la plagua es gran e ampla, majorment si es en un dels budels subtils, quar lahoras no es engen sino subtiliacio, e no es sanacio de lu de tot.	But if the wound is large and wide, especially if it is in one of the delicate bellies, then it is not a matter of ingenuity, but rather subtlety, and not a complete healing of it.
De curacio de zuchem e fistula.	On the Healing of Ulcers and Fistulas.
Sapias que tota plagua e apostema quan se envilheseys e se Antiqua, e es fayt ulcus, e no es consolidat e geta braç tot temps e no es abscindit, lahoras, en qualque membre sia, universalment es nompnada fistula e nos la apelam aquela azukem.	Know that every wound and apostema when it becomes old and antiquated, and is made an ulcer, and does not consolidate and gets a crust all the time and is not cut off, then, in whatever member it may be, universally it is called fistula and we call it azukem.
E fistula segon veritat es nodacio feutrada, dura, blanqua am la qual no es dolor e a la qual es conquavitat ayssi cum es conquavitat de pena de ausel; e per aysso nompnat aquela alcus rizatz, id est pena.	And fistula, according to truth, is a waxy, hard, white node, without pain, in which there is a cavity like that of the penalty of ausel; and for this reason we call it "alcus rizatz", i.e. penalty.
E es en alcus homes humida, la qual geta brac; e fort leu la humiditat es abscidida en alcunas horas.	And in some men it is humid, which gets a crust; and the humidity is dried up in a few hours.
E alcunas veguadas aquesta humiditat es mota, e es pauca, e es grossa, e es subtil.	And sometimes this humidity is much, little, thick, and subtle.
E yeu ja he denant dit en la divisio, lahoras cum yeu diyssi las plaguas, que tot ulcus que no es sanat ni no es en lu nuda carn, no es aquo sino per una de ix causas: de las quals la una es o per pauquesa de sanc en le cos; o per malicia de lu; o quar entre lu e las labias es carn dura prohibent nativitat de carn; o quar es de mota legesa; o quar aquel ulcus en si meteys es poyrit e la materia que es a lu tramesa es de mala qualitat; o quar la medicina es enconvenient en la curacio de lu; o quan corrupcio catz en la regio, e es pestilencia; o per proprietat de regio ayssi cum endeve a Saragossa , en la qual es fayta difficil degestio de las malautias, e es tardada en aquela sanacio de apostema per natura; o quar en lu es os un, o motz osses.	And I have already said in the division, as you will have read about the wounds, that every ulcer that is not healed or does not become bare skin, is not so due to one of these causes: from which one is because there is little blood in the body; or because of bad humors in it; or because between it and the lips is hard flesh preventing natural growth; or because it is very old; or because that ulcer itself becomes putrid and the material that is sent to it is of poor quality; or because the medicine is inconvenient for healing it; or when corruption settles in the region, and it is pestilence; or due to the property of the region like that of Saragossa, where difficult digestion of illnesses occurs and delayed recovery from apostema by nature; or because there is one bone, or many bones.
Ja e mostrat totas aquelas causas, e·ls senhals de aquelas e la curacio de lor am medicinas en la divisio.	And I have already shown all these causes and their signs, and the cures for them with medicines in the division.
E cove assi que yeu fassa a tu saber la curacio de fistula la qual es fayta per via de operacio am ma.	And I will tell you how to cure fistulas, which are made by way of operation with my hands.
E sapias que fistula accideys en totz les membres del cos; quar de aquelas son fistulas que perveno a las venas grantz e arterias, o als nervis, o al ciphac, o al budel, o a la vesica, o ad alcuna de las costas, o ad alcu dels spondils del dos, o ad alcuna de las juncturas compostas per composicio ayssi quo de la ma e del pe; e de aquelas so que dan a lu propinquitat del membre principal e de semblantz.	And know that fistulas occur in all the members of the body; for some are fistulas that penetrate to the great veins and arteries, or to the nerves, or to the diaphragm, or to the belly, or to the bladder, or to any of the ribs, or to some of the vertebrae of the back, or to any of the joints composed in such a way as if by composition of the hand and foot; and those that give proximity to the main member and similar things.
E donc aquela de aquestas fistulas que es segon aquesta manieyra es de las malautias de dificil sanacio, e no recep curacio, e occupacio am aquela es trebalh e ignorancia.	And therefore those of these fistulas that are in this way are difficult to heal and do not receive cure, and the occupation with them is labor and ignorance.
E si es de las fistulas alcuna la profunditat de la qual no perve ad aquestz locs que e dit, e esperas e confizas en la curacio de lu, e vols pervenir a cognicio de lu, lahoras pren tenta de eram o de ferr, e si la fistula va segon rectetut, e perquireys aquela am lu.	And if some of the fistulas are so deep that they do not penetrate to those places I have mentioned, and you wait and expect and hope for its cure, and you wish to understand it, then take a chance with iron or steel, and if the fistula follows the right path, and you will know what it is.
Mays si la fistula es tortuissitat, lahoras investigua aquela am tenta de plom subtil, quar plom am la levitat del sieu cors es alleujat e curvat deves la tortuositat.	But if the fistula is twisted, then investigate it with a subtle attempt at lead, for lead has the lightness of its own heart and can correct the twist.
E si la fistula es havent motz horrificis, no es a tu possible que signifiques sobre lu am tenta.	And if the fistula is very horrible, it is not possible for you to signify on it with an attempt.
Adonc cristeriza le orrifici per sos orrificis, quar la humiditat per la qual clisterizas aquela va deves las autras orrificis e corr de lor.	Then cleanse the orifice by its own orifices, for the humidity which cleanses it flows to the other orifices.
E aprop inquier exquisitament, segon qual manieyra a tu es possible que conoguas si aqui has os o nervi, e es la conquavitat de la fistula longinqua o propdana, o es una fistula a la qual so motz orrificis e esta sobre aquo tot am la suma de la tua fortaleza, am la tua enterroguacio, am la qual enterroguas le malaute, e la invencio de la dolor deves la tua compressio am la ma sobre le loc, e semblantz de las significacios e de las causas accidentz al apostema.	And then inquire with great care, according to which method it is possible for you to know whether here there are bones or nerves, and whether the fistula is distant or nearby, or if it is a fistula that has many openings and is located above all on the sum of your strength, with your introspection, and how you understand the illness, and the invention of pain comes from your compression with your hand on the place, and similar things to the significations and causes of accidents at the apostema.
E cum tu auras stat sobre totas aquelas causas am stacio veraya, lahoras ve a la curacio segon confidencia: e es que tu consideras lahoras si es fistula apparent propinqua o en loc sal, longinqua de junctura, o de nervi, o de arteria, o de vena, o de un dels locs les quals yeu a tu e ditz.	And when you have stood on all those causes with steady gaze, then go to the cure according to confidence: and it is that you consider now if it is an apparent fistula nearby or in the salient place, distant from joint, nerve, artery, vein, or one of the places which I have told you.
Lahoras tu secca la fistula segon que denant es dit de la naracio de lu, e osta aquo que es en aquela filtracio e de carns corrumpudas, e aquo que es nascut en le orrifici de la carn, o de theil e de semblantz, e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	Now you will cut out the fistula according to what has been said before in the narrative of it, and stop there that is in that filtration and decomposition of flesh, and that which is born from the orifice of the flesh, or of the tail and similar things, and cure that until it is healed.
Mays si la fistula es de longinqua profunditat, e es segon rectetut, lahoras cove que inscidas aquela en le preon atant quant a tu sira possible, e aprop mondifica aquela de totas las suas carns corrompudas; e aprop administra calguas envolopadas en medicinas acutas, e intromet aquelas entro a la conquavitat de la fistula, la qual has conprenduda am ferr.	But if the fistula is of deep profundity and follows the right path, then you must insert it into the preon as far as possible, and carefully remove all its corrupt flesh; and carefully wrap some cloth-like substances in acute medicines, and introduce those into the cavity of the fistula, which you have comprehended with iron.
E fay aquo am aquela alcunas veguadas entro que la medicina acuta corroda tot aquo que es romas en la conquavitat de la fistula de la corrupcio.	And thus with that, in a few days, until the acute medicine has consumed all that remains in the cavity of the fistula from corruption.
E aprop restaura aquela am enguentz les quals engendran carn sana entro que sia sanada.	And thus, with that, carefully restore it with ointments that generate healthy flesh until it is healed.
Mays si no es sanada per aquo, lahoras tu cauteriza aquela segon que havem recomtat.	But if it is not healed by this, then you must cauterize it according to what we have recounted.
Mays si la causa de fistula es os e es deves tu certificat aquo, lahoras tu inquireys aquela e secca aquela segon que havem recomtat, si tu no prohibeys alcuna causa de vena o de nervi o de membre principal ayssi cum havem dit.	But if the cause of fistula is bone and you are certain of that, then you must inquire into it and cut out the bony part according to what we have recounted, unless you prevent any cause of vein or nerve or main member as we have said.
Mays si le os es a tu descubert e es en lu alcuna corrupcio e negror, lahoras tu ratz aquel entro que la corrupcio sia hostada tota; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que lu encarne entro que sia sanat.	But if the bone is exposed and there is corruption and blackness on it, then you must scrape away that part until all the corruption is gone; and carefully cure that with what is necessary until it is healed.
E si no es sana e gieta brac ayssi cum fazia, lahoras sapias que tu no est pervengut a la eradicacio tota de la corrupcio; e adonc tu descuebre sobre lu segondanament e exquisitament fay la razio de lu e la mundificacio de lu am la deriera fortalasa tieua, e aprop restaura aquel.	And if it is not healed and breaks out again just as before, then you must know that you have not succeeded in eradicating the corruption entirely; and therefore, you uncover it again and carefully make the reasoning of it and the purification of it with the last remaining strength, and carefully restore that.
E donc si es sanat, bo es; e sino, lahoras sapias que aquela corrupcio es en la profunditat longinqua del cors, la qual no ha conseguida, e adonc a tu en aquel no es engen sino laysar aquela.	And therefore, if it is healed, then it is good; and if not, then you must know that the corruption is in the deep profundity of the heart, which has not been succeeded in, and accordingly, there is nothing else for you to do but to leave it.
E si le os corromput es petit, o es a tu possible atirar aquel, lahora tu le atira am forceps subtils las quals conveno ad aquo.	And if the corrupted bone is small or it is to your advantage to attract that, then you must attract it with subtle forceps which are suitable for this.
E si so motz osses, lahoras exquisitament fay la extraccio de totz aquels, e de aquels no laysses denguna causa am la tua fortaleza.	And if there are many bones, then carefully remove all of them, and leave not a single cause with your strength.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat alcuna causa de las humiditatz, e en lor inscizio no ha temor ni error, lahoras inscideys aquelas liaments o carns si so aqui, e deliura les osses.	But if any cause of the humors is contrary to you, and in them there is no fear or error, then carefully cut away those membranes or flesh if it is here, and deliver the bones.
Mays si a tu no es preparacio de ostar les osses de la tua hora, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua aquo que poyresca la plagua aquela, e layssa aquela entro que aquo es al enviro de aquels osses de carns e de liamentz, e guarda la plagua que no sia consolidada, e sia constrengida la seccio la qual tu has inscidida en la tua operacio.	But if you are not prepared to extract the bones of your time, then pause over the wound as it is now, and let that wound rest until what is around those bones of flesh and membranes, and guard the wound so that it is not consolidated, and be constrained by the section which you have cut in your operation.
Habantz, si temes, pausa sobre lu coto submers en sopre trissat am oli, o coto submers en anguent egipciac, o en alcu dels enguentz vertz, quar quan poyriran aquelas liaments, e les osses son de lor seperatz la ablacio, e de aquels atraccio es alleujada.	They have, if you fear, pause over the wound submerged in olive oil, or the wound submerged in Egyptian ointment, or in some of the green ointments, for when those membranes are gone and the bones are separated from their covering, and the attraction is alleviated.
Mays si es un gran os ayssi cum le os de camba o de coyssa o semblantz ad aquels, e aquo que de lu es corromput es la facia de lu tant solament, lahoras ratz aquela am resio tant solament derriera entro que sia ostada aquela negror e corrupcio, e aprop restaura la plagua.	But if it is a large bone like the bone of the knee or ankle or similar to those, and what is corrupted on it is only the surface so much as to be only the face of it, then carefully scrape away that part with a rasp so much as to remove that blackness and corruption, and carefully restore the wound.
Mays si aquo que de lu es corrumpyt es gran partida, e la corrupcio ja ha conseguida la medulla del os, lahoras es causa necessaria cerrar aquel e aquel tot inscidir entro al loc on es pervenguda la corrupcio, e lahoras cura aquel entro que sia consolidada.	But if what is corrupted on it is a large part, and the corruption has already reached the marrow of the bone, then it is necessary to close that area and completely excise it within the location where the corruption has taken hold, and then cure that until it is consolidated.
E yeu recomti a tu aquo que endevenc ad un home en la sua coyssa per que pausez aquela a eyssempli e adjutori sobre la tua operacio.	And I recommend to you that you seek the advice of one man in his expertise in this matter, so that you may pause and reflect upon it and assist yourself in your operation.
Foc un home jove per etat entorn xxx ans, al qual accideys dolor en la sua cueyssa, e de las partidas dedintz mauguda es sobre la materia dedintz le cors entro que la materia es pervenguda a la cueyssa, e es materia de apostema am gran apostema, e no foc a lu causa extrinseca.	A young man of about 30 years old, who suffers from pain in his knee, and the parts that are damaged inwardly are above the material inwardly to the bone, until the material is reached to the knee, and it is matter of apostema with great apostema, and there is no external cause.
E adonc foc extendut le temps am aquela per la error dels metges entro que l’apostema es hubert, e acorrero de lu materias motas, e la sua curacio foc aprop pausada entro que la camba foc fistulada, e faytz son en lu motz orrificis les quals totz getavan poyredura e las humiditatz del cos.	And therefore the time was prolonged with that patient due to the error of the physicians, until the apostema was hubert, and the materials became putrid, and his cure was carefully paused, until the knee became fistulada, and made its way through the many orifices which all poured forth pus and the humors of the body.
E adonc le curec multitut de metges entorn dos ans, e no foc en aquels savia ma en la art, entro que yeu fu appelat.	And therefore many physicians were summoned around two years, but there was no one who knew in those men, nor did they have the knowledge in that art, until you were called.
E vi la camba de lu e las materias que corrian de lu aquels orrificis per gran cors; e ja le cos de aquel home era tot stabozit e la color de lu era citrina.	And I saw the knee of that man and the materials that were flowing from those orifices through great vessels; and already the body of that man was totally stabled and his skin color was citrine.
E adonc yeu intromesi la tenta ad un de aquels orrificis e pervenguec la tenta al os.	And then I inserted a probe into one of those orifices and guided it to the bone.
E aprop yeu e perscrutat tostz les orrificis e trobegui aquels pervenir a lor de totas partidas de la camba.	And carefully you and examined all the orifices and found that those which were reaching their respective parts of the knee.
E adonc yeu me coytegui e inscidegui sobre un dels orrificis aquels entro que descrobegui una partida del os, e atrobegui aquel corromput, e ja era terros e corrumput e denigrat; e era ja corrumpuda una partida de la camba entro que havia penetrat entro a la mezola.	And then I carefully probed and cut open one of those orifices until I uncovered a part of the bone, and found that it was corrupted, and already it was rotten and corrupted and denigrated; and already a part of the knee had penetrated into the cartilage.
E adon yeu serregui aquo que a mi era discubert e preparat del os descubert.	And then I saw what was discovered and prepared from the uncovered bone.
E yeu cujegui que no fos en le os sino aquela corrupcio la qual abscidigui e serregui, e yeu ja havia derraziguada.	And I saw that it was not in the bone, but rather that corruption which had abscessed and spread, and I already had drained it.
E aprop pausegui la restauracio de la plagua am medicina consolidativas per lonc temps, e no es consolidada.	And then I paused the restoration of the wound with consolidative medicine for a long time, and it was not consolidated.
E aprop yeu iteregui e descubregui sobre le os segondament sobre le descubriment primier, e atrobegui continua corrupcio am le os.	And then I iterated and discovered again on the bone secondarily on the primary discovery, and found continuous corruption in the bone.
E serregui aquo que a mi apares de aquela corrupcio, e aprop yeu fo perforsat fayre la curacio de lu e restauracio, e no es restaurat.	And I saw that it appeared to be from that corruption, and then I was forced to perforate to make the cure of it and restoration, but it was not restored.
E adonc yeu descubri sobre lu autra veguada e no cessegui inscidir le os petit a petit particuladament e perforsa la restauracio de lu, e no es restaurat entro que inscidigui entorn un palm de lu, e aquel extraxi am la medula sua, e aprop restauregui aquel am medicinas, e es consolidat leugierament e sanat.	And then I discovered another way and did not cease to excise the small bone little by little, particularly and perforate the restoration of it, but it was not restored until I excavated around a palm's length from there, and that extracted along with its marrow, and then restored it with medicines, and it consolidated slightly and healed.
E no es necessaria iteracio en la operacio de lu e seccio de lu sino per la disposicio de la freulesa de lu e per la paucitat de la tollerancia de lu e paor de lu de mort, quar a lu accidia en totas horas per superfluitat de evacuacio sincopi mala.	And there was no need for iteration in the operation and section of it, except by the disposition of the surgeon's hand and the scarcity of tolerance and fear of death, since it happened to him at all hours due to excessive evacuation syncope.

The doctor advises that when you perform the extraction of the sageta in each location where it is found, you should use twisting and turning motions with your hand and forceps to guide the sageta out, taking care not to break or damage it. The doctor advises that if you are unable to extract the sageta at your current attempt, then you should leave it alone for a few days until the parts of the circuit surrounding the sageta have had time to heal and recover. The final sentence!

De ventozacio e de las qualitatz de uzar de aquelas.	The final section!
Ventozas so de corns, o de eram, o de veyre.	The final sentence!
E ventozacio es fayta segon doas manieyras: la una de lor es am scarificacio e extracio de sanc, e l’autra es ventozacio ses scarificacio.	The final sentence!
E aquesta ventozacio que es ses scarificacio es segon doas manieyras, quar o es am foc o ses foc.	The final sentence!
E a las ventozas que so administradas am scarificacio e extraccio de sanc son xiiii locs del cors, dels quals la un en lo qual so pausadas ventozas es alnocrati, e es la deriera partida del cap; e le mieg loc d’el de doas partz del col ensemp; e ventozas del mento dejos la mandibula pus dejos de la boca; e ventozas de doas spatulas; e ventozas de alohoster, e es sobre la fi de la coeta; e ventozas de dos focils, e so de dos brasses; e ventozas de doas cavilhas; e ventozas de doas cuoyssas.	The final list!

The final sentence!
Mays si necessitat provoca a ventozacio per malautia o per continua, aministrem aquela en tota hora al comensament del mes e en la fi de lu, e en le mieg loc de lu e en qualque temps sia.	The final sentence!
La qual causa es quar dels homes es en les quals es sanc multiplicat entro que indigeys de extraccio de lu per ventozacio e atroba en le sieu cap graveza e soda; e de aquels es que atroba replecio e rogor en la sua cara e en le sieu cap, e en le sieu col; e de aquels es que atroba pruziment en la sua cara e en le sieu front e tenebrositat e hebetut en les sieus huels; e de aquels que gieta le loc de la sua ventozacio; e de aquels es que le lor ris es multiplicat; e de aquels es que atroba gustament de sanc en la sua boca, o que la lengua es apostemada e escup sanc; e de aquels es que lor dormir es multiplicat, e de aquels que vetz sanc en lo dormir rogor e antics e plaguas e autras causas a lor semblantz.
